I have known Brian Shannon for years and have been impressed with his clear-headed, structured approach to technical analysis.In his latest book he takes trader education to a new level,elaborating how to make use of Anchored VWAP(AVWAP)and explaining in detail how and why it is a valuable trading tool.Each chapter itself is anchored by
specific,practical objectives and charts and examples nicely illustrate the trading ideas. Particularly insightful is a description of how institutions execute large orders in the
stock market and an explanation of how AVWAP can help traders take advantage of
their actions.Also quite helpful is an account of how AVWAP can help traders exploit    breakout patterns and trends.This is a clearly written text that can benefit developing and experienced traders alike.
Brett N.Steenbarger,Ph.D.Author of The Daily Trading Coach @steenbab Brian Shannon takes an esoteric institutional trading tool called volume-weighted
average price(VWAP)and brings it current for retail investors using an anchoring
technique(AVWAP).He thoroughly breaks down the market mechanics of how large
institutions use VWAP and why it's important.Then,Shannon presents an expanded set of use cases for the retail trader that builds on the anchoring work of Paul Levine,PhD.  The entire book is written in plain English and rooted in a common sense approach that  pervades Shannon's cannon of trading tutelage.

FORWARD
It has been estimated that during the year 2020,some ten million people opened a brokerage account for the first time.In the first six months of
2021,another ten million new brokerage accounts were opened.If the
statistics are to be believed,then in a span of eighteen months we've seen the start of the investing careers of over twenty million Americans.
According to the brokerage firm Charles Schwab,approximately 15%of its 31.5 million retail customers first got into the stock market in 2020.The
timing,frankly,has  not  been  great.
While the pandemic gave rise to a generational boom in curiosity about
investing and trading,the aftermath has been a punishing experience for most participants.In attempting to estimate the damage of 2022's bear
market,JPMorgan Chase researchers have determined that in the first ten  months of the year,the typical personal portfolio has fallen by 44%.Among some of the younger,more aggressive traders in this newly arrived class,    you can imagine the losses being significantly worse.The anecdotes and
chatter make it abundantly clear that we now have millions of people
risking their money each day in the stock market while very few ofthem
FORWARD
据估计，2020年有大约一千万人在首次开设经纪账户。2021年上半  年，又新增了一千万个经纪账户。如果统计数据可信，那么在十八   个月的时间里，我们见证了超过两千一百万名美国人的投资生涯的   开始。根据经纪公司Charles      Schwab的数据，其3150万零售客户   中约有15%的人在2020年首次进入股市。坦率地说，时机并不理想。
尽管疫情激发了人们对投资和交易的代际热潮，但其后续影响对大   多数参与者来说却是一场严酷的考验。在试图估算2022年熊市造成  的损失时，摩根大通的研究人员确定，在该年的前十个月里，典型  的个人投资组合下跌了44%。对于这个新出现的群体中一些更年轻、 更激进的交易者来说，你可以想象他们的损失会严重得多。轶事和   闲聊使人们清楚地意识到，现在有数百万人每天都在股市中冒险，
而其中很少有人
have any education or strategy beyond reading chat rooms and pressing buttons.
Undoubtedly,in the aftermath of a financial market plunge,people will be out seeking better information about investing.The desire for education   always comes after a lot of money has been lost,never beforehand.And
that's perfectly normal.Every generation has to learn for themselves.The stories ofveterans or the lessons found in books will never be able to
replace the power of firsthand experience with losses.
Many of the new entrants will make the decision that they'd like to do a lot   less overall and leave more of their results in the hands of the market gods. These investors willeventually discover ishares and Vanguard,the SPY
and the QQQ.They'll make simpler decisions about asset allocation and let   the future take care of itself.They'll buy index funds and pursue dollar cost averaging strategies and find something else to talk about at backyard
barbecues now that the desire to trade stocks has come and gone.
But not everyone.
For many,it will become more than just a hobby or a passing fad.The
passion to trade and be involved in the markets willbe a lifelong pursuit.A daily activity.In some cases,a calling.Among the generation of 2020's new  market entrants,millions of people willfind themselves in this category of active trader.And they're going to be on the hunt for methods,strategies    and insights that can help themimprove what they're doing.They'llbe in   search of structure and meaning.Actual expertise.Rules.Signal.Clarity.
One can only hope that they'll encounter the teachings of Brian Shannon, as early as possible,upon theirjourney.
有任何教育或策略，除了阅读聊天室和按按钮之外。
毫无疑问，在金融市场暴跌之后，人们会出来寻找更好的投资信息。 对教育的渴望总是在大量金钱损失之后才会出现，永远不会提前。
这是完全正常的。每一代人都要自己学习。老兵的故事或书中找到 的教训永远无法取代亲身经历损失的力量。
许多新进入者会做出决定，他们希望整体上做得更少，并将更多结果 交给市场神明。这些投资者最终会发现iShares和Vanguard、SPY
和QQQ。 他们会就资产配置做出更简单的决定，让未来自行处理。
他们会购买指数基金，追求美元成本平均策略，并在交易股票的渴望 已经过去后，在backyard       barbecues  上找到其他话题谈论。
但并非所有人。
对许多人来说，这会不仅仅是一个爱好或一时的风尚。参与市场的交 易热情将是一种终身的追求。一种日常活动。在某些情况下，一种使 命。在2020年新进入市场的人群中，数百万人会发现自己属于积极
交易者这一类别。他们将会寻找能够帮助他们改进所做的事情的方法、 策略和见解。他们会寻找结构、意义。真正的专业知识。规则。信号。
清 晰 。
人们只能希望在他们旅途中尽早遇到布莱恩 ·沙恩的教诲。
I first became aware of Brian Shannon toward the end of the aughts decade, in the aftermath of the Great Financial Crisis,when I began writing publicly about stocks and investing on my blog.Then,like now,millions of people
were in search ofgood answers about investing and trading.They watched as some of the most storied investment houses on Wall Street had blown
themselves to smithereens,having ignored even the most basic tenets of   risk management in their own proprietary trading.Was there anyone else out there worth listening to?Worth trusting?The more you'd ask this
question of professionaltraders,the more you'd hear Brian's name.Again and again,the people who knew referred to Alphatrends and Brian
Shannon.
Intrigued,I decided to take a look at what all the buzz was about.Brian was popular among traders on social media,but so were a lot of people.
Watching his early videos,made in the infancy of YouTube,you could tell
there was something meaningful going on,with all kinds ofinstruction and  narration as the screen flashed upon his latest charts and trading setups.    He had an explanation for why he was doing things,and there was a depth   of detail going into his decisions each day you simply did not see elsewhere. His work spoke for itselfandhis popularity as both a teacher and a leader    was not surprising.Brian Shannon is a trader's trader.His influence can be  seen and heard among trading communities around the world.
So Ihad become a fan of Brian's work before meeting him in person.We
eventually got together and bonded over a powerful idea about there being truth in price.Honesty in what people actually do in the markets versus
what they say they do.Price isn't always right but it is absolutely always
the reality ofwhat's taken place that day.Undeniable.So there we were-
he,a trader,and me,an investor,working on very different timeframes and behaving quite differently in the markets each day.But we agreed that
there is meaning to be distilled from the actual buying and selling of real
我第一次意识到布莱恩 ·沙恩是在零点年代末期，在大萧条之后，当
我开始在博客上公开撰写关于股票和投资的文章时。那时，现在一样，' 成千上万的人在寻找关于投资和交易的好答案。他们看着华尔街最负
盛名的投资公司把自己炸得粉碎，因为他们在自己的自营交易中甚至  忽略了最基本的风险管理原则。还有其他人值得倾听吗?值得信任吗? 你问得越多专业交易员这个问题，就越会听到布莱恩的名字。一次又  一次，那些知情者都提到了阿尔法趋势和布莱恩 ·沙恩。
感到好奇，我决定看看这一切的喧嚣是怎么回事。Brian  在社交媒体 上的交易者中很受欢迎，但很多人也是如此。观看他早期制作的
YouTube  视频时，你能看出正在发生一些有意义的事情，屏幕上不 断闪现他的最新图表和交易设置，伴随着各种指导和解说。他对自己 的行为有解释，并且每天在决策上的详细程度是你在其他地方看不到 的。他的工作本身就足以证明一切，他作为教师和领导者的受欢迎程 度也就不足为奇了。Brian  Shannon是交易者的交易者。他的影响 力在世界各地的交易社区中可见可闻。
所以，在见到他之前，我已经成了布莱恩作品的粉丝。我们最终走到一起，并在一个强大的   想法上建立了联系——价格中存在真相。人们实际在市场上做的事情，与他们的说法之间的   诚实对比。价格并不总是正确的，但它绝对永远是那天发生的事情的现实。不可否认。所以， 我们就在那里——他，一个交易员，而我， 一个投资者，我们在不同的时间框架上工作，每   天在市场上表现也截然不同。但我们同意，从实际买卖中可以提炼出意义。我们两人都更倾   向于尊重价格的概念，而不是跟随我们的感觉。我最终内化了并采纳了他最著名的俗语之一：
只有价格会说话。布莱恩喜欢指出，人们可以痴迷于他们想要观察的市场的任何方面或维度， 但最终，股票(或债券、商品、或加密货币)的价格将决定每个市场参与者是赚了还是亏了。 没有条件，没有例外，没有脚注，也没有重来的机会。
market participants.Both ofus preferred the concept of respecting price  as opposed to following our feelings.Ieventually internalized and adopted one of his most well known colloquialisms:Only Price Pays.Brian likes to point    out that one can obsess over any aspect or dimension of market-watching    that they'd like,but,in the end,the price of the stock(or bond,or
commodity,or coin)is the thing that will determine how much has been
made or lost by every market player.There are no conditions,no asterisks, no footnotes and no do-overs.
In his new book,Brian introduces the concept of the Anchored Volume
Weighted Average Price or AVWAP,an evolution of the work he's been
doing for decades.Brian likes to point out that he didn't invent looking at   volume weighted average prices for information,but that he has certainly become the VWAP's adoptive father in terms of promoting its use as a
trading tool.Brian's explanations of this approach to trading,along with
over one hundred color charts,will serve as a definitive framework for
understanding the three most important components in the market:price, time and volume.His constant emphasis on risk management and market   psychology will fill in a lot of the knowledge gaps that so many traders are  currently struggling with,regardless of how long they've been working on  their  craft.
I was fortunate to meet and begin learning from Brian early enough in my career that it's made a meaningful difference in how I think about and
process the things I see across my screens each day.I hope he will have a similar impact on the next generation who will be discovering him for the first time as a result of this book.
Downtown Josh Brown
Ritholtz Wealth Management LLC
Long Island,New York,October 2022
市场参与者。我们两人都更倾向于尊重价格的概念，而不是跟随我们   的感觉。我最终内化了并采纳了他最著名的俗语之一：只有价格会说   话。布莱恩喜欢指出，人们可以痴迷于他们想要观察的市场的任何方  面或维度，但最终，股票(或债券、商品、或加密货币)的价格将决   定每个市场参与者是赚了还是亏了。没有条件，没有例外，没有脚注， 也没有重来的机会。
在他的新书里，布莱恩介绍了锚定成交量加权平均价 (AVWAP)    的 概念，这是他几十年研究成果的演进。布莱恩喜欢指出，他并非第  一个研究成交量加权平均价来获取信息的人，但他无疑成为了
VWAP  推广为交易工具的领路人。布莱恩对这种交易方法的解释，
加上一百多张彩色图表，将作为理解市场三个最重要组成部分——价 格、时间和成交量——的权威框架。他对风险管理和市场心理学的持 续强调，将填补许多交易者目前正苦苦挣扎的知识空白，无论他们  从事这项技艺有多长时间。
我很幸运在职业生涯早期就遇到了布莱恩，并开始向他学习，这对   我如何思考和处理每天屏幕上看到的事物产生了深远影响。我希望   这本书能对下一代产生类似的影响，让他们首次通过这本书认识他。
市中心乔什 ·布朗里索尔特财富管理 公司长岛，纽约，2022年10月
PREFACE
How I Discovered and why
I Usethe Anchored VWAP   Bot
(AVWAP)
I wrote this book to introduce the Anchored Volume Weighted Average
Price(AVWAP)to new users.For those who are familiar with it,this book will advance new concepts and strategies to help you become more
profitable.
Before you dive in,Ithought you'd be interested in how I became an expert on this important tool.Here's my "origin story.”
In the late'70s when I was about ten or eleven years old,I had a clue that I  would do something in the stock market as a career.My father was a doctor and when he wasn't on call we watched Wall $treet Week with Louis
序 言
我是如何发现它的以及原因
我使用锚定的VWAR          Bot (AVWAP)
我写这本书是为了向新用户介绍锚定成交量加权平均价(
AVWAP) 。 对于熟悉它的人来说，这本书将介绍新的概念和策略， 以帮助您获得更高的利润。
在你深入之前，我想你可能对我是如何成为这个重要工具的专家感兴趣。这 是我的“起源故事。”
在20世纪70年代末，我大约十岁或十一岁的时候，我隐约感觉到自己将来 会在股票市场领域发展事业。我父亲是一名医生，在他不值班的时候，我们 会一起看路易斯主持的《华尔街周报》。
Rukeyser on PBS.It's on Bloomberg now,but it started out on Maryland Public   TV.
I was a teenager when LoJack made local news for giving Boston Police
transponders to help with the skyrocketing rate of auto thefts in the city.
With a few years ofw$W under my belt,I had the bright idea to take all the  money I'd earned caddying and delivering newspapers and buy some LoJack stock.At the time it was trading at $5/share and my dad agreed to go in
with me.I turned over my$500 and he bought 1,000 shares.Yes,you're right,he gave me 10:1 leverage and I didn't even realize it at the time.
The shares doubled in about three months.From that point on I wanted to be a “stockbroker,"not because I wanted to sell stocks,but because that's  the onlyjob description I'dheard for someone who works with stocks and  bonds.
After studying business management in college,I started at a firm that is
best described as a boiler room operation.The lines out of the Ben Affleck   movie Boiler Room were basically our sales pitches,but I didn't want to be in sales.I wanted to buy and sell stocks.
Like most brokers learning the ropes,I moved from firm to firm.No one was  teaching technical analysis,they just told you what they wanted you to sell. While I was working at Lehman Brothers,the best producer in my office
used the strategy of buying companies that recorded positive earnings
surprises and used charts to back them up.That's where I learned to be a
salesman,which is an important life skill,but again,not what I wanted to do all day.I'dbeen reading Investors Business Daily,which had some charts,
but I'd still never even heard ofthe concepts ofeither AVWAP or the very closely related Volume Weighted Average Price(VWAP).
Rukeyser    在PBS 上。它目前在彭博上，但最初是在马里兰公共电视台开 播的。
我十几岁的时候，LoJack 因为给波士顿警察提供定位器以帮助解决   城市中急剧上升的汽车盗窃率而上了当地新闻。在W$W  工作几年后， 我突发奇想，想把打高尔夫球和送报纸赚来的所有钱都用来买
LoJack 的股票。当时每股交易价格为5美元，我爸爸同意和我一起投 资。我把500美元交给他，他买了1000股。是的，没错，他给了我
10:1的杠杆，而我当时甚至没有意识到这一 点。
股票大约三个月后翻了一番。从那时起，我想成为一名“股票经纪人”,  不是因为我想卖股票，而是因为那是我听到的唯一一个与股票和债券相关 的工作描述。
在大学学习企业管理后，我创办了一家最佳描述为“锅炉间”操作的 经纪公司。本 · 阿弗莱克电影《锅炉间》中的台词基本上就是我们的  销售口号，但我不想做销售。我想买卖股票。
像大多数刚入行的新手一样，我从一家公司转到另一家公司。没有人  教技术分析，他们只是告诉你该卖什么。在我效力于雷曼兄弟公司期  间，我们办公室最优秀的交易员使用的是买入那些报告了盈利超预期  的公司的策略，并用图表来佐证。这就是我学会了如何成为一名销售  员，这是一项重要的生活技能，但再次，这不是我想要整天做的事情。 我一直阅读《投资者商业日报》,上面有一些图表，但我仍然从未听  说过AVWAP或与之非常相关的成交量加权平均价 (VWAP)   的概念。
Denver lured me from the East Coast in 1991 and I had learned about
technical analysis and started trading online with a 24k dial-up modem.
During the years between 1995 and 1998,I taught a class for the guys in my office on my own methods of technical analysis,even though I still hadn't
been exposed to VWAP.One day I saw an ad,"Trade with our capital.20:1 leverage"which intrigued me.I kid you not,the advertiser's name was
Generic Trading out of New York.They said to trade their funds you had to have $25,000 and be a registered broker.
In 1993,when I was only 23-24,living in a little house with my wife and a
new baby.I didn't have much,but I had my brokers license.So I scraped the money together and quit myjob.It was a completely foolish decision,but it  was also the best decision because it worked out.I controlled$500,000 in
buying power as a trader.The firm gave me almost no support other than a basic quote package.There must have been charts,but I can't remember
them.They would have been basic.They took ten percent of my profits and   part of my commissions.Their idea of support was,"Here's how well you did and here's your check.”
You might not believe that a young man didn't take big advantage of the
leverage,but I couldn't afford to lose money.My$25,000 was really just a
stop loss for my firm,not something I was prepared to lose.I made money
every month using a strong risk management philosophy that sticks with
me to this day:I don't chase things.Risk management is “Job#1”as a trader.
In 2002,I left Generic Trading and worked for MarketWise Securities in
Colorado,where I taught technical analysis and trading classes and headed up the proprietary trading department.MarketWise is where I started
using RealTick software and saw VWAP for the first time.At that time,I saw it as atrendline tool.Most software charts allowed you to draw a straight
horizontal or vertical line.This software had an option to see a VWAP line. Instead of going horizontal it would follow the price up(or down)and then
1991年，丹佛吸引我离开了东海岸，我学习了技术分析，并开始用
24k 拨号调制解调器在线交易。在1995年至1998年期间，我为我办公
室的同事们独自教授我的技术分析方法，尽管我仍然没有接触过
VWAP 。 有一天，我看到一则广告：“用我们的资金交易。20:1杠杆”, 这让我很感兴趣。我向你保证，广告商的名字是纽约的Generic
Trading。 他们说要用他们的资金交易，你必须有25,000美元，并且 是一名注册经纪人。
1993年，我只有23-24岁，和妻子以及刚出生的新宝宝住在一间小房   子里。我没什么,但我有我的经纪人执照。所以我东拼西凑凑够了钱， 辞掉了工作。这是一个完全愚蠢的决定，但它也是一个最好的决定，
因为最终结果是好的。作为一名交易员，我控制着50万美元的购买力。 公司几乎不给我支持，除了一个基本的报价包。肯定有图表，但我记  不清了。它们应该是基本的。他们拿走了我利润的百分之十和我部分   佣金。他们所谓的支持是，“这是你的业绩，这是你的支票。”
你可能不信，一个年轻人没有充分利用杠杆，但我负担不起亏损。我 的2.5万美元对我来说实际上只是我公司的止损点，而不是我准备失  去的东西。我每个月都用一种强烈的风险管理哲学赚钱，这种哲学至 今仍与我同在：1不要追逐。风险管理是交易员“第一要务”。
2002年，我离开了Generic       Trading, 在科罗拉多州的MarketWise
Securities   工作，在那里我教授技术分析和交易课程，并负责自营交易  部门。MarketWise   是我开始使用RealTick  软件并首次看到VWAP的地 方。当时，我将它视为一条趋势线工具。大多数软件图表允许你画一条 水平的或垂直的直线。这款软件有一个选项可以显示VWAP线。它不会 保持水平，而是会随着价格上涨(或下跌),然后
hit a point and bounce.“What is that bounce?”I figured out that it was the average price and concluded that something's here that makes people buy (or sell)at the VWAP level.I knew it was a measure of market psychology   and supply and demand.
RealTick displayed a VWAP for only one day and I found a way to get a five- day VWAP out ofit.I couldn't anchor to the middle of the day or anything
else,but started noticing that it was useful anyway.For a long while I would anticipate with it-use it as an extra piece of information to build my
confidence on a trade I was already looking at.It wasn't my primary tool
then,but was becoming more important.I wanted to know more,like what if I could look at a chart with a VWAP for more than five days?What about
tracking at the start of when a company reported earnings 13 days ago?
The tool wasn't designed to do that,so I hacked it to see the VWAP that way.
I didn't realize why it was important,but knew that it was.
That's when I started wondering how I could view VWAP similar to a moving average instead ofjust a horizontal line.I wrote my first article about it in
2005,“Chase the Gap or Wait for VWAP.”
I continued to track and use the VWAP as I moved on to other business
ventures,including running a day-trading office.In 2015,when Michael
Thompson from the trading platform TC2000 asked me to use their software for teaching my technical analysis classes and in my training videos.I said,   "If you can create a point-and-click volume weighted average price tool for   me that allows me to set multiple starting points and move them around,I'll use your software.”A couple of months later,they did.
TC2000 called this new feature“Anchored VWAP by Alphatrends.”Others  developed their own versions of the same software features and came up   with their own names.I've listed some of these in AppendixC,“Sources for Anchored VWAP on Charts.”
触及一个点并反弹。“那是什么反弹?”我意识到那是平均价格，
并得出结论，在VWAP 水平上存在某种因素促使人们买入(或卖出)。 我知道这是市场心理和供需的衡量标准。
RealTick 仅显示了一天的VWAP,  而我找到了一种从中获取五天VWAP的  方法。我无法锚定在一天的中途或任何其他地方，但开始注意到它仍然很有   用。很长一段时间里，我会用它来预判——将其作为我已关注的交易的一个额 外信息来增强我的信心。那时它还不是我的主要工具，但正变得越来越重要。 我想了解更多，比如如果我能在图表上查看超过五天的VWAP 会怎样?又比  如跟踪公司在13天前报告收益时的起始情况?这个工具并非设计用来做这些  的，所以我修改它来查看这种方式的VWAP。 我当时没意识到为什么这很重  要，但知道它确实如此。
那时我开始思考如何将VWAP 类似于移动平均线一样来查看，而不是仅仅一 条水平线。我在2005年写了我的第一篇文章关于它，“追逐缺口还是等待
VWAP 。”
我继续追踪和使用VWAP,   同时涉足其他商业项目，包括经营一个日 内交易办公室。2015年，当交易平台TC2000 的迈克尔 ·汤普森(
Michael        Thompson)  邀请我使用他们的软件来教授我的技术分析课 程以及制作我的培训视频时，我说：“如果你能为我创建一个可以设 置多个起点并移动它们的点选式成交量加权平均价工具，我就使用你  们的软件。”几个月后，他们做到了。
TC2000 将这个新功能称为“Alphatrends 定制的VWAP”。  其他 人开发了相同软件功能的自己的版本，并提出了自己的名称。我在  附录C, “图表上Anchored    VWAP的来源”中列出了其中一些。
INTRODUCTION
HOW TO USE THIS BOOK
My goal for this book is to give you a thorough understanding of the VWAP and the AVWAP so you can learn how to interpret market action more
accurately.This knowledge will allow you to make better trades.
The typical technical analysis tools to look at on charts are;moving
averages,Moving  Average  Convergence/Divergence(MACD),relative
strength,etc.—they're all part of the universal curiosity people have for
trying to crack “the secrets”of the market.After three decades,I realized
that simplicity is the market's greatest disguise.Simple works.I focus on
the current price,the price's behavior over a few different timeframes,a
couple of moving averages over different timeframes,the volume,and the
AVWAP.The beauty of the AVWAP is it represents the absolute truth of the   relationship between a stock's supply and demand and it is a 100%objective tool.It may be too obvious to repeat here,but the interaction between
supply and demand is the primary determinant of price and the AVWAP is the best tool to show us supply and demand.
This book has three sections.
引言
如何使用本书
本书的目标是让您全面了解 VWAP 和 AVWAP,   以便您能够更准
确地解读市场动态。这些知识将使您能够进行更好的交易。
在图表上典型的技术分析工具包括：移动平均线、移动平均收敛/发散 (MACD)、   相对强弱等——它们都是人们试图破解“市场秘密”的 普遍好奇心的一部分。三十年后，我意识到简单是市场最大的伪装。
简单有效。我关注当前价格、价格在不同时间框架内的行为、不同时 间框架的几条移动平均线、成交量以及AVWAP 。AVWAP 的美妙之  处在于它代表了股票供求关系的绝对真理，并且是一个100%客观的  工具。重复在这里可能太明显了，但供求之间的相互作用是价格的主 要决定因素，而AVWAP  是展示供求的最佳工具。
这本书有三个部分。
PartI,Foundations     of     VWAP/AVWAP-It will benefit both novice and veteran traders to start here.This material is the foundation for
understanding VWAP and AVWAP.You may be familiar with a lot of the
terms and concepts presented,but they have never been presented in
AVWAP analysis.It covers the components of VWAP and AVWAP,how and    why institutions use it,how it is calculated,and the psychology of it.This is a fresh approach.The material laid out here is the foundation for the
strategy  heavy  PartII
Part   II,Using   AVWAP-This is the strategy section ofthe book.It is
packed with charts and detailed strategies you can use in the markets
every day.You will learn how price changes in public markets so you can
find the highest-probability,lowest-risk trade ideas suited to your
personality,timeframe,and objectives.We will study examples ofAVWAP
where it was a definitive signal to act and also study examples where it
provided no value.Nothing works all the time in the markets.Therefore,I
emphasize risk management in every example.I want this book to help you to better understand supply and demand in the markets so you can make
more money.There is nothing more accurate than the AVWAP to guide our   analysis objectively.These are the same strategies Iuse in my daily trading.
Part       III,Appendices-Newer traders who may not be familiar with the
foundations of technical analysis will benefit the most from this section.
They might even want to read this first to see how the information in the
rest of the book fits with concepts I have written about over the last three decades.These are primers on market structure and the Understanding
Market Structure Chart(including the market stages of:Accumulation,
Markup,Distribution  and  Decline),moving  averages,trend  alignment  and   more.You will also find some reference materials to download and software providers ofAVWAP.
第一部分，VWAP/AVWAP  的基础——它将使新手和资深交易者都能 从中受益。这些材料是理解VWAP 和AVWAP的基础。您可能熟悉这 里提出的许多术语和概念，但它们从未在AVWAP 分析中提出过。它 涵盖了VWAP 和AVWAP的组成部分，机构如何以及为什么使用它， 它是如何计算的，以及它的心理学。这是一种全新的方法。这里概述 的材料是策略密集的第二部分的基础。
第二部分，使用AVWAP- 这是本书的策略部分。其中充满了你可以   每天在市场中使用的图表和详细策略。你将学习公共市场的价格变化， 以便找到最适合你性格、时间框架和目标的最高概率、最低风险的交   易想法。我们将研究AVWAP的实例，其中它是明确的行动信号，以   及它没有提供价值的实例。在市场中没有任何东西是永远有效的。因  此，我在每个例子中都强调风险管理。我希望这本书能帮助你更好地  理解市场的供需关系，以便你能赚更多钱。没有什么比AVWAP 更能   客观地指导我们的分析了。这些是我日常交易中使用的相同策略。
第三部分，附录-对于可能不熟悉技术分析基础的新交易者来说，本 节将最有益。他们甚至可能想先读这部分，看看书中其余部分的内容 如何与过去三十年我写过的概念相契合。这些是关于市场结构以及理 解市场结构图(包括市场阶段：积累、拉升、派发和下跌)的入门知 识，还有移动平均线、趋势一致性等更多内容。你还会找到一些可下 载的参考资料以及AVWAP  的软件供应商。
I geared most of the material towards swing trading.Swing traders hold a
stock from a few days up to a couple of months.Swing traders attempt to
have  their  money  in  stocks  that  are  in  a  longer-term  trend,whether  higher or  lower.When  momentum  wanes,it  is  time  to  harvest  profits.Their  goal  is to leverage time and capital by being involved in the primary trend moves   and  to  avoid  the  natural  trend  corrections.When  done  properly,swing
trading attains the goals of steady growth of capital and avoids large losses.
It is up to you whether you want to use technical analysis as a stand-alone   tool,combine  it  with   fundamental  analysis,or  use   other  methods   oftrading and investing.I am not here to convince anyone what to do with their
money,only to provide  a  comprehensive  overview  of the technical tool
which has given me the best results.I have written this book in a way that is  easy to understand,andIam  convinced that you will  choose to make the AVWAP part of your arsenal.
Brian  Shannon,CMT @alphatrends
我将大部分材料都针对波段交易。波段交易者会持有股票几天到几个 月不等。波段交易者试图让他们的资金处于一个长期趋势中的股票， 无论是上涨还是下跌。当势头减弱时，就是收获利润的时候。他们的 目标是通过对主要趋势行情的参与来杠杆时间和资本，并避免自然趋 势修正。如果操作得当，波段交易就能实现资本稳步增长并避免重大 亏损。
您可以选择将技术分析作为独立工具使用，将其与基本面分析结合，或使用 其他交易和投资方法。我并非要说服您如何处理自己的资金，只是提供一种 技术工具的全面概述，该工具给我带来了最佳结果。我以易于理解的方式撰 写了这本书，并坚信您会选择将AVWAP   作为您武器库的一部分。

第一章
VWAP  和 AVWAP
“如果你有知识，就让它照亮别人的蜡烛。”
—马格丽特 · 富勒
1. 了解VWAP 和AVWAP 的区别
2. 了解VWAP 和 AVWAP 的构建方式
3. 了解VWAP 和 AVWAP 的应用
4. 学习VWAP 和 AVWAP 如何成为分析工具
技术分析指标是时机工具，其中VWAP  和AVWAP   是两种。它们被创建是为了帮助我们识别在 正确的时间、以正确的价格交易正确的股票，从而获得交易成功。在我的■年交易生涯中，我 研究过所有流行的技术分析工具，从MACD、RSI、  随机指标、峰度、甘氏理论、艾略特波浪
理论等等。其中很多都有帮助，但我无法在它们的解释中找到真正的连贯性。我对市场供需的 深刻理解始于2003年，当时我第一次遇到了VWAP 。这本书重点介绍VWAP,   甚至更多是
AVWAP。
Wave,and more.A lot of them were helpful,but I couldn't find true
consistency in their interpretation.My deep understanding of supply and demand in the market came about in 2003 when I first encountered the
VWAP.This book focuses on the VWAP,and even more so,the AVWAP.
Components of the VWAP and
AVWAP:Price,Time,and   Volume
Our study of market action with AVWAP will begin with a study of the three most important variables in  auction markets.Those  are price,time,and
volume and they are the components which build the AVWAP.
Price  is how we keep score.It is how we determine success or failure;there is nothing subjective about its measurement.
Time is a constant.We cannot change or manipulate it.Time is how we
organize market data,and it becomes the most subjective component when you decide where to anchor your VWAP starting point.
Volume  is a variable that is affected by the decisions of allmarket
participants to buy,sell,or stand aside.At any specific price point or within a price range,the number of buyers and sellers varies depending upon a
number of factors.You will learn about these factors in this book.
The study of these market components allows us to glean greater insight  into who has control of price action:buyers or sellers,and how committed they  are  to  their  respective  intentions.Together,price,time  and  volume, helpus to execute more profitable trades.
波浪，等等。其中很多都有帮助，但我无法在它们的解释中找到真正的连 贯性。我对市场供需的深刻理解始于2003年，当时我第一次遇到了
VWAP。 这本书重点介绍VWAP,  甚至更多是AVWAP。
VWAP  和 AVWAP   的组成部分：价
格、时间和成交量
我们的AVWAP   市场行为研究将从拍卖市场中最重要的三个变量开
始。这些是价格、时间和成交量，它们是构建AVWAP  的组成部分。
价格是我们计分的方式。它是我们确定成功或失败的方式；它的测量没有任 何主观性。
时间是恒定的。我们不能改变或操纵它。时间是我们在组织市场数据时使用 的工具，当你决定你的VWAP 起始点时，它成为最主观的组成部分。
成交量是一个受所有市场参与者买卖或观望决策影响的变量。在任何 特定的价格点或价格范围内，买方和卖方的数量取决于许多因素。你 将在本书中学习这些因素。
对这些市场组成部分的研究使我们能够更深入地了解谁控制着价格 行动：买方还是卖方，以及他们对各自意图的承诺程度。价格、时 间和成交量共同帮助我们执行更盈利的交易。
Volume Weighted Average Price
(VWAP)
The  Volume  Weighted Average Price(VWAP)is  the  cumulative average price of a stock traded during one day. The calculation ofthe VWAP
begins the moment the market opens,builds throughout the day,and
concludes at the close ofthe session.For equities,users can choose
whether to use pre/post market hours in the calculation.The daily VWAP resets at the start of each new day.
Because price is weighted by volume,not time,the VWAP is the true dollar average for the time period studied.Each share traded(by retail and
institutional traders,long  and  short)receives  equal  weight in the
calculation.The VWAP is more responsive to volume trends than price
action because ofits volume weighting feature.Accordingly,as volume
levels  change(pace  oftrade)throughout  the   day,heavier  volume  periods have more impact on the movement of the VWAP while lighter volume
periods have less impact on the movement of the VWAP.The VWAP is a straightforward  study.There  are  no  settings,adjustments,or  offsets  to complicate  its  measurement.
Anchored Volume Weighted Average    Price(AVWAP)
The AVWAP is the same as the VWAP except that the starting point(the anchor)for the volume weighted average price calculation is set by the
user at a specific meaningful point;that is,it is not simply the start of the trading  day.
成交量加权平均价(VWAP)
成交量加权平均价 (VWAP)   是在一天内交易的股票的累积平均价。 VWAP  的计算从市场开盘时开始，全天逐步构建，并在交易会结束   时结束。对于股票，用户可以选择是否在计算中使用盘前/盘后时段。 每日VWAP  在每个新一天的开始时重置。
由于价格按成交量加权而非按时间加权，因此VWAP  是所研究时间段内的 · 真实美元平均价。每一笔交易的股票(无论由散户或机构交易者、多头或
空头交易)在计算中获得的权重相同。由于成交量加权的特性，VWAP  对  成交量趋势的反应比价格行为更敏感。因此，随着日内成交量水平的变化  (交易速度),成交量较高的时段对VWAP  的变动影响更大，而成交量较 低的时段对VWAP  的变动影响较小。VWAP  是一项简单的研究。它没有  设置、调整或抵消项来复杂化其测量。
锚定成交量加权平均价 (AVWAP)
AVWAP   与 VWAP   相同，只是体积加权平均价格计算的起始点
(锚点)由用户在某个有意义的特定点上设置；也就是说，它不是 简单地从交易日开始。
When we start the VWAP calculation at a point other than the start of the current  day,it  becomes“anchored”to  that  first  point  and  we  call  it  an
“AVWAP.”The AVWAP allows us to measure VWAP from any point,on any  timeframe,for any interval.The trader chooses a starting point at which to  anchor the VWAP and once the starting point is so anchored,then from that point forward the AVWAP calculates the cumulative price and volume of
each transaction,the result being elegantly displayed like a moving average along with price.
As you will learn,the “anchor point”is the most subjective part of our
analysis.We will explore many valid anchor points to begin our analysis
and why we anchor at those points. The AVWAP broadcasts the message of the market,that is whether sellers or buyers are driving the then-current   price trend,more clearly than any other technical tool I have studied in     my 30+year obsession with the stock market.
The book explains in detail the AVWAP,it's components,calculation,how to choose the anchor point,AVWAP strategies,and how you can use it to
increase your profitability.
There are two VWAP lines in Chart 1.1,the first one(light blue)is anchored to a large price movement event.Because it starts at a point other than the beginning ofa new day,it is an AVWAP.The second one(dark blue)begins   with the new day,this is the traditional VWAP calculation.
当我们从当前日的开始点以外的某个点开始VWAP  计算，它就会
“锚定”到该第一个点，我们称之为 “AVWAP 。”AVWAP      允许我 们从任何点、任何时间周期、任何间隔来测量VWAP。  交易者选择一 个起始点来锚定VWAP,   一旦起始点被锚定，从该点开始，
AVWAP   计算每个交易的累积价格和成交量，结果优雅地显示为价格 沿移动平均线。
正如你所学的，“锚点”是我们分析中最主观的部分。我们将探 讨许多有效的锚点以开始我们的分析，以及我们为什么选择这些 锚点。AVWAP   比我所研究的任何其他技术工具都更清晰地传递 了市场的信息，即卖家或买家是否在推动当时的当前价格趋势。
这本书详细解释了AVWAP,  它的组成部分、计算方法、如何选择锚 点、AVWAP 策略，以及你如何使用它来提高你的盈利能力。
图1.1中有两条VWAP线，第一条(浅蓝色)锚定在一个大的价格变动事件 上。因为它从新一天的开始点以外的位置开始，所以是AVWAP。 第二条  (深蓝色)从新一天开始，这是传统的VWAP计算。

VWAP      和  AVWAP  如何成为分析工
具
VWAP  和AVWAP   已经从执行测量的基准转变为市场参与者在不同  时间框架内用于辅助趋势识别和买卖决策时机的技术工具。我第一 次在交易平台RealTick  上注意到 “VWAP”   是在2003年。在当时， 查看VWAP  的唯一方式是从新交易日的开始。我发现我可以更改查 看累计的天数
VWAP for as many days as I wanted and this allowed me to choose the day
where I could set my anchor.
This “hack”allowed me to experiment with the week-to-date(WTD),
month-to-date(MTD),and year-to-date(YTD),as well as from gaps and even IPOs.VWAP analysis immediately fascinated me and,more
importantly,I started to make more money in my trading with it.I was hooked by the possibilities  of AVWAP analysis.It remains my most   important technical analysis tool to this day.
It wasn't until 2015 that a major technical analysis platform(TC2000)added
"Anchored VWAP by Alphatrends"to their excellent chart platform.This
was a significant breakthrough for its simplicity and the ability to point and click the anchor from any point on the chart,on any timeframe.From that    introduction to the trading world,there have been several chart
applications that have added the“Alphatrends Anchored VWAP”to their platforms.I am truly grateful that the trading world has embraced the
value of AVWAP analysis and am humbled that my efforts have made it
possible to access the Anchored VWAP on many great chart platforms.See the list of chart platforms with AVWAP in AppendixC,"Sources for
Anchored VWAP on Charts.”
How   VWAP   and   AVWAP   Help
Traders
The way the AVWAP combines price,time,and volume into one easy-to-
understand indicator gives us a blended view of whether it is the buyers or sellers who are in control.This also applies to the VWAP,but for purposes  of this book we are generally focusing on the AVWAP.
VwaP  持续多长时间，我都想，这让我可以选择我设置锚点的日子。
这个“技巧”让我可以尝试周至今(WTD)、 月至今
(MTD) 和年至今(YTD),   以及从缺口甚至IPO  开始。
VWAP  分析立即让我着迷，更重要的是，我开始用这个交 易赚更多钱。我被AVWAP 分析的可能性迷住了。它仍然 是我最重要的技术分析工具。
直到2015年， 一个主要的技术分析平台(TC2000)  才在他们的优秀
图表平台上添加了“Alphatrends 锚点VWAP”。  这对于它的简单  性和从图表上的任何时间点点击锚点的功能来说是一个重大突破。从 那时起，交易世界中有几个图表应用程序添加了 “Alphatrends      锚点 VWAP”  到他们的平台。我非常感激交易世界接受了AVWAP   分析  的价值，也很荣幸我的努力使许多优秀的图表平台可以访问锚点
VWAP。  参见附录C,  “图表上锚点VWAP  的来源”中的图表平台
列表。
VWAP  和 AVWAP   如何帮助交 易者
AVWAP   将价格、时间和成交量结合为一个易于理解的指标的方式， 让我们能够综合地了解是买方还是卖方在掌控市场。这也适用于
VWAP,   但出于本书的目的，我们通常主要关注AVWAP。
This valuable information allows us to better understand market structure SO we can:
·Identify    low-risk,high-probability    market     and    individual     stock opportunities.
·    Time   our  entries  into  the  market   and  individual   stocks  more accurately.
·Stand aside through periods of uncertainty.
·Cut  our  losers  early  based  on  objective  recognition  of  price   action.
·Hold our winners longer.
·Exit   our   winners   more   efficiently.
In short,AVWAP is a tool which can help any timeframe participant   (from daytraders to longer-term investors)make better market timing decisions and achieve greater market profitability.
On  a  chart,the  VWAP  is  represented  as  a  line  along  with  price.The  way  it   builds  with  each  piece  of  data  allows  us  to  recognize  nascent  trends.In  the  chart 1.2,on the left it shows that buyers are in control of the daily session while  the  stock  is  above  the  ascending  VWAP.The  chart  on  the  right  shows
that the sellers maintain control while prices are below the declining VWAP.
Who is in Control?Bulls or Bears?
The  AVWAP  shows  us  the  genuine  relationship  between  price  and  volume    over  any  period.Which  side  is  in  control  and  gaining  or  losing  control  of  the trend,buyers(bulls),or    sellers(bears)?Ourjob    is     to    “objectively     listen    to
这些有价值的信息使我们能够更好地理解市场结构，以便我们能够：
*识别低风险、高概率的市场和个人股票机会。
4更准确地把握进入市场和个股的时间。
*在不确定性时期保持观望。
*根据对价格走势的客观认识，及早止损。
*更长时间地持有盈利头寸。
4更高效地退出盈利头寸。
简而言之， AVWAP   是一个可以帮助任何时间周期参与者(从日内 交易者到长期投资者)做出更好的市场时机决策并实现更高市场盈 利的工具。
在图表中，VWAP   以一条与价格并行的线表示。它通过每一条数据构建的方式使我 们能够识别新兴趋势。在图表1.2中，左侧显示买方控制着每日交易时段，而股票  价格高于上升的VWAP。右侧的图表显示卖方在价格低于下降的VWAP时保持控 制。
谁在控制?是多头还是空头?
AVWAP   显示了在任何时间段内价格和成交量的真实关系。哪一方在掌控趋 势并 gaining   或 losing        control,是买家(多头),还是卖家(空头)?我 们的工作是“客观地聆听
the message of the market”for the timeframe we wish to engage in our   trades.The  AVWAP  provides  as  much  certainty  as  we  can  hope  for  in  the study  of  price  action.
We can measure AVWAPon any security or market where price and
volume data are available.That includes individual stocks,ETFs,futures contracts,cryptocurrencies,and Forex markets.

VWAP还是AVWAP?
不要让VWAP 、AVWAP   和 “VWAP      anchored      from” 这些术语让你困 惑。在这份材料中，你可以假设任何单独提到的VWAP  都是指一天。如  果提到AVWAP,    则是指Anchored         VWAP,我们也可能说 “the
VWAP        from”, 意思是“从锚点开始”,这样就构成了AVWAP。
There are dozens oftechnical indicators that we can choose to use in our
analysis of stocks and other markets.The VWAP and ability to anchor it
from key price points as an AVWAP is the most accurate visual
representation of who is in control of the market from any specific point.At first glance,the study and implementation of an AVWAP may seem
complicated,but it is a simple study anyone can learn and easily apply to   their market analysis and decisions,regardless of timeframe.By the time   you have read this book,you will recognize the ways the AVWAP simplifies how to observe and more accurately analyze market action.

What is Price and Why is it Important?
We define price as an amount of currency that will purchase a finite
quantity,weight,or other measure of a good or service.In the markets,it    represents the price where the last transaction occurred.It is said,"don't   confuse price with value."Nowhere is this truer than in the markets.Price is the fastest moving market variable.
完美的组合

价格是什么?为什么它是 重要的?
我们将价格定义为一个可以购买有限数量、重量或其他商品或服务 措施的货币金额。在市场中，它代表最后一次交易发生的价格。人 们说，“不要将价格与价值混淆。”在市场中，这一点比任何地方 都更真实。价格是变化最快的市场变量。
Price Creates New Information
Price reflects the aggregate of traders'strategies and expectations about
the market's future behavior,and,as a part of that,the current news
headlines and events which affect our economy.It also creates new
information.When prices change,it can cause others to enter or exit the
market based solely on that price move.That is what technical trading is all about.
Price as Cause and Effect
In a supply and demand driven market,also known as a “liquidity market,” price change is not only the effect of participants'actions,but it can also be the cause which motivates participants to act.
The Most Important Price
Whether we gain or lose on a trade is based solely on the movement of
price.There is no other meaningful measurement ofsuccess in the
markets.It is all about your profit and loss,"your P&L"Ifyou have a
position in a stock,the most important price is what you paid and how the market has responded since you got involved.
Time and Multiple Timeframes
Without any other reference,a simple statement such as,"I will call you at nine o'clock,"has little value.Is that AM or PM?Which time zone are we
talking about,what day,this week?In the markets,time and trends can also be ambiguous.When people say they are bullish or bearish,those
pronouncements have little value without a reference to time.
价格创造新信息
价格反映了交易者对市场未来行为的策略和预期，以及作为其中一部 分的当前影响我们经济的新闻头条和事件。它也创造了新信息。当价 格变化时，它可能导致其他人仅基于该价格变动进入或退出市场。这 就是技术交易的全部内容。
价 格 作 为 因 果 关 系
在一个由供需驱动的市场中，也称为“流动性市场”中，价格变化不 仅是参与者行为的效应，还可以是促使参与者行动的原因。
最重要的价格我们是否在交易中获利或亏损完全取决于
价格的变动。市场中没有其他有意义的成功衡量标准。这一切都关 于你的盈亏，“你的P&L” 。 如果你持有一个股票头寸，最重要的 价格是你支付的价格以及自你参与以来市场如何作出反应。
时间与多时间框架
在没有其他参考的情况下，一个简单的陈述，例如，“我将在九点钟给  你打电话，”几乎没有价值。是上午还是下午?我们谈论的是哪个时区， 哪一天，这周?在市场上，时间和趋势也可能是不明确的。当人们说他  们是看涨或看跌时，如果没有时间参考，这些声明几乎没有价值。

While it may make sense to say to a friend or business associate,“I will call you at 9 p.m.next Tuesday,"in looking at market trends we cannot be so
precise with our bullish or bearish labels because trends may conflict on different  timeframes.
Ifyou were to ask if the stock in Chart 2.1 was in an uptrend or a
downtrend,either answer could be correct.It depends on your timeframe.
The longer-term trend is clearly higher(as represented by the big green
arrow)but it doesn't mean you couldjust buy at any point and make money. Ifyou purchased at the start of the smaller red arrows,that mark short-
term downtrends,you wouldn't benefit from the longer-term uptrend until the trends came into alignment.

虽然对朋友或商业伙伴说，“我将在下周二晚上九点给你打电话” 可能是有道理的，但在看市场趋势时，我们不能对我们的看涨或看  跌标签如此精确，因为趋势在不同的时间框架上可能会冲突。
如果你问图表2.1中的股票是处于上升趋势还是下降趋势，两种答案  都可能正确。这取决于你的时间周期。长期趋势显然更高(如大绿箭 所示),但这并不意味着你可以在任何时间点买入并赚钱。如果你在 较小的红箭开始处买入，这些箭头标记短期下降趋势，你不会从长期 上升趋势中获益，直到趋势趋于一致。
Why and How to use Multiple Timeframes
We    have    established     that    multiple    trends     exist    for    the     same    stock     on
different     timeframes.The      best     approach      is      to     use      the     timeframes      together. When   we    do   this,we    avoid   the    confusion   of   bull    or    bear   labels    so   we    can
focus    on    how    the    market    operates    and    how    to    make    more    money.
First,we     start      with     the     long-term      timeframe     to      determine     overall      money
flows.Next,we      move      to      the       intermediate-term      to      plan      our       trade.Finally,we consult    the     short-term     chart    to     fine     tune    our     entries     and    exits.

为什么以及如何使用多个时间框架
我 们 已 经 确 定 同 一 股 票 在 不 同 时 间 周 期 上 存 在 多 种 趋 势 。 最 佳 方 法 是 结 合 使 用 这 些 时 间 周 期 。 当 我 们 这 样 做 时 ， 我 们 避 免 了 牛 熊 标 签 的 混 淆 ， 因 此 可 以 专 注 于 市 场 如 何 运 作 以 及 如 何 赚 更 多 钱 。
首先，我们从长期时间框架开始确定整体资金流向。接下来，我们转向中期 时间框架来规划我们的交易。最后，我们参考短期图表来微调我们的入场和 出场。

referenced in the middle chart are shown in more detail:30-minute candles instead of daily candles.This middle chart's data is a closer look at the data  shown in the blue-highlighted portion of the leftmost chart;however,the    middle chart shows activity at 13x magnification(there are 1330-minutes   periods per trading day).
The blue shaded part on the middle chart is further magnified on the one-   day chart on the right.The activity on the one-day chart is displayed in 5-   minute candles instead of the 30-minute candles in the middle chart.If you look closely,you'll notice that this final chart shows only the last day of the left chart.Since the one-day chart is constructed of 5-minute candles,of
which there are 78 in each 390-minute trading day,it is like looking at 78x magnification of the left daily chart.
Volume
Volume is the“V”in the VWAP.Volume simply measures the number of   shares(contracts,options,and the  like)transacted  at  a price  or  in  a  price range for various time increments.Vertical bars display trade volume
under the price information.Volume is usedto confirm or reject price direction,not as a timing signal.
When we learn to interpret the price/volume relationship correctly,it
allows us to better gauge the strength of a trend and thus,greater
confidence in our own decisions to buy,sell,or stand aside.Here are a few ways volume is important to our analysis:
·It  assigns  meaning  to  movement,measured  in  a  more  subjective,but more in-depth manner than price action alone.
到更短的时间周期时，它允许我们看到更长的时间周期的更多细节， 就像通过放大镜看一样。中间图表中提到的三周在更详细地显示：
30分钟蜡烛图而不是每日蜡烛图。这个中间图表的数据是对左侧蓝色 高亮部分所示数据的更近距离观察；然而，中间图表以13倍放大倍数 显示活动(每个交易日有13个30分钟周期)。
中间图表中蓝色阴影部分在右侧的一日图表上进一步放大。一日图表 上的活动以5分钟蜡烛图显示，而不是中间图表中的30分钟蜡烛图。
仔细观察，你会发现这个最终图表只显示了左侧图表的最后一天。由 于一日图表由5分钟蜡烛图构成，每个390分钟交易日有78根蜡烛图， 因此它就像观察左侧每日图表的78倍放大。
成交量
成交量是VWAP 中的 “V” 。 成交量简单地衡量在特定价格或价格   范围内、不同时间增量内交易了多少股(合约、期权等)。垂直条  形图在价格信息下方显示交易量。成交量用于确认或否定价格方向， 而不是作为时间信号。
当我们学会正确解读价格/成交量关系时，它使我们能够更好地判断趋势的 强度，从而对自己的买入、卖出或观望决策更有信心。以下是成交量对我 们分析的一些重要性：
*它为运动赋予意义，其衡量方式比仅靠价格行为更主观，但更深入。
·It offers insight into market psychology;it allows us to measure the emotional intensity level of the participants in the market being
studied.
·   It adds a dimension to price study that can confirm price action or signal caution   that   a    move   may    have   difficulty    sustaining   momentum.

Price and Volume Relationship
Volume is the best representation of how committed participants  are to a market at any point.A healthy market move will see volume expand in
the  direction  of  the  primary  trend,peak  near  turning  points,and diminish on the counter trend moves.
High-volume(relative to normal trading activity)can signal times of
stronger confidence in a move,while low-volume times are often a healthy pause as the market digests a price move and traders consider their next    trades.
A drop in volume in an uptrend is not always bearish.It is often a simple
lack of supply in a stock with healthy demand.We want to be aware of the
volume trend,but ifit doesn't confirm price action with a volume expansion in the direction of the trend,it is not a reason to act,just something to be
aware of.The purple line overlaid on the volume bars is the 20-day moving average.
条形图表示当日收盘价高于开盘价的蜡烛图，红色交易量条形图表示 收盘价低于开盘价的日子。
价格与成交量关系
成交量是衡量参与者对市场在任何时间点承诺程度的最佳指标。 一个健康的市况变动将看到成交量在主要趋势方向上扩大，在  转折点附近达到峰值，并在逆势变动中减少。
高成交量(相对于正常交易活动)可以表明对某个变动的更强信心， 而低成交量时期通常是市场消化价格变动并交易者考虑其下一笔交  易的健康暂停。
在上升趋势中，成交量下降并不总是看跌。这通常是股票需求健康时 供应量不足的简单表现。我们想要关注成交量趋势，但如果它没有以 趋势方向扩大的成交量来确认价格行动，那么它就不是采取行动的理 由，而只是需要留意的事情。叠加在成交量柱状图上的紫色线是20日 移动平均线。

Volume is Always Second to Price
Volume  analysis  can  supply  us  with  important  information  about  the
conviction of the buyers and sellers in a market.It is important to
remember that volume  is  always  secondary  to  price,as  in  the  end,price  is
the only thing that pays.We now turn to how institutional investors use
VWAP and AVWAP concepts.

成交量总是次于价格
成交量分析可以为我们提供关于市场买卖双方决心的重要信息。重   要的是要记住，成交量总是次于价格，因为最终只有价格是有效的。 我们现在转向机构投资者如何使用VWAP 和AVWAP 概念。

机构背景与算法 交易

Chapter Objectives
1.Understand how and why institutions use VWAP and AVWAP
2.Understand institutional orders
This chapter delves into how and why the VWAP became,and remains,
so important to the largest participants in the market,institutional   investors.If we know how institutions use VWAP as an execution tool,we have a better understanding of how to apply it as an analysis tool for our  benefit.When we can recognize the actions of the largest market
participants on a chart,we can join in on emerging trends in individual stocks and the overall market.
Why Institutions Use VWAP
The Volume Weighted Average Price(VWAP)was first referred to in March of 1988 in The Journal of Finance article entitled“The Total Cost of
Transactions on the NYSE”by Stephen Berkowitz,Dennis Logue,Eugene NoserJr.This is essentially when the VWAP was “invented.”
In the article,the authors stated that"The volume weighted average price   on any day represents the price a “naive"trader can expect to obtain.”This article ignited the study,analysis,and implementation of VWAP strategies,  which continues to be developed to this day.
Originally,the VWAP was a benchmark to measure whether an
institutional customer received a fair execution of their order by the broker who bought or sold a stock on their behalf.The difference between the
章节目标,
1.了解机构如何以及为何使用VWAP 和AVWAP2.  了解机构订单
本章深入探讨了VWAP 如何成为以及为何对市场最大参与者—— 机构投资者——如此重要。如果我们了解机构如何将VWAP 作为执
行工具使用，我们就能更好地理解如何将其作为分析工具为我们所 用。当我们能够在图表上识别出最大市场参与者的行动时，我们就 能参与到个股和整体市场的趋势中。
机构为何使用VWAP
成交量加权平均价 (VWAP)   最早于1988年3月在《金融学杂志》的文章 《纽约证券交易所的交易总成本》中由Stephen     Berkowitz 、Dennis
Logue 和Eugene  Noser  Jr.提及。这基本上就是VWAP的“发明”时刻。
在文章中，作者们指出：“任何一天的成交量加权平均价代表了一个 ‘天真’的交易者可以预期的价格。”这篇文章点燃了对VWAP 策略
的研究、分析和实施，这一过程至今仍在不断发展。
最初，VWAP  是一个基准，用于衡量机构客户是否通过为其买卖股 票的经纪商获得了公平的订单执行。VWAP 与
reported price of a trade to the institutional customer and the VWAP let the customer objectively determine if their broker did a fairjob in the
execution of their order.The customer wants to know if they received “fair- value"for the time it took the trades to complete.
A portfolio manager wants to know how the price they paid compares to the average price of the stock during the time it took for the order to fill.If an
order is filled at a price worse than VWAP,it brings into doubt the trading ability of the broker and may cause the manager to reevaluate the
relationship and give their lucrative commission business to another firm.
Institutional  Benchmark  Example
If the broker purchased 2 million shares at an average price of $20.45 and
the VWAP during that time was $20.60,then the customer should be happy they paid$0.15/share less than the average transaction during that time.   If,however,the customer order was purchased at $20.80 when the VWAP
was $20.60,the customer would be unhappy with the broker.No one wants   to pay more than the price a "naive trader can expect to obtain."Customers give more business to firms who consistently do well for them,which means bigger revenues and bonuses at year's end.This objective measure aligns
the goals of the broker and their customer.
This easy-to-understand benchmark comparison is why algorithmic VWAP orders make up most institutional activity.Alarge percentage of
institutional orders in the markets today are executed as“VWAP orders.”
These orders try to obtain a buy or sell price as close to,or better than
VWAP during the time it takes to complete the buy or sell order.Most
brokerages allow their customers to receive a“guaranteed VWAP”price for their orders.These orders reinforce the importance of VWAP,and thus
AVWAP,through volume participation algorithms.
交易向机构客户报告的价格之间的差异，使客户能够客观地确定其经 纪商在订单执行方面是否做得公平。客户想知道他们是否在交易完成 所花费的时间内获得了“公允价值”。
一位投资组合经理想知道他们支付的价格与订单成交期间股票的平均 价格相比如何。如果订单以低于VWAP  的价格成交，这会引发对经纪 商交易能力的质疑，并可能导致经理重新评估合作关系，并将他们有 利可图的佣金业务转给另一家公司。
机构基准示例
如果经纪商以平均价格20.45美元购买了200万股，而该期间的
VWAP 为20.60美元，那么客户应该很高兴他们支付的价格比该期间 的平均交易价格低0.15美元/股。然而，如果客户的订单在VWAP  为
20.60美元时以20.80美元的价格成交，客户会对经纪商感到不满。没
有人愿意支付比“一个‘天真交易者’可以预期的价格’更高的价格。” 客户会把更多业务交给那些始终为他们做得好的公司，这意味着年底
会有更高的收入和奖金。这一客观指标使经纪商和客户的目标保持一 致 。
这个易于理解的基准比较说明了为什么算法VWAP  订单构成了大部
分机构活动。如今市场中很大一部分机构订单都是作为 “VWAP  订单” 执行的。这些订单试图在买入或卖出订单完成的时间内，获得尽可能
接近或优于VWAP  的买入或卖出价格。大多数经纪商允许其客户为  其订单获得“保证VWAP”   价格。这些订单通过成交量参与算法，强 化了VWAP  的重要性，从而也强化了AVWAP   的重要性。
Volume Participation
Since large blocks of securities are rarely bought or sold in one single
transaction,the true aim for a large VWAP order execution is not the best  price,but liquidity;the goal is to make sure the order gets filled in the time allocated with minimum market disruption.The time to fill the order is
irrelevant,it can be a large fund buying millions of shares of a stock over a month,or a longer period,or it could be an order to sell 250,000 shares of a stock between noon and the 4 p.m.close.Market direction is not an actual  concern for VWAP order algorithms,the goal is to take part in volume
proportionately through the  day(or whatever the period)it takes to execute the order in full.
Algorithms
We often hear traders mention “the algos”in a stock.This refers to the
automated buy and sell programs run by large institutions.A trading
business will try to squeeze performance and margins anywhere possible;  it's about being efficient.The pursuit of efficiency in the markets has led to the development of computerized models to remove some variables where  humans might not do as good ajob as a computer.Trading can be tedious
for a person;a computer can refresh or change bids for offers with no
human interaction.Sometimes,to complete a single order,it might take  hundreds ofindividual trades to fulfill it.Computers do not get tired,and the algorithms do what they are programmed to do without mistakes.
Institutions do not want to disrupt the market with large orders,so their
algorithms slice a large order into smaller orders.The smaller orders also mask the true size of their order from other market participants.This is
important so that their orders are not front run(cut in front of)by other
participants.These programs reduce  market  impact  cost,which,of course, help  increase  performance  measurements.
成交量参与
由于证券的大额交易很少在一次交易中完成，因此大型VWAP  订单  执行的真实目标不是最佳价格，而是流动性；目标是确保订单在分配 的时间内完成，并尽量减少市场干扰。订单的完成时间无关紧要，它 可以是某个基金在一个月内买入数百万股股票，或者更长时间，也可 以是在中午到下午4点收盘之间卖出25万股股票的订单。市场方向 对 VWAP  订单算法来说并不是实际问题，目标是参与成交量，在执 行订单的整个时间(或whatever the period) 内按比例进行。
算法
我们经常听到交易员提到股票中的 “algos” 。 这指的是由大型机构   运行的自动买卖程序。一个交易业务会尽可能挤压绩效和利润空间；  这是关于效率的问题。市场中对效率的追求导致了计算机化模型的开  发，以去除一些人类可能不如计算机做得好的变量。对于一个人来说， 交易可能很繁琐；计算机可以刷新或改变报价，无需人工交互。有时， 为了完成一个订单，可能需要数百笔单独的交易来履行。计算机不会   疲劳，算法会按照编程要求执行，不会出错。
机构不希望用大额订单扰乱市场，因此它们的算法将大额订单拆分 成小额订单。这些小额订单也掩盖了它们订单的真实规模，从而不 让其他市场参与者知晓。这一点很重要，这样它们的订单就不会被 其他参与者抢先成交(抢在前面成交)。这些程序降低了市场冲击 成本，当然，这也帮助提高了业绩指标。
Market Impact Cost
Market impact cost is the effect a market participant has on the price of the asset it is trying to buy or sell.If a stock trades 1 million shares per day on   average and you try to buy or sell so many shares that they constitute a
large portion of the average daily volume of those shares,those buy and
sell orders are likely to move the price of the stock.The pressure your buy order places on the supply and demand equation can cause an adverse
price move,which forces you to buy at a higher price than intended.The
same is true for a large sale of a stock.Your own sell orders have the
potential to push the price lower,which makes your average sale price
lower than intended.VWAP trading algorithms attempt to minimize overall costs by reducing the market impact cost of the execution ofa large order.
Market Impact Cost is Reduced By:
intervals.
·Breaking  large(parent)orders  into  smaller  size(child)orders.
·Opposing buy and sell orders with different brokerages.
Different    Institutional    Goals
The focus of the strategies in this book are VWAP based trend trading and momentum,but it is important to recognize there are other strategies
implemented every day by other style and timeframe participants.Some
institutions buy more shares of a stock if it is under the VWAP because they perceive it has value relative to the average participant price that day.
These same buyers will then sell shares into the stronger demand for   shares when the stock is above VWAP since,by doing so,they receive a “premium”over value during that period.
市场冲击成本
市场冲击成本是指市场参与者对其试图买入或卖出的资产价格产生的 影响。如果一个股票平均每天交易100万股，而你试图买入或卖出的  股份数量占到了这些股票平均日交易量的很大一部分，那么这些买入 和卖出订单很可能会推动股票价格变动。你的买入订单对供需方程施 加的压力可能导致价格不利变动，这迫使你以高于预期价格买入。对 于大额卖出股票也是同样的情况。你自己的卖出订单有可能将价格压 低，这使得你的平均卖出价格低于预期。VWAP  交易算法试图通过减 少大额订单执行的市场冲击成本来降低总体成本。
市场冲击成本降低如下：
*订单分散的时间长度，以及间隔。
*将大(父)订单拆分为小(子)订单。
*使用不同经纪商的买卖订单进行对冲。
不同的机构目标
本书中的策略重点是基于VWAP的趋势交易和动量，但重要的是要认  识到，其他风格和时间框架的参与者每天都在实施其他策略。如果一  只股票低于VWAP,   一些机构会购买更多股票，因为他们认为它相对  于当日平均参与者价格有价值。当股票高于VWAP  时，这些买家会将  股票卖入更强的需求中，因为这样做，他们在该时期会获得“溢价” 的价值。
As a group,institutions are as diverse in their strategies andtimeframes as "retail'traders.There is no one strategy that fits all.It is notjust as simple  as saying “institutions buy below VWAP.”It may be the goal ofa“value”
institution to make their purchases while stocks are below VWAP,but a
momentum fund might try tojuice a trade in which they have a long
position in order to induce others to buy the rising stock and create further upside momentum.As we will show in Part Two,Chapter 10,when we
discuss short squeezes,buyers will sometimes become very aggressive about their purchase,hoping to inflict pain on trapped short sellers.
Parent and Child Orders
Large market participants do not want to tip their hand and reveal to the market that there is a big buyer or seller present.They needto disguise
their orders to reduce “information leakage.”To disguise a large order and avoid having their orders front-run and reduce their market impact cost,   large(parent)orders to buy or sell an individual stock get broken into
smaller(child)orders.
A study of VWAP trades executed by the International Trading Group
discusses this point in detail."The sample size is 243,772 parent orders.   The algorithm executed 13,468,847 child trades,meaning that on average each parent order turned into 55 child executions.”1
In his testimony to Congress in 2021,Ken Griffin,the CEO of Citadel Trading stated,"Today,virtually all trades executed by institutional investors are in the form of program trades,such as VWAP and other algorithm trades.”
According to their website,Citadel Trading “executes approximately 35%of all U.S.-listed retail volume,making us the industry's top wholesale
market maker."2
作为一个群体，机构在策略和时间框架上的多样性不亚于“零售”交 易者。没有一种策略适合所有人。不仅仅是简单地说“机构在
VWAP  下方购买。”一个“价值”机构的目的是在股票低于V
WAP 时进行购买，但一个动量基金可能会试图在他们对股票有长期  头寸的交易中注入动力，以诱使其他人购买上涨的股票并创造进一步 的上行动量。正如我们在第二部分，第10章中讨论短期挤压时将展示 的，买家有时会变得非常激进，希望对被困的空头卖家造成痛苦。
Parent and Child Orders
大型市场参与者不希望暴露意图，向市场透露有大量买家或卖家在场。他  们需要伪装订单以减少“信息泄露”。为了伪装大订单并避免订单被抢跑， 减少市场冲击成本，大型(父)订单在买入或卖出个股时会被拆分成更小  的(子)订单。
一项关于国际交易集团执行的VWAP 交易的研究详细讨论了这一点。 “样本量是243,772个父订单。该算法执行了13,468,847个子交易，  这意味着平均每个父订单变成了55个子执行。”!
在2021年向国会作证时， Citadel  Trading的首席执行官肯 ·格 里芬表示，“如今，几乎所有机构投资者执行的交易都是程序 化 交 易 ，例 如VWAP  和其他算法交易。”根据他们的网站，
Citadel  Trading “执行了美国上市零售交易量的约35%,使我 们成为行业顶尖的批发做市商。"
Griffin said"VWAP trades are not large trades,it is not like there are  10
million shares to be bought,it is a trade that is sliced into small slices(100 or 200 shares)and executed over the course of aday,aweek or amonth.”I
emphasized Mr.Griffin's words about timeframe because they show directly that VWAP orders are notjust for one day,they are also used for larger
trades,which can take days,weeks,or months to execute.Remember this point when we study how longer-term VWAP levels will often act as
support  and  resistance  levels.
Example:Large Institutional Sale Order
Let's consider a situation where a mutual fund owns 3%of the total
outstanding shares of a stock.For whatever reason,they want to reduce
their position size by half.If there are 500 million shares outstanding,they own 15 million shares andwould have to sell 7.5 million shares ofthe stock to sell half oftheir position.Let's say this stock trades 2,000,000 shares per day.If the fund dumped all7.5 million shares ofthe stock on the open
market,they would flood the market with close to four times its average  daily volume with this transaction alone.Asale of this magnitude would  cause a huge imbalance in supply and demand,and the stock would drop considerably to find enough liquidity to fillthe order.A"sloppy"sale like this would cost the fund a lot of money and hurt their performance.
Rather than dump their stock all at once,it is more likely the fund would   contact their broker and let them know they have a large block of stock to sell.The broker may choose to purchase the stock directly from the
customer at a negotiated price.The broker would then sell it over a period which would allow the large supply to be absorbed into the market more    easily.In this scenario,the broker takes the risk of selling the stock,and
they could probably purchase the 7,500,000 shares at a discount to the
current price.The discounted price given to the fund is to compensate the
格里芬表示， “VWAP 交易不是大额交易，不像有1000万股需要买入， 它是一笔被分割成小份(100股或200股)并在一天、一周或一个月内  执行的交易。”我强调格里芬先生关于时间跨度的说法，因为它们直   接表明VWAP 订单不仅用于一天，也用于更大额的交易，这些交易可   能需要几天、几周或几个月来执行。在研究长期VWAP 水平通常如何   充当支撑和阻力位时，请记住这一点。
示例：大型机构销售订单
让我们考虑一个情况，其中一只共同基金拥有某股票总流通股的3%。 无论出于什么原因，他们想将仓位规模减半。如果流通股为5亿股，
他们拥有1,500万股，并且需要卖出7,500万股股票才能减半其仓位。 假设这只股票每天交易2,000,000股。如果该基金在公开市场上一次 性抛售全部7,500万股股票，他们将通过这一笔交易使市场充斥接近 其平均日交易量四倍的交易量。如此规模的出售将导致供需严重失  衡，股票价格将大幅下跌以寻找足够的流动性来满足订单。这种
“草率”的出售将使基金损失大量资金，并损害其业绩。
与其一次性抛售所有股票，基金更有可能联系他们的经纪人，并告知 他们有一大块股票要出售。经纪人可能会选择以协商价格直接从客户 手中购买这些股票。然后，经纪人会将这些股票分阶段出售，以便大 宗供应更容易被市场吸收。在这种情况下，经纪人承担了销售股票的 风险，他们可能会以低于当前价格的价格购买750万股。基金获得的 折扣价格是为了补偿
brokerage for taking on the price uncertainty and associated risks during the time it would take them to liquidate the stock.
If the fund was not inclined to accept a discounted price of the shares in
return for the transfer of the risk as well as for the immediate liquidity
created were the broker to buy all of the 7,500,000 shares,the fund may
instead hire the broker to sell the stock using a sophisticated VWAP
algorithm.In this scenario,the fund may decide to have the brokerage
execute the order over the next 30 trading days and approximately  125,000 shares would get sold per day(just 6.25%of the average daily volume);a
number that the stock would be better able to handle rather than a sale of all 7,500,000 shares at once.
Time Slicing
Even with the liquidation ofjust 125,000 shares per day,there are certain
precautions the broker will take to ensure they do not cause a disruption in the market that would impact their efforts for a fair price.Just because
traders generally will accept the price a "naive"trader would expect
doesn't mean traders are dumb.The broker will not simply sell 125,000
shares at one point in the day.Instead,this is where “time slicing”of the
order comes into play.The broker considers the average daily volume of the stock for the number of days it expects it would take to liquidate the order
in full.In our example,they might consider the 30-day average volume.
Once they assess that there is sufficient liquidity to handle their 125,000    shares per day,they would then consult a volume distribution chart of the stock over narrower timeframes.
他们在股票清算期间承担的价格不确定性及相关风险。
如果基金不愿意接受以股份折价的方式换取风险转移以及立即流动性，而经 纪商购买全部750万股，基金可能会选择雇佣经纪商使用复杂的VWAP 算法 来卖出股票。在这种情况下，基金可能会决定让经纪商在未来30个交易日执 行订单，并且每天大约会卖出12.5万股(仅占平均日交易量的6.25%);这 个数量比一次性卖出全部750万股更能让股票承受。
时间切片
即使每天仅清算12.5万股，经纪人也会采取某些预防措施，以确保他 们不会造成市场混乱，从而影响他们获取公平价格的努力。交易者通 常接受“天真”交易者预期的价格，并不意味着交易者很笨。经纪人 不会在一天中的某个时间点简单地卖出12.5万股。相反，这就是订单 “时间切片”发挥作用的地方。经纪人会考虑股票的日平均成交量， 以及他们预计完全清算订单所需的天数。在我们的例子中，他们可能 会考虑30天的平均成交量。一旦他们评估出有足够的流动性来处理每 天12.5万股，他们就会参考股票在更短时间框架内的成交量分布图。

Morning SurgeDay Surge
Morning Surge
Chart 3.1 This volume distribution chart is constructed of 5-minute candles.It shows a
typical volume pattern over the course of one day.
It is common to see this “U-shaped”curve in the markets,with the heaviest volume in the first and last hours of the day.This U-shape pattern occurs in the broad indices and in individual stocks.The typical day experiences a
volume surge in the morning,a midday slowdown,and a larger volume into the close.It is like a runner who starts a race quickly,settles into a
sustainable rhythm,and then tries to finish the event with everything they can.Because of volume participation orders,the programs reinforce this U- shaped pattern.Not all institutions will use the same time periods,they
may be 5-,10-,or 15-minute periods,or any time equally divided by the 390 minutes in a trading day.
To achieve a price execution as close to the daily VWAP as possible,our
institution would carve their 125,000 shares per day"parent"”order into
several “child"orders.Let's say the first 5-minute period of the day,the
stock typically trades 2%of the full daily volume.The institution would
then sell 2%of their 125,000 share order,that is,2,500 shares in the first
five minutes of the day.By using atime increment,the institution executes a larger portion of their order at the most liquid times of the day,and they
结束 日 增早 晨  J 增
结束 日 增
图3.1此成交量分布图由5分钟蜡烛图构成。它显示了一天中典型的成交量模式。
在市场中常见到这种“U 形”曲线，成交量在一天的开始和结束时段   最为集中。这种U 形模式出现在主要指数和个股中。典型的交易日经   历早晨的成交量激增、午间的放缓以及收盘前的更大成交量。这就像   一个跑步者，快速开始比赛，进入可持续的节奏，然后尽力完成比赛。 由于成交量参与订单，程序会强化这种U形模式。并非所有机构都会   使用相同的时间段，可能是5分钟、10分钟或15分钟的时间段，或者
任何在一天390分钟交易时间内均等划分的时间段。
为了尽可能接近每日的VWAP  实现价格执行，我们的机构会将他们  每天125,000股的“父”订单分成几个“子”订单。假设在一天中的 前5分钟时段，股票通常交易全天总成交量的2%。然后，机构会卖出 他们125,000股订单的2%,即在前五分钟卖出2,500股。通过使用时  间增量，机构在一天中最具流动性的时段执行了他们订单的大部分， 并且他们
sell fewer shares during the less liquid times of the day.Participation in a small portion of volume during each period makes it less likely that other traders will detect the broker's selling activity,and even less chance that  the broker's sales would be harmful to the average price the stock trades through the day.
Institutional orders may take place all day or during a time slice of the day. VWAP orders are set by:duration(buy or sell over a portion of the day,full  day,week,month,or  other  relevant  period),price  limits,volume
percentage  limits,or  other pertinent  criteria.There  is  no  standard  time
increment for a VWAP program to slice its orders.It is up to each
institution to choose how granular they want to be.An example of a
shorter-term VWAP order could be “buy 250,000 shares ofAAPL from 1-4
p.m.,pay no more than 0.25%above VWAP and don't constitute over 10%of the volume.”
Often,the brokeragefirm does not know the true intention of the customer they represent on a transaction to buy or sell.In fact,customers often use   multiple brokers to avoid the market's knowing their true intent.It is not
uncommon for a net buyer ofa stock to give sellorders at certain levels with competitive algorithms that drive the price back down to VWAP,
where they have a larger buy order ready to be filled.
What About Dark Pools?
Dark pools are private exchanges designed to facilitate block trades
between institutional investors.These transactions are not reported to the exchanges in the consolidated tape,which can be a criticism of VWAP
analysis.The volume on darkexchanges is generated by funds who swap large positions with other institutions at a negotiated price,and are not  buys and sells that effect price change.If we don't see these transactions
在一天中流动性较低的时段卖出的股票较少。在每个时段参与一小 部分成交量，使得其他交易者不太可能发现经纪人的卖出活动，甚 至经纪人销售对股票全天平均交易价格的影响也更小。
机构订单可以全天进行或在工作日的某个时间段内进行。VWAP  订  单由以下方式设置：持续时间(在一天的部分时间、整天、 一周、一 个月或其他相关时间段内买入或卖出)、价格限制、成交量百分比限 制或其他相关标准。VWAP  程序没有标准的分割订单的时间增量。
每个机构都可以自行选择其粒度。一个较短期限的VWAP  订单的例 子可能是“从下午1点到4点买入25万股AAPL,  最多支付
VWAP  上浮0.25%,且不超过10%的成交量。”
通常，经纪公司并不知道其客户在交易中买入或卖出的真实意图。事 实上，客户经常使用多个经纪公司来避免市场了解其真实意图。对于 净买入股票的客户来说，在特定水平下达卖单，并使用竞争性算法将 价格推回VWAP,   在那里他们有一个更大的买单准备成交，这种情  况并不少见。
什么是暗池?
暗池是专为机构投资者之间进行大宗交易而设计的私人交易场所。这 些交易不会在综合交易带上向交易所报告，这可能是对VWAP 分析的 批评。暗池交易量是由基金在协商价格下与其他机构互换大量头寸所 产生的，而不是影响价格变动的买卖交易。如果我们看不到这些交易
and neither do other participants who look to volume for directional clues, does it matter?Does a tree make a sound when it falls in a forest?
The fact is,we never have the complete picture of who or why someone
transacts in a stock,if their position is hedged,or if their trade is part of a
more  complicated  strategy.Risk  is  ever present  in the market  and  one  risk   is a lack of complete information.We must make certain assumptions in our analysis,which is why risk management is always at the cornerstone of any strategy  we  implement.
Even Warren Buffett Uses VWAP
Chart 3.2 shows how Warren Buffett sold his entire position in Southwest
Airlines over a two-day period.The reported price he received from the
sale of his 2.3 million shares was $32.22,which was the exact VWAP for
those two days.It is likely that Mr.Buffet negotiated a“guaranteed VWAP” price for his  sale with the broker.Looking at the chart,it doesn't  seem like  the broker made money on this order since,for most of the time,the stock
traded below the declining VWAP of the time it took to fill the order.Warren wins  again.
而且，其他参与者也不根据成交量寻找方向性线索，这有关系吗?当树在森 林里倒下时，它会发出声音吗?
事实上，我们永远无法完全了解某人交易股票的原因或身份，也无法确定其 头寸是否被对冲，或者其交易是否是更复杂策略的一部分。市场中的风险始 终存在，而缺乏完整信息就是一种风险。在我们的分析中，我们必须做出某 些假设，这就是为什么风险管理始终是我们实施任何策略的核心。
即使是沃伦 · 巴菲特也使用VWAP
图表3.2显示了沃伦 · 巴菲特如何在两天内卖掉他在西南航空公司的全部头寸。 据报道，他出售的230万股的售价为32.22美元，这是这两天exact
VWAP。 很可能沃伦 · 巴菲特与经纪商协商了一个“保证VWAP”  的售价。 从图表来看，经纪商在这个订单上似乎没有赚钱，因为大部分时间里，股票 交易价格都在订单成交时间的下降VWAP 下方。沃伦再次获胜。

第四章市场情绪工  具、心理学和锚 定效应
“如果你不知道你是谁，市场就是一个昂 贵的地方来寻找答案。”—亚当 ·斯密
章节目标
1.定义市场情绪工具
2. 识别AVWAP 作为市场情绪工具
3.Understand  how  your  psychological  makeup  impacts  your trading
4.Understand the anchor bias and how we relate it to our trading
Tn  the  prior  chapter,we  discussed  several  aspects  of  how  institutions
accomplish  their  trading  goals  andhow  their  trading  creates  an  impact
on  the  market.While  institutional  traders   and  their  trading   strategies  have a large influence on the market,they are not the only influence on the
market.Less  tangible  but  very  important  factors  are  the  psychological  and behavioral motivations  ofall  traders.We now  look  at  some  ofthe  micro
(you)and  the  macro(the  market)psychological  and  behavioral  factors  that effect  trading.
Your mental makeup,how you handle stress,and how you think about and manage risk are all important components that will matter more to your    success than any system or perceived edge you bring to the market.
Behavioral  finance  attempts  to  understand  financial  decisions  through  the   combined analysis of psychology and investing.It is the study of how human and social-emotional biases can affect price behavior and how to measure
it.As with  any  market measurement,the  goal  is  to  gain  insight  to  increase profits.
Any  discussion  of"market  psychology"can  sound  intimidating  at  first,but
we do not have to possess an advanced degree to understand what drives
market  behavior.Instead,we  need  to  have  some  commonsense  psychology.  Look at any chart and imagine how you would feel ifyou were long,short,or
3. 了解你的心理构成如何影响你的交易
4,了解锚定偏差以及我们如何将其与交易联系起来
在前一章中，我们讨论了机构如何实现其交易目标以及其交易如何对 市场产生影响。虽然机构交易者和他们的交易策略对市场有很大的影 响，但它们不是市场唯一的影响因素。不太具体但非常重要的因素是 所有交易者的心理和行为动机。我们现在来看看一些影响交易的微观 (你)和宏观(市场)心理和行为因素。
你的心理构成、你如何处理压力以及你如何思考和管理工作风险，这些都是比任 何系统或你认为带来的市场优势都更重要的组成部分，将对你成功至关重要。
行为金融学试图通过心理学和投资的综合分析来理解金融决策。它是 研究人类和社会情感偏差如何影响价格行为以及如何衡量它的学科。 与任何市场测量一样，目标是获得洞察力以增加利润。
关于“市场心理”的任何讨论一开始都可能听起来令人望而生畏，但我们 不必拥有高等学位才能理解是什么驱动市场行为。相反，我们需要具备一 些常识心理学。看看任何图表，想象一下如果你是多头、空头或
in cash.As we analyze multiple timeframes and use tools like the Anchored VWAP,we gain a greater sense of market psychology.
Market Sentiment
"Market sentiment refers to the overall attitude of investors toward a particular security or
financial market.It is the feeling or tone of a
market,or    its    crowd    psychology,as     revealed
through the activity and price movement of the  securities traded in that market.In broad terms, rising prices indicate bullish market sentiment,  while falling prices indicate bearish market
Sentiment attempts to quantify a nebulous concept of the collective
psychology of the market participants.While quantitative  studies measure facts about price behavior,we can think of sentiment as “opinion mining.” Market sentiment represents the mood of the market,bullish or bearish.It tries to measure crowd psychology.The market does not care about the
opinion of an individual.It is the cumulative opinions and actions of participants and price movement that matter.
Why are we Interested in Market Sentiment?
Crowd behavior determines how and why trends begin,continue,stall,and reverse.People are more alike than different and that is certainly true in   the markets and in what drives our emotions to buy and sell.If we
现金持有者。当我们分析多个时间周期并使用像锚定VWAP这样的工具时， 我们会更深入地理解市场心理。
市场情绪
“市场情绪是指投资者对特定证券或金融市场 的总体态度。它是市场的感受或基调，或其群 体心理，通过该市场中交易的证券活动和价格 变动所揭示。广义而言，上涨的价格表明看涨 的市场情绪，而下跌的价格表明看跌的市场
情绪试图量化市场参与者集体心理的模糊概念。虽然定量研究测量价格行为  的事实，但我们可以将情绪视为“意见挖掘”。市场情绪代表了市场的情绪， 看涨或看跌。它试图衡量群体心理。市场不关心个人的意见。重要的是参与  者的累积意见和行动以及价格变动。
我们为什么对市场情绪感兴趣?
群体行为决定了趋势如何开始、持续、停滞和逆转。人们比想象中更相 似，这在市场以及驱动我们买卖情绪的因素中尤其如此。如果我们
understand  the  individual  factors  that  motivate  the  crowd,we  can  put  our    personal  biases  aside,anticipate  crowd  behavior  and  plan  our  trade  around their   actions.
There are things to be aware ofin the market that do not always equate to a reason  to  buy  or  sell.Seasonal  tendencies,and  extreme  bullish  or  bearish
measurements  are  good to be  aware  of,but they play  a minor  supportive
role to price  action.The goal of sentiment measurements is to gain insight   into the psychology of the other market participants in order for you to find an edge and determine whether they may be buyers or sellers of the overall market  or  individual  stock.
Traditional  Sentiment  Measures
There  are  no   shortage  oftraditional  measurements   of  market  sentiment.
Some of the popular ones such include the CBOE Volatility Index(VIX),the NYSE 52-week highs versus lows,The NYSE Bullish Percentage,the
percentage of stocks above or below a 50-or 200-day moving average,
Investors  Intelligence   Sentiment  Poll,and   others.More  recently,data  from  social media messages on Twitter and StockTwits or Google searches can be usedby“smart  algorithms”to  assess  the  mood  of  the  market.
Markets are Not Always Logical and Rational
Sentiment  can  change  for  events  that  seem  unreasonable(or  lack  a
reason),but  there  is  always  a  reason  for  price  change.We  simply  aren't
always privy to the“news.”This can be a source of frustration for many
market  participants.Emotions  and  biases  influence  traders  and  investors, but they  also  blend  with  rational  thought processes.Human biases  are  a
significant  reason  that  algorithmic  trades  have  become  the  dominant
source of buying and selling in our markets.Humans make mistakes and act
理解了促使群体行为的个体因素，我们就能抛开个人偏见，预见群体行为， 并围绕他们的行动来规划我们的交易。
市场上存在一些情况并不总是等同于买入或卖出的理由。季节性趋势， 以及极端看涨或看跌的衡量指标是需要注意的，但它们对价格行动的  支持作用较小。情绪衡量指标的目标是洞察其他市场参与者的心理，
以便你找到优势并确定他们可能是整体市场或个别股票的买家或卖家。
传统情绪衡量指标
市场情绪的传统衡量指标并不少见。 一些流行的指标包括芝加哥期权 交易所波动率指数 (VIX)、  纽约证券交易所52周高低点、纽约证券 交易所看涨百分比、高于或低于50天或200天移动平均线的股票百分 比、投资者智能情绪调查等。最近，来自推特和StockTwits 的社交
媒体消息或谷歌搜索的数据可以被“智能算法”用来评估市场的情绪。
市场并非总是逻辑和理性的
情绪可能会因为看似不合理(或缺乏理由)的事件而改变，但价格变 化总有原因。我们并不总是能掌握“新闻”。这对许多市场参与者来 说可能是一种挫败感。情绪和偏见会影响交易者和投资者，但它们也 会与理性思维过程融合。人类偏见是算法交易成为我们市场主要买卖 来源的一个重要原因。人类会犯错并受冲动和情绪驱动；算法的设计 目的是为了最小化人为错误。
on impulses andemotions;algorithms are designed to minimize human errors.
It is easy to get bogged down in the intellectual aspects of markets and
trading in order to gain an edge but,as we know,only price pays.This
brings about the need for an objective measurement and Anchored VWAP
serves that purpose because the AVWAP can simplify and helpus distill or   quantify the market sentiment by allowing us to measure the result of all of the sentiment-influencing biases,news and behaviors,rather than
obsessing over those factors.
"In  the  short  run,the  market  is  a  voting
machine,but  in  the   long  run  it  is  a  weighing
machine."
-Benjamin     Graham

Personal Psychology and Anchoring
Before we attempt tounderstand the behavior of crowds,we need to begin with an assessment of our own mental inventory and the factors that
influence the decisions we make in the markets.The market does not care about our individual opinions of price action or when we buy and sell.It is  the collective actions of the participants(both by humans and by the
algorithms programmed by humans)that create crowd psychology.
"I  fear  not  the  man  who  has  practiced   10,000
kicks  once,but  I  fear  the  man  who  has  practiced
one  kick  10,000  times.”
—Bruce Lee
受情绪驱动；算法的设计目的是为了最小化人为错误。
在市场和交易中陷入智力层面很容易以获得优势，但正如我们所知，
只有价格起作用。这带来了对客观测量的需求，Anchored  VWAP 就 能满足这一需求，因为AVWAP 可以通过允许我们衡量所有影响情绪 的偏见、新闻和行为的综合结果来简化并帮助我们提炼或量化市场情  绪，而不是过度关注这些因素。
“在短期内，市场是一台投票机，但在长
期内它是一台称重机。”
—本杰明 ·格雷厄姆
