个人心理与锚定效应
在尝试理解群体行为之前，我们需要从评估我们自己的心理库存以 及影响我们在市场中决策的因素开始。市场不在乎我们对价格行动 的个别看法或我们何时买入和卖出。是参与者(包括人类和人类编 写的算法)的共同行为创造了群体心理。
“我害怕的不是练过一万次踢腿的人，而是练过一 次踢腿一万次的人。”
一李小龙
A few ofthe personal factors that play into individual financial psychology include  age,timeframe,risk  tolerance,funds  available,time  available  to
commit to the markets,whether you are a fast or slow thinker,and others. One of the first goals of any market participant should be to find a
combination of:1)an approach or strategy and 2)a timeframe,which
together fits your personality.These two critical pieces of the puzzle are
often overlooked,as people jump from style to style without ever
committing to one.Always be curious about alternative approaches,but try to become a specialist injust a few setups,developed from your experience in trading as you follow an overallplan that suits your personality,so that   you can consistently profit.
Anchoring Bias
Daniel Kahneman is a psychologist and economist who won the 2002 Nobel  Memorial Prize in Economic Sciences.One of the investor biases identified   by Kahneman is the Anchoring Bias.Investopedia defines Anchoring Bias as “the tendency to be over-influenced by the earliest information presented   tous when making decisions,thus allowing oneselfto be driven to a
decision or conclusion that is biased towards that initial piece of
information,the “anchor.”Anchoring is a cognitive bias known as a "heuristic"or “rule of thumb.”
In the markets,our cost basis is the personal scorecardby which we
measure the success or failure of our trade or investment.The price we   paid becomes our anchor point.It is the basis of our“price memory.”It is our subjective anchor point which can influence our future buying and    selling decisions.
Here are several types of anchoring biases that can negatively affect your trading strategy ifyou are not mindful of them.
影响个人财务心理的几个个人因素包括年龄、时间范围、风险承受能 力、可用资金、投入市场的可用时间、你是快速思考者还是慢速思考 者，以及其他因素。任何市场参与者最初的目标之一应该是找到一个 组合：1)一种方法或策略和2)一个时间范围，两者结合起来适合你
的性格。这两块关键拼图经常被忽视，因为人们在不同风格之间跳来   跳去，却从未真正坚持一种。始终保持对替代方法的好奇心，但尝试  成为少数几个设置的专业人士，这些设置是从你在交易中的经验中发   展而来的，你遵循的是适合你性格的整体计划，这样你才能持续获利。
锚定效应
丹尼尔 ·卡尼曼是一位心理学家和经济学家，获得了2002年诺贝尔经
济学奖。——卡尼曼识别出的一种投资者偏见是锚定效应。维基投资
词典将锚定效应定义为“在做出决策时，过度受最早提供的信息影响，  从而让自己被驱动到偏向于最初那部分信息的决策或结论，即‘锚点’。 锚定是一种认知偏见，被称为‘启发式’或‘经验法则’。”
在市场中，我们的成本基础是我们衡量交易或投资成功或失败的评 分卡。我们支付的价格成为我们的锚点。它是我们‘价格记忆’的 基础。它是我们的主观锚点，可能影响我们未来的买卖决策。
如果你不注意，以下几种锚定偏差可能会对你的交易策略产生负面影响。
Personal Anchors
We all have personal dates that we anchor from.Think of your birth date or “our IPO”and the annual celebrations of that day.We also attach
significance  to  other  dates,such  as  graduations,anniversaries,or  holidays. Or even casual anchors,"she seems so much happier since she met Bob."    These are mental reference points to which we assign meaning in order to  keep track of our progress or lack of it.These subjective events can
influence our thoughts and even our behaviors.
Iexperienced the anchoring bias after going through a divorce.My account  equity was divided in halfin the divorce settlement,andI was anchored to   the previous higher balance.I found myself swinging for the fences because I had a smaller account and tried to get it all back at once.Because my
anchor was the previous higher balance,it clouded my judgment and
decision making.When I quickly grew my post-divorce account balance by    50%,I didn't view it as a victory.I was still anchored to the pre-split balance and viewed the account as being down 33%from the former peak.My
anchor point didn't allow me to see my positive performance for what it
was,a 50%gain.It wasn't until I got back to my anchor of my predivorce    equity high that I was able to view my gains as more than simply a return back to even.
Price Target Mental Anchors
Consider the danger of price targets as anchors for a stock.Ifan influential  analyst appears on television and mentions that he is bullish on XYZ stock, which currently trades at$55,but that his price target is $150.When
people hear such a bullish proclamation,they often get anchored to that target  and  neglect  risk  management.Instead  ofraising  their  stop(to
protect accumulated gains)as the stock climbs,they fixate on the price target  “the   expert”projected.
个人锚定
我们都有个人锚定的日期。想想你的生日或“我们的IPO”, 以及那 天每年的庆祝活动。我们还重视其他日期，例如毕业典礼、周年纪念 日或假期。甚至偶然的锚定，“自从她遇到Bob 以来，她似乎快乐多 了。”这些都是我们赋予意义以跟踪我们的进展或缺乏进展的心理参 考点。这些主观事件会影响我们的想法，甚至我们的行为。
我在经历离婚后体验到了锚定效应。我的账户权益在离婚协议中分了 一半，我被锚定在了之前的较高余额上。由于账户较小，我试图一次 性全部收回损失，因此采取了冒险策略。由于我的锚点是之前的较高 余额，这蒙蔽了我的判断和决策。当我在离婚后迅速将账户余额增长 了50%时，我没有将其视为胜利，我仍然锚定在分拆前的余额，并将 账户视为从峰值下跌了33%。我的锚点使我无法看到我的实际表现， 即50%的涨幅。直到我回到离婚前的权益高点锚定后，我才能够将我 的收益视为不仅仅是回到盈亏平衡点。
价格目标心理锚定
考虑将价格目标作为股票的锚点的风险。如果一个有影响力的分析师在电视 上出现并提到他对XYZ股票持牛市看法，该股票目前交易价格为55美元， 但他的价格目标是150美元。当人们听到这样的牛市宣言时，他们通常会  锚定那个目标并忽视风险管理。当股票上涨时，他们不是提高止损位(以保 护累积的收益),而是专注于“专家”预测的价格目标。
It is a shame to see anyone purchase a stock at$55,ride it up to $100 or
more and refuse to sell as it weakens because,"the analyst said it would go to $155.”Don't get stuck on a price target and refuse to take gains when it   is prudent,or worse,ride the stock all the way back down to the purchase   price,or lower.Winners do not “take care of themselves.”You need to
manage winning positions based on price action.We will discuss the use of AVWAPs as stop levels in the strategies section.
Whenever I share a trade idea for a stock,I have a general idea of where the price has the potential to go,but I seldom mention a specific price target.
Often,the level I believe the stock can move to is an AVWAP from a prior
high,which becomes a "level of interest"where resistance,which is
discussed in detail later in this book,may be found.I look at these levels not as “price targets”but a place we could reasonably expect the stock to travel to.Rather than mention a price target,I refer to“worst case”stop levels
pertinent to my timeframe.I don't want to fill people's heads with ideas of riches fueled by outrageous price targets.Instead,I want people to
remember the cardinal rule:risk management is always job#1.
Influence of Market Anchors
An anchor price held by a larger group of participants will have far greater significance than one held by a handful of people.The greater the market's price memory for a stock the more likely that memory effect will influence   future crowd behavior.The market“crowd”is a more reasonable
measurement than our personal anchors because it represents a
consensus of the market participants'mindset.We can never possibly know the reasons or motivations ofeach individual participant to buy or sell,and  fortunately,we do not need to.
看到任何人以55美元的价格买入股票，然后将其推升至100美元或
更高，并在其走弱时拒绝卖出，因为“分析师说它会涨到155美元”, 这是件令人遗憾的事。不要执着于一个价格目标，在明智的时候拒绝  获利，或者更糟，让股票一路跌回购买价格，甚至更低。赢家不会
“照顾好自己”。你需要根据价格行动来管理盈利头寸。我们将在策 略部分讨论AVWAP 作为止损位的使用。
每当我分享一只股票的交易思路时，我通常对价格可能的运行方向有一个 大致的了解，但很少提及具体的价位目标。很多时候，我认为股票可能运 行到的水平是一个来自先前高点的AVWAP,   这成为一个“值得关注的水 平”,在这个水平上可能会找到阻力位——本书后面将详细讨论这一点。 我看待这些水平，不是作为“价位目标”,而是我们合理预期股票可能运 行到的位置。我更倾向于提及“最坏情况”的止损位，这些止损位与我所 使用的时间框架相关。我不想让人们被不切实际的价位目标所驱动的财富 幻想所填满。相反，我希望人们记住最基本的规则：风险管理永远是第一 要务。
市场锚点的影响
一个由更大群体参与者持有的锚价将比少数人持有的锚价具有更大的意义。 股票的市场价格记忆越强，记忆效应就越有可能影响未来的群体行为。市场 “群体”比我们个人的锚更合理的衡量标准，因为它代表了市场参与者心态 的共识。我们永远不可能知道每个个体参与者买卖的原因或动机，而且幸运 的是，我们也不需要知道。
Important Anchor Points                                                                     重要的锚点
We  derive  shared  market  anchors  from  various  events  deemed  significant to  the  market.When  there  is  an  event  which  causes  a  big  shift  in  the
market's  psychology,it  becomes   a  level  to   anchor  a  AVWAP.These   events can  be  a  price  breakout  for  no  reason  other  than  price  action,or  we  may   associate  it  with  a  fundamental  catalyst  such  as  an  earnings  report,
industry  or  sector  news,or  an  economic  report.We  will  explore  the
individual  catalysts  and  specific  anchor  points   in  depth  in  the  strategy section.
Suggestions   and   Ideas   for   Personal   Trading Practices
Understand What You Can Control
There  is  little  we  can  control  in  the  market.This  can  be  a  source  of
frustration  to  those  without  a  solid  understanding  of  market   structure   and a  plan  to  deal  with  uncertainties  and  market  surprises.The  illusion  of
control  is  greater  than  its  reality  because  of  the   subjective  nature  of  our
analysis.While  we  may  do  our  best  to  make  sure  our  analysis  is  unbiased,   the  market  will  throw  surprises  at  us,which  can  devastate  our  accounts  in the  short-term.We  want  to  plan   for  the  best   and  prepare   for  the  worst.
That  is  why  an  exit  strategy  for  our  losers  is  so  important.
Working With Heightened Uncertainty
Initially,you  can  control  the   size  you  commit  to   a  trade,but  market
environments  are  never  the  same.Sometimes  the  market  seems  to  fire  on
all  cylinders,and  it  feels  as  though  you  can  do  no  wrong  and  those  are  times to  “go  for  it.”Other  times(often  during  earnings  season-the  times  of  the
year  that  earning  reports  are  published)there  is  a  greater  sense  of  caution
我们从被认为对市场有重大意义的各种事件中推导出共享市场锚。当出现： 一个导致市场心理发生重大变化的事件时，它就成为一个用于锚定
AVWAP   的水平。这些事件可以是无缘无故的价格突破，或者我们可以将  其与基本面催化剂联系起来，例如盈利报告、行业或部门新闻或经济报告。 我们将在策略部分深入探讨各个催化剂和具体的锚点。
个人交易实践的建议和想法
了解你能控制什么
在市场中我们能够控制的东西很少。对于那些缺乏对市场结构和应对不确定 性与市场意外的计划的理解的人来说，这可能会成为一个令人沮丧的来源。 由于我们分析的客观性，控制的错觉大于其现实。虽然我们可能尽力确保我 们的分析是无偏的，但市场会给我们带来惊喜，这可能会在短期内摧毁我们 的账户。我们希望计划最好的情况，并为最坏的情况做好准备。这就是为什 么对亏损的退出策略如此重要的原因。
应对高度不确定性
最初，你可以控制你投入交易的规模，但市场环境永远不会相同。有 时市场似乎运转得非常顺利，感觉你做什么都不会错，那些就是“放 手一搏”的时候。其他时候(通常是在财报季——即发布盈利报告的 年份 — — 期间)市场会显得更加谨慎
in the market  and those heightened periods  of uncertainty  are the time to slow  things  down.
If we were to investigate the daily P&L of an
emotionally intelligent trader,we would find
occasions   of   trading    actively   and   occasions   of
standing back.We would see periods of high-risk taking and periods of caution.All markets are
not created equal:some bring more opportunity,
some less.The self-aware trader knows when
"it's my market"and goes into opportunity-
seeking mode.That same trader knows when
"it's not my market"and preserves capital.
—Dr.Brett Steenbarger Trading Psychology 2.0
In  Uncertainty,Cash  is  a  Position
We  can  adjust  our market  exposure with  a reduction  in  our  share  size(risk amount)per  trade,be  more  selective  in  the  stocks  we  trade,switch  to  a
shorter  timeframe,or  maybe  employ  a  different  strategy  than  what  we
typically do.We can alsojust sit on the sidelines in cash.Cash can be the
best position ifyou don't perceive an edge or insight that will help you be
profitable.Cash  gives  us  the  ability  to  observe  objectively,rather  than  force inferior trade  setups.One  of my  favorite  market  phrases  is,“It  is  better  to
be on the sidelines and wish you were in,than it is to be in the market and wish you were out.”
,市场中的不确定性会加剧，而那些高不确定性时期就是时候放慢脚步了。
如果我们调查一个情商高的交易者的每日损益表，我们  会发现交易活跃和观望的场合。我们会看到高风险承担  和谨慎的时期。所有市场并非平等：有些带来更多机会， 有些则较少。自我认知的交易者知道何时“这是我的市  场”,并进入寻求机会的模式。那位交易者也知道何时
“这不是我的市场”,并保全资本。—— Brett
Steenbarger    博士交易心理学2.0
Dt
在不确定性中，现金是一种头寸
我们可以通过减少每笔交易的持股比例(风险金额)来调整我们的市  场敞口，更谨慎地选择我们交易的股票，切换到更短的时间框架，或  者采用与我们通常不同的策略。我们也可以选择持有现金观望。如果  你没有意识到任何能帮助你盈利的优势或洞察力，现金可能是最好的  选择。现金让我们能够客观地观察，而不是强迫自己进行劣质交易设  置。我非常喜欢的一个市场短语是，“在边线上观望并希望自己在场， 比在场内并希望离场要好。”
Fear of Missing Out(FOMO)                                                                       错失恐惧症(FQMO)
Before we move on,let's discuss the Fear of Missing Out(“FOMO”).FOMO is described as anxiety caused by the belief others may have more fun or,in    the markets,may make more money than you do.Those who have a plan
and buy stocks properly do not experience FOMO.
It is the  “Johnny-come-latelys”who read news  about  a  company,look  at the soaring price and cannot resist but to get involved.Rather than wait for a
low-risk  entry  point,they  throw  caution  to  the  wind  and  buy(chase)the
stock higher.The fear is that a stock will soar to record highs while they do not have a position.This can be a powerful motivation to chase the stock,    even  after  it  has  already  experienced  a  large,short-term  move  and  may  in  reality  have  little  or  no  further  upside.These  are  risky  purchases  because  it is difficult to keep tight stops and limit losses ifthe stock reverses.
Ifyou miss out on the first move a stock makes,then it is better to wait.
Often,the  stock  will  undergo  an  orderly  correction(by  price  or  through
time)and then provide  a  low-risk  opportunity  to  get  involved.If the  stock doesn't pull back and give you a new buy point,remember this phrase
“missed opportunity is better than lost money.”Embrace the JOMO(joy of missing  out)because  you  stayed  disciplined  with  your  approach.
Contrarian Trading
We define a contrarian as  someone who opposes or rejects popular opinion. In  the  markets,it  means  to  trade  against  trends,to  buy  when  the  trend  is
lower  and  to  sell  when  the  momentum  is  higher.Sentiment  indicators
attempt  to  identify  extreme  levels  where  a  trend  may  tire,so  a  contrarian can make a trade in the opposite direction.
As you may have guessed,I am not a contrarian trader.I believe “the trend is your friend until it bends or ends.”To trade in the direction of the trend  is  mathematically  correct.In  an  uptrend,the  sum  of the  rallies  is  always
在我们继续之前，让我们讨论一下错失恐惧症( “FOMO”)。
FOMO  被描述为因相信他人可能比你有更多乐趣或在市场中可能赚更 多钱而产生的焦虑。有计划并正确购买股票的人不会经历FOMO。
正是那些“后来者”读了关于某公司的新闻，看到股价飙升，便忍不 住要参与其中。他们不是等待低风险的入场点，而是置若罔闻，追高 买入股票。他们担心股价会飙升到历史新高，而自己却空仓。这种恐 惧感可以成为追高的强大动力，即使股价已经经历了大幅短期波动，
并且实际上可能已经没有或几乎没有进一步上涨的空间。这些购买行  为风险很高，因为如果股价反转，很难设置严格的止损点并限制损失。
如果你错过了股票的第一次启动，那么最好等待。通常，股票会进 行有序的修正(通过价格或时间),然后提供一个低风险参与的机 遇。如果股票没有回调并给你一个新的买入点，请记住这句话“错 过的机会胜于亏损的钱”。拥抱JOMO   (错过的喜悦),因为你坚 持了你的方法纪律。
逆向交易
我们定义逆向交易者为反对或拒绝流行观点的人。在市场中，这意味 着逆势交易，即在趋势较低时买入，在动能较高时卖出。情绪指标试 图识别趋势可能疲惫的极端水平，因此逆向交易者可以在相反的方向 进行交易。
正如你可能猜到的，我不是一个逆向交易者。我相信“趋势是你的朋友，直 到它弯曲或结束。”顺应趋势交易在数学上是正确的。在一个上升趋势中， 反弹的总和总是
greater than the sum of the declines.If we buy correctly(as a move begins, and not by chasing prices after the trend is underway)and manage risk
(with an appropriate trade size and a strategy to cut losses quickly),there is no reason to be“smarter”than the rest ofthe market.
It may be difficult to accept price action as being reasonable when stocks make big runs.It is said,"the collective intelligence of the crowd sinks to the level of the least educated participant.”If price action makes little
sense,it is not a reason to be a "contrarian"and bet against the crowd's
behavior.It is a reason to study the action more carefully on shorter
timeframes and plan for a potential reversal.There is no such thing as a    stock's being “up too much”if there are more buyers.Likewise,there is no such thing as a stock's being “down too much”ifthere are still sellers
present.
A Brief Discussion of Stop Losses
A stop loss order is designed to protect your capital after you start a new
position in a stock.As we know,risk management is always job#1.Thatjob begins in the planning stage of the trade when you determine what your
maximum risk will be on the trade.There are two common types of stop loss orders,the stop market and the stop limit.A stop market order simply says, “if the stock trades at 24.35,sell my stock at the market.”The stop limit
order gives you more control of the order.It might be entered as,"stop
24.35,with a limit of 24.20."For the stop limit,it will sell the stock as soon  as the stop is triggered with a trade at 24.35 and it will continue to sell the stock down to a limit of 24.20.The placement of stop orders is discussed
later in more detail.
大于下跌的总和。如果我们正确地买入(在行情开始时，而不是在 趋势展开后追涨)并管理风险(使用适当的交易规模和快速止损的 策略),就没有理由比市场其他参与者“更聪明”。
当股票大幅上涨时，人们可能难以接受价格行为是合理的。据说，“群体 的集体智慧会下降到最受教育程度最低的参与者的水平。”如果价格行为 缺乏意义，那并不是成为“逆向操作者”并赌对群体行为的原因。而是一 个原因，需要更仔细地研究较短时间框架内的行为，并计划潜在的逆转。 如果有更多的买家，股票就不存在“涨得太高”的情况。同样地，如果有 仍然存在的卖家，股票也不存在“跌得太低”的情况。
关 于 止 损 的 简 要 讨 论Astop   loss   order   is   designed   to protect your capital after you start anew
股票中的位置。众所周知，风险管理始终是第一要务。这项工作始于 交易的规划阶段，当你确定交易的最大风险时。有两种常见的止损指 令类型，即止损市价单和止损限价单。止损市价单简单地说，“如果 股票交易在24.35,以市价卖出我的股票。”止损限价单让你对订单  有更多的控制。它可能被输入为，“止损24.35,限价24.20。”对于 止损限价单，它将在触发止损并以24.35的价格成交时立即卖出股票， 并继续以不超过24.20的限价卖出股票。止损指令的放置将在后面更  详细地讨论。

Averaging
4.   了解如何使用AVWAP  实现市场目标
W
e can measure the VWAP and AVWAP for any financial product where price and volume data are available.The traditional VWAP is the volume
weighted arithmetic mean ofall trades for one day.When we change our   measurement period from the start of the day,it becomes“anchored”to a user defined starting point.
The idea for a point-and-click anchoring of the VWAP is one that Ihad been thinking about from the first time I used the VWAP in 2003.It was in 2015
when TC2000 implemented this feature at my request.Since then,dozens of other technical analysis platforms have followed their lead and made it
available on their charts.By calculating the volume weighted average price starting at an anchor point,the VWAP becomes an AVWAP(Anchored
VWAP).The AVWAP calculates the cumulative and dynamic(adjusts in real time)VWAP from the anchor point forward.With the AVWAP,you can
better understand the shifts between buyers and sellers that occur over all timeframes,notjust from the start of a day.
The calculation and interpretation of VWAP and the AVWAP is the same
regardless of the anchor point or the timeframe analyzed.In short,the
Anchored VWAP is a VWAP with a specific time anchor point chosen by the   trader.If the VWAP begins at any point other than the start of a new day, it  is  the“VWAP  anchored from”the  start  of the  measurement,or
AVWAP.
我们可以测量任何价格和成交量数据可用的金融产品的VWAP  和
AVWAP 。传统的VWAP 是一天内所有交易的成交量加权算术平均值。当 我们把测量周期从一天的开始改变时，它会“锚定”到一个用户定义的起 始点。
关于VWAP 的点按式锚定想法，是我从2003年第一次使用VWAP 时就 开始思考的。是2015年，TC2000  根据我的要求实现了这个功能。从  那时起，数十个其他技术分析平台都效仿并推出了他们的图表上。通  过从锚定点开始计算成交量加权平均价格，VWAP  变成了AVWAP
(锚定VWaéP) 。AVWAP     从锚定点向前计算累积和动态(实时调整) 的VWAP。  有了AVWAP,   你可以更好地理解买卖双方在所有时间段
内发生的转变，而不仅仅是从一天的开始。
VWAP 和AVWAP  的计算和解释与锚点或分析的时间段无关。简而言之，锚定
VWAP 是由交易者选择特定时间锚点的VWAP。 如果VWAP 不是从新一天的开 始点开始，那么它就是“从测量开始锚定的VWAP”,  即AVWAP。

In the AVWAP calculation,each share receives equal weight.It does not
assume that an institutional share traded is more important than a share traded by a retail trader;one share,one vote. The AVWAP averages price and volume from any point to show us who is really in control ofthe
trend.It is a quick and easy way to identify the trend from the start of the anchor point.It keeps us on the right side of the market,"the trend
is your friend.”The AVWAP is a technical tool that allows us to determine who is in control(buyers or sellers)from any point.It shows us how well

在AVWAP   计算中，每份股票都获得相等的权重。它不会假设机构 交易的股票比散户交易者交易的股票更重要；一份股票，一票。
AVWAP  从任何一点平均价格和成交量，以显示谁真正控制着趋势。 它是一种快速简便的方法，从锚点开始识别趋势。它让我们站在市   场的正确一边，“趋势是你的朋友。”AVWAP 是一种技术工具，  让我们能够从任何一点确定谁在控制(买方或卖方)。它告诉我们
they maintain control,or if there are signs of a trend slowdown or potential reversal.

proven innocent"and“innocent until proven guilty."What Imean by them is that the benefit of the doubt should go to the direction ofthe trend.A
trend,once established is more likely to continue than reverse.That is a tenet oftechnical analysis.

无论时间跨度如何，当股票价格高于AVWAP   时，买方掌控局面；当 股票价格低于AVWAP时，卖方掌控局面。在本书的其余部分，你会 发现我使用“有罪直到被证明无罪”和“无罪直到被证明有罪”这样 的短语。我所说的意思是，疑虑应该倾向于趋势的方向。 一旦趋势确 立，它更有可能继续而不是反转。这是技术分析的一个信条。
AVWAP:An Unbiased Analysis of
Market Flow
AVWAP analysis allows us to be more discerning in our analysis and in the trades we make,because it gives us a stronger understanding of how
capital flows through markets.It helps us to identify important price levels in the market where sentiment is likely to change.When we recognize
these levels in advance,we can study them more closely,on shorter timeframes.
On these shorter timeframes,we look for evidence where buyers or sellers   may gain an edge.We want to identify the key levels where we can plan our trade,whether  entering  or  exiting  the  market,by  figuring  the risk/reward  ratio.Then we patiently wait for price confirmation before we execute and  put our money at risk.Once in a position,ourjob switches from analyst to    risk  manager.
Dollar Cost Average(DCA)
The easiest way to understand the Volume Weighted Average Price(VWAP) is to consider the investment strategy known as “Dollar Cost Averaging.”
The DCA strategy is to invest a fixed dollar amount at a regular interval,
such as once per month.When you invest the same amount each month;
whether the market is up,down,or sideways,it reduces the timing risks for longer-term investors.DCA is more about "time in the market"versus
“timing the market.”
Ifyou invest$1,000 each month into your favorite long-term stock,at the end of one year,you will have invested$12,000 in the stock.When you
decide to sell your stock,you need to report your cost basis to the IRS so
they can collect their "fair share"of the profits.How do you calculate your
AVWAP: 市场流量无偏分析
AVWAP  分析使我们能够更细致地进行分析和交易，因为它让我们对 资本如何在市场中流动有了更深入的理解。它帮助我们识别市场中可 能改变情绪的重要价格水平。当我们提前认识到这些水平时，我们可 以在较短的时间框架下更仔细地研究它们。
在这些较短的时间框架内，我们寻找买方或卖方可能获得优势的证据。 我们希望识别我们可以规划交易的关键水平，无论是进入还是退出市  场，通过计算风险/回报率。然后我们耐心等待价格确认，然后再执   行并将我们的资金置于风险之中。一旦建立头寸，我们的工作就从分  析师转变为风险管理者。
美元成本平均法(DCA)
理解成交量加权平均价(VWAP)  最简单的方法是考虑一种称为“美  元成本平均法”的投资策略。DCA 策略是在固定的时间间隔内投资  固定金额美元，例如每月一次。当你每月投资相同金额时；无论市场 是上涨、下跌还是横盘，它都能降低长期投资者的时机风险。DCA
更注重“市场中的时间”而非“把握市场时机”。
如果你每月投资$1,000到你最喜欢的长期股票中，一年结束时，你将在该 股票上投资了$12,000。当你决定出售你的股票时，你需要向IRS 报告你的 成本基础，以便他们可以收取他们“公平份额”的利润。你如何计算你的
average cost per share?Do you take the  12 separate purchase prices,add them up and divide by twelve?These may give you an approximate price, but the IRS will not like it when you give them this “halfassed”calculation when it is time to pay taxes on your big gains.
Table 5.3 shows the stock price paid for each of the 12 purchases.When you invest a constant dollar amount($1,000/month)and the price of the stock   fluctuates,you will purchase a different number of shares each month.
When the price of the stock is lower,you will purchase more shares(see month  1)and when the price is higher(see month  12)you will purchase fewer  shares.
At the end of this 12-month period,you will have accumulated 209.05
shares ofthe stock.Your dollar cost average paid for the stock would be $57.40($12,000 divided by 209.05).In essence,$57.40 is the Volume
Weighted Average Price(VWAP)of your investment.The mathematical average,based on price alone,would be $59.42,which is not the correct number.
平均每股成本?你是取12个单独的购买价格，加起来然后除以十二? 这可能给你一个近似的价格，但在报税时，IRS 不会喜欢你给出这
种“敷衍了事”的计算结果。
表5.3显示了12次购买的每笔股票的股价。当你投资一个固定的金额 ($1,000/月)且股价波动时，你每个月购买的股票数量会不同。当 股价较低时，你会购买更多股票(参见第1个月),而当股价较高
(参见第12个月)时，你会购买较少股票。
在这个12个月期结束时，你将积累209.05股该股票。你的美元成 本平均价为$57.40($12,000除以209.05)。本质上，$57.40是 你投资的成交量加权平均价 (VWAP)。   仅基于价格计算的平均 值为$59.42,这不是正确的数字。

VWAP   Calculation
VWAP=Sum(price x volume at price/sum Total Volume)
In plain English,we multiply the price of the trade by the total number of
shares traded  at  each price,and that number  is then  divided by  the total
number of shares traded to come up with VWAP.Fortunately,we do not
have  to  do  these  calculations;they  are  built  into  any  decent  chart  platform. The  VWAP  starts  at  the first  data  point(whether  it  is   1-minute,30-
minutes,daily,or other period)and builds with each new trade.The
more  volume  traded  at  a  certain  price  level,the  greater  the  weighting
(and  more  impact)that  price  has  on  VWAP.Similarly,the  larger  the
timeframe  calculated,the  less  impact  each  new  period  will  have  on  the
weight.
VWAP  计算
VWAP             (成交量x 价格)
■成交量
VWAP 总和(价格x 成交量at 价格/总和总成交量)
用简单的语言来说，我们将每个价格下的交易价格乘以交易的 总股数，然后将这个数字除以交易的总股数，从而得出
VWAP。幸运的是，我们不必进行这些计算；它们已经内置在   任何可靠的图表平台中。VWAP  从第一个数据点(无论是1分钟、 30分钟、每日或其他周期)开始，并随着每一笔新交易而累积。 在某个价格水平上交易量越大，该价格对VWAP  的权重(和影   响)就越大。类似地，计算的时间跨度越大，每个新周期对权   重的影响就越小。
The AVWAP calculation begins with the firstcandle.In most platforms,the first value isthe actual VWAP of that first candle.绑The   boxed   in   area   on   the   largertimeframe    is    magnified    in    the box   to   the   right.It   shows   thestarting   value   of   the   VWAP.

Data Settings
When the user chooses the timeframe to study VWAP,there may be an
option for how the VWAP is calculated in your charting software.To
achieve the most accurate VWAP value,you want to use the shortest
timeframe available without affecting the ability to see it clearly on the
chart(see Chart 5.5 to see how the data can appear to be“scrunched up”on shorter timeframes where there are more candles).Unless we use tick data, which uses every transaction in the calculation,all VWAPs that do not use    tick-data will be a very close approximation to the actual VWAP.For our
purposes,the variances are not critical.Just remember,the shortest time increments willprovide the most accurate VWAP approximation.

数据设置
当用户选择研究VWAP  的时间跨度时，您的图表软件中可能会有一个 选项来决定如何计算VWAP。为了获得最准确的VWAP值，您希望使 用最短的时间跨度，同时不影响在图表上清晰地看到它(参见图表
5.5,以了解在较短时间跨度上数据如何看起来“拥挤”在一起，因为 有更多的蜡烛图)。除非我们使用逐笔数据(它使用每笔交易进行计  算),否则所有不使用逐笔数据的VWAP  都将非常接近实际的
VWAP。对于我们来说，这些差异并不关键。请记住，最短的时间增 量将提供最准确的VWAP近似值。
For intraday trading,tick data is the absolute accurate number for VWAP
because it averages every single trade.Many platforms do not allow for
such precise data,and  some allow for intra-minute(10,15,30  second)price bars(or candles).For all but the most active of intraday scalpers,a1-
minute period is short enough to understand the VWAP intraday.The
longer the period of price data studied,the longer timeframe you can “get away with,"but it is sometimes valuable to refer to the shorter timeframe for a more accurate look at the true value.

Active traders should start the day with a 1-minute timeframe for the first    part of the day,and then use longer timeframes as the data gets “scrunched up”and it becomes difficult to differentiate the candles.A shorter
timeframe slightly increases accuracy at new anchor points,but the longer timeframes allow more clarity of the larger picture.Shorter term
timeframe traders will be the participants who will benefit the most from the  intraday  charts.
对于日内交易， tick  数据是VWAP  的绝对准确数字，因为它平均了 每一笔交易。许多平台不允许使用这种精确数据，而有些平台允许使 用分钟级(10、15、30秒)价格柱(或蜡烛图)。对于大多数日内  剥头皮交易者来说，1分钟的周期足够短，可以理解VWAP  的日内  表现。所研究的价格数据周期越长，你“能容忍”的时间框架就越  长，但有时参考较短的时间框架可以更准确地了解真实价值。

活跃的交易者应该在一天的开始时，使用1分钟的时间框架进行白天  的第一部分，然后随着数据“挤压”在一起，并且难以区分蜡烛时， 使用更长的时间框架。较短的时间框架略微提高了新锚点的准确性， 但更长的时间框架允许更清晰地了解大局。短期时间框架的交易者将 是从日内图表中受益最多的参与者。
When considering where to set your anchor,the most common choices     are  to   anchor  from  the:open(0),high(H),low(L),or  close(C).The  most accurate AVWAP measurement will include as much data as possible,so  the OHLC/4 is best,as it is the most inclusive of the data available.This   simply means the weighting ofthe AVWAP will not be overly influenced    by the open,high,low or close,it treats them all equally.
Is the AVWAP a Moving Average?
When viewed on a chart,it is easy to confuse AVWAP with a traditional
periodic(or rolling)time weighted moving average.Time is part of the
calculation ofthe AVWAP,but it is not the typical rolling time-based
method used in the calculation of a moving average,where older data drops off and is replaced with newer data.
The AVWAP is the cumulative average price,weighted by volume.The
value of AVWAP changes with the continued addition of new price and
volume data,from the fixed starting point of our anchor.As time
progresses,the amount of data builds cumulatively and the AVWAP will
move up or down.We can view this as a gauge of an emerging trend.The
AVWAP is displayed as a line,and it moves up and down as time progresses, and while the AVWAP looks like a rolling period average price-the
AVWAP is materially different(and more valuable)because it starts at a signficant event and builds with each new data point.
Momentum  and  Trend  versus  Value
Like any indicator,the analysis ofthe AVWAP will have different
applications to various market participants.A long momentum participant will view the positive slope ofthe AVWAP as confirmation that their
position is working.When this occurs,they want to stay involved and
在考虑设置锚点位置时，最常见的选项是从：开盘价(0)、最高价
(H)、 最低价 (L) 或收盘价 (C) 进行锚定。最准确的AVWAP  测  量将包含尽可能多的数据，因此OHLC/4 是最好的，因为它包含了可用 数据中最全面的部分。这意味着AVWAP  的权重不会过度受到开盘价、 最高价、最低价或收盘价的影响，它将它们都平等对待。
AVWAP 是移动平均线吗?
在图表上查看时，很容易将AVWAP  与传统的周期性(或滚动)时  间加权移动平均线混淆。时间是AVWAP   计算的一部分，但它不是  移动平均线计算中常用的典型滚动时间方法，其中旧数据会消失并被 新数据取代。
AVWAP 是按成交量加权的累积平均价格。AVWAP 的值随着新价格 和成交量数据的持续添加而变化，从我们的锚点固定起始点开始。随 着时间的推移，数据会累积增加，AVWAP   会向上或向下移动。我们 可以将其视为一个新兴趋势的指标。AVWAP   以线条形式显示，随着 时间的推移上下移动，虽然AVWAP  看起来像滚动周期平均价格—— 但AVWAP  本质上不同(且更有价值),因为它从一个重要事件开  始，并随着每个新数据点而累积。
动量与趋势对比价值
像任何指标一样，AVWAP   的分析对不同市场参与者有不同的应用。 一个长期动量参与者会将AVWAP   的正斜率视为其头寸正在起作用  的确认。当这种情况发生时，他们希望保持参与并
possibly add to their position after pullbacks to the rising AVWAP.If the  momentum holder observes prices below declining AVWAP,they will not want to take new positions and might consider a sale of their longs,or to even go short the stock.
For an institutional trader who may take weeks to fill a large buy order,
they are more concerned with price and value.They willbe less aggressive about buying while the stock is above AVWAP and more aggressive while
the stock is below AVWAP.Theirjob is to purchase the shares as close to,or lower than,AVWAP.They want to buy at“discounts”to the AVWAP to help   improve the average price paid.
Speed and Lag
The amount of data used in any calculation of an average affects the rate of change of that calculation.I refer to this rate of change as"speed."All
averages become slower to respond when more data is brought into the equation.The number of data points increases throughout the period
studied;this typically makes the indicator lag as we average more data.
Unlike a moving average,the AVWAP does not always slow down with the   addition of more time and data.The volume weighting makes it possible for the AVWAP to speed up as time progresses if there is an unusual surge in   volume.
Briefly summarizing,all averages suffer from some lag as the amount of   data being averaged grows.The lag becomes more significant later in the relevant time period.New data points have diminished weight and will
continue to have less weight as time progresses.The longer the period averaged,the smoother an average line will appear.With AVWAP,
however,volume is the most important factor in the calculation and a
在回调到上升的AVWAP   后可能加仓。如果动量持有者观察到价
格低于下降的AVWAP,   他们不会想开新头寸，并可能考虑卖出
他们的多头，甚至做空该股票。
对于可能需要数周时间才能完成一个大额买入订单的机构交易员来说， 他们更关注价格和价值。当股价高于AVWAP  时，他们会较少地积极   买入；而当股价低于AVWAP 时，他们会更积极地买入。他们的工作   是在接近或低于AVWAP的位置购买股票。他们希望以低于
AVWAP的“折扣”价格买入，以帮助提高平均买入价格。
速度和滞后
用于计算平均值的任何数据量都会影响该计算的速率变化。我将这种 速率变化称为“速度”。当引入更多数据时，所有平均值都会变得更 慢地响应。在研究期间，数据点的数量会增加；这通常会导致我们平 均更多数据时，指标出现滞后。
与移动平均线不同，AVWAP  并不总是随着时间和数据的增加而减慢。 如果成交量出现异常激增，成交量加权使得AVWAP  有可能随着时间  的推移而加速。
简而言之，所有平均值都会随着被平均的数据量增加而出现 一定的滞后。这种滞后在相关时间段的后期会更加显著。新 数据点的权重会逐渐减小，并且随着时间的推移，其权重会 继续降低。平均周期越长，平均线看起来就越平滑。然而， 在使用AVWAP  时，成交量是计算中最重要的因素，并且
line     displaying     AVWAP      will      rapidly     change      shape,that     is,speed      up      or down,as        volume        surges.
In     chart     5.6,notice     how     the     VWAP"speeds     up"as     large     volume     spikes     enter the    marketjust     after     12:00    p.m.and     2     p.m.The    VWAP/AVWAP     is    unique     in    that    the     average     price     can     experience     spikes     with     more     volume,while     a
time-based     average     would     have     a     smoother     arc.

Standard Deviation and Percent Offset Bands
Sometimes    you     willsee    standard     deviation    bands     on     a    chart     with    AVWAP
(see    Chart     5.7).AVWAP     bands     are     areas     plotted     at     standard     deviation     levels
above    and    below    the    AVWAP    line.Percent    offset    bands    are    also    used    for    the
显示AVWAP      的 线 条 会 迅 速 改 变 形 状 ， 也 就 是 说 ， 随 着 成 交 量 的 激 增 ， 速 度 会 加 快 或 减 慢 。

标准差和百分比偏移带
有时你会在带有AVWAP  的图表上看到标准偏差带(参见图5.7)。AVWAP  带是在AVWAP  线上方和下 方绘制的标准偏差级别的区域。百分比偏移带也用于相同的目的，只是它们会以固定的百分比在
AVWAP的上方或下方显示。有些人选择显示这些附加信息，以识别股票“超买或超卖”的区域。这些信 息有助于他们根据历史波动模式来把握入场和出场时机。
same purpose,except they will display at a fixed percentage above or below the AVWAP.Some people choose to display this additional information to
identify  areas  where  a  stock  is  “overbought  or  oversold.”This  information helps  time  their  entries  and  exits  based  on  historical  volatility  patterns.
My preference is to not use any type of volatility band displayed over
AVWAP.I prefer a cleaner look to the charts andto manage risk based on trends,not  on  mathematical  tendencies.As  with  any  analysis  tool,ifyou  find value in it,you should continue to use it.Do what works for you.
Chart 5.7 Daily chart with AVWAP and standard deviation bands.Chart:@Trendspider
Volume Weighted Moving Average(VWMA)
Do not confuse a VWMA with the VWAP or AVWAP.AVWMA is a periodic (time-based)moving  average where more weight  is  given  to bars with
heavy volume and less emphasis on price points where less volume is   traded.While VWMA is similar to VWAP and AVWAP in that it takes the
相同的目的，只是它们会以固定的百分比在AVWAP  的上方或下方显  示。有些人选择显示这些附加信息以识别股票“超买或超卖”的区域。 这些信息有助于他们根据历史波动模式来把握入场和出场时机。
我的偏好是不使用任何显示在AVWAP  上方的波动率带。我更喜欢图表看 起来更干净，并根据趋势而不是数学趋势来管理风险。像任何分析工具一 样，如果你觉得它有价值，就应该继续使用它。做对你有效的事情。
图5.7日线图，包含AVWAP  和标准差带。图表：@Trendspider
Volume Weighted Moving Average(VWMA)
不要将VWMA 与 VWAP 或 AVWAP 混淆。VWMA 是一种周期性(基 于时间)的移动平均线，其中赋予交易量大的K 线更大的权重，而较少  关注交易量较小的价格点。虽然VWMA   与 VWAP  和AVWAP  类似，因 为它也考虑了
volume  of trading  into  consideration,the  VMWAis  fundamentally  different from VWAP and AVWAP because it is a rolling average that continually
drops off older data as it adds in newer data.The VWMA is not a focus of this material because  it  is  a  rolling  average.We  are  interested  in  the
measurement of supply and demand forces from a specific time,not an
average  period.A  rolling  time-based  average  ruins  our  entire  reason  for anchoring  from  a  specific point.

CHAPTER 1
STRATEGY
OVERVIEW
“The trend is your friend.”
—Martin Zweig
ike many useful concepts,AVWAP is simple.It can be over-complicated
by people who try to be“smarter”than everyone else,rather than
simply focus on making money in the markets.Do not confuse simple with ineffective.I wrote this book as an easy-to-understand manual on how to
use this dynamic analysis tool for better stock selection,timing entries,risk management,and  exit techniques.Ifyou  are  interested  in  sifting  through
academic studies for further information about VWAP,you can find some of these studies in the bibliography.Trust me,some of them are dense.
I hope you can profit from these strategies and use them to create and fine- tune strategies of your own.Ifyou follow my work on Twitter
(@alphatrends),you know I never suggest anyone blindly buy or sell a
stockjust because someone else(including myself)suggested it as a buy or
第一章策略概 述
“趋势是你的朋友。 ”
马丁 ·Zweig
L* 许多有用的概念，AVWAP 很简单。它会被那些试图比所有人
“聪明”的人过度复杂化，而不是专注于在市场中赚钱。不要把简单 和无效混淆。1写这本书是为了作为一个易于理解的指南，教你如何 使用这个动态分析工具进行更好的股票选择、入场时机、风险管理和 退出技巧。如果你有兴趣通过学术研究进一步了解 VWAP  的信息，
你可以在参考文献中找到其中一些研究。相信我，其中一些研究很密 集。
我希望你能从这些策略中获利，并利用它们来创建和优化自己的策略。如果 你关注我在Twitter  上的工作(@alphatrends),     你就知道我从不建议任何 人盲目买入或卖出股票，仅仅因为其他人(包括我自己)建议了它作为买入 或
sell.If you buy a stock,it should mean you did your own analysis and you know where you willplace your stop to limit losses ifyou are wrong.It is your money,so take responsibility for it.
It doesn't matter where you find an idea.Once you put your money into it,it means that it makes sense to you,and you must accept responsibility for
the outcome.If you constantly ask others what they think you should do
with your money,you probably shouldn't be trading.I hope this book will
help you to become self-sufficient and make your own trade decisions.It is a great feeling to have the confidence in your analysis so that you can spend   more time working on yourself(independent thinking and discipline)and    your strategies than listening to the opinions of others.
NOTE:THIS BOOK USES A TREND-FOLLOWING APPROACH.Trend-
following is exactly as it sounds:we look to enter an established trend at a   low-risk point and hold the stock until the trend slows or reverses.In many of the  strategy examples we examine momentum/trend trades.
Remember These Principles
Limit        Losses
Most of the examples in this book are trades that would have worked out.  The lesson is to look for the right setups and then manage risk.The losing trades shown in this book(5-10%of the total)will all have one thing in
common-small losses.Losing trades are part of the business,and how you handle them can distinguish between success or failure in the markets.
Focus      on      Price
I often say,"only price pays."People often misunderstand that statement and think I consider only price action and ignore all other information
卖出。如果你买入一只股票，这意味着你做了自己的分析，并且你知道如 果判断错误，你将在哪里设置止损以限制损失。这是你的钱，所以要对它 负责。
你在哪里找到想法并不重要。一旦你把钱投进去，这意味着它对你来 说是有意义的，你必须对结果负责。如果你不断询问别人他们认为你 应该怎么处理你的钱，你可能就不应该进行交易。我希望这本书能帮 助你变得自给自足，并做出自己的交易决策。有信心相信你的分析， 让你能花更多时间提升自己(独立思考和自律)以及你的策略，而不 是听取他人的意见，这是一种很棒的感觉。
注意：这本书采用趋势跟踪方法。趋势跟踪就是它听起来那样：我们在低风 险点进入既定趋势，并持有股票直到趋势放缓或反转。在我们研究的许多策 略示例中，我们都会分析动量/趋势交易。
记住这些原则
限制亏损
这本书中的大多数示例都是可能成功的交易。教训是寻找正确的设
置，然后管理风险。这本书中展示的亏损交易(占总交易量的5-10%) 都将有一个共同点——小亏损。亏损交易是生意的一部分，你如何处  理它们可以在市场中区分成功或失败。
关注价格
我经常说，“只有价格才管用。”人们常常误解这句话，认为我只考虑价 格行为，而忽略了所有其他信息
when I analyze a stock.Nothing could be further from the truth.The
markets are an auction process and prices alone tell us the price levels or
ranges where business took place.Current price simply tells us the present value assigned by all market participants.Price alone does not reveal other significant pieces of the complicated market puzzle.At the end of the day,
price is the scorecard.As my friend Jeff Cooper says,"Price is the final arbiter.”
Pay Attention to Multiple Timeframes
One of the biggest issues with many books about the market is that they are written with a single timeframe dimension.They are all written for either    investors,swing traders,or day traders.This material explains how to use   the AVWAP regardless ofyour timeframe.You willsee examples for many    timeframes,and you will learn how to combine the timeframes together
(multiple timeframe analysis)for better timing accuracy.
Recognize That Markets Are Fractal
We do not need to understand mathematics or geometry to recognize
fractals.If we take the time to carefully observe and understand human
nature and how stock market participants interact,we will see similar
patterns in different markets and on various timeframes.All the concepts of trend alignment and AVWAPs are transferable to other timeframes     because of the fractal nature of chart formations.
The fractal nature of markets allows  short-term traders to experience,on
smaller timeframes,what longer-term investors may take years to observe. This allows the shorter-term participant to learn market structure more
rapidly.Ifyou have a disdain for short-term trading,try to think of it as an opportunity to shorten your learning curve even if you do not participate in that timeframe.Shorter-term traders should also learn how shorter-
当我对一只股票进行分析时。这完全不是事实。市场是一个拍卖过程， 价格本身告诉我们交易发生的价格水平或区间。当前价格仅仅告诉我  们所有市场参与者赋予的现值。仅凭价格无法揭示复杂市场拼图中的  其他重要部分。归根结底，价格是记分牌。正如我的朋友杰夫 ·库珀所  说，“价格是最终的裁决者。”
注意多个时间周期
许多关于市场的书籍最大的问题之一是它们只使用单一的时间周期维 度来撰写。它们要么是为投资者、波段交易者或日内交易者撰写的。 本材料解释了如何使用AVWAP,   无论你的时间周期是什么。你会看 到许多时间周期的例子，并学习如何将时间周期结合起来(多时间周 期分析)以提高时机准确性。
认识到市场是分形的
我们不需要理解数学或几何来识别分形。如果我们花时间仔细观察 和理解人性以及股票市场参与者的互动方式，我们将在不同的市场 和不同的时间周期中看到相似的模式。由于图表形成的分形性质， 趋势一致性和 AVWAP 的所有概念都可以转移到其他时间周期。
市场的分形特性使短期交易者能够在较小的时间框架内体验到，而长 期投资者可能需要数年才能观察到的事物。这使得短期参与者能够更 快地学习市场结构。如果你对短期交易有厌恶感，试着将其视为一个 缩短你学习曲线的机会，即使你不参与那个时间框架。短期交易者还 应该学习如何较短-
term  trends  fit  together  in  a  longer-term  market  move.This  knowledge  can help you hold your winners longer.
Recognition of this fractal tendency is key to understanding why we can
apply the same analysis techniques to completely different markets and on any timeframe.We only need to learn the basics in one timeframe,and we   can apply those principles to all timeframes.The most accurate price
analysis comes from a recognition of the interplay of various timeframes together for a more complete understanding of market structure.
Don't Get Hung Up on Timeframe
My personal preferred timeframe in the market is from a few days to
several weeks.Most of the examples will be that timeframe.Please do not  get hung up on the timeframe shown on any of the charts.It is the concept that is most important.Many of the examples do not show the timeframe    because it is unnecessary to understand the point on the chart.
You Can be the “Smart Money”
We often hear that"smart money"is buying or selling  some  stock or doing something we should strive to do in the market.We are meant to feel
inferior  to  this  mysterious  group  of  participants.Here  is  the  truth,smart
money doesn't mean institutional money or a roomful of PhDs.It only
means  the  group  who  controls  the  trend(meaning  that  they  are  on  the
correct  side  ofthe  trend).It  is  a  mix  of  institutions  and  retail  traders;the
same  group  that  makes  up  the  “dumb  money”in  the  markets-the  people  on the wrong side of a trend.You can be the smart money if you understand
market structure and use the best tools properly.AVWAP is one of the most important tools you need to understand to be in the smart money camp.
期趋势如何在长期市场走势中契合在一起。这些知识可以帮助你更长时间地 持有赢家。
认识到这种分形趋势是理解我们为什么可以将相同的分析技术应用于 完全不同的市场和任何时间框架的关键。我们只需要在一个时间框架 中学习基础知识，就可以将这些原则应用于所有时间框架。最准确的 价格分析来自于对各种时间框架之间相互作用的认知，以便更全面地 理解市场结构。
不要纠结于时间框架
我个人在市场中的首选时间框架是从几天到几周。大多数示例将使 用这个时间框架。请不要纠结于任何图表上显示的时间框架。最重 要的是概念。许多示例没有显示时间框架，因为理解图表上的要点 是不必要的。
你可以成为“聪明资金”
我们经常听到“聪明资金”正在买入或卖出某些股票，或者正在做我 们应该在市场中努力做的事情。我们被意味着要感到不如这个神秘的 参与者群体。以下是真相，聪明资金并不意味着机构资金或一屋子里 的博士。它仅仅意味着控制趋势(这意味着他们站在了趋势的正确一 边)的群体。这是机构和个人交易者的混合体；就是构成市场“愚蠢 资金”的同一群体——趋势错误方的人。如果你理解市场结构并正确 使用最佳工具，你就可以成为聪明资金。
Create Your Own Process                                                                     创建你自己的流程
At the 1969 Woodstock Festival,Jimi Hendrix performed what has become one of the most recognized versions of the  "Star-Spangled Banner."Jimi
Hendrix most likely looked at the same sheet music that Francis Scott Key wrote  155  years  earlier,but what Jimi played versus what Francis  Scott
wrote was much  different.As  an  artist,Jimi“made the  song  his  own.”
This book is the "sheet music"for a market approach.You can try to play it note for note in the market,and probably do well with it.If you really want  to stand out and be a star in the markets,you will take this information for  what I intended it to be:a guide.I wrote this book for you,as a “market
artist,"to use as part of your method in the creation of a masterpiece of your  own,your  trading  process.
No one knows what will happen in the future.If we anticipate all potential  outcomes,we willnever be  surprised  and we will be ready  for  anything the  market gives us.An unemotional plan allows us to prepare for all  scenarios in case our primary thesis is proven wrong.Part of our trade plan needs to  account  for the times price  action moves  against  our  trade position.We
must be able to objectively cut an unprofitable trade before it grows into a large loss that is more difficult to recover from.
Work with Momentum
The goal of momentum trades is to buy stocks as they rise,sell them when they look to have peaked,and to avoid the  subsequent  selloff.If the trader can move from one winning stock to another,they can leverage time to
keep their  equity  in  stocks  when  trends  are  working to their  advantage.
Momentum  trading  is  about"buying  high  and  selling  higher."Of  course,we know it doesn't mean that you should chase stocks that are moving higher   but,rather to buy them as their momentum begins  so then we can manage   risk   properly.
在1969年的伍德斯托克音乐节上，吉米 · 亨德里克斯表演了成为最广为人
知的“星条旗永不落”版本之一。吉米 · 亨德里克斯很可能看了与弗朗西斯 · 斯科特 ·基155年前写的相同乐谱，但吉米演奏的与弗朗西斯 ·斯科特写的差  异很大。作为一名艺术家，吉米“让这首歌成为他自己的。”
这本书是市场方法的“乐谱”。你可以在市场中逐音符地演奏它，并： 且很可能因此做得很好。如果你真的想脱颖而出，在市场中成为明星， 你会把这条信息理解为我想让它成为的样子： 一份指南。我写这本书  是为了你，作为一个“市场艺术家”,作为你创造自己的杰作——你   的交易过程——方法的一部分来使用。
没有人知道未来会发生什么。如果我们预见到所有可能的结果，我们 就永远不会感到惊讶，并且我们会为市场给予我们的一切做好准备。
一个不带情绪的计划使我们能够为我们的主要论点被证明是错误的情 况准备所有场景。我们交易计划的一部分需要考虑到价格行为与我们 的交易头寸相反的时候。我们必须能够客观地提前结束一个无利可图 的交易，以免它发展成一个更难挽回的大损失。
与趋势共舞
动量交易的目的是在股价上涨时买入股票，在股价看似达到顶峰时卖 出，并避免随后的抛售。如果交易者能够从一个盈利的股票转移到另 一个盈利的股票，他们可以利用时间来保持他们的股票头寸，当趋势 对他们有利时。动量交易是关于“高价买入，更高价卖出。”当然， 我们知道这意味着你不应该追逐上涨的股票，而是应该在动量开始时 买入它们，这样我们才能正确管理风险。
To emphasize concepts,and not get hung up on the names of the
companies,I have removed all the symbols from the charts. The names of market winners and losers will change with different market cycles,the laws of supply and demand do not.
The "breakout"buyers are often
late to a short-term trend since they buy when the price rises above the
prior high.The breakout buys are
noted by the red arrows.

allow you to be in a position of strength from the start,rather than chasing prices higher,which increases risk levels.Put another way,ifyou wait to    buy until the price exceeds(breakout)a prior high,you miss the upward
momentum and risk the possibility that the new high fails and turns into the start ofa downward trend.

图1.1日K线图，包含传统突破买入和动量买入。图源：TC2000.com
图1.1显示了低风险动量买入的位置(绿色
箭头)作为股价重新获得上涨动量时。这些买入
让你从一开始就处于强势位置，而不是追逐
更高的价格，这会增加风险水平。换句话说，如果你等待， 买入直到价格超过(突破)之前的最高点，你错过了上涨的 势头，并承担了新高点失败并转为
下行趋势的起始的可能性。

trader.

What About Extended Hours Trading?
This book is focused on the regular trading hours for U.S.
equities,which are 9:30 a.m.to 4:00 p.m.Eastern Standard Time. The opportunity does exist to trade stocks in the pre-market as  early as 8 a.m.and in the post-market as late as 8 p.m.For most  stocks,volume is much lighter than in the regular trading
hours and that creates liquidity issues.Trades placed outside
traditional trading hours have a unique set ofrisks and,as such, are not for everyone.
large moves are often made in some stocks which may be
issuing earnings reports or reporting other news.Itypically do  not get involved in these stocks.I seldom enter new positions in the pre-market but there are opportunities for those who are
attracted to the very fast moves that can occur in these hours. That being said,IfIam holding a stock,I do like to take profits   when there are large moves in the pre-market.It is all about    your personality and your preferences.
Post-market moves are more common for the stocks of bigger companies,especially during earnings season when many
companies report their quarterly results after the 4 p.m close. This can affect some of the largest stocks in existence and the   trading can be very liquid and volatile.
What About Extended Hours Trading?
本书主要关注美国股票的常规交易时间，即东部标准时间 上午9:30至下午4:00。确实存在提前交易和盘后交易的机 会，分别最早可早至上午8点，最晚可晚至晚上8点。对于 大多数股票，盘前和盘后的交易量远低于常规交易时段， 这会导致流动性问题。在传统交易时段之外进行的交易具 有独特的风险，因此并非适合所有人。
有时开盘前时段会比较繁忙。
某些股票在提前交易时段往往会发生大幅波动，这些股票 可能正在发布盈利报告或其他新闻。我通常不会参与这类 股票。我很少在提前交易时段建立新仓位，但那些喜欢这 些时段可能出现的极快波动的人会有机会。话虽如此，如 果我在持有某只股票，当提前交易时段出现大幅波动时， 我确实喜欢获利了结。这一切都取决于你的个性和偏好。
上市后的股价波动在大型公司中更为常见，尤其是在财  报季，许多公司在下午4点收盘后报告其季度业绩时。这 可能影响一些现存的最大型股票，交易可能非常活跃且  波动性很大。
如果你容易追涨股票或无法控制你的情绪冲动，那么在延 长交易时段内成功交易将非常困难。只有你自己才能知道 是否适合你的性格在延长交易时段内进行交易。在你弄清 楚之前，在延长交易时段内保持较小的持股规模。
如果你容易追涨股票或无法控制你的情绪冲动，那么在延 长交易时段内成功交易将非常困难。只有你自己才能知道 是否适合你的性格在延长交易时段内进行交易。在你弄清 楚之前，在延长交易时段内保持较小的持股规模。
If you are prone to chasing stocks or unable to control your
emotional urges,it will be difficult for you to trade successfully in the extended hours.Only you will know ifit makes sense for
your personality to trade during the extendedhours sessions. Until you know,keep your share size small in extended trade  hours.

CHAPTER 2
SUPPORT AND
RESISTANCE
"Never  turn  a  trade  into  an  investment  or
an  investment  into  a  trade."
—Barry Ritholtz
Chapter     Objectives
1.Define Support and identify levels of Support on a chart
2.Understand Support as a level ofdemand
3.Define Resistance and identify levels of Resistance on a chart
4.Understand Resistance as a level of supply
5.Identify "levels ofinterest"on a chart
6.Use AVWAP to analyze levels of Support and Resistance
7.Use AVWAP slope to determine if buyers or sellers are in control ofthe action
第二章支撑位和阻 力位
“永远不要把交易变成投资，或者把投资 变成交易。”-Barry     Ritholtz
章节目标
he  continual  struggle  for  control  between  the  bulls   and  bears  makes  the
I     t~lmalnta                                    fncinetin~ud  f+Le            becicle      funnl             and
stock      market       a      fascinating       study      of       the      basic       laws      of      supply       and
demand.Support   and  Resistance  levels   are  where  we  understand  how markets    move.
The goal of a trader is to study how a stock reacts to the ever-present
supply and demand battles.When a trend exerts  strength,in either
direction,we must be ready to be on the correct side sowe can take part in the directional moves that follow.
AVWAPs can reveal order in the market where none appears from
traditional technical analysis tools.This is how Ifirst recognized the value ofthe AVWAP when I noticed it in 2003.Ifyou do not use AVWAP in your
analysis,you cannot see important levels of Support and Resistance that others are using successfully to make more money.
The simplest and most effective use of the AVWAP is to find “hidden”levels of Support and Resistance.How do they hide?The answer is simple:you
can't see them if you don't place the AVWAP on the chart.Once we identify Support and Resistance with the AVWAP,then we can use those levels as   the basis of our trade plan.
When we buy or sell a stock as it emerges from the battlegrounds of
Support and Resistance levels,we can also control risk easily and
objectively by placing stops outside of the consolidation range after our
entry into a new position.Therefore,it is essential to understand the
concepts of Support and Resistance in order to identify where to place the stop.
牛熊之间的持续控制权斗争使T 股票市场成为研究供求基本规律 的一个引人入胜的课题。支撑和阻力位是我们理解市场如何运作的地 方。
交易者的目标是研究股票如何应对无处不在的供需博弈。当趋势展现 出力量，无论方向如何，我们必须准备好站在正确的立场，以便参与 随之而来的方向性走势。
AVW2APs   可以揭示传统技术分析工具无法显现的市场秩序。这就 是我在2003年首次认识到AVWAP 价值的方式。如果你在分析中不 使用AVWAP,  你就无法看到其他人正在成功利用的重要支撑位和 阻力位，从而赚取更多利润。
AVWAP 最简单且最有效的使用方式是找到“隐藏”的支撑位和阻力 位。它们是如何隐藏的?答案很简单：如果你不在图表上放置
AVWAP,   就看不到它们。一旦我们通过AVWAP 识别出支撑位和阻 力位，我们就可以将这些水平作为我们交易计划的基础。
当我们买入或卖出在支持位和阻力位战场上出现的股票时，我们也可以通过在建立 新仓位后，将止损单设置在盘整区间之外，轻松且客观地控制风险。因此，理解支 持位和阻力位的概念对于确定止损单的位置至关重要。
What is Support?                                             什么是支持?
Support in the markets,or an individual stock,is an area where prices drop and there is enough buying interest(demand)to overwhelm selling
(supply)and prices level out where they find Support.Look at the thick
green line in Chart 2.1.Temporary price equilibrium after a pullback is
known as Support.This is a price range rather than a precise price point. This tendency reveals itself more in longer timeframes,where ranges are typically       larger.

Support areas form as various participants feel compelled to buy in the
same approximate area.The stock becomes more neutral or “trendless”as it builds upenough pent-upenergy from buyers and sellers for the next
trend to emerge.During a transition from a market controlled by supply to
市场中的支持位，或个股的支持位，是指价格下跌且存在足够的买入 兴趣(需求)以压倒卖出(供应)并找到支撑位使价格稳定的区域。 查看图表2.1中的粗绿线。回调后的暂时价格均衡被称为支持位。这  是一个价格区间，而不是一个精确的价格点。这种趋势在更长的时间 框架中更为明显，其中区间通常更大。

图2.1传统(非AVWAP)   支撑水平在图表上显示为一条水平区域，买方支持价格且价格 无法下跌。图表：TC2000.com
支持区域形成，因为各种参与者感到有压力在同一大致区域购买。随着买卖 双方积累足够的潜在能量，为下一趋势的出现做准备，股票变得更具中性或 “无趋势性”。在从由供应控制的市场过渡到由需求控制的市场期间，卖方 变得不那么激进，而买方则对其出价更加坚决。
control by demand,sellers become less aggressive and buyers become more assertive with their bids.
For example,participants with an open short position can be motivated to   cover(buy back)their positions profitably.Long holders who want to add to their positions perceive value,which induces them to place bids.This level  of value at Support might also motivate sidelined cash to get involved.The   collective action of participants at these price levels results in less supply
and more demand,which halts downward price activity and provides
support for the stock.This is why you should think of Support as a demand area.
What is Resistance?
Similar to Support,Resistance is not a precise level,it is an“area.”It is common for Support and Resistance to form a loose range.
Think of Resistance as an area of supply.Resistance levels halt an upward price move,at least temporarily and is the opposite of Support.At
Resistance  sellers  provide  enough  pressure(supply)to  overwhelm  the buying(demand)and  prices  "resist"going  higher.Buyers  become  less   aggressive,and sellers become more aggressive.
The formation of Resistance is a transition from a demand controlled
market to a supply controlled market(shown with the thick red line on
Chart 2.2).Resistance levels can be areas where three things occur:longs will exit,buyers will slow their purchases,and shorts will consider entry.
控制，卖方变得不那么激进，而买方则对其出价更加坚决。
例如，持有开仓短头寸的参与者可能会被激励以盈利的方式平仓(买 入)。想要增加头寸的多头持有者认为存在价值，这促使他们出价。 在支撑位这个水平的价值也可能激励被闲置的资金参与进来。在这些 价格水平上参与者的集体行动导致供应减少而需求增加，从而停止了 下跌的价格活动并为股票提供支撑。这就是为什么你应该将支撑位视 为一个需求区域。
阻力位是什么?
与支撑位类似，阻力位也不是一个精确的水平，而是一个“区域”。支 撑位和阻力位通常形成一个松散的范围。
将阻力位视为一个供应区域。阻力位会阻止价格上涨，至少在短期 内，它是支撑位的对立面。在阻力位上，卖方提供足够的压力(供 应)来压倒买方(需求),价格“抵制”上涨。买方变得不那么积 极，而卖方变得更加积极。
Resistances 的形成是从需求控制市场向供应控制市场的转变(如图 2.2中的粗红线所示)。 Resistances    水平可以是三个事情发生的区  域：多头将退出，买家将减缓他们的购买，空头将考虑入场。

Potential.Add this word to your vocabulary.You will often read phrases like "The market has support at xxx."Most of the time “xxx”refers to a price
area below where the current price resides.It is also common to hear this about  a  prior  level  of Resistance,“There  is  strong  resistance  at  xxx.”The  Resistance  levels  refer  to  areas  ofprior  price  consolidation  areas  above
current  price  levels.

我们如何使用支撑位和阻力位?
潜力。把这个词加到你的词汇中。你经常会读到像“市场在xxx   处   有   支撑。”这样的话。大多数情况下， “xxx” 指的是当前价格所在位  置下方的价格区域。也常见于谈论一个先前的Resistance 水平，“在 xxx   处有强大的Resistance。”Resistance  水平指的是当前价格水平 上方的前期价格整合区域。
没有人知道真正的支撑位和阻力位在哪里，直到事后才知晓。直到一只. 股票从之前的整理区域反弹，短期
consolidation is simply a potential Support or Resistance level.I like to call them a “level of interest.”Stocks often continue along their current
trajectory longer than people expect and through a perceived level of Support or Resistance.This can confuse participants who try to time a reversal.
Here are two phrases to remember if you get burned with an entry at unproven Support and Resistance levels.
·Fear  knows  no  Support
·   Greed knows no Resistance
Market Psychology:Levels of
Interest
It is best to not consider a potential level of Support or Resistance to be an automatic place to do business,but rather an area where you should look   for evidence that confirms or refutes your thesis.
How do we find evidence?Examine the level ofinterest on a shorter-term
timeframe and look for a price area where you expect something will
happen-typically a reversal or breakout.This is the cornerstone of the
concept of multiple timeframe analysis.Gather evidence,observe
objectively,and patiently wait for the trade opportunity to reveal itselfin a low-risk way before you commit your hard-earned money to a risk position.
Every television detective says a criminal always returns to the scene of the crime.This is often true in the markets,which will often revisit and test the  prior consolidation(Support or Resistance)zone.When we look for a prior   level ofinterest to become Support or Resistance,what we really look for is  for that area to transform into an area where price is reevaluated by
整理区仅仅是一个潜在的支撑位或阻力位。我喜欢称它们为“兴趣位”。 股票往往会沿着当前轨迹运行的时间比人们预期的要长，并且会穿过
一个感知到的支撑位或阻力位。这可能会让试图把握反转时机的人感 到困惑。
如果你在不被证实的支撑位和阻力位上被入场烧伤，请记住以下两个短语。
c 恐惧不知支撑
*贪婪不知阻力
市场心理：兴趣水平
最好不要将潜在的支撑位或阻力位视为自动的交易点，而应将其视 为一个你应该寻找证据以确认或反驳你论点的区域。
我们如何寻找证据?在较短期的时间框架内检查兴趣水平，并寻找你 预期会发生某种事情的价位区域——通常是反转或突破。这是多时间 框架分析概念的基础。收集证据，客观观察，耐心等待交易机会以低 风险的方式显现，然后才将你辛苦赚来的钱投入风险头寸。
每个电视侦探都说罪犯总会回到犯罪现场。这在市场上往往是真的，市场经 常会重新审视并测试之前的整理(支撑或阻力)区域。当我们寻找一个之前 的兴趣水平成为支撑或阻力时，我们真正寻找的是让该区域转变为一个价格 被重新评估的区域，这个区域有足够的参与者，成为一个我们可以进行低风 险、高概率入场的地点。
enough participants to become a place where we can make a low-risk,high- probability entry.You only want to make a stock purchase once you have
actual evidence of buyers stepping in and regaining control.Never buy blindly at a level on the chart.
Our mission is to anticipate areas(levels of interest)where the buying or
selling may become significant enough to halt a price advance(Resistance)  or halt a decline(Support).After we identify levels of interest,some people place a bid in that area and hope it does,in fact,become Support.My
preference is to use that area as a place to drill down the analysis to a
shorter timeframe to look for actual evidence that the buyers are gaining
control.Don't buy the dip,buy strength after the dip.Once that evidence is   present,the next step is to plan a trade based on the perceived risk relative to the reward potential.The focus should always be risk management to
assure any loss taken is small.

uptrend       and       Resistance       in       a        downtrend.Charts:@TrendSpider
你只有在有实际证据表明买方介入并重新获得控制权时，才想要购买 股票。永远不要在图表上的某个水平盲目购买。
我们的使命是预见可能出现的交易区域(兴趣水平),在这些区域中， 买入或卖出的行为可能变得足够重要，以至于会阻止价格上涨(阻力)  或阻止下跌(支撑)。在确定兴趣水平后，有些人会在该区域挂出买  单，并希望它确实成为支撑。我的偏好是使用该区域作为一个切入点， 将分析时间缩短，以寻找买家实际掌控市场的证据。不要买入下跌，
要在下跌后买入强势。一旦出现这些证据，下一步就是根据感知的风 险与潜在回报来制定交易计划。始终应关注风险管理，以确保任何亏 损都是可控的。

图表2 . 3和2 . 4展示了锚定VWAP   如何在上升趋势中充当支撑位，在下降趋势中充 当 阻 力 位 。 图 表 ： @TrendSpider
Notice the direction of the AVWAP is more important than an occasional
piercing ofthe AVWAP.One of these charts is constructed of daily data and the other with  15-minute data.Regardless of timeframe,the principles are the  same.
How Does AVWAP Play Into Support
&Resistance?
The AVWAP helps us to determine:
·How the market digests a price move
·Whether the market accepts or rejects new price activity from the onset ofa new trend
Trend and momentum traders want to be buyers when the AVWAP is
increasing and want to be sellers when AVWAP is decreasing.In a trending market,prices stay above an up-sloping AVWAP,and in a decline,prices
stay below a descending AVWAP.
注意AVWAP的方向比偶尔刺穿AVWAP 更重要。其中一个图表由日 线数据构成，另一个由15分钟数据构成。无论时间周期如何，原则  都是相同的。
AVWAP 如何影响支撑与阻力?
AVWAP 帮助我们确定：
*市场如何消化价格变动
4市场是否从一开始就接受或拒绝新趋势的价格活动
趋势交易者和动量交易者在AVWAP  上升时想买入，在AVWAP  下降 时想卖出。在一个趋势市场中，价格保持在上升的AVWAP 上方，而 在下跌中，价格保持在下降的AVWAP 下方。

Chart 2.5 Buyers  are  in  control  of the  stock  while  it  is  above  a  rising  AVWAP  and  sellers are  in  control  while  prices   are  below   a   declining  AVWAP.Chart:TC2000.com
Chart 2.5 shows buyers in control above the AVWAP and sellers in control    below it.If buyers show up on pullbacks to a rising AVWAP(1),on Chart 2.5, there is a continued appetite for the stock,which makes it more likely the    stock will continue higher.Those are the stocks we want to own.When
prices drop below AVWAP(2),it reveals less demand and we do not want to make new purchases.The lack of Support for the stock also tells us to be on our guard for potential reversals and we should shift from considering new purchases to managing our risks on any open position.

图2.5当股票价格高于上升的AVWAP  时，买方控制股票；当价格低于下降的 AVWAP 时，卖方控制股票。图：TC2000.com
图表2 . 5显示在AVWAP   上方买家掌控市场，下方卖家掌控市场。如果买家出 现在对冲上升的AVWAP   的 回 调 中 ( 1 ) , 在 图 表 2 . 5 中 ， 市 场 对 股 票 的 需 求  持续存在，这使得股票更有可能继续上涨。这些是我们想要持有的股票。当 价 格 跌 破AVWAP(2)         时，这表明需求减少，我们不想进行新的购买。股
票缺乏支撑也告诉我们要警惕潜在的逆转，我们应该从考虑新的购买转向管 理我们任何持仓的风险。
让我们首先看 一 个关于单日VWAP   支撑和阻力的例子(请注意，这些概念适 用 于 所 有 时 间 周 期 ) 。 当
stock is in a trend day(that is,trending up or down during a day),it is likely to finish near the high (long)or low(short)of the day.
Two examples in charts 2.6&2.7 show one-minute charts for one day.The chart on the left shows price action alone,and the one on the right shows
price along with the daily VWAP,which starts from the first minute of   trading.Atrader can observe Support and Resistance at VWAP/AVWAP levels in all timeframes,from the shortest intraday charts to multiple    years.
The only difference between the two charts is the addition of the daily
VWAP to the one on the right.This stock gapped higher(1)and
immediately found supply from sellers.This drove the price lower(2).After the first few minutes of trading,the buyers regained control as the stock
traded back above the daily VWAP(3)just before 10 a.m.This early
shakeout action often precedes a continuation of the direction of the
original gap.Notice how two subsequent tests ofthe VWAP also found
demand(Support)from buyers(4 and 5).There are no other technical tools which would have led you to think buyers wouldemerge where the two
blue arrows are located.Without an understanding of the proper use of the VWAP,you would never be able to see that.In fact,there is a trend upward  over the relevant timeframe.Without the VWAP you would think that the    price was entering a downward trend when the tool shows that it is more
likely that buyers will be upping their purchases(4 and5).
股票处于趋势日(也就是说，在一天内上涨或下跌),它很可能在当天的最 高点(做多)或最低点(做空)附近结束。
图表2.6&2.7中的两个示例显示了为期一天的分钟图。左侧的图 表仅显示价格行为，而右侧的图表显示了价格以及每日的VWAP
(成交量加权平均价),它从交易的第一分钟开始计算。交易者可 以在所有时间框架内观察到在 VWAP/AVWAP     水平上的支撑和阻 力，从最短的日内图表到多年图表。
这两个图表之间的唯一区别是在右边的图表中增加了每日VWAP。  这 只股票向上跳空(1),并立即从卖家中找到了供应。这导致价格下  跌(2)。在交易的前几分钟，买方重新获得控制权，因为这只股票  在上午10点之前交易回每日VWAP 之上(3)。这种早期的洗盘行动  通常预示着原始跳空方向的上行延续。注意，随后的两次VWAP 测试 也发现了买方(需求) (4和5)的支持。没有其他技术工具会让你认 为买方会出现在两个蓝色箭头所在的位置。如果不了解VWAP的正确 使用方法，你永远无法看到这一点。事实上，在相关时间段内存在一 个上升趋势。如果没有VWAP,   你会认为价格正在进入下行趋势，而 工具显示更有可能的是买方会加大购买量(4和5)。

VWAP  和AVWAP   可以揭示其他分析方法无法显示的买方和卖方兴 趣的重要水平。在上面的图表中，我们看到在图表中添加VWAP 如 何向我们展示 “ 隐藏 ” 的阻力水平 。
Chart 2.8 shows price action only while Chart 2.9 shows price along with
the daily VWAP.Notice how the stock gapped lower on the day(1)and
stayed below the declining VWAP throughout the  session.When the  slope of the VWAP is lower,it is best to stay away from the long side(that is,not to buy or hold onto  shares).In fact,with the example above,it would have
made sense to short the stockjust before  10:45  a.m.when  it rallied to the
declining  VWAP(2)and  then  resumed  its  decline.Without  the  VWAP,it
would have been much more difficult to identify where Resistance might be  found.The development of the VWAP  showed an objective measure of trend activity to compare price to as it unfolds.
Market Psychology:Support and Resistance
Consider  Support  and Resistance areas as places where a bounce might
occur,but  look  for  other  confirmations  before  making  a  purchase.Ourjob  is to  anticipate  price  scenarios,not  predict  them.
Once we identify a key level of Support or Resistance,we wait for price
confirmation(prices  begin  to  move  higher)on  a  shorter  timeframe  before putting  hard  earned  money  to  risk.
We want to be involved in an emerging move at the onset,not after atrend campaign is well underway and the risks are higher.Do not chase price
action.Ifyou miss  out,it  exposes you to too much risk.
Be aware that the more obvious a level seems to be,the more likely it is
that other traders will also know that level and they will use it as an area for a stop loss or to exit a portion of their position.This can make the
obvious level a place where failed moves are likely,so be careful with stops in  these  areas.
图表2.8仅显示价格行为，而图表2.9则显示价格以及每日 V
WAP 。 注意当日股票开盘价下跌(1),并在整个交易时段内维持在  下降的VWAP  下方。当VWAP  的斜率较低时，最好远离多头(即不 买入或持有股票)。实际上，根据上述示例，在上午10:45之前，当  它反弹至下降的VWAP(2)       并随后继续下跌时，做空该股票是有道 理的。如果没有VWAP,    将很难确定阻力位可能出现在哪里。
VWAP 的发展显示了价格变化的客观趋势活动指标，可以将其作为 比较的基准。
市场心理：支撑与阻力
将支撑和阻力区域视为可能发生反弹的地方，但在做出购买决定之前，寻找 其他确认信号。我们的任务是预见价格情景，而不是预测它们。
一旦我们识别出关键的支持或阻力位，我们会在较短的时间框架内   等待价格确认(价格开始上涨),然后再将辛苦赚来的钱冒险投入。
我们希望在趋势初期就参与其中，而不是在趋势已经全面展开且风险更   高的之后。不要追逐价格行动。如果你错过了，会让你面临过多的风险。
请注意，一个级别看起来越明显，其他交易者就越可能知道这个级别，并会 将其用作止损区域或退出部分头寸的点位。这可能使明显的级别成为失败操 作可能发生的区域，因此在这些区域设置止损时要小心。
We want to anticipate whether a price zone will be a level where a
breakout or reversal is likely to occur.To do that we try to understand at   what price zone enough participants will get involved to shift the balance of supply and demand.The AVWAP allows us the ability to better find this potential price zone because it  allows us to  compare the  instantaneous
prices  with  the  trending  price.
When you identify potential levels of Support and Resistance consider:
·Where  will  longs  be  forced  to  fearfully  liquidate  before  they sustain  a  larger  loss?
·Where  will  short  sellers  become  nervous  about  growing  losses
and become motivated to  cover their bearish bets?This  could lead to  a  short  squeeze.
·Where  will  sidelined  cash  be  unable  to  resist  getting  involved?
市场心理：自我强化
市场心理：自我强化
Market          Psychology:Self-Reinforcing
Role
The  natural  question  is,why  do  certain  price  areas  attract  enough  buyers and  sellers  to  provide  Support  or  Resistance  to  price  movement?Support  and  Resistance  areas  are  often  “self-fulfilling”in  nature.When  you  first
learn  about  technical  analysis,you  likely  heard  something  like,the  bulls  live above the 50-day moving average(DMA)and bears live below the 50- DMA.
Well,guess  what?Countless  market  participants   share  this  rule   of  thumb. Ifenough of them believe it to be true,they will perceive a value
opportunity as a stock pulls back towards the 50-DMA and it will play out in this  way.For  example:
我们希望预判一个价格区间是否会成为突破或反转可能发生的级别。 为此，我们试图理解在什么价格区间会有足够的参与者介入，从而   改变供需平衡。AVWAP 使我们能够更好地找到这个潜在的价格区   间，因为它允许我们将瞬时价格与趋势价格进行比较。
当你识别出潜在的支撑位和阻力位时，请考虑：
*长头寸将在遭受更大损失之前，在何处被迫恐惧性平仓?
*空头将在损失扩大时感到不安，并受激励平仓看跌头寸?这 可能引发空头挤压。
4闲置的资金将在何处无法抗拒参与?
自然的问题是，为什么某些价格区域会吸引足够的买方和卖方，为价格运动提供支 撑或阻力?支撑位和阻力位通常具有“自我实现”的性质。当你第一次学习技术分 析时，你可能会听到类似的说法，例如，多头生活在50日移动平均线(DMA)  之 上，空头生活在50-DMA之下。
好了，猜猜看?无数市场参与者都遵循这个经验法则。如果足够多的人认为 它是真的，他们就会将价值机会视为股票回调至50日均线时，事情将按以下 方式发展。例如：
·Short  sellers  who  may  have  sold  higher  as  the  stock  was  extended (stretched far above the 50-DMA)stop selling and may buy to
cover their bets at this perceived level of value.
·    Institutions that own a lot of the stock will sell some of it as it
becomes “extended”from the 50-DMA in order to reduce their
position,and then rebid  for  those  shares  at  lower  prices  as  the stock drops back down toward the 50-DMA.This allows them to sell  some  shares  at“high”prices  relative  to  the  50-DMA  and
replace  them  at  cheaper  prices.As  they  replace  the  quantity  of shares  they  sold(at  higher  at  the  prices)with  shares(at  the
now-lower prices)this  could  help  to  create  Support  at  the  50- DMA.The  stability  from  their  purchases  encourages  others  to participate  at  the  50-DMA  which  helps  further  strengthen
Support.
·e Holders of cash who are standing on the sidelines might now come in to purchase the stock at what they believe to be a bargain
price.
The  collective  action  of these  participants  results  in  diminished  supply  and increased  demand.That  is  how  Support  gets  formed.In  the  charts  below,
the emphasis is on the direction of the significant moving averages.
*空头可能会在股票上涨(远高于50日均线)时卖出，此时他 们停止卖出，并可能在此被感知的价值水平上买入以平仓。
*持有大量股票的机构会将其中的部分股票在价格从50-DMA“延伸”后卖 出，以减少其仓位，然后在股票回落至50-DMA 时以较低的价格重新买入  这些股票。这使它们能够以相对于50-DMA的“高价”卖出部分股票，并  以更便宜的价格替换它们。随着它们用(现在较低价格的)股票替换(高  价卖出的)股票数量，这有助于在50-DMA 附近形成支撑。它们的购买稳  定性鼓励其他人参与50-DMA 的交易，这有助于进一步强化支撑。
站在场边的现金持有者现在可能会进入购买他们认为便宜的价格的 股票。
这些参与者的集体行动导致供应减少和需求增加。这就是Support 形成的原理。在下面的图表中，重点在于主要移动平均线的方向。

Charts   2.10   and   2.11   The   50-day   moving   average   is   a   basic   trend   identification  tool.
Chart:TC2000.com
For charts 2.10&2.11 the daily chart on the left shows a stock in an
uptrend,but note that the price drops below the 50-DMA twice.This shows that the 50-DMA is an area of interest for further study,not necessarily a
point where you should automatically buy or sell.Likewise,the chart on the right shows the declining 50-DMA as a reason not to trust rally attempts in  a downtrend.As we will see later,we will make a shorter-term analysis
using the 5-DMA in the same way.
Of course,the 50-DMA is just one example of where and how a price level
may attract enough activity to bring about a shift in supply and demand and create a level of Support or Resistance.The supply and demand battles for    control of a trend can,and often do,occur at other levels of technical
significance you may be familiar with,such as Fibonacci retracement or extension levels,a prior consolidation area,or widely watched moving  averages.Our focus here is AVWAP,which complements all the other
analysis  techniques.

图表2.10和2.1150日移动平均线是一种基本的趋势识别工具。图表：
TC2000.com
对于图表2.10&2.11,左侧的日线图显示一只股票处于上升趋势，但 请注意价格两次跌破50-DMA 。这表明50-DMA 是一个值得进一步  研究的区域，不一定是你应该自动买入或卖出的点。同样，右侧的图 表显示下降的50-DMA 是不信任下降趋势中反弹尝试的原因。正如
我们稍后将要看到的，我们将以相同的方式使用5-DMA  进行短期分 析。
当然，50-DMA 只是价格水平可能吸引足够活动以引起供需变化并创  建支撑或阻力水平的一个例子。控制趋势的供需战可以，并且经常发   生在其他你熟悉的技术重要性水平上，例如斐波那契回调或扩展水平、 之前的整固区域或广泛关注的移动平均线。我们在这里关注的是
AVWAP,   它补充了所有其他分析技术。
It is also important to recognize that ifone or more other technical factors show up in the same general area,it can reinforce that area's level of
significance because more participants may be forming their decision to
buy,sell,or stand aside in the same area,but each for different reasons.The more people coming to the same price conclusion,in the same area,
increases the likelihood it will become Support or Resistance.
How Would You Feel?
Beyond mere recognition of Support and Resistance zones,true market
understanding comes from anticipation of how other participants will act in different scenarios.When you look at a chart,try to imagine how you would  feel,and possibly act,if you were long,short,or in cash.
If Support breaks,who will buy,sell,or cover?How about when Resistance is broken?Understand the psychology of why Support and Resistance
develop,and you will have a significant advantage over most participants who simply lookat patterns.
Going Deeper:Slope ofthe AVWAP
One of the most common questions about the volume of trading activity is
whether the volume was in buying or selling?Well,of course,it is both.For  every buyer,there is a seller and vice versa.What we really want to know is who is more aggressive and who is in control,the buyers or sellers?The
direction andslope ofthe AVWAP allows us to answer that question easily and  accurately.
AVWAP allows us to quantify who has control at any point,buyers or
sellers.The Chart 2.12 demonstrates how to determine the directional bias by the slope ofthe AVWAP.The slope of AVWAP(higher or lower)shows
同样重要的是要认识到，如果其他一个或多个技术因素出现在同一大 致区域，它可以加强该区域的重要性水平，因为更多参与者可能会在 同一区域形成他们的买入、卖出或观望的决定，但每个原因都不同。 更多的人在同一区域得出相同的价位结论，会增加它成为支撑或阻力 的可能性。
您会如何感受?
超越对支撑位和阻力位的简单识别，真正的市场理解来自于对其他参 与者将在不同情况下如何行动的预期。当你看一张图表时，试着想象 如果你是多头、空头或现金，你会如何感受，并可能如何行动。
如果支撑位被跌破，谁会买入、卖出或平仓?当阻力位被跌破时呢? 理解支撑位和阻力位形成的原因，你将比大多数只看模式的人拥有  显著的优势。
深入探讨：AVWAP的斜率
关于交易量最常见的问题之一是交易量是在买入还是卖出?当然，两 者都有。每个买家都有一个卖家，反之亦然。我们真正想知道的是谁 更激进，谁在控制，是买家还是卖家? AVWAP  的方向和斜率使我们 能够轻松准确地回答这个问题。
AVWAP允许我们量化在任何时间点上谁拥有控制权，是买方还是卖方。
图2.12展示了如何通过AVWAP  的斜率来确定方向性偏好。AVWAP  的斜 率(更高或更低)显示
whether the dollar average paid per share for the period studied is rising or declining.When the slope rises,buyers are in control from the anchor  point.When the direction of the AVWAP is lower,we know sellers are in    control from the anchor point.
The direction and rate of change of the AVWAP is often more important  than simply being above or below it. The steeper the slope of AVWAP,the more aggressive the trend and higher the likelihood the AVWAP will act as Support on pullbacks and the stock will experience a bounce.The AVWAP  can be the reason Support is found as sellers become less aggressive and
buyers place bids closer to “fair value.”The AVWAP becomes and reinforces Support levels.The reverse of this takes place when the trend is in the
other direction;the AVWAP becomes and reinforces Resistance levels as sellers become more aggressive relative to buyers.We see this below in chart 2.12.
该时期每股平均支付美元是否在上升或下降。当斜率上升时，从锚  点开始买方处于控制地位。当AVWAP   的方向较低时，我们知道卖 方从锚点开始处于控制地位。
AVWAP 的方向和变化率通常比仅仅高于或低于它更重要。
AVWAP   的斜率越陡峭，趋势就越激进，AVWAP   作为回调支撑的可 能性就越高，股票也更有可能反弹。AVWAP  可以成为支撑的原因， 因为卖方变得不那么激进，买方在“公允价值”附近挂出买单。
AVWAP   变成并强化支撑位。当趋势向相反方向发展时，情况则相反； 随着卖方相对于买方变得更为激进，AVWAP   变成并强化阻力位。我   们在图2.12中看到这一点。

As the slope ofthe AVWAP flattens out,it shows that there is greater
market acceptance of the value and the market likely needs more time(and perhaps a price shakeout)before the original trend resumes.
When a flat AVWAP gets tested more frequently,it is more likely to flip from Support to Resistance and Resistance to Support.The goal is to use that
information to identify low risk,high probability trades.
Rising AVWAP
A stock with a rising AVWAP shows that buyers are more aggressive than    sellers during the timeframe in question.The market must rotate to higher

当 AVWAP 的斜率变平时，这表明市场对价值的接受度更高，市场 可能需要更多时间(并且可能需要价格洗盘)才能恢复原始趋势。
当平坦的AVWAP被频繁测试时，它更有可能从支撑位转变为阻力位，以及  从阻力位转变为支撑位。目标是利用这些信息来识别低风险、高概率的交易。
上升的AVWAP
一 支AVWAP   上升的股票表明，在所讨论的时间范围内，买方的态度比卖方 更积极。市场必须转向更高
prices in search ofliquidity(supply)to satisfy the quantity of buy orders
(demand).In Chart 2.13 we set the anchor to the gap on the 27th on this 65- minute timeframe(1).Notice how the AVWAP provided support(green
arrows)as buyers stepped up their purchases near the AVWAP on the pullbacks in its uptrend.

Chart 2.13 The rising AVWAP often acts as Support in an uptrend.Chart:TC2000.com
Chart 2.14 emphasizes why one should not automatically change from bullish to bearish on a short-term break ofthe VWAP/AVWAP.
As evidence that the market is reversing an advance,the direction of the
VWAP will typically flatten out,prices will cross below,get trapped under the VWAP,and then decline.Earlier in the day,or during whatever the
timeframe being studied,the slope of the VWAP is typically at its most
extreme level because the number of data periods being averagedis lower.
价格在寻求流动性(供应)以满足买入订单(需求)的数量。在图  2.13中，我们将锚点设置为65分钟时间框架(1)上的27日缺口。请 注意，在AVWAP的上升趋势回调中，买家在AVWAP附近加大购买 时 ，AVWAP  提供了支撑(绿色箭头)。
图2.13上升的AVWAP 常常在上升趋势中充当支撑。图：TC2000.com
图2.14强调了为什么不应该自动从
从看涨转为看跌，在VWAP/AVWAP   的短期突破时。
作为市场正在逆转上涨的证据，VWAP  的方向通常会趋于平缓，价格 会跌破，被困在VWAP下方，然后下跌。在一天中的较早时候，或者 在研究的任何时间段内，VWAP  的斜率通常是其最极端的水平，因为 被平均的数据周期数量较低。
As the day progresses,and each transaction has less impact on the average, it is natural to see the slope of the VWAP become less pronounced.

GENERAL NOTE:All moving averages should be used as a reference point  to compare price trends.They should not be considered as automatic levels to do business when they are touched,but as a reason to observe the price  action on a shorter-term timeframe,where we formulate a plan.We
generally give the benefit of doubt to buyers when the 50-DMA trend is higher,and to sellers when the slope is lower.
Takeaways on Rising AVWAP:
·When  the  direction  of  the  AVWAP  is  trending  higher,we  should have a long bias and avoid new short positions.
·The  increase  in  price  shows  on  the  chart  as  a  bullish  trend  above the rising AVWAP.Consider these  stocks  innocent until proven    guilty  during  the  timeframe  that  this  occurs.
·Buyers  should  seek  opportunities  to  buy  after  pullbacks  toward   the AVWAP,but first wait for evidence of actual support.If there is,then prices will likely rise and we have a logical place for our  stop.
·The first one or two touches of an important AVWAP are more likely to experience a strong bounce.This tendency occurs as
sidelined buyers,who thought they missed the move,rush in to purchase shares.
·    As the life of the trend stretches out,the bounces occur with less enthusiasm,which raises our level of caution and our defensive
posture.When a bounce is less vigorous it's because buyers are a  less motivated source of demand;thus,the trend more vulnerable to failure.
通用说明：所有移动平均线都应作为比较价格趋势的参考点。当它们   被触及时，不应将其视为进行交易的自动水平，而应将其视为观察短； 期时间框架内价格行为的理由，我们在此制定计划。当50日移动平均   线趋势较高时，我们通常对买家持有利态度，而当斜率较低时，我们   对卖家持有利态度。
关于上升AVWAP   的要点：
当AVWAP  的方向呈上升趋势时，我们应该持有多头倾向，并避
免建立新的空头头寸。
价格上涨在图表上表现为在上升的AVWAP  上方的看涨趋势。在 发生这种情况的时间框架内，应考虑这些股票是无辜的，直到被 证明有罪。
买家应寻求机会，在回调至AVWAP时买入，但首先等待实际支撑的证 据。如果存在，那么价格可能会上涨，我们就有了一个合理的止损位。
重要AVWAP 的前一两个触碰更有可能经历强劲的反弹。
这种倾向发生时，原本认为错过了行情的旁观买家会急于 购买股票。
随着趋势生命的延伸，反弹的发生变得不再那么热情，这提高了  我们的警惕水平并加强了我们的防御姿态。当反弹不那么强烈时， 是因为买家是需求的一个不那么有动力的来源；因此，趋势更容  易失败。
·As with any level of Support,the more times and more frequently Support gets tested without a bounce away from the AVWAP,the more likely it is to fail in the near-term.
Declining  AVWAP
When a stock is below a declining AVWAP,it tells us that sellers are more
motivated than buyers.Transactions occur at lower prices,which show on a chart as a bearish trend,below the declining AVWAP.
In a decline,the market does not accept the supply at current levels,so
prices fall to levels where there is sufficient demand to absorb the supply. When the AVWAP is in a downtrend,the stance to take is a short bias and   use caution on open long positions.Consider these stocks guilty until
proven innocent on the timeframe where this occurs.
Ifyou have a long position that you want to get out of,rallies up to the
AVWAP are often an excellent point to exit before the stock heads back
lower.Ifyou want to enter a short position,you can start new positions as prices fall away from the declining AVWAP,with a stop above the most
recent and relevant lower-high for your timeframe.
Chart 2.15 shows how sellers will provide Resistance at a declining AVWAP. We set the initial anchor to the start of the large move lower,which began   near $60 per share(1).Notice how the sellers showed up on the touches of  the AVWAP(red arrows at 3,5,7,and9)as the prices continued their
decline.Sellers have picked up momentum after tests ofthe AVWAP from $60(1).
When prices fall away from the declining AVWAP,we sell short(green
circles)in expectation that the trend will continue lower.If the stock
reverses back up through the AVWAP,we want to have a stop in place to
4与任何级别的支撑位一样，支撑位在未经反弹地远离AVWAP  时 被测试的次数越多、越频繁，它在短期内失败的可能性就越大。
下降的AVWAP
当股票低于下降的AVWAP时，它告诉我们卖方比买方更有动力。交易发生 在较低的价格，这在图表上表现为下降的AVWAP下方的看跌趋势。
在下跌中，市场不接受当前水平的供应，因此价格会跌至有足够需  求吸收供应的水平。当AVWAP 处于下跌趋势时，应采取看空倾向， 并对开多头头寸保持谨慎。在这些时间段内，应考虑这些股票有罪， 直到被证明无罪。
如果你有一个想平仓的多头头寸，价格上涨至AVWAP  通常是平仓 前的绝佳点位，以避免股票再次下跌。如果你想开空仓，可以在价 格远离下降的AVWAP时开新仓位，止损位设在你时间框架内最新 的相关更低高点之上。
图表2.15显示了卖方在下降的AVWAP  处提供阻力的情况。我
们将初始锚点设在大幅下跌的开始处，即每股60美元附近(1)。
注意，当价格继续下跌时，卖方在AVWAP  的触碰点(红色箭 头在3、5、7和9处)出现。卖方在从60美元(1)测试
AVWAP   后获得了动力。
当价格远离下降的AVWAP 时，我们做空(绿色圆圈),预期趋势将继续 下跌。如果股票通过AVWAP反转回升，我们希望在此时设置一个止损位 以
minimize any loss.This stop is placed above the recent lower-high,
represented  with  red  arrows(3,5,7,9).For  instance,ifwe  sell(2)our  stop wouldgo above the previous high(3),and so on as the stock continues its decline.
It is common for large institutions to set multi-week AVWAP programs at
the start of an event.Those programs become more aggressive as prices
approach the AVWAP from the start of the event and provide overwhelming supply which forms resistance.

最小化任何损失。这个止损位设置在最近的较低高点之上，用红色箭头  (3,5,7,9)表示。例如，如果我们做空(2),止损位会设置在之前的最 高点(3)之上，以此类推，随着股票继续下跌。
大型机构在活动开始时通常会设置多周的AVWAP  计划。当价格从活 动开始时接近AVWAP 时，这些计划会变得更加激进，并提供过剩的 供应，从而形成阻力。
