图表2.15显示了使用65分钟蜡烛的大约一个月的数据。图表：TC2000.com
The daily VWAP is shown on Chart 2.16.When the direction of the VWAP is lower,be  careful  not  to  get  bullish  on  the  first  crossing  of  price  above  the
VWAP(blue  circle).For  the  market  to  reverse  a  decline,the  direction  ofthe VWAP  will  first  flatten  out,prices  will  cross  above  and  then  stay  above  the   VWAP.
Takeaways on Declining AVWAP
·When  the  direction  of  the  AVWAP  is  lower,we   should  have  a  bias toward  short  positions   and  avoid  new   long  positions.
·The  decrease  in  prices  appears  on  the  chart  as  a  bearish  trend below  the   declining  AVWAP.Consider  these   stocks   guilty  until proven  innocent  on  the  timeframe  this  occurs.
·Short   sellers   should   seek   opportunities   to   sell   after   the   price rallies  up  to  the  AVWAP,finds  Resistance  and  then  falls.
·The  first  one  or  two  touches  ofan  important  AVWAP  are  more likely  to  experience  a  quick  selloff  which  makes  them  great
candidates  for  a  short  sale.
·As  the  life  of  the  trend   stretches  out,the  declines  occur  with  less   vigor,which  raises  our  level  of  caution  and  our  defensive  posture towards   new   short   sales.
·As  with  any  level  of  Resistance,the   more  times  and  more
frequently  Resistance  gets  tested  without  a  decline  in  price,the more  likely  it  is to  fail  in the near term.
每日VWAP  显示在图表2.16中。当VWAP  的方向较低时，小心不要在价 格首次穿越VWAP   (蓝色圆圈)时变得看涨。要让市场逆转下跌，
VWAP  的方向首先会趋于平缓，价格会穿越VWAP  然后保持在VWAP   上 方。
AVWAP   下降的要点
当AVWAP的方向较低时，我们应该倾向于做空头仓位，并避免 建立新的多头仓位。
价格下降在图表上表现为下降的AVWAP  下方的看跌趋势。在这
些时间段内，考虑将这些股票视为有罪，直到被证明无罪。
空头卖家应在价格上涨至AVWAP、  找到阻力位然后下跌后 寻找卖出机会。
重要的AVWAP  的前一两个触碰更有可能经历快速抛售， 这使得它们成为空头卖出的理想候选。
随着趋势的持续延长，下降的力度减弱，这提高了我们的警惕水 平，并增强了我们对新的空头卖出的防御姿态。
与任何级别的阻力一样，阻力在不导致价格下跌的情况下   被测试的次数越多、越频繁，它近期失败的可能性就越大。

Oscillate Above and Below AVWAP
When you observe a flat AVWAP with prices crossing above and below it,my advice is to avoid the stock on that timeframe.This action is neutral and
there is no edge in being long or short.
Rather than  complain  about  choppy  action  or  lack  of opportunity,we should interpret the message of the market as meaning one of three
things to us;cash is a good position for now,find another market or

图2.16一天内某股票的2分钟时间框架图表。注意不要在第一次穿越VWAP 或AVWAP 时 变得看涨。图表： TC2000.com
在AVWAP   上下波动
当 你 观 察 到 一 条 平 坦 的AVWAP,        并 且 价 格 在 其 上 下 穿 越 时 ， 我 的 建 议 是 避
免在该时间周期内交易该股票 。 这种操作是中性的 ， 做多或做空都没有优势 。
与其抱怨动作不连贯或缺乏机会，我们应该将市场的信息解读为对 我们意味着三种可能之一：现金是目前一个好的位置，寻找另一个 市场或
stock  to  trade,or  switch  to  a  different  timeframe  to  find  a  better opportunity   to   get   involved.
It  is  good  to  recognize  these   stocks.The  lack  of  current  opportunity  frees   up  our  time  to   focus  on  more   actionable  setups.Chart  2.17   shows  multiple crosses  above  and below the AVWAP.

In Chart 2.17 we anchored the AVWAP to an important low(1)on the stock
above.Initially,the   buyers    regained   control(2),but    as    the   stock    traded
above  and  below  the  AVWAP(3).The  stock  needed  more  time  to  let  the
buyers and sellers battle it out for control.Trend traders should avoid these
stocks  until  there  is  greater  clarity  of  who  has  control.

识别这些股票是好事。当前机会的缺乏让我们有时间专注于更具操 作性的设置。图2. 17显示了多个在AVWAP   之上和之下的交叉。

图2.17 AVWAP  之上和之下的交叉代表犹豫不决。图：TC2000.com
在图2.17中，我们将AVWAP  锚定在上方股票的 一个重要低点(1)上。 最初，买方重新获得控制权(2),但随着股票在AVWAP  上下交易
(3)。股票需要更多时间让买方和卖方为控制权展开争夺。趋势交 易者应避免这些股票，直到谁的控制权更加明确。
Once again,it is important to realize that these concepts are the same for stocks of all prices and on all timeframes.Do not focus on the price or the  specific timeframe on any of the charts shown.
Market    Psychology:Institutions'
Role
For an institutional trader who wants to buy a large amount of a stock in an uptrend,it makes sense to place bids for the stock as it pulls back down to   AVWAP since it is an opportunity for them to scoop up shares at the “fair
value”relative to the open and the price they might expect it to close.
Risk Management
When we anticipate a level of interest which has the potential to become    Support or Resistance,it becomes ourjob to observe that area on a shorter timeframe for evidence of whether it is the buyers or sellers that are
gaining  control.
The lowest risk-trades are the ones where we have a clear plan in advance. A clear plan anticipates an area of transition where we observe the action   on a shorter-term timeframe before we get involved.Some of the most
common trade mistakes occur from reactive FOMO decisions.
同样重要的是要认识到，这些概念对所有价格和所有时间框架的股 票都是相同的。不要关注任何图表中显示的价格或特定时间框架。
市场心理：机构的作用
对于希望在上升趋势中买入大量股票的机构交易者来说，当股票回调 至AVWAP  时出价是有道理的，因为这是他们以相对于开盘价和可能 预期的收盘价而言的“公允价值”扫货股票的机会。
风险管理
当我们预期一个可能成为支撑位或阻力位的兴趣水平时，我们的任 务是在较短的时间框架内观察该区域，以判断是买方还是卖方正在 获得控制权。
风险最低的交易是我们提前有一个清晰的计划。一个清晰的计划预见  了一个过渡区域，我们在参与之前在该较短的时间框架内观察到行动。 一些最常见的交易错误来自于反应性的 FOMO  决策。
KEY TAKEAWAYS·The   concepts   of  Support   and   Resistance   apply   to   all timeframes.·   AVWAPs can reveal order in the market that traditional technical analysis tools cannot.·The simplest and most effective use of the AVWAP is to find “hidden”levels of Support and Resistance.·Unlike   the   more    common   Support    and   Resistance   levels which are seen as horizontal price consolidations,theSupport  and  Resistance  levels  of  an  AVWAP  are  dynamic. They adjust with each trade.·AVWAP allows us to quantify who has control from any point,buyers or sellers.·The slope ofthe AVWAP easily identifies directionalmomentum.When it rises,buyers are in control from the start   of   the    anchor.Conversely,if   the    slope   falls,sellers   are  in  control  from  the   start  of  the  anchor.
KEY TAKEAWAYS
·The   concepts   of  Support   and   Resistance   apply   to   all timeframes.
·   AVWAPs can reveal order in the market that traditional technical analysis tools cannot.
·The simplest and most effective use of the AVWAP is to find “hidden”levels of Support and Resistance.
·Unlike   the   more    common   Support    and   Resistance   levels which are seen as horizontal price consolidations,the
Support  and  Resistance  levels  of  an  AVWAP  are  dynamic. They adjust with each trade.
·AVWAP allows us to quantify who has control from any point,buyers or sellers.
·The slope ofthe AVWAP easily identifies directional
momentum.When it rises,buyers are in control from the start   of   the    anchor.Conversely,if   the    slope   falls,sellers   are  in  control  from  the   start  of  the  anchor.
关键要点
支撑和阻力概念适用于所有时间框架。
AVWAPs  可以揭示传统技术分析工具无法发现的市场秩序。
AVWAP   最简单且最有效的使用方法是找到“隐藏”的 支撑位和阻力位。
与常见的支撑位和阻力位(被视为水平价格盘整)不同， AVWAP  的支撑位和阻力位是动态的。它们会随着每一  笔交易进行调整。
AVWAP   允许我们从任何时点量化谁占据控制权，是买 方还是卖方。
AVWAP 的斜率可以轻松识别方向性动量。当它上升时， 买方从锚点开始就占据主导地位。相反，如果斜率下降， 卖方从锚点开始就占据主导地位。
·Support and Resistance areas have a self-reinforcing  role,which makes the psychology of the participants' motivations important to understand.·We   only    know    Support    and   Resistance    levels    in   hindsight. They are “levels of interest”until confirmed bysubsequent price action.·Don't buy the dip,buy strength after the dip.
·Support and Resistance areas have a self-reinforcing  role,which makes the psychology of the participants' motivations important to understand.
·We   only    know    Support    and   Resistance    levels    in   hindsight. They are “levels of interest”until confirmed by
subsequent price action.
·Don't buy the dip,buy strength after the dip.

CHAPTER 3
AVWAP ENTRY AND
EXIT TECHNIQUES
“You've got to know when to hold'em,
know when to fold’em,Know when to walk
away,and know when to run.”
—Kenny Rogers
Chapter   Objectives
1.Understand  two   options  for  entry:
a.Option A-buy the touch of AVWAP
b.Option B-buy strength or sell short after the touch (momentum)
2.How to decide which entry is correct for you
3.Understand how  Support becomes  Resistance  and vice-versa
4.Understand Support and Resistance failures and how to trade on  these  reversals
第三章
AVWAP   入场和出 场技术
“你必须知道何时该坚持，何时该放弃， 知道何时该离开，知道何时该逃跑。”
-Kenny Rogers
章节目标
1. 了解两种入场选项：
a. 选项A-买入AVWAP  的触碰
b. 选项B-在触碰后买入力量或卖空 (momentum)
2. 如何决定哪个条目适合您
3. 了解支撑位如何变成阻力位以及反之亦然
4. 了解支撑位和阻力位的失败情况以及如何交易 在这些反转中
T    raders should use the AVWAP's ability to identify levels of Support or
I   Resistance to their advantage.One way to do that is to wait for a test of
an AVWAP level and to purchase the stock on the first touch ofthe AVWAP  and hope that it holds.The other option is to observe the action around the AVWAP and treat it as a "level ofinterest"on a shorter timeframe.
If your choice is to observe,the next step is to wait for evidence that the
buyers are serious about their actions and will defend AVWAP.Once it is
clear the stock has found Support or Resistance at the AVWAP,we can
enter the stock and place a stop.Now we will explore both options in more detail.
Option  A:Buy  the  Touch
Purchase(or sell short)just as the stock touches AVWAP.This is not my
preference as Iam more risk averse and there is no assurance the stock will bounce from the AVWAP.
Paul Levine,PhD was a pioneer in AVWAP analysis and gave the term
“porosity”to describe how AVWAPs are general areas,not precise
numbers.That said,there are times when a stock will touch the AVWAP to the penny and reverse immediately.
When a stock is far beyond the AVWAP(Point 2 in Chart 3.1),I view this
intuitively,while others may use standard deviation bands.Chart 3.0 shows the AVWAP as well as standard deviation bands.
交易者应利用 AVWAP   的识别支撑位或阻力位的能力。一种方 法是为AVWAP 水平的测试等待，并在AVWAP  首次触及时购买股 票，希望它能保持。另一个选项是观察AVWAP   周围的走势，并将  其视为较短时间框架内的“兴趣位”。
如果你选择观察，下一步是等待证据表明买家认真对待他们的行动  并将捍卫AVWAP 。一旦明确股票在AVWAP 处找到了支撑位或阻 力位，我们就可以进入股票并放置一个止损。现在我们将更详细地  探讨这两种选择。
选项A:   买入触碰
在股票触碰 AVWAP 时买入(或做空)。这不是我的首选，因为我更 厌恶风险，而且没有保证股票会从AVWAP   反弹。
Paul       Levine,PhD是 AVWAP  分析的先驱，并将“渗透性”一词 用于描述AVWAP 是一般区域而非精确数字。话说回来，有时股票 会精确地触碰AVWAP 并立即反转。
当一只股票远远偏离AVWAP(图表3.1中的点2)时，我直观地看待这种情  况，而其他人可能会使用标准差带。图表3.0显示了AVWAP  以及标准差带。
Chart 3.0 This stock shows the standard AVWAP(purple)along with a 2 standard
deviation band ofthe AVWAP.Chart:ThinkorSwim.com
As always,any trade setup is more likely to be successful when trends are aligned with longer timeframes of the stock and the trend of the overall
market.If you buy at each touch of AVWAP,it is sometimes possible to
purchase  at the  exact turning point,but you run  the risk the  stock may
continue lower(Point 4 in Chart 3.1).If the stock does not bounce from the AVWAP,it's difficult to find a price-based level for your stop because there is often a lack of a lower-high nearby to place the stop under.
The stock in Chart 3.1 made an important near-term low on October 24th (1).That  is  where  we  set  our  anchor.Note,that  large  distance  between
price and the AVWAP(2).When prices extend far from the AVWAP,new purchases  are  considered  to  be  riskier.
On November 2,the stock pulled back to the AVWAP(3)from that low and bounced precisely from that level.Two days later,the  stock came back to  the AVWAP(4)and this time failed to bounce.
图表3.0此股票显示了标准的AVWAP (紫色)以及AVWAP的2个标准差带。 图表：ThinkorSwim.com
一如既往，当趋势与股票的较长时间周期以及整体市场的趋势一致  时，任何交易设置更有可能成功。如果你在每次AVWAP 触碰时买  入，有时有可能在精确的转折点买入，但你有风险股票可能会继续  下跌(图表3. 1中的点4)。如果股票没有从AVWEAP  反弹，很难找 到一个基于价格的水平来设置你的止损，因为附近通常缺乏一个较  低的高点来放置止损。
图表3. 1中的股票在10月24日(1)做出了一个重要的短期低点。 这就是我们设置锚点的地方。注意，价格和AVWAP   之间的大距   离(2)。当价格远离AVWAP   时，新的购买被认为风险更大。
在11月2日，股票从那个低点回落至AVWAP(3),     并精确地从那个水平
反弹。两天后，股票回到AVWAP(4),     但这次未能反弹。
Chart 3.1 Not all pullbacks to AVWAP can be expected to bounce.Chart:TC2000.com
This example shows one instance where the trader would have made
money immediately ifhe purchased the touch ofthe AVWAP(3).It also  shows where the stock continued to decline through the AVWAP,which would have resulted in a loss(4).
AVWAP levels are not always an automatic place to do business and you    must decide through trial and error if you prefer to buy the touch or wait for the stock to bounce from the AVWAP before you make a purchase.I     cover this at length in Chapter 7,"Buy Pullbacks and Breakouts?"
The stock in Chart 3.2 continued in its uptrend from the early February    anchor point,but the purchases right at the AVWAP(green arrows)from the  low  didn't  all  immediately  result  in  a  gain.

AVWAP 水平并非总是自动的买卖点，你必须通过反复试验来决定是 买入触碰还是等待股票从AVWAP  反弹后再进行购买。我们将在第 7章，“买入回调和突破?”中详细讨论这一点

It can be better to purchase when the stock rises again(the bounce).The
green dots show these points.When we purchase with momentum,we take part as the new trend begins.We can place a stop below the preceding
higher-low,to protect us in the event that the price action does not follow through.A purchase right at the AVWAP touch does not allow us to have a consistent low-risk stop level,based on price action.
Option B:Enter with Momentum
Purchasing the stock after it tests the AVWAP and bounces away from it is the lower-risk entry.A short sale after a test of AVWAP followed by a
decline is the lower-risk short entry.In this type of set-up we have
evidence that buyers have defended the AVWAP successfully before we put

当股价再次上涨时(反弹)购买会更好。绿色圆点显示了这些点。当 我们有动量时购买，我们就会成为新趋势的开始。我们可以将止损设 置在之前的更高低点下方，以防价格行动没有如期发展。在
AVWAP触及时立即购买，无法让我们根据价格行动有一个一致的低 风险止损水平。
选项B: 有动量入场
在股票测试AVWAP 并反弹后买入是较低风险的入场方式。在测试
AVWAP  后卖出并下跌时做空是较低风险的做空入场。在这种设置中， 我们有证据表明买方在我们在{.….}之前成功捍卫了AVWAP。
our money  at risk.Momentum  is  on  our  side with these  entries,long  and short.
The AVWAP allows us to find exactly where and when the sellers are
overwhelmed  and  buyers  have  regained  control.This  type  ofentry  allows us to enter at the onset of new momentum  and easily define our risk.
Ilike to be right from the  start and enter a trade with momentum.Let
others jump  the  gun,do  the  "dirty  work,"and  take  the  larger  associated    risks  while  Support  forms.Ifyou  are  in  the  right  neighborhood,there  will still be plenty of opportunity for profit and with less risk.
Wait patiently for the signal(a general guideline would be 3-5 bars for the timeframe you are on)to enter so you have a level to trade against.We
want to  enter AFTER buyers  or  sellers have regained  control.Buy  strength after the  dip  and  short  weakness  after the rip.
我们的资金面临风险。在这些交易中，势头在我们这边，包括多头和空头。
AVWAP  使我们能够精确找到卖方被压倒而买方重新掌控市场的时机。
这种交易方式让我们能在新势头初现时入场，并轻松定义我们的风险。
我喜欢从一开始就做对，并带着势头入场交易。让其他人抢跑、做 “脏活”,并承担更大的相关风险，而支持位正在形成。如果你处 于正确的区域，仍然会有很多盈利机会，且风险更小。
耐心等待信号(一般建议您所在的时间段为3-5格)进入，以便您有 一个交易参考水平。我们希望在买家或卖家重新获得控制权之后才  入场。在回调后买入强势，在拉升后做空弱势。

In Chart 3.3,the stock made an important high in earlyJanuary.Once the  stock dropped for a few days,that high became the logical place to set our AVWAP(blue      arrow).
There were several touches ofthe AVWAP(red arrows)where the stock
could have been shorted with minimal initial loss and that makes it
tempting   to   short   at   the   AVWAP.With   the   benefit   of  hindsight,we   know
these trades would have been profitable,but at that moment,when these   trades might have been initiated,the momentum and stop placement price was not clear.That makes these entries risky.
The other option is to wait for the stock to drop away from the AVWAP and  short   as    the    downward   momentum    builds(green   dots).We    could    then   place

图表3.3'The lower-risk short éntries occurafterthe AVWAP has.been tested. 图表：
TC2000.com
在图表3.3.中，股票在1月初达到了一个重要的高点。一旦 股票下跌了几天，那个高点就成了我们设置
AVWAP  (蓝色箭头)。
AVWAP   (红色箭头)出现了几次触碰，股票可以在此做空且初始损 失最小，这使得在AVWAP时做空很有诱惑力。凭借后见之明，我们 知道这些交易将会盈利，但在那一刻，当这些交易可能被发起时，动 量和止损位置价格并不明确。这使得这些入场点有风险。
另一种选择是等待股票价格远离AVWAP,    并在下跌动能增强时(绿色点) 做空。然后我们可以放置
a  stop  above  the  preceding  high(red  arrows).
This  latter  entry  point  assures  the  stockis  moving  in  the  desired  direction before our entry.It also provides us with an easily identifiable level for our stop loss in case the stock reverses back higher.
In Chart 3.4 we can see how selling short as the stock touches AVWAP(red arrows)would  have  resulted  in  choppy  trading  or,worse,losses.
As noted,I prefer to start a short position as the stock drops away from the AVWAP(indicated by the green dots),where the downward momentum is
confirmed.Then we  can place  a  stop  above  the most recent relevant lower- high.When you set your stop level based on price action,it allows for
greater  certainty  and  confidence  in  the  trade  from  the  start.
在之前的最高价上方设置止损(红色箭头)。
这个后端入口确保股票在进入前朝着期望的方向移动。它还为我们提 供了一个易于识别的止损水平，以防股票反转回更高。
在图3.4中，我们可以看到当股票触及AVWAP   (红色箭头)时做空会如何 导致波动性交易，或者更糟，导致亏损。
如所注，我倾向于在股票从AVWAP   (由绿点指示)下方回落时开短 仓，此时下跌动能得到确认。然后我们可以在最新的相关较低-高点  上方设置止损。当你根据价格行为设置止损位时，从一开始就能让交 易具有更大的确定性和信心。

Which is Right for You?
There is no one right way for everything,only the right way for you.
Whether  you  decide  your  approach  is  to  buyjust  as  the  stock  touches  the   AVWAP,or  ifyou  wait  for  further  evidence  before  you  make  an  entry.Most people  will   gravitate  toward   one  or  the   other.You  might  have   a  natural
preference  about  the  entry  location,or  it  might  take  time  to  develop  your preference  as  you  try  both  methods.

图3.4当价格频繁在AVWAP上方和下方穿越时，控制风险很困难。图：

哪种更适合您?
没有一种方法适用于所有情况，只有适合你的方法。无论你决定在  股票触及AVWEP  时立即买入，还是等待更多证据再入场。大多数人 会倾向于其中一种。你可能对入场位置有自然偏好，或者可能需要
尝试两种方法来培养你的偏好。
Some people might even prefer to take a hybrid approach where they start their position on the first touch ofthe AVWAP and then add to the position  after it proves to be momentum Support or Resistance.As always,do what   is right for you.Make the trade your own.
Market Psychology:Price Has Memory,so Use It
One of the basic tenets of the study of price history is that “broken support acts as resistance."The opposite is also true,"broken resistance acts as
support.”
Support Becomes Resistance
Have you ever purchased a stock,watched it decline in price and wish you could just get out at a breakeven?Me too.This type of buyer's remorse
shows up on a chart as Resistance.
When the stock rallies back to the purchase price and you place your sell
order,it adds supply,which becomes a block,however temporary,to the
price advancement.Obviously,one person's sale of stock won't typically
offer much Resistance.When sales occur at a widely recognized level(price memory)shared by many participants,such as a significant moving
average or average of AVWAP level,it becomes much harder for the stock to work through the large supply being offered before it can move higher.
Don't forget about  short  sellers here,too.When  Support breaks,short
sellers are in control of the stock and they will try to defend their short
position by adding more supply in hopes of not only adding to their short
position,but also to scare long holders to liquidate their positions in fear of larger losses,which benefits their short bet.
有些人甚至可能更喜欢采取混合策略，即在第一次触及AVWAP  时开 始建立仓位，然后在它证明是动量支撑或阻力后再加仓。一如既往， 做对你正确的事。让这笔交易成为你自己的。
市场心理：价格有记忆，所以 利用它
价格历史研究的基本原则之一是“跌破支撑位会形成阻力位”。反之亦然， “跌破阻力位会形成支撑位。”
支撑位变成阻力位
你有没有买过股票，看着它价格下跌，希望你能刚好在盈亏平衡点 卖出?我也是。这种买后懊悔的情绪在图表上表现为阻力位。
当股票回升到购买价格时，你下达卖出指令，这会增加供应量，从而  成为价格上涨的一个障碍，无论多么暂时。显然，一个人的股票卖出  通常不会提供太多阻力。当在许多参与者共同认可的水平(价格记忆) 上发生销售，例如一个重要的移动平均线或AVWAP 平均线时，它变  得非常困难，使得股票在上涨之前需要克服大量供应。
不要忘记这里的卖空者。当支撑位被跌破时，卖空者控制着股票，他 们会试图通过增加更多供应来捍卫他们的卖空头寸，希望不仅增加他 们的卖空头寸，而且吓跑多头持有者，让他们因担心更大的损失而平 仓，这对他们的卖空赌注有利。
Charts 3.5(left)and 3.6(right)show how AVWAP Support became Resistance.Chart:
TC2000.com
Notice that in Chart 3.5 there were no actual tests of the rising AVWAP.
This is an example ofa  "non-textbook example."We often give analysis of AVWAP,or  any  market  approach,an  improbable  expectation  of  success.In real trading,it isn't as perfect as some books would lead you to believe.
Remember,there is the science of analysis and the more difficult art of trading.
Chart 3.6 is a more straightforward example of how the AVWAP,which once provided    Support(green   arrows)became   Resistance(red   arrows).
图表3 . 5(左)和3 .6(右)显示了AVWAP  支撑位如何变成阻力位。图表来源：
TC2000.com
请注意，在图表3.5中，并没有对上升的AVWAP 进行实际测试。这  是一个“非教科书案例”的例子。我们经常对AVWAP 或任何市场方 法抱有不切实际的成功的期望。在真实交易中，它并不像一些书所
引导你相信的那样完美。记住，有分析的科学，还有更难掌握的交 易的艺术。
图3.6是一个更直接的例子，展示了AVWAP  如何从曾经提供支撑(绿色箭 头)变成阻力(红色箭头)。

Chart 3.7 This stock demonstrates how Support(green arrows)when broken,turns to
Resistance(red arrows).This can occur on more than one instance on the same chart.
Chart:TC2000.com
In Chart 3.7,the AVWAP from the October low(blue arrow on left)showed    Support  twice(1)and(2)before  it  flipped  to  Resistance  in  early  January(3) and then  again in  early February(4).Ifyou  find me  on  Twitter  in  a  situation like this,you might hear me refer to points(3)and(4)as  “AVWAP  Tap  and   Crap"or “AVWAP Thump and Dump.”
When the green AVWAP is anchored from the January low(5),notice how the AVWAP acted as Resistance twice after the start of the decline:(6)in   early    February,and(7)in    mid-February.
We use price  charts to understand the  collective reasoning  and  psychology of market  participants  so  we  can  objectively  prepare  our  trade  plan.When

图3.7-这支股票展示了当支撑位(绿色箭头)被突破时，如何转为 阻力位(红色箭头)。这可能在同一图表上出现多次。
图表：TC2000.com
在图3.7中，从10月份的低点(左侧蓝色箭头)开始的AVWAP 展示了 两次支撑(1)和(2),然后在一 月初(3)和二月初(4)转变为阻力。 如果你在推特上看到我处于这种情况，你可能会听到我称点(3)和(4) 为 “AVWAP   Tap   and   Crap” 或 “AVWAPThump       and       Dump”。
当绿色AVWAP 从1月份的低点(5)锚定后，请注意AVWAP 在下跌 开始后两次充当阻力位：2月初(6)和2月中(7)。
我们使用价格图表来理解市场参与者的集体推理和心理，以便我们能够 客观地制定交易计划。当
traditional Support breaks and then acts as Resistance,it means that there has been a greater number of participants anchored at that price level
which,in turn can lead to a larger opposite move when the price breaks.
When price breaks a major level of Support,the trapped longs will have a    propensity to get out at breakeven and as they sell shares,the supply from these participants helps to form Resistance.
Resistance Becomes Support
The same emotions come into play when a stock forms Support on a chart. Have you ever sold a stock after it has done nothing for months and then    see it almost immediately turn higher without you?It is as if“they”know   you are out and agree to take the stock higher without you.
Ofcourse this doesn't really happen,but you probably wish you could buy   your shares back at your original cost.As sellers start to take advantage of the rising price,causing the stock to pull back toward the breakout level,    you may decide to get back in.Others,with sidelined cash may also be
motivated tojoin in on what appears to be a new uptrend
传统支撑位被跌破后然后充当阻力位，这意味着在该价格水平上有更   多的参与者锚定，这反过来可能导致价格跌破时出现更大的反向波动。
当价格突破一个主要支撑位时，被困的多头将有倾向在盈亏平衡点出 局，而随着他们卖出股票，这些参与者的供应有助于形成阻力。
阻力变为支撑
当一只股票在图表上形成支撑位时，同样的情绪会发挥作用。你有没有在一  只股票几个月毫无动静后卖出，然后看到它几乎立即反转上涨而你没有参与? 就好像“他们”知道你出局了，并同意在没有你参与的情况下将股票推高。
当然，这并不会真的发生，但你可能希望你能以原始成本买回你的股 票。当卖家开始利用价格上涨的优势，导致股价回落至突破水平时， 你可能会决定重新入场。其他手头有闲置资金的人也可能被这看似新 的上升趋势所吸引。

Chart 3.8 shows traditional Support and Resistance.Chart:TC2000.com
Don't forget about those short sellers.Ifyou were shorting the stock and it breaks out,it may motivate you to purchase your stock on the pullback
before it begins a move higher.These short-covering purchases are strictly about limiting losses,which can quickly spiral out of control if the stock
follows through on the breakout.These actions,repeated by many buyers and sellers,form Support for a stock's price.
Charts 3.8 and 3.9 show traditional (horizontal)Resistance versus AVWAP Support and Resistance(with 3.8 as traditional and 3.9 as AVWAP).The
AVWAP provides dynamic evidence of Support and Resistance.

图3.8显示了传统的支撑位和阻力位。图：TC2000.com
别忘了那些做空者。如果你做空了这只股票，并且它突破了，这可能 会激励你在回调开始之前以较低的价格买入股票。这些平仓买入严格 是为了限制损失，但如果股价在突破后继续上涨，这些损失可能会迅 速失控。许多买方和卖方的这些行为，形成了对股票价格的支持。

3.8为传统，3.9为AVWAP) 。AVWAP 提供了支撑和阻力的动态证据。

Both techniques of measuring Support and Resistance are valuable,but by  using  AVWAP,pricing  activity  is  revealed  to  be  more  granular  and  you  can   see subtle changes in trends.This makes it easier for you to more precisely time a purchase or sale.

测量支撑和阻力的两种技术都有价值，但使用AVWAP时，价格活  动显示出更精细的粒度，你可以看到趋势中的微妙变化。这使得你更 容易更精确地把握买入或卖出的时机。

Chart 3.11 The AVWAP that provided Support became Resistance soon after prices broke below the AVWAP.Charts:TC2000.com
Charts 3.10 and 3.11 also illustrate the differences of the two methods of finding levels of Support and Resistance.
Active traders who use traditional measures of Support would miss a
number of opportunities to buy or sell.For example,based on what you've read so far,can you see in Chart 3.11 where the two green arrows show
areas of interest for setting up trades?These areas are not so easily
identified in Chart 3.10.By using AVWAP,traders can see the transition from Support to Resistance more quickly and precisely.
The more times Support or Resistance is tested,the more likely it is to
fail.This  is  a   simple,but  important  concept. Traders'impatience    is
demonstrated by the frequency of tests made to Support and Resistance.
Monitor this impatience carefully for signs of potential for the price to
move out of the current range.Price level breakouts may trigger an
important turn in the trading activity of the average participant and,as we will see,they are excellent places from which to anchor our AVWAP.
When traditional Resistance breaks and then acts as Support,larger moves often occur on the upside.When prices break a major level of Resistance,
the trapped shorts will look to get out at break even by purchasing shares to cover their positions and the demand from these participants helps to   form Support.The two charts below show the concept of how broken
Resistance becomes Support.I came up with a couple of corny ways to remember them,"AVWAP Kiss and Run"or“AVWAP Tap and Snap.”
Chart 3.12 shows two instances where Resistance provided by the AVWAPs anchored to  separate  points,broke(1,2)and  then  flipped  to  Support(3,4)   over the course ofjust four days.
图3.11提供支撑的AVWAP在价格跌破AVWAP后很快变成了阻力。图表：
TC2000.com
图表3.10和3.11也说明了两种寻找支撑和阻力水平的方法之间的差异。
使用传统支撑指标的活跃交易者会错失许多买入或卖出的机会。例  如，根据你到目前为止读到的内容，你能在图表3.11中看到两个绿 色箭头标出的交易设置兴趣区域吗?这些区域在图表3.10中并不那 么容易识别。通过使用AVWAP,   交易者可以更快、更精确地看到 从支撑到阻力的转变。
支撑或阻力被测试的次数越多，它就越有可能失效。这是一个简单但   重要的概念。交易者的急躁可以通过对支撑和阻力的测试频率来体现。 仔细监控这种急躁，以寻找价格可能突破当前范围的迹象。价格水平   突破可能会引发普通参与者交易活动的重要转折，正如我们将看到的， 它们是我们锚定AVWAP  的绝佳位置。
当传统阻力位被突破后转为支撑位时，往往会在上方出现更大的行情。 当价格突破一个主要阻力位时，被困的空头将寻求在盈亏平衡点卖出   以平仓，通过购买股票来覆盖其仓位，这些参与者的需求有助于形成   支撑位。下面两个图表展示了阻力位如何转变为支撑位的这一概念。
我想到一些有点土的方法来记住它们， “AVWAP   Kiss   and   Run” 或 “AVWAP   Tap   and   Snap 。”
图表3.12显示了两个实例，其中由锚定在不同点的AVWAP  提供 的阻力被突破(1,2),然后在短短四天内翻转至支撑(3,4)。
In Chart 3.13,the daily chart saw the AVWAP from the early peak act as Resistance(red arrows)before buyers took control and then defended   pullbacks to the AVWAP,where it formed Support(green arrows).
Eventually,the buyers soaked up all the supply offered,and the stock experienced a great run higher.

minute timeframe.The repetition of the pattern on different timeframes is a great example of a fractal playing out with Support and Resistance.
Chart 3.13 On this daily chart we see AVWAP Resistance flip to Support.Chart:
TC2000.com
The longer a consolidation zone(period ofrelative stability in price)has
taken time to develop,the greater the move away from it will be as more
energy has built up.There is a larger group of traders who will benefit from a momentum push away from the consolidation.A good way to remember
this  is:the  bigger  the  top,the  bigger  the  drop  and,the  bigger  the  base,the  higher  in space.
We will delve more into market structure and trends,which are formed by directional Support and Resistance zones.
在不同时间周期上重复出现的模式是支持位和阻力位中分形展开的一个很好 的例子。

一个整理区(价格相对稳定的时期)花费的时间越长来发展，它远离 的移动就会越大，因为更多的能量已经积累。将会有一个更大的交易 群体将从动量推动远离整理区中受益。记住这个的好方法是：顶部越 大，下跌越大，底部越大，空间越高。
我们将更深入地探讨市场结构和趋势，这些是由方向性支撑和阻力区域形成 的 。

Key Levels and Price Targets

traditional  Support  or  Resistance to be  found  on  the  chart(except  for the AVWAP),it is a good idea to look at prior important highs and lows as
anchor   points.

关键水平和价格目标
当我们购买一只股票时，了解它有潜力的去向以及从先前重要高点开  始的AVWAP 往往会成为该股票的阻力位。当一只股票出现大幅波动， 而在图表上找不到传统的支撑位或阻力位(除了AVWAP),     那么查  看先前的重要高低点作为锚点是一个好主意。

It is uncanny how often you will see a stock halt at an AVWAP from a prior    high or low.Knowledge of these levels in advance allow us to approximate a "target"for the price move.Price targets are not necessarily a place to take profit,but to manage risk with tighter stops,so that if the stock does
reverse,we can lockin large gains.
If you bought this stock(3.16)based on your analysis of shorter timeframes, it would have been wise to be aware of where the AVWAP lies in relation to  the peaks(green dots).The stock made two quick moves up to the AVWAP    and then came back down.This is a common occurrence in stocks that
experience a bounce up toward the AVWAP.

AVWAP 的股票中是一种常见现象。

当一支处于较长上升趋势中的股票出现大幅下跌时，交易者通常会在价 格下跌至锚定在重要前期较低价格的AVWAP时开始买入，如图3.17所 示  。
一个空头锁住利润的地方应该是在绿色点，即价格与紫色
AVWAP  相遇的地方。这个点是从一个先前的关键低点设定的，并 且是一个价格反弹的合理位置。
Going Deeper:Support and 电阻故障
Support  and  Resistance  levels  are  not  concrete.They  are  not  guaranteed  to hold.Eventually  the  tone  of  the  market  will  change  from  bullish  to  bearish   and  vice  versa.When  key  Support  and  Resistance  levels  break,be  ready  to   act  to  protect  your   accumulated  gains  because   large  moves   in  the   opposite  direction  can  come  quickly.The  next  four  charts  illustrate  two  bullish(3.18  and   3.19)and   two   bearish(3.20    and   3.21)examples.

Daily-8 Months
Chart 3.18 On this daily chart,we see how the more frequently AVWAP Support is tested
the more likely it is to fail.
支撑和阻力水平并非固定不变。它们并不能保证有效。最终市场的基调将从 看涨变为看跌，反之亦然。当关键的支撑和阻力水平被突破时，准备好采取 行动以保护你的累积利润，因为相反方向的巨大波动可能会迅速发生。接下 来的四个图表说明了两个看涨(3.18和3.19)和两个看跌(3.20和3.21)的 例子。
图表3.18在这张每日图表上，我们看到AVWAP 支撑位被测试得越频繁，就越有可能失 I 败。
Chart 3.19 On this 65-minute chart,we see how the more frequently AVWAP Support is
tested the more likely it is to fail.Charts:TC2000.com
Charts 3.18 and 3.19 show stocks which repetitively tested the AVWAP from the prior  significant low before the trend reversed lower.As the  stocks
experienced decent rallies,the rate of ascent in the AVWAPs  slowed,
resulting in even more frequent market testing of the AVWAPs.Prices
eventually broke the AVWAP Support and began quick declines.
Recognition of this tendency will allow you to exit winners with the bulk of   your  profits  intact  before  reversals  take  place.For  more  aggressive  traders, the drop away from AVWAP can also provide an early entry into a reversal.
图表3.19在这张65分钟的图表上，我们看到AVWAP支撑位被测试得越频繁，就越有可 能失败。图表?TC2000,com
图表3.18和3.19显示了股票在趋势反转下行前，反复测试了之前的
AVWAP 显著低点。随着股票经历不错的反弹， AVWAP 的上升速率 放缓，导致市场对AVWAP 的测试更加频繁。最终，价格突破了
AVWAP 支撑位并开始快速下跌。
认识到这一趋势将使你能够在反转发生前，保住大部分利润退出赢家。 对于更激进的交易者，
从AVWAP   的回落也可以提供一个反转的早期入场点。
Chart 3.20 On this intraday timeframe,we see that the more frequently Resistance is
tested,the more likely it is to fail.

图表3.20在这个日内时间框架内，我们看到阻力被测试的频率越高，就越有可能失败。
Chart 3.21 On this daily timeframe,we see that the more frequently Resistance is
tested,the more likely it is to fail.Charts:TC2000.com
The two stocks in Charts 3.20 and 3.21 were in downtrends and consistently found sellers at the AVWAPs(red arrows),which were anchored to the
significant high prior to the decline.As the stocks declined further,the
AVWAPs were tested repeatedly,which eventually overwhelmed sellers
and the stock reversed to an upward trend.The repeated tests ofAVWAP   chewed through supply as the persistent buyers became more aggressive.
You can use the concepts ofAVWAP Support and Resistance on a stand-
alone basis for a trade system,andyou will probably achieve positive
results.Of course,you also must manage risk effectively.Do not confuse
simple with ineffective.All too many people want a complicated
approach,but  simplicity  is  the  market's  greatest  disguise.After  all,stock prices move because of supply and demand.We don't have to be obsessed
with the“why”behind the moves.The strategies in the chapters ahead will
assume you have read and understand the concepts discussed here.They are the building blocks ofthe layers we add on top of basic Support and
Resistance.
Risk Management
It can be difficult to wait patiently for conditions to develop into your ideal  time to make a trade and to resist the temptation to get involved early.Too many times,traders give into FOMO and buy before AVWAP provides
evidence confirming who has regained control.Thus,they suffer needless losses.For longer than I care to admit,this was a problem for me.I would
"be sure"a stock was ready to go,so I would get involved before the price
action confirmed momentum.Once in a while,I would get lucky on this type ofentry,but over the long-term,these trades ended up costing me money.
图3.21在这个日线周期中，我们看到阻力被测试得越频繁，就越有可能失败。图表：
TC2000.com
图表3.20和3.21中的两只股票处于下跌趋势，并始终在AVWAP
(红色箭头)处找到卖家，这些AVWAP   基于下跌前的显著高点锚  定。随着股票进一步下跌，AVWéPs  被反复测试，最终压倒了卖家， 股票反转形成上升趋势。AVWAP  的反复测试消耗了供应，因为持续 的买家变得更加激进。
您可以在独立基础上使用AVWAP 支撑和阻力概念来构建交易系统， 您可能会取得积极的结果。当然，您还必须有效管理风险。不要混淆
简单与无效。太多人想要复杂

方法，但简单是市场最大的伪装。毕竟，股票。 价格会因供需而变动。我们不必痴迷于
背后的“原因”。接下来的章节中的策略将         假设你已经阅读并理解了这里讨论的概念。它们

风险管理
耐心等待条件发展成你理想的交易时机，并抵制过早参与的诱惑可能 很困难。太多时候，交易者屈服于FOMO  并 在AVWAP   提供证据确 认谁重新掌控局面之前买入。因此，他们遭受不必要的损失。比我愿 意承认的时间更长，这个问题一直困扰着我。我会“确信”一只股票 准备好上涨，所以在价格行动确认动量之前就会提前参与。偶尔，我 会在这种类型的入场中幸运地获利，但从长远来看，这些交易最终让 我亏钱。
KEY TAKEAWAYS·AVWAP Support often becomes Resistance once it is broken.·AVWAP Resistance often becomes Support once it is broken.·Key AVWAP levels can indicate where the stock may lose momentum.·Do not  confuse  simple  with  ineffective.Too  many  people want  a  complicated  approach,but  "simplicity  is  themarket's  greatest  disguise.”·The more times AVWAP Support or Resistance is tested, the more likely it is to fail.

market's  greatest  disguise.”

关键要点一旦AVWAP 被突破，它往往就会成为阻力。AVWAP阻力位一旦被突破，往往会成为支撑位。关键的AVWAP水平可以指示股票可能失去动力的位置。不要将简单与无效混淆。太多人想要复杂的方法，但 “简单是市场最大的伪装。”AVWAP支撑位或阻力位被测试的次数越多，就越有可能失 败。

objectively and gain an edge in our buy and sell decisions.When we begin  our VWAP measurement from any point other than the beginning of one day,it becomes an“anchored”VWAP(AVWAP)and it is cumulative
from that point forward.Our interpretation of price action is relative to the direction and slope ofthe AVWAP.
The concepts introduced in this chapter are the basis of the strategy
chapters that follow.As always,the timeframe shown on the chart is
irrelevant.The same concepts apply to charts whether they are plotting stock price candles month-by-month or minute-by-minute.
The“science of technical analysis”is the theory you read about in many
trading books,including this one.So far,we have covered the objective
"science"of how  the AVWAP  forms  and  why  it  is  significant  to  our  analysis.
a.当价格是新闻时
b.使用基于价格的锚点

a.本周累计
b.本月累计

6. 锚定VWAP 交接和挤压
7.市场心理：锚定艺术
本章的目标是确定设置锚定的最宝贵位置。有了这个，我们可
以客观地衡量供需力量，并在我们的买入和卖出决策中占据优势。
当我们从一天的开始点以外的任何点开始我们的VWAP  测量时，它
就变成了“锚定”VWAP(AVWAP),        并且从该点向前累计。我们 对价格行为的解释相对于AVWAP  的方向和斜率。
本章介绍的概念是后续策略章节的基础。 一如既往，图表上显 示的时间段无关紧要。这些概念适用于图表，无论它们是按月 还是按分钟绘制股票价格蜡烛图。
“技术分析的科学”是你在许多交易书中，包括这本书中读到的理论。到目 前为止，我们已经涵盖了AVWAP 形成的客观“科学”原理及其对我们分析 的重要性。
Now it is time to address the subjective “art”ofwhere to start the anchored VWAP to assist in buy and sell decisions.This helps us better manage risk    and ultimately make more money.
The “art of trading”is what separates the successful traders from the   analysts.Learn the science of technical analysis and raise it to an art form as you implement it with your trades.
It is said that you can show a good trader a mediocre setup and he will make money and you can show a mediocre trader a great setup and he will still
lose money.Strive to be an objective analyst of the price-to-AVWAP
relationship on multiple timeframes and you willbe an even better trader. Successful traders practice their craft and spend time on layering their
experience-based intuition onto their technical analysis.
"The  best  long-term  performers  in  any
probabilistic    field,such    as    investing,sports    team management    and    pari-mutuel    betting-all
emphasize   process    over    outcome.”~Michael
Mauboussin
Anchor to High-Volume Events
The greater the volume of trading at a particular price level,the larger the number of participants with an emotional connection to that price level.
Therefore,the price levels aroundhigh-volume events can be useful levels to set your AVWAP anchor.Unusually high-volume(loosely defined as 1.5x normal volume)price events can"shock the market"and"reset"the
psychology of the crowd.The introduction of new information to a market,   whether news events or technical information,can trigger or create a large volume in trading that shakes the market loose from a level of
现在，是时候探讨主观的“艺术”了，即如何确定锚定VWAP  的起始点以 协助买入和卖出决策。这有助于我们更好地管理风险，并最终赚更多钱。
“交易的艺术”是区分成功交易者和分析师的关键。学习技 术分析的科学，并在实际交易中将其提升为艺术形式。
据说你可以向一个优秀的交易者展示一个平庸的设置，他仍然能赚钱； 但你可以向一个平庸的交易者展示一个绝佳的设置，他仍然会亏损。
努力成为价格与AVWAP  关系在多个时间框架下的客观分析师，你将 成为一个更好的交易者。成功的交易者磨练他们的技艺，并将基于经 验的直觉融入他们的技术分析中。
“在任何概率领域(如投资、体育团队管理和 博彩)中，表现最佳的长期者——无一不强调 过程而非结果。” Michael     Mauboussin
锚定高成交量事件
在特定价格水平上的交易量越大，与该价格水平有情感联系的交易参 与者数量就越多。因此，高交易量事件周围的价格水平可以是有用的 设置AVWAP 锚的水平。异常高交易量(大致定义为正常交易量的  1.5倍)的价格事件可以“冲击市场”并“重置”群体的心理。向市  场引入新信息，无论是新闻事件还是技术信息，都可能触发或创造大 量交易量，使市场摆脱某个水平。
consolidation.This  is  called  a  breakout.The  breakout  creates  a  sense  of
urgency  as  the  current  valuation  is  quickly  questioned  and  reevaluated  by many    participants.
When we set the AVWAP from high-volume areas,it helps us to see clearly if buyers  or  sellers  maintain  control  from  the  event.Unusually  large
volume  at,or  associated  with,a  breakout  increases  the  likelihood  of the
price  trending  in  the  direction(higher  or  lower)of  the  price  from  the
break.If the AVWAP from the event offers Support or Resistance,price will typically  experience  a  tradeable  continuation  as  price moves  away  from
AVWAP.If,instead,the AVWAP is undercut and the price remains under AVWAP,the stock is likely to reverse lower.Tests of the AVWAP from a
high-volume  event will  often become  a  battleground between buyers  and sellers,and the emerging trend can  set the tone  for the  stock for days,
weeks  and  even  months.
Large price moves,accompanied by a  surge in volume  are excellent anchor points  because  they   are  where   innumerable  “price  memories”live.The
price action and development of AVWAP  starting at these anchor points
becomes an objective reference point where we can make an unbiased
analysis of price action.From these points,the AVWAP helps us observe the real time changes in market values caused by the constant push and pull
between  bulls  and  bears.
Charts 4.1 and 4.2 show bullish and bearish high-volume levels as being a
good place to set an anchor.Chart 4.1 shows a large volume gap higher(1)   and  the  AVWAP(2)from  that  levelremained  important  almost  nine  months after the  initial  move began.
这被称为突破。突破会创造一种紧迫感，因为当前的估值会被许多参与者 迅速质疑和重新评估。
当我们从高成交量区域设置AVWAP   时，它有助于我们清晰地看到买 方或卖方是否在事件中保持控制权。在突破点或与突破相关的异常大 成交量会增加价格朝突破方向(更高或更低)趋势的可能性。如果事 件中的AVWAP 提供支撑或阻力，价格通常会随着价格远离
AVWAP   而出现可交易的延续。如果相反， AVWAP   被跌破且价格保 持在AVWAP 下方，股票可能会反转下跌。对高成交量事件中的
AVWAP   的测试往往会成为买方和卖方之间的战场，而形成的趋势将 决定股票在数日、数周甚至数月内的基调。
大幅价格波动伴随着成交量激增是极好的锚点，因为它们是无数“价 格记忆”所在之处。从这些锚点开始的价格行动和AVWAP   的发展成 为我们可以进行无偏见价格行动分析的客观参考点。从这些点出发， AVWAP 帮助我们观察多头和空头之间持续推拉所导致的市场价值实 时变化。
图表4.1和4.2显示了高成交量水平作为设置锚点的良好位置。图表 4. 1显示了一个较大的向上跳空缺口(1),并且从该水平开始的
AVWAP(2)      在初始运动开始后近九个月仍然非常重要。

图4.2高成交量柱是下降趋势中的重要锚点。图表：TC2000.com
图4.2是一 只处于下降趋势的股票图表，价格在第一个向下跳空 (3)时加速下跌，并在此点达到了迄今为止最大的成交量。从(3) 点开始计算的AVWAP    在12月和1月期间起到了阻力作用。1月中
还有一个较大的向下跳空，且成交量更为巨大(4)。这是一个很好的 例子，说明为什么不应该购买看起来“跌得太惨”的股票。
在可测量的事件处放置锚点
In its simplest form,a “measurable event”is a point where there is a clear shift in the supply and demand dynamics ofthe stock or market.A
measurable event typically involves a larger than normal price move
accompanied by a surge in trading volume.As Ialways say only price pays, so volume is secondary to the price action.Measurable events occur in
three  different  circumstances:
·Fundamental(news)events
·    Price-based  technical  events
·Time-based     events
We will explore allthree categories here to lay the foundation for the strategies in the following chapters.
The unique benefit ofthe AVWAP comes from the ability to start our
objective supply and demand measurement from any point that we choose. We don't want to anchor AVWAPs to random points on the chart.The
AVWAP is an elegant tool that allows us to measure the combination of
price,volume,and time together from any point.The question is,where to  set the anchor to help us see the market forces more clearly and ultimately make more money?
Anchoring to Fundamental Events
Fundamental events that may become the catalyst for a large price change could be earnings reports,FDA announcements,Federal Reserve
announcements  or  any  other  company's,sector's,or  market's  impactful
report.These may cause a higher volume of trading,but it is important to distinguish between a catalyst such as news and a simple supply and
demand shock that might not have been created by a specific news event.
在其最简单的形式中，“可衡量事件”是指股票或市场的供需动态 发生明显变化的某个点。可衡量事件通常涉及异常的价格变动，并 伴随着交易量的激增。正如我常说的，只有价格才是最终的裁判， 因此交易量相对于价格行为来说是次要的。可衡量事件发生在三种 不同的情况下：
*基本面(新闻)事件
*基于价格的技术事件
*基于时间的事件
我们将在此探讨所有三种类别，为后续章节中的策略奠定基础。
AVWAP的独特优势在于它能够让我们从任何我们选择的位置开始进 行客观的供需测量。我们不想将AVWAP  锚定在图表上的随机点。
AVWAP 是一个优雅的工具，允许我们从任何点一起测量价格、交易   量和时间。问题是，如何设置锚点以帮助我们更清晰地看到市场力量， 并最终赚更多钱?
锚定到基本事件
可能成为重大价格变动催化剂的基本事件可能包括盈利报告、F
DA 公告、美联储公告或任何其他公司、行业或市场的重大报告。这 些事件可能导致交易量增加，但重要的是要区分催化剂(如新闻)
与简单的供需冲击，后者可能并非由特定新闻事件引发。
It is good practice to know when potential market moving catalysts(such as earnings report dates)are due in the market.Awareness of these catalysts   minimizes the chance we will be surprised by what could be a large price
move against our position.It is important to know that a price movement
after a fundamental announcement is often counterintuitive.The market is a discounting mechanism and"good news,"which was expected,is often
welcomed as a profit taking opportunity by those who had the correct
position ahead of the event.Price speaks louder than the opinions of the
loudest  cheerleaders  for the  stock,because  the post-announcement trading actions of buyers and sellers speak louder than words.
Earnings Reports
The releases of individual corporate earnings reports are consistently
useful anchor points because they are when investors and traders will
refine their beliefs and trading strategies about the companies whose stock they are holding,or are considering as trade candidates.Corporate results  get reported every three months.At the end of each calendar quarter,
companies prepare their financial documents for the results of the
previous three months.The earnings reports are then reported to the
public.The “earnings season”refers to the quarterly period where
companies report their results.The earnings season begins one or two
weeks  after  the  last  month  ofeach  quarter(March,June,September,and
December)and continues for approximately sixto eight weeks.In chart 4.3 below you can see three different anchor points set at the times that the
earnings  reports  were  released.
了解潜在市场变动催化剂(如盈利报告日期)何时到期是一种良好的 实践。对这些催化剂的认识可以最大限度地减少我们因可能出现的重 大价格变动而感到意外的机会。重要的是要知道，在基本公告后价格 变动往往是非直觉性的。市场是一个折价机制，预期的“好消息”通 常被那些在事件前持有正确头寸的人视为获利了结的机会。价格比股 票最狂热支持者的观点更有说服力，因为公告后的买卖交易行为比言 语更有说服力。
盈利报告
个别企业盈利报告的发布始终是很有用的锚点，因为它们是投资者和 交易者调整其持有的股票或考虑作为交易候选公司的信念和交易策略 的时机。企业业绩每季度报告一次。在每个日历季度的结束时，公司 准备过去三个月的财务文件。然后，盈利报告会向公众发布。“盈利 期”指的是企业报告其业绩的季度时期。盈利期在每个季度最后一个 月(3月、6月、9月和12月)之后的一两周开始，并持续大约六到八 周。在下面的图表4.3中，你可以看到在盈利报告发布时设定的三个  不同的锚点。

occasions.Earnings  2(red  AVWAP)shows  a  negative  response  to  earnings and then two subsequent tests of the AVWAP as shares were sold into the  market  and  provided  Resistance.Earnings  3(blue  AVWAP)shows  an
acceleration  of  selling(notice  the   steeper  slope)as  sellers  reacted  to  the
contents of the report.Notice how the next four tests of the AVWAP  showed
Resistance.

Other news-related events that can become good anchor points include
Federal Reserve meetings and speeches,FDA announcements,activist
events around annual meetings,merger and acquisition news and rumors, patent  awards,secondary  stock  offerings,strategic  alliances,lawsuits  and  product  recalls,court  decisions,new  contracts,and  supplier  issues.
Corporate events such as new products,a change in management,dividend announcements,and share buybacks can also be anchor points.I do not
mean this list to be all-inclusive,nor is it meant to intimidate you.You do not have to follow all these events to know where to anchor.The  best
anchor points will become obvious to you as you become more practiced in the everyday application of AVWAP.

Chart 4.4 Federal Reserve announcements change the psychology of the market and
are important AVWAP points.Chart:TC2000.com
其他可以成为良好锚点的新闻相关事件包括美联储会议和讲话、FDA 公告、 围绕年度会议的激进活动、并购新闻和传闻、专利奖项、二次股票发行、
战略联盟、诉讼和产品召回、法院判决、新合同以及供应商问题。
公司活动，如新产品发布、管理层变动、股息公告和股票回购， 也可以作为锚点。我并非意在将此列表穷尽，也不是想吓唬你。 你不必关注所有这些活动就能知道如何锚定。随着你在日常生  活中更熟练地应用AVWAP,     最佳的锚点会变得显而易见。

图表4.4美联储公告改变市场心理，是重要的AVWAP  点。图表：TC2000.com
On the macroeconomic side of the news,a few of the catalysts for price
change that might be a good anchor point include economic numbers such as GDP,PPI,CPI,andjobs reports.Other events would include elections,
wars,and weather related events.Chart 4.4 illustrates an AVWAP from a  Federal Reserve announcement.Notice how that level became supported several days after the event.
Federal           Reserve           Announcement
Chart 4.4 is a major market ETF with the anchor set at 2 p.m.(1)on the day of the Federal Reserve policy announcement.After the initial volatility
between 1and 2,which is normal with an FOMC release,the buyers
regained control(2)and the trend continued higher.Five days later,the
AVWAP from the FOMC release was tested(3)and showed Support.We can use this AVWAP level as a place to set stops or to identify new buying
opportunities as the stock bounces higher from the AVWAP.
Price-Based         Events
When    Price    IS    the    News
Price action often is “the news,"but it doesn't get reported by the media
accurately.They try to assign a “reason”for every move.Price movement is based on supply and demand imbalances as new information comes to and    is absorbed by the market.We will briefly lookat some of the price-based
anchors to consider before we explore them in greater detail in the chapters to follow.
在新闻的宏观经济方面，一些可能作为良好锚点的价格变动催化剂  包括GDP 、PPI 、CPI  和就业报告等经济数据。其他事件包括选举、 战争和与天气相关的事件。图4.4展示了从美联储公告中得出的
AVWAP。  注意该水平在事件发生后几天内如何成为支撑位。
美联储公告
图表4.4是一个主要市场ETF, 其锚点设定在美联储政策公告当天的 下午2点(1)。在FOMC  发布后的1点到2点之间的初始波动，这是  FOMC  发布时的正常现象，买家重新掌控了局面(2),趋势继续上
升。五天后，FOMC 发布时的AVWAP 被测试(3)并显示出支撑。 我们可以将这个AVWAP  水平用作设置止损点或识别股票从
AVWAP  反弹时的新买入机会的地方。
基于价格的交易事件
当价格就是新闻时
价格行为往往是“新闻”,但媒体不会准确地报道它。他们试图为每 一次变动分配一个“原因”。价格变动是基于供需失衡，随着新信息 到达并被市场吸收。在接下来的章节中，我们将更详细地探讨它们之 前，简要地看一下一些基于价格的基础锚点。

Chart 4.5 Swing high points are important places to place an anchor.Chart:

The  obvious  andimportant highs  and  lows  are  easy  to recognize  after the   fact,but  that  doesn't  mean  they  aren't  useful.Highs  where  prices  reversed lower are some of the best anchor points for the AVWAP,as the following    tests of that AVWAP often prove to reveal the Resistance level.
Chart 4.5 shows how an AVWAP from a significant high will often act as
Resistance  for the  stock  on  short-term  bounces.When  a  stock  breaks
downward  from  a previous uptrend,an  anchor to  the most recent high  is  one of the best places to set an anchor.The anchor would probably not be set until  somewhere  in  mid-November(1),as  that  is  when  it  became  clear the early November high was an important one.While the stock is below

Chart 4.6 Swing low points are important AVWAPanchor points.Chart:TC2000.com
An important low is also easy to recognize after the fact.Even ifit takes a   couple ofdays for the low to become obvious,it makes sense to monitor to  see  ifbuyers  defend  the  average  price  from  that  low.Chart  4.6,shows  how an AVWAP from a significant low will often act as Support for the stock on  pullbacks.
When the stock makes an important low,we will recognize it a few days
after the fact(1)and then anchor our AVWAP from that now-identifiedlow
从那个高点开始的AVWAP 时，应将其视为“有罪，直到被证明无 罪。”注意在从锚定点开始的长期下降AVWAP 期间，向上的反弹 在接下来的三个月内(2)多次遇到阻力。总的来说，短期反弹时 的股票买家正在亏损，而空头控制着市场。

图4.6摆动低点是重要的AVWAP锚点。图：TC2000.com
一个重要的低点事后也容易识别。即使低点要过几天才变得明显， 也有意义地监控买方是否从那个低点捍卫平均价格。图4.6显示， 从一个重要的低点开始的AVWAP   往往会成为股票回调时的支撑。
当股票创下重要低点时，我们会在事后几天内识别它(1),然后从那个现 在已被确认的低点锚定我们的AVWAP
(0).The value and direction ofthe AVWAP might not be clear for days to
weeks later until after it is tested and(in this case)provides  Support(2)for the  stock.
When the stock is above the rising AVWAP,consider it“innocent until
proven guilty.”This means buyers are in control and sellers are fighting a losing game.
Anchoring to Specific Time-Based
Events
A third category of places to which to anchor the VWAP is time based.Many decisions of portfolio managers are based on time increments(daily,week- to-date,month-to-date,or   even   year-to-date).
People often say that institutions only use VWAP for one day in their trade executions;that is simply not true.As we learned in Part One,Chapter 3
institutions may set buy or sell programs for as short as a couple of hours. It is also common for institutions to use AVWAP programs to buy or sell
individual stocks or to buy or sellbroad-based markets and to execute one large order for periods such as a calendar week,month,quarter,or even   year,for very large orders.
(0).AVWAP 的值和方向可能需要几天到几周后才能变得清晰，直到它被测 试后(在这种情况下)为股票提供支撑(2)。
当股票价格高于上升的AVWAP时，可以将其视为“无罪，直到被   证明有罪”。这意味着买方掌控局面，而卖方在打一场输不起的仗。
锚定于特定时间事件
VWAP的另一个锚定点是基于时间的。许多投资组合经理的决策是基于时 间增量(每日、本周至今、本月至今，甚至本年至今)。
人们常说机构只在一天的交易执行中使用VWAP;   这根本就不正确。 正如我们在第一部分第三章中所学到的，机构可以设置持续几小时   甚至更短的买入或卖出程序。机构也常用AVWAP  程序来买入或卖出 个股，或买入或卖出广泛市场，并执行一个为期日历周、月、季度   甚至一年的大额订单，特别是对于非常大的订单。

Chart  4.7  I  always  set  an  AVWAP  at  the  beginning  of  a  new  week.Chart:TC2000.com
The bottom line is that institutions have strategies and timeframes that are as varied as the techniques used by individuals.Why wouldn't they?Below   we will look at some examples of broad market ETFs and individual stocks
where there is clear evidence on the chart that buy and sell programs are time based.
Week-to-Date(WTD)
Swing traders should keep an AVWAP that begins at the start ofeach week on their charts.You will see how often it comes into play as Support or
Resistance as the week progresses.
The     week-to-date     AVWAP(1)in     Chart     4.7(page     91)is     one     I      start     each Monday morning on all my charts.

图表4.7我总是在新的一周的开始设置一个AVWAP..  图表：TC2000.com
底线是，机构有与个人使用的技巧一样多样化的策略和时间范围。他  们为什么不呢?下面我们将查看一些宽市场ETF 和个股的例子，在   这些例子中，图表上有明确的证据表明买入和卖出计划是基于时间的。
本周至今(WTD)
波段交易者应该在他们图表上保持一个每周一开始的AVWAP。随着 一 周 的 推 进 ， 你 会 看 到 它 如 何 成 为 支 撑 或 阻 力 。
本周累计AVWAP(1)    在图表4 . 7(第91页)中是我每个周一早上在我所有
图表上都会关注的一个指标。
The  WTD  AVWAP  will   act  as   Support(2)and  Resistance(3),and  on  the chart,those   roles(on   all   timeframes)can    and   often   do   reverse.
Month-to-Date(MTD)
When  you  start  an  AVWAP  at  the  beginning  of the  month,it  might  not  show it's value until a week or two later.Once you have a MTD AVWAP on your
chart,as  seen  in  Chart  4.8,you  will  see  how  often  it  does  become  Support  or Resistance.
One  month  oftrades  is  shown  in  Chart  4.8.The  anchor  is  set  to  the  start  of  the  month  and  builds  from  there.Some  institutions  may  decide  to  purchase a  stock  over  the  course  of  a  month  and  their  programs  purchase  as  many
shares  as  they  can  at  “fair  value  for  the  month”on pullbacks  to  the  AVWAP (1).Notice  the  black  arrow(2).The  stock  opened  well  below  the  AVWAP
that   day,but   immediately   reversed    higher.
本周累计 AVWAP   将充当支撑(2)和阻力(3),在图表上，这些角色( 在所有时间周期)都可以并且经常发生反转。
当月累计(MTD)
当你月初开始一个AVWAP 时，它可能要到一周或两周后才会显示其价值。
一旦你在图表上有一个 MID    AVWAP,如图表4.8所示，你就会看到它成为 支撑或阻力的情况有多频繁。
一个月的交易情况显示在图表4.8中。锚点设置为月份的开始，并从  此处构建。 一些机构可能会在一个月内决定购买股票，他们的程序在 回调至AVWAP(1)       时以“月份的公平价值”购买尽可能多的股票  份额。注意黑色箭头(2)。那天股票开盘远低于AVWAP,    但立即  反转上涨。

Chart 4.8 I always keepan AVWAP from the start of the month on my charts.Chart:
TC2000.com
It is always best to  set your  stop-loss  orders AFTER the market  is  open.
Doing  so  will  save  you  from  throwing  your  stocks  away  on  a  manipulated lower  open  in  search  of stop  orders.The first few  minutes  of the  trade
day  can  be  more  volatile  as  deep-pocketed  participants  “hunt  for  stop  orders.”To  avoid  the  initial  volatility,I  generally  use  the  low  ofthe  first   five minutes ofa new day as the new stop if the previous  stop was traded through on a gap lower.
Quarter-to-Date(QTD)
Some  institutions(pensions  and  mutual  funds)will  make  the  decision  to
buy or sell a large position in a stock over the period of a calendar quarter.

图表4.8我总是在图表上从月初保持一个AVWAP。 图  表  ：TC2000.com
始终最好在市场开盘后设置你的止损订单。这样做将让你避免在寻找 止损订单时因人为操纵的低位开盘而抛售股票。交易日的前几分钟可 能波动更大，因为资金雄厚的参与者会“寻找止损订单”。为了避免 初始波动，如果前一个止损单在向下跳空时被成交，我通常使用新一 天前五分钟的最低价作为新的止损点。
本季至今(QTD)
一些机构(养老金和共同基金)会在一个日历季度内做出买入或卖出某只股 票大量头寸的决定。
These decisions are often based around earnings reports.
Chart 4.9 shows the price action for one calendar quarter.Notice how the  AVWAP from the first day of the quarter(1)acted as Support on pullbacks (2).
Some institutions make quarterly decisions to execute massive orders that need time to be filled.Always be aware of the slope ofthe AVWAP as prices approach and test it.The steeper the angle of the AVWAP,the greater the   evidence that buyers are more active than sellers and the more likely it is   that the AVWAP provides Support.Thus,it is more likely that stock will
bounce higher after an AVWAP touch.
ram:
这些决定通常基于盈利报告。
图表4.9显示了某个日历季度的价格走势。注意季度第一天(1)的 AVWAP  如何成为回调(2)时的支撑位。
一些机构会按季度做出决策来执行需要时间的巨额订单。始终要关  : 注价格接近时AVWAP  的斜率，并进行测试。AVWAP   的角度越陡峭， 买方比卖方更活跃的证据就越大，AVWAP  提供支撑的可能性也越高。 因此，AVWAP 被触碰后，股价更有可能反弹上涨。

Year-to-Date(YTD)
It's important to understand how some institutional portfolio managers use
YTD AVWAP.In short,it is part of how they are paid.Fund managers are
paid based not only on the absolute performance of their funds,but also on how   they   perform   relative   to    a   benchmark    index   or    relative   to    the
performance of their portfolio.

图表4.9从季度开始计算AVWAP  通常很有用。图表：

年初至今(YTD)
了解一些机构投资组合经理如何使用YTD AVWAP很重要。简而言之， 这是他们获得报酬的一部分。基金经理的报酬不仅基于其基金的绝对   表现，还基于他们相对于基准指数的表现，或相对于其投资组合的表   现。
As an example,a manager who runs a semiconductor fund will want to
make sure his average cost for the semiconductor stocks his fund owns is at least as good as the AVWAP from the first of the year.If the fund manager    buys stocks above the YTD AVWAP,it will hurt the performance of the fund  on a relative basis and,as a result,he will be paid less.If,instead,he is able to purchase the stocks in the portfolio at a price less than the YTD AVWAP, that fund will likely outperform others and he will earn more.
For stocks in strong uptrends,the YTD AVWAP will often act as Support as    fund managers purchase shares at this “fair value”of the stock for the year. Conversely,when the stock is in a downtrend,fund managers will use
rallies up to the YTD AVWAP to lighten up on their positions while the stock is closer to "fair value."
Chart 4.10 shows AVWAPs from the start oftwo different years.The start of a new year(1and 2)is a level that institutions willmeasure risk against,
both in the markets and in their individual stocks.What is often surprising is the AVWAP from the previous year(1)will still take on significance as a   level of Support or Resistance well into the next year.
例如，一位管理半导体基金的经理将希望确保其基金持有的半导体股 票的平均成本至少与年初的AVWAP 相当。如果基金经理在YTD
AVWAP 以上购买股票，它将相对损害基金的表现，结果他将获得更 少的报酬。如果相反，他能够以低于YTD    AVWAP的价格购买投资  组合中的股票，那么该基金可能会超越其他基金，他也将赚得更多。
对于处于强劲上升趋势中的股票，YTD    AVWAP通常会起到支撑作 用，因为基金经理会在此股票的“合理价值”处购买股票。相反，当 股票处于下降趋势时，基金经理会利用上涨至YTD    AVWAP的机会 来减轻仓位，而股票更接近“合理价值”时。
图表4.10显示了两个不同年份开始时的AVWAP 。新年的开始(1和  2)是机构衡量风险的水平，无论是在市场还是在他们各自的股票中。 通常令人惊讶的是，前一年(1)的AVWAP 仍然会在接下来的一年   中作为一个支撑或阻力水平具有重要意义。

锚定VWAP  交接和挤压
交接
当价格从原始锚点加速时，我们可以设置一个新的附加锚点来帮助 定义更强的动量。这个概念在图表4.11中介绍。
The blue AVWAP anchored to the low point shows an uptrend.Stocks can find renewed interest and accelerate dramatically from such an existing  trend.When this occurs,we can set a new AVWAP to help identify this
strength.The new purple AVWAP(1)can help with new entries and stop
蓝色的AVWAP  锚定在低点显示出上升趋势。股票可以从这种现有的趋势 中找到新的兴趣并显著加速。当这种情况发生时，我们可以设置一个新的 AVWAP   来帮助识别这种强度。新的紫色AVWAP(1)     可以帮助新入场和
止 损
placement in open positions.The place we anchor the new AVWAP(1)is
the "Handoff"area.It can also be referred to as a new “layer of momentum.”
Pinch
When we have identified key swing high and key swing low levels and the
stock coils between those two AVWAPs,they pinch together.The “pinch”is  a compression ofenergy(that is,the aggregate of traders'reevaluation of   strategies and their plans to buy or sell as soon as the price breaks one way or the other).When the stock exits the pinch,it is often an excellent trade   in the break's direction.Chart 4.12 is an example of an AVWAP pinch.

Going Deeper:Anchor to Price Gaps                                         深入探讨：锚定价格缺口
In Chart 4.13,a gap shows up on the chart when there is a large imbalance between supply and demand on the open and the market must open well
above or below the prior day close to find liquidity to fill the opening order. This leaves a “gap”or area where no trades appear on the chart.These
gaps reveal a strong shift in sentiment and become excellent anchor points to measure subsequent action from.This is so important that I wrote
Chapter 9,"AVWAP Gap Trading,"to thoroughly explain it.Chart 4.13,is   one example of an AVWAP from a gap to familiarize the concept before we study it in greater detail.

Chart 4.13 Price gaps show a sudden shift in supply and demand dynamics,which make
them valuable anchor points.Chart:TC2000.com
Chart 4.13 shows the anchor set to the gap in price action.This is the
circled area where the first candle opens higher than the prior day's close.
在图表4.13中，当开盘时供需出现巨大不平衡时，图表上会出现一个 缺口。市场必须大幅高于或低于前一日的收盘价才能找到流动性来满 足挂单。这留下了一个“缺口”或区域，图表上没有出现任何交易。 这些缺口揭示了情绪的强烈转变，并成为衡量后续行动的绝佳锚点。 这如此重要，以至于我写了第9章《AVWAP 缺口交易》,以详细解  释它。图表4.13是一个从缺口到AVWAP  的例子，让我们在深入研究 之前先熟悉这个概念。

图4 . 13价格缺口显示了供需动态的突然变化，这使得它们成为有价值的锚点。图：

图表4.13显示了价格行为中的锚点与缺口。这是第一个蜡烛开盘价高于前一 天收盘价的圆圈区域。
Notice the first test of the gap AVWAP(1)is not quite perfect Support,but   tests(2,3,4,and5)find buyers almost exactly at the AVWAP from the gap.
Notice price action at points 3-5 where the AVWAP is repeatedly tested
with very little bounce in the price.This is a clue that the stock may be
weak(for various reasons participants may collectively lose interest in
buying),and you should raise stops tojust below the low(2)to ensure you book profits before a larger selloff comes.
Market Psychology:The Art of Anchoring
The art of anchor placement is something that makes more sense as you  experiment with using the AVWAP in your daily analysis.It is easy to fall into the trap of "curve fitting"an AVWAP tojustify a level you want to
believe is Support or Resistance.Technical analysis is the study of price action,but more importantly,it is the study of the motivations of other   participants and where they make decisions to buy and sell.
Because the market"has memory,"we want to know the levels that are
most likely to have the highest emotional attachment for other traders and then measure how price action develops around those levels.These levels   are often driven by fundamental catalysts,but they can also be purely price driven.
Risk Management
The fear of missing out(FOMO)can ruin the best laid plans for a trade.
Learn to anticipate the trade setup and then WAIT for price confirmation before you participate in the trade.One technique Iuse to combat FOMO
注意，缺口AVWAP(1)   的第一次测试并非完美的支撑，但测试(2、3、 4和5)几乎在缺口处的AVWAP  找到了买家。
注意价格在3-5点的动作，AVWAP   被反复测试且价格几乎没有反弹。 这是一个线索，表明股票可能较弱(由于各种原因，参与者可能集   体失去购买兴趣),你应该将止损位提高到略低于低点(2),以确  保在更大规模的抛售到来之前锁定利润。
市场心理：锚定艺术
锚定位置的艺术随着你使用AVWAP  在日常分析中实验时，会更有 意义。很容易陷入“曲线拟合”AVWAP   以证明你想要相信的支撑 或阻力水平的陷阱。技术分析是价格动作的研究，但更重要的是， 它是其他参与者动机的研究，以及他们在哪里做出买入和卖出的决 策。
由于市场“有记忆”,我们想知道其他交易者最有可能对哪些水平有 最高的情感依恋，然后测量价格动作如何围绕这些水平发展。这些水 平通常由基本面催化剂驱动，但也可能纯粹由价格驱动。
风险管理
错失恐惧症 (FOMO)  可能会毁掉你最好的交易计划。学会预期交易设置， 然后在参与交易前等待价格确认。我用来对抗FOMO 的一种技术
entries is to set alerts ahead of a potential buy or sell level.Rather than set a buy stop,the alert simply tells me to take a closer look at the stock as it
approaches the key level.When the alert is triggered,I will watch the stock more carefully and decide whether it is time to take action or ifthe stock
needs more time.IfI decide the stock still needs more time for a new
position,I will set a new alert and repeat the process until I decide to enter a trade.This method allows me to become familiar with the short-term
action in the stock and to fine tune any adjustments to my plan,including where to set my stop.
Telegram:
是提前设置潜在的买入或卖出水平的警报。与其设置买入止损，警报  只是告诉我，当股票接近关键水平时，要更仔细地观察它。当警报被   触发时，我会更仔细地观察股票，并决定是否是采取行动的时候，或  者股票还需要更多时间。如果我决定股票仍然需要更多时间来建立新  仓位，我会设置一个新的警报并重复这个过程，直到我决定进入交易。 这种方法让我熟悉股票的短期走势，并微调我对计划的任何调整，包  括在哪里设置止损。

KEY TAKEAWAYS
·Some  of  the  most  important  levels  to  anchor  the  AVWAP to include:
o Fundamental (news events)
o Price-based/technical events
o  News   events   such   as;earnings   reports,Federal
Reserve announcements,jobs reports,and other Ot institutional publications or press releases
o Time-based events
·AVWAP  techniques  build  on  each  other  and  strategies
can be  formed  based  upon  patterns  or  situations  such  as the“AVWAP  Handoff”and“AVWAP  Pinch.”
·Time-based AVWAP anchors include traditional daily
VWAP as well as week-to-date,month-to-date,quarter- to-date,and year-to-date.
·Price gaps occur from a sudden shift in perception of value  of the  stock  and  those  levels  become  important
关键要点
*一些最重要的用于锚定AVWAP 的级别包括：
o 基本面(新闻事件)
o 基于价格/技术事件
◎新闻事件，如：盈利报告、美联储公告、就业 报告以及其他机构出版物或新闻稿
o 基于时间的事件
*AVWAP   技术相互关联，可以根据模式或情况(如“ AVWAP 交接”和 “AVWAP  挤压”)形成策略。
*基于时间的AVWAP 锚点包括传统的每日VWAP  以及 本周至今、本月至今、本季度至今和本年至今。
*价格差距源于对股票价值的突然转变，这些水平变得重 要

CHAPTER 5
THE AVWAP PINCH
“Energy and persistence conquer all
things.”
-Benjamin Franklin
Telegram:
Chapter         Objectives
1.Recognize a Pinch as it forms
2.Recognize when to get involved in a Pinch
3.Recognize who is in control of a Pinch
4.Understand why a Pinch is not a reason to buy or short a stock
5.How to manage risk when a stock breaks free of a tight Pinch
C  tocks that move out of a Pinch can offer some of the lowest-risk,
highest-probability trend continuation trades.Learn to recognize how   this AVWAP strategy forms and how to trade it effectively for larger profits.
第五章
AVWAP压缩
“能量和毅力可以征服一切。”
—本杰明 · 富兰克林
识别压缩的形成
识别何时应参与一个Pinch
识别谁控制着一个 Pinch
理解为什么一个Pinch   不是买入或做空股票的理由
5. 如何在股票摆脱一个紧密Pinch   时管理风险
从Pinch  中移动的股票可以提供一些风险最低、概率最高的趋势延续交易。 学习如何识别这种AVWAP  策略的形成方式，以及如何有效地交易它以获得更大 的利润 。
Markets are not one dimensional,there are trends within trends.When a longer-term trend begins to pull back,it forms a short-term downtrend
within the longer-term uptrend.An AVWAP Pinch refers to a compression   ofenergy from buyers and sellers for a stock or broad-based market as the  range tightens between two different AVWAPs.The original AVWAP acts as Support or Resistance from the longer-term,more powerful trend.The
newer AVWAP contains price action from the counter-trend(corrective) move within the larger timeframe.
Look for high-probability trades when the shorter-term trend comes into alignment with the longer timeframe trend.The emergence of an AVWAP Pinch is often the start of that alignment.
Market movement occurs with a price(and volume)expansion and
contraction,often alternating.The AVWAP Pinch forms when the battle for control creates a compression ofenergy,represented by a tighter trade
range.Eventually the range breaks and the buyers or sellers take control of the trend to create a new momentum campaign.
While the stock is "in the Pinch,"it is just a setup,not a reason to buy or
sell.We should not take action until it breaks out of the consolidation area  by   making    a   higher-high(long)or    a    lower-low(short).Chart    5.1    shows    how the a Pinch forms between a longer-and shorter-term AVWAP.
In Chart 5.1,we recognize the anchor(1)as a significant low only after the stock has built momentum from that level(2).
As the stock progressed higher,it didn't break to a lower-low until(4).At that point,we know to set an anchor to the highest-high(3).
Then the stock began to "Pinch,"that is staying at a price between the
AVWAP starting(1)and the AVWAP starting(3).When the stock breaks out
市场不是 一 维的，其中存在趋势内的趋势。当长期趋势开始回撤时，
它会在长期上升趋势内形成一个短期下跌趋势。AVWAP   Pinch指
的是在两个不同的AVWAP   之间范围收窄时，买方和卖方对股票或  广泛市场能量的压缩。原始AVWAP  从长期、更强大的趋势中充当  支撑或阻力。新的AVWAP  包含了更大时间框架内反趋势(修正性) 移动的价格行为。
当短期趋势与长期时间周期趋势 一致时，寻找高概率交易。
AVWAP  Pinch的出现通常是这种一致性的开始。
市场运动伴随着价格(和成交量)的扩张和收缩，通常交替发生。当控制权的争夺导 致能量压缩时，AVWAP   Pinch就会形成，表现为更紧密的交易区间。最终区间会突 破，买方或卖方将‘控制趋势’以创造新的动量战役。
当股票处于 “Pinch”     状态时，这只是一个布局，不是买入或卖出的理由。
我们不应采取行动，直到它通过形成更高的高点(长线)或更低低点(短线) 突破整理区域。图5.1显示了Pinch  如何在较长期和短期AVWAP 之间形成。
在图5. 1中，我们只有在股票从该水平(2)建立起动量后，才将锚点(1) 识别为重要低点。
随着股价上涨，它直到(4)才跌破更低低点。在那个点上，我们知道要设置 一个锚点到最高高点(3)。
然后股价开始“挤压”,即维持在AVWAP开始(1)和AVWAP开始(3)之间的价格。当股 价突破挤压(6)时，可以在“最近且最相关的更高低点”附近(5)下方设置止损买入。
of the Pinch(6),it can be purchased with a stop below the “most recent and relevant higher-low”near(5).

How the Pinch Forms
While  the  stock  is  in  a  Pinch,it  is  a  battle  between  buyers  and  sellers.As
the range narrows,it shows a constriction ofenergy,and the stock comes
closer to a state of equilibrium.The dynamic Support and Resistance ranges formed  by  the  converging  AVWAPs  show  the  interplay  of  the   larger
timeframe    trend    and    the    shorter-term    counter    trend    movement
当股价突破挤压(6)时，可以在“最近且最相关的更高低点”附近(5)下方 设置止损买入。

挤压的形成方式
当股票处于紧缩状态时，这是买方和卖方之间的博弈。随着波动范围的收窄， 显示出能量的收缩，股票更接近于均衡状态。由汇聚的AVWAP   形成的动态  支撑和阻力范围显示了更大时间周期趋势和短期反趋势运动的相互作用
(correction).Think of the Pinch like squeezing a spring together,the
energy gets compressed until the spring is let go and an energetic move follows.
Trading volume and price range tend to contract simultaneously during a
counter-trend move(i.e.,a pullbackin an uptrend or short-lived rally in a
primary downtrend).This action shows a lack of near-term certainty by
buyers and sellers. There is no advantage to be involved in the stock as
this battle continues and the stock is “in the pinch.”Instead,we want to watch the stock for the reemergence of the primary trend so we can
participate as the short-term trend comes into alignment with the longer, more powerful trend.While the stock is in the narrow range of a Pinch,we   want to prepare our trade and think through the scenarios of how the trade might  work  out.This  process  is  where  we  develop  our  risk/reward
scenarios.We set alerts on our trade software,so we know the moment price  begins  to  move.Large  moves  often  emerge  from  a  Pinch  as  many   participants are not alert to the quick price changes,so they end up
chasing the momentum.
As  we  discussed  in  Part  One,Chapter  2,stocks  alternate  between  periods  of price range compression and price range expansion.We want to identify
where the range compresses,prior to the next momentum campaign,so
that we can anticipate the breakout of that range.When we buy the stock   as  close  as  we  can  to  the  emergence  of  a  new  trend,we  maximize  gains  and minimize  our  risk.
When trends come into alignment,they present us with low-risk,high- probability  trades.How  we  participate  as  a  stock  breaks  from  a  Pinch  is illustrated,along with the appropriate stop placement,in Chart 5.2.
The stock in Chart 5.2 experienced a strong run from(1)and began to pullback(3)so we set a new AVWAP(in red)back(2).
(修正)。将紧缩想象成挤压弹簧，能量被压缩，直到弹簧被释放， 随后会出现有力的行情变动。
在逆势行情中，交易量和价格区间往往会同时收缩(即，上升趋势中  的回调或主要下降趋势中的短暂反弹)。这种行动表明买卖双方短期  内缺乏确定性。随着这场博弈继续进行，而股票处于“困境”中，参  与其中并无优势。相反，我们希望观察股票主要趋势的重新出现，以  便在短期趋势与更长期、更强大的趋势一致时参与其中。当股票处于  Pinch   的狭窄区间内时，我们希望准备交易并思考交易可能的结果场  景。这个过程是我们制定风险/回报场景的地方。我们在交易软件上设 置警报，以便在价格开始移动时知道。大幅波动往往从Pinch   中产生， 因为许多参与者没有对快速的价格变化保持警惕，结果他们追涨了动
能 。
正如我们在第一部分第二章中讨论的，股票价格会在区间收窄和区间 扩张的时期之间交替。我们希望识别出区间收窄的位置，以便在下一 轮动量行情开始之前，能够预判该区间的突破。当我们尽可能接近新 趋势的出现时买入股票，可以最大化收益并最小化风险。
当趋势形成一致时，它们会为我们提供低风险、高概率的交易机会。股 票从Pinch  突破时我们如何参与，以及适当的止损位设置，在图5.2中进 行了说明。
图表5.2中的股票从(1)开始经历强劲上涨，随后开始回调(3),因此我们在
(2)处设置了一个新的AVWAP (红色)。
The stock then pinched between the green AVWAP that started(1)and the
red  AVWAP  that  started(2).
At(5)the stock made a higher-high above the red AVWAP from the peak(2), so it made sense to purchase the stock with a protective stop loss below(6)  to assure that we take only a small loss if the stock reverses lower.

注意看股票并没有立即找到更高的动能。如果股票没有违反初始止损(在这  个例子中是6),就给股票一个运作的机会。当股票创下新高(7)时，我们  将止损提高到(8),因为这是一个更高低点，发生在更高高点之后。随着每 个新高的出现，我们
raise the stop to under each new higher-low.In Chart 5.2 we raised the stop to the new higher-low(10),when the stock made another new high(9).
When to Get Involved
The ideal time to buy a stock is as it breaks free of a tight range.The
early entry to an emergent trend gives us two advantages.One,we
become involved just as the trend begins,so we have the greatest profit  potential.Two,if the  breakout  cannot  hold,we  can  place  our  stop  close by.
For long positions,we place our stops below the most recent and relevant higher-low and for short sales,we place our stops above the most recent  lower-high.The simple definition of trend tells us there is more
opportunity when we buy stocks in uptrends and short the stocks in
downtrends.All too often,Isee traders fight this commonsense approach and attempt to purchase stocks in downtrends.They are irrationally
anchoredto a previous price level and view it as a bargain while prices
decline.Or they try to short stocks which appear to be “up too much,”
rather than  embrace  the higher probability(and  lower  stress)profits  that
come from an approach that follows the trend.The tighter the stop we
have,the greater share size we can trade while keeping our R-Multiple a constant.
Eventually,one side will take control of the trend.It is most likely that the direction ofthe AVWAP of the longer timeframe will resume it's trend
because “once a trend is established it is more likely to continue than to
reverse."When price comes out of the contraction found in a Pinch,it
shows whether the buyers or the sellers from the longer timeframe AVWAP
将止损提高到每个新的更高低点之下。在图表5.2中，我们将止损提高到新的 更高低点(10),当股票创下又一个新高(9)时。
何时参与
买入股票的理想时机是在它突破一个紧密区间时。早期进入一 个新兴趋势给我们带来两个优势。第一，我们就在趋势开始时 参与，因此我们拥有最大的利润潜力。第二，如果突破无法持 住，我们可以将止损设置在附近。
对于多头仓位，我们将止损设置在最近且相关的最高低点下方，对于空头销 售，我们将止损设置在最近最低高点上方。趋势的简单定义告诉我们，在上 升趋势中买入股票和在下降趋势中做空股票时，机会更多。我经常看到交易 者与这种常识性方法作斗争，并试图在下降趋势中购买股票。他们不合理地 锚定先前的价格水平，并在价格下跌时将其视为便宜货。或者他们试图做空 那些“涨得太高”的股票，而不是拥抱跟随趋势的方法所带来的更高概率
(和更低压力)的利润。我们的止损越紧，我们就能在保持R-Multiple不变 的情况下交易更大的仓位。
最终，一方将控制趋势。最有可能的是，较长时间周期的AVWAP方向将恢复 其趋势，因为“一旦趋势形成，它继续的可能性比反转的可能性更大。”当价 格走出Pinch 中的收缩区域时，它显示了较长时间周期AVWAP的买家或卖家 是否处于控制地位，以及是否合理预期一个可持续的趋势移动已经开始。
are in control and whether it is reasonable to expect that a sustainable trend move has begun.
The longer timeframe participants become emboldened by their profitable positions and are likely to defend the trend.The shorter timeframe
participants,who  bet  on  the  less  powerful,shorter-term  trend,feel
trapped.When feeling trapped,they may exit their losing positions or even flip from short seller to buyer,or buyer to short seller.All of this makes a
continuation of the longer timeframe trend more likely.
In contrast,Chart 5.3 shows a Pinch with a reversal of the longer-term
trend.This stock pinched between red AVWAP that began(1)and the green AVWAP that began(2).As it made a higher-high above the red AVWAP(3),it was time to purchase the stock with a stop(4).
When the stock makes another higher-high(5)we raise the stop to(6).The stock then made a large surge(7).A strong move like this is often an
excellent opportunity to sell part of the stock and then raise the stop on the balance to the higher-low(8).
是否处于控制地位，以及是否合理预期一个可持续的趋势移动已经 开始。
时间周期越长，参与者越倾向于根据其盈利仓位变得大胆，并可能捍 卫趋势。时间周期越短的参与者，则押注于较弱的短期趋势，感觉被 困住。当感觉被困住时，他们可能会退出亏损仓位，甚至从空头转变 为多头，或从多头转变为空头。所有这些使得较长时间周期趋势的延 续变得更加可能。
相比之下，图5.3显示了一个压力位，伴随着长期趋势的反转。这只股票在红 色AVWAP(1)   开始和绿色AVWAP(2)   开始之间被挤压。当它形成高于红 色AVWAP(3)   的新高点时，就是用止损单购买这只股票(4)的时候了。
当股价再次形成更高的高点(5)时，我们将止损位提高到(6)。随后  股价出现了一次大幅拉升(7)。像这样强劲的行情往往是卖出部分股票 并随后将剩余部分的止损位提高到更高的低点(8)的绝佳机会。

Chart 5.4 shows us why we do not get involved until the actual break of the Pinch occurs.The AVWAP pinch is typically(not always)resolved in the
direction  of the  primary  trend.

图5.3另一个向上解决的Pinch 案例。图：TC2000.com
在图5.3中我们看到(9),短期绿色AVWAP向上穿越了长期红色
AVWAP,   而长期红色AVWAP  是从当时的最高点(1)开始的锚点。一些  交易者认为AVWAP穿越是有用的，但我并未发现它们有显著的交易优势。
图表5.4显示了我们为何在Pinch   实际发生断裂之前不会介入。
AVWAP    Pinch通常(并非总是)会沿着主要趋势的方向得到解决。
Not all pinches will resolve in the direction of the longer,more powerful trend.
The stock in Chart 5.4 pinched(3)between the AVWAPs'anchor points
(green at 1 and red at 2).Because we know atrend once established is more likely to continue with the primary trend,we would have expected an
upside move beyond the red AVWAP(2).Instead,the stock broke a lower- low(4)and then experienced a large and fast move lower.

并非所有Pinch   都会沿着更长时间、更强大的趋势方向得到解决。
图5.4中的股票在AVWAP的锚点(绿色在1和红色在2)之间被挤压(3)。 因为我们知道一旦趋势确立更有可能继续与主要趋势，所以我们预期股票会 向上突破红色AVWAP(2) 。 相反，股票打破了一个更低低点(4),然后 经历了一次大而快速的下跌。

这种走势显示了为什么在价格上涨之前等待价格确认突破才买入是 很重要的 。 如果你在向上动能确立之前买入 ， 你会看到一次大而不 必要的损失 。
Some traders might think the failure of the upside break was an
opportunity  for  a  short  sale.Remember,this  book  is  not  about  counter-    trend  trades  or  "fading  the  trend."We  are  focused  on  trend-based  trades, which is the higher probability of success way to trade.Readers are
encouraged to use the information in this book to enhance their favorite trade  strategies,whatever  they  may  be.
Market Psychology:Recognize Who has Control
You may be familiar with names of patterns such as:head and shoulders,    triangles,flags,pennants,and   cup    and   handle.These   patterns    represent   a contraction  of price range,which then typically  leads  to  a  continuation  of  the  price  trend.
We can also apply the concepts we learned about the AVWAP Pinch to those patterns  on  all  timeframes.The  compression  ofrange  simply  represents
the tug of war between buyers and  sellers as they wrestle for control of the trend.The emergence of a new trend out of this compression shows which  side  has  gained  control(buyers  or  sellers)and  it  becomes  their  game  to
lose.We  can never  fully trust that the buyers  or  sellers will maintain   control once the new trend emerges,which is why risk management is always job number one.
Ifa move  does not  continue in the  anticipated  direction,we want to place our stop to ensure that any exit minimizes the risk of a large capital loss. When the  stock does move in the  expected direction,ourjob becomes risk management  for  the  open  position.
Winners  do  not  take  care  ofthemselves.Chart  5.5  shows  an  inverted  head and shoulders pattern which is further defined by the AVWAP Pinch.
一些交易者可能会认为向上突破的失败是一个做空的机会。记住， 这本书不是关于逆势交易或“逆势操作”的。我们专注于基于趋势 的交易，这是交易中成功率更高的方式。鼓励读者使用本书中的信 息来增强他们最喜欢的交易策略，无论是什么。
市场心理：识别谁掌控着局面
您可能熟悉一些模式的名字，例如：头肩顶、三角形、旗形、三角旗 形和杯柄形态。这些模式代表价格范围的收缩，这通常会引致价格趋 势的延续。
我们也可以将关于AVWAP    Pinch学到的概念应用于所有时间框架上 的这些模式。范围的压缩简单地代表了买方和卖方之间的拉锯战，他 们争夺着趋势的控制权。从这个压缩中形成的新趋势显示了哪一方已 经获得了控制权(买方或卖方),这成为他们需要输掉的游戏。 一旦 新趋势出现，我们永远无法完全相信买方或卖方会保持控制权，这就 是为什么风险管理永远是第一要务。
如果移动没有继续预期的方向，我们希望放置我们的停止以确保任何退出 最小化重大资本损失的风险。当股票确实按预期方向移动时，我们的工作 变成了对开放头寸的风险管理。
赢家不照顾自己。图5.5显示了一个倒转头肩模式，该模式进一步由 AVWAP   Pinch定义。
If you are familiar with the classic chart pattern,the “head and shoulders,” Chart 5.5 shows how the AVWPA adds further clarity to an inverted head
and shoulders pattern.For simplicity I've labeled Left Shoulder (LS),Head (H),and Right Shoulder(RS).

图5.5 AVWAP   叠加在倒置的“头肩”形态上。LS   左肩；Hl 头部；RS     右肩。图 ：

一旦股价跌破每股54美元(2),我们就知道要设置一个锚点到最近的近 期高点(1)。然后股价形成了倒置的头肩形态。从峰值(1)开始的
AVWAP阻力位在点(3)处，买家在此测试价格。
随着右肩形成了一个更高低点，我们在头部最低的蜡烛处重新锚定了一个新 的AVWAP (绿色)。在(4)处，股票形成了一个
higher-high.This  is  where  the  stock  could  be  bought  with  a  stop  just  below the most recent and relevant higher-low(5).
In  Charts  5.6  and  5.7,we  see  an  example  of  a  stock  in  a  longer-term  uptrend that  broke  out  of  the  Pinch  in  the  opposite  direction  of  the  primary  trend.It is  important  to  always  wait  for  price  confirmation  before  you  put  your
hard-earned  money  at  risk  while  the  stock  is  in  a  Pinch.
The  stock  in  Chart  5.6  showed  two  important  anchor  points  with  large  gaps on  the  day  the  company  reported  earnings.At  the  first  earnings  report,
AVWAP(1)didn't  show  its  significance  as  Support  until  after  the  2nd AVWAP(2)was    set.

Chart 5.6 The primary trend is higher so it would be expected to continue higher.Chart:
TC2000.com
In late December and early January,the first AVWAP(green)showed
repeated Support(green arrows)for the stock.The AVWAP from the 2nd
earnings report(red)showedstrong  Resistance(red  arrows)and  it
resulted in the stock getting pinched.We would monitor this stock for a
potential upside break.Chart 5.7 shows that a break in the direction is not   assured.Point(3)shows how the price broke lower than the longer upward trend(the first AVWAP in green).
Chart 5.7 uses the same stock as Chart 5.6.This time,we see the result of trading after a third earnings report(3)was issued.This was a genuine    surprise to the market,as the stock failed miserably after that report.
Notice how the stock continued lower for the next month after the earnings report(4).There are three lessons here.One,do not purchase a stock while it is in the trendless period of a Pinch.Two,new purchases of a stock before  earnings releases can be perilous.Three,there is no rush to buy stocks that might   appear  to  be   a   “value”after   a   large   selloff
图5.6主要趋势向上，因此预计将继续向上。图表：TC2000.com
在12月底和1月初，第一个AVWAP   (绿色)显示了多次对股票的支撑(绿  色箭头)。来自第二份盈利报告(红色)的AVWAP   显示了强烈的阻力(红 色箭头),并导致股票被压制。我们将监控这只股票，以观察潜在的向上突 破。图表5.7显示，方向的突破并不确定。点(3)显示了价格如何低于更长 的上升趋势(第一个绿色的AVWAP)。
图表5.7使用了与图表5.6相同的股票。这一次，我们看到在第三份盈利报告
(3)发布后交易的结果。这对市场来说是一个真正的惊喜，因为该股票在那 份报告后表现惨淡。
注意，在盈利报告(4)发布后，股价在接下来的一个月里继续下跌。  这里有三个教训。第一，不要在 Pinch 的无趋势时期购买股票。第二， 在盈利报告发布前购买股票可能很危险。第三，在大幅抛售后，不要   急于购买那些看起来像是“价值”的股票。

Market   Psychology:How   Committed Are  Buyers  and  Sellers?
If prices move quickly and have larger than normal volume levels,it can
show us there may be traders and investors from different timeframes
competing for the available supply(upside breaks).This behavior is known as a “range break.”An opportunity to buy after a pull back might not
