图5.7并非所有缺口都将沿着主要趋势方向得到解决。图： TC2000.com
市场心理：买方和卖方的承诺有多坚定?
如果价格快速移动且成交量水平异常高，这可能表明不同时间框架的 交易者和投资者正在争夺有限的供应(向上突破)。这种行为被称为 “区间突破”。在回调后买入的机会可能不
present itself for several days.The speed of a range break can reveal how motivated one side is and may change your entry technique.
This can be especially true of stocks that break out when they are
accompanied  by  a  fundamental  event,such  as  an  earnings  report.The  stock in Chart 5.8 came out ofits Pinch with a small gap(7).
As  always,the  concepts  and  setups  discussed  occur  in  all  timeframes.Chart 5.8 is constructed of 1-minute candles for the first 50 minutes of this day.
Anchor(1)occurred  at  the  start  of the  day  after  the  stock  gapped significantly higher  from the previous  day  close.
Initially,buyers held control of the stock,but then it broke below the daily VWAP(red)(2).
A day trader could start a short position with a stop above the high of the day(3).After  the  initial  bounce,the  stock  found  Resistance  at  the  daily
VWAP(4  and  5)and  stops  could  be  lowered tojust  above these  short-term peaks.A  new  AVWAP(green)was  anchored  to  the  new  lower-low(6).The  selling sped up(7)as the stock gapped below the AVWAP from(6).
Longer-term traders may look at this and not see the value of trading on a 1-minute  chart,but  shorter-term  traders  could  have  the  opportunity  to
profit from more than a 2-point decline in less than an hour.
持续数天出现。区间突破的速度可以揭示一方有多大的动力，并可能改变 你的入场技巧。
这尤其适用于在基本面事件(如盈利报告)伴随下突破的股票。图 5.8中的股票从其挤压状态以一个小缺口(7)突破出来。
一如既往，讨论的概念和设置发生在所有时间框架中。图5.8由当天  的前50分钟内的1分钟蜡烛图构成。锚点(1)发生在股票从前一天收 盘价显著跳高后当天的开始时。
最初，买方控制着股票，但随后它跌破每日VWAP  (红色)(2)。
日内交易者可以从当天的最高价(3)上方开始一个短头寸，并设置止
损：在初步反弹后，股票在每日VWAP(4   和5)处遇到阻力，止损可
以降低到这些短期峰值的上方。一个新的AVWAP  (绿色)锚定在新的
更低低点(6)。当股票从(6)处跳空低于AVWAP时，卖方加速(7)。
长期交易者可能会看到这一点，但并不认为在1分钟图上交易有价值，
但短期交易者可能会在不到一个小时的时间里从超过2点的下跌中获利。

The Anchored VWAP Pinch is a setup that typically gives us plenty of time to anticipate the trade setup as the stock “ping pongs”between the two    significant AVWAP levels.You may be tempted to enter the stock before it
exits the Pinch and makes a higher-high(longs)or lower-low(shorts)but, as we saw with the preceding examples,an AVWAP Pinch is not areason  to buy or short the stock.
We should enter the trade when the stock breaks out of the Pinch to participate in the emergent momentum.Of course no trade plan is   complete without setting a stop after the entry to protect against
catastrophic losses.

锚   定VWAP       捏合是一种通常给我们足够的时间来预期交易设置 的设置，因为股票在两个重要的AVWAP   水平之间“弹跳”。 您可能会在股票退出捏合并形成更高高点(多头)或更低低点 (空头)之前进入股票，但正如我们从前面的例子中看到的， AVWAP   捏合并不是买入或做空股票的理由。
当股票突破压力位时，我们应该入场以参与新兴的动能。当然，
没有在入场后设置止损的交易计划是不完整的，以防止灾难性 的 损 失 。
Risk Management                                             风险管理
Trends are not one dimensional,there are trends within trends,and therefore we wait for price confirmation before getting involved.
An AVWAP Pinch is most likely to break in the direction of the primary    trend.The tighter the pinch,the more likely it is to experience a powerful break.When a stock breaks free of a tight pinch,we can keep close stops and trade more shares with the same R-Multiple at risk.
legram:                             Bot
趋势不是一维的，存在趋势中的趋势，因此我们在参与前等待价格确 认。
AVWAP     Pinch最有可能在主要趋势的方向上破裂。挤压越紧，越 有可能经历强大的突破。当股票从紧挤压中突破时，我们可以保持 紧密止损，并以相同的R-Multiple 承担更多股票的交易风险。
Telegram:@Group     Buys_Bot
KEY TAKEAWAYS·An AVWAP Pinch is a tightening of the price range.·   The break of the Pinch often leads to excellent trend trades.·The action point of an AVWAP Pinch is when it breaks free of it's consolidation.·The ideal time to buy a stock is as it breaks free of a tight  range.The early entry to an emergent trend gives us two advantages.One,we become involved just  as the trendbegins,so  we  have  the  greatest  profit  potential.Two,ifthe breakout cannot hold,we can place our stop close by.·It  is  more  important  to understand the psychology  of how a Pinch is formed than it is to simply recognize patternformations.·   Not all Pinches will be resolved in the direction of theprimary trend,which is why we wait for price to confirm the break before we get involved.
KEY TAKEAWAYS
·An AVWAP Pinch is a tightening of the price range.
·   The break of the Pinch often leads to excellent trend trades.
·The action point of an AVWAP Pinch is when it breaks free of it's consolidation.
·The ideal time to buy a stock is as it breaks free of a tight  range.The early entry to an emergent trend gives us two advantages.One,we become involved just  as the trend
begins,so  we  have  the  greatest  profit  potential.Two,if
the breakout cannot hold,we can place our stop close by.
·It  is  more  important  to understand the psychology  of how a Pinch is formed than it is to simply recognize pattern
formations.
·   Not all Pinches will be resolved in the direction of the
primary trend,which is why we wait for price to confirm the break before we get involved.
关键要点
AVWAP   Pinch是价格区间的收紧。
Pinch 的突破往往能带来绝佳的趋势交易。
AVWAP   Pinch的动作点是指它突破其盘整区域时。
买入股票的理想时机是当它突破一个紧密区间时。早期 进入一个新兴趋势给我们带来两个优势。第一，我们刚 趋势开始时就参与其中，因此利润潜力最大。第二，如 果突破无法持住，我们可以将止损设置在附近。
理解Pinch  形成时的心理比单纯识别模式形成更为重要。
并非所有Pinch 都会在主要趋势的方向上得到解决，这 就是为什么我们要等待价格确认突破后再参与。
·   AVWAP Pinches are formed and are actionable on all timeframes.

CHAPTER 6
NEW ANCHOR
POINTS INA TREND (THE HANDOFF)
“We ought neither to fasten our ship to   one small anchor,nor our life to a single hope.”
—Epictetus
Chapter Objectives
1.Define“Handoff”
2.Identify  a  Handoffin  uptrends,downtrends,and  in   all timeframes
3.How to time entries and exits using Handoffs
4.When to combine Handoff and Pinch
第六章
趋势中的新锚点 (交接)
“我们既不应将船系在一根小锚上，也 不应将生命系于一个希望。”
—爱比克泰德
章 节 目 标
1.定义“交接”
2.在上升趋势、下降趋势以及所有时间段中识别一个交接点
3.   如何使用Handoffs   计时出入
4,何时合并Handoff  和Pinch
A  s we have learned,primary trends rarely move in a smooth line.They
几    1s…low ddow…n and s~peed up at…v:…ariousm :tpLoofints before an even…t1u-al rever~1sal.
This is why we will have multiple anchor points on a chart.When a trend
accelerates from the original anchor point,in either direction,it is useful to create a new AVWAP to help measure the renewed momentum.This gives    us the ability to better define and manage risk for existing positions,as well as for new entries.
We anchor a new AVWAP when a trend begins to accelerate after the
original AVWAP was touched(or nearly touched).This is our "Handoff
point,"a term I coined.A Handoff helps us to visualize and take advantage of the changes in the rate of momentum in a primary trend.
t
We leave the original or preceeding AVWAP on the chart for future
reference because the stock will often find Support(in uptrends)or
Resistance(in downtrends)at or near that original Handoff point.In this chapter's charts you'll see my own best practice of changing the new
AVWAP's color with each new anchor point.
Handoffs  in  an  Uptrend
The best tool I have to explain Handoffs is through example.Please look at the Chart 6.1 and follow the comments.
This stock was in a downtrend(A)prior to the low(1)in April.We can't
know that(1)is an important level(either high or low)until the price
moves significantly.At(2)the significant upward movement away from(1)
如我们所学，主要趋势很少以平滑的线条移动。它们在各个点会减速 和加速，最终发生反转。这就是为什么我们在图表上会有多个锚点。 当趋势从原始锚点加速，无论方向如何，创建一个新的AVWAP   以帮 助衡量重新获得的动量是有用的。这使我们能够更好地定义和管理现 有头寸的风险，以及为新入场提供支持。
当原始AVWAP 被触及(或几乎触及)后，趋势开始加速时，我们  会锚定一个新的AVWAP 。这是我们所说的“交接点”,是我创造  的术语。交接点帮助我们可视化并利用主要趋势中动量变化的速度。
我们将原始或之前的AVWAP   保留在图表上以供将来参考，因为  股票通常会在原始交接点或附近找到支撑(在上升趋势中)或阻力 (在下降趋势中)。在本章的图表中，你会看到我个人最佳实践：
随着每个新的锚定点，更改新AVWAP   的颜色。
上升趋势中的交接点
解释交接点的最佳工具是通过示例。请查看图表6.1并跟随注释。
这只股票在4月份的低点(1)之前处于下跌趋势 (A) 。 直到价格显著移动 后，我们才能知道(1)是一个重要水平(无论是高点还是低点)。在(2) 处，显著的向上移动远离(1)
indicated that(1)was an important low.This is when we set our initial anchor(1).
As the stock progressed higher over the next several months,the
momentum remained until the pullback in October(3).Since the stock   quickly bounced from the original AVWAP(green)and showed renewed upward momentum from(3),we set a new anchor(and a new AVWAP in blue)(3).The "Handoff'hasjust taken place from green to blue.

表明(1)是一个重要的低点。这就是我们设置初始锚点(1)的时候。

(3)显示出新的上涨动能，我们设定了 一 个新的锚点(并在蓝色中 设定了新的AVWAP)(3) 。   “交接”刚刚从绿色切换到蓝色。

图6.1周时间框架上的上升趋势中的股票，有三个不同的Handoffpoints (产生四个 AVWAP) 。 图 ：TC2000.com
The stock continued to show strength for the next eight months until a
pullback in August(4)saw a test of the blue AVWAP that had been anchored at  the  first  Handoff(3).
At(5)the stock bounced from our blue AVWAP,indicating a more
aggressive  source  of  demand.By  setting  a  new  anchor  at(5)and  using  red as the color for the newest AVWAP,we can capture the essence of the
demand.The  second  Handoff  has  taken  place(5).
At(7)the stock continued down to the blue AVWAP that we had anchored (3)and once again  found buyers.As the  speed  of the upward momentum   increased,we recognized a new control point to hand off with another
AVWAP(in   purple)(7).
When  we  have  several  Handoff points  on  the  chart,it  looks  like  there  are different  “layers”of trend  to  measure,which  is  why  we  can  also  refer  to  an AVWAP Handoff as layering.
Going Deeper:Entry and Exit with
Uptrend Handoffs
Chart 6.2 uses a different stock to show how to implement Handoffs.Our
goal  is  to  enter  an  existing  trend  at  low-risk,high-probability  points.This  is an important strategy that helps us avoid FOMO purchases and take
unnecessary  risk  by  entering  with  renewed  momentum.
股价在接下来的八个月内继续显示出强势，直到8月的回调(4)测试了在第 一次“交接”(3)时锚定的蓝色AVWAP。
在(5)处，股价从我们的蓝色AVWAP   反弹，表明需求来源更加激进。通 过在(5)处设置新的锚点，并将红色用作最新的AVWAP  颜色，我们可以 捕捉需求的本质。第二次Handoff 已经发生(5)。
在(7)处，股价继续下跌至我们锚定的蓝色AVWAP(3),   并再次找到买 家。随着向上动量的速度增加，我们识别出新的控制点以Handoff, 并 使用另一个AVWAP (紫色)(7)。
当图表上有多个 Handoff    点时，看起来像是不同的“趋势层”需
要测量，这就是为什么我们也可以将AVWAPHandoff       称为分层：
深入探讨：上升趋势Handoff 的入 场和出场
图表6.2使用不同的股票来展示如何实施转手。我们的目标是进入低风险、 高概率的现有趋势点。这是一个重要的策略，它帮助我们避免FOMO 购买， 并通过以新的势头入场来避免不必要的风险。

Chart 6.2 Daily chart in an uptrend with entries(green dots using odd numbers)and
stop    levels(blue     arrows     using    even     numbers)based     on    the     Handoff    technique.Chart:
TC2000.com
At(1),the new uptrend begins for the stockin Chart6.2 and the green
AVWAP is anchored there.Notice that there are two Handoff points(4 and
8)chosen several days after the stock touched the green AVWAP and more   invigorated buyers appeared.The smart trader would choose these Handoff points to anchor new AVWAPs(blue at 4 and purple at 8)in light of strong    price movements away from the touches.These Handoffs show a renewed
commitment of buyers,which makes themimportant levels.
The chart shows several examples(green dots)of where we might want to purchase this stock as it came back to test the blue and purpose AVWAPs    from the Handoff points.The even numbers without dots(2,4,6,8,10,and  12)show where people who purchased at the pullback to the most recent   AVWAP may have purchased.
A岭                        Sep                                                  Qut图6.2每日：使用Handoff 技术绘制的图表呈上升趋势，包含入场点(绿色圆点-使用奇数)和止损位(蓝 色箭头-使用偶数)。图表：TC2000.com
A岭                        Sep                                                  Qut
在(1)处，图表6.2中的股票开始新的上升趋势，并且绿色
AVWAP 就锚定在那里。请注意，在股票触及绿色AVWAP  几天后， 出现了更积极的买家，选择了两个转手点(4和8)。聪明的交易者会  根据强劲的价格运动远离触及点，选择这些转手点来锚定新的
AVWAP(4    处为蓝色，8处为紫色)。这些转手点显示了买家重新 承诺的意愿，这使得它们成为重要的水平。
该图表展示了几个示例(绿点),即我们可能希望购买该股票的地 方，因为它回到了测试蓝色和目的AVWAP   的 Handoff  点。没有 点的偶数(2、4、6、8、10和12)显示了在最近AVWAP 的回调 时购买的人可能购买的地方。
In all the instances except(12),buying as the stock first touches the
AVWAP would have resulted in a profitable trade.Yet,(12)showed no
significant bounce and instead failed,which would have resulted in a loss.  As stated in earlier chapters in the book,the point of first contact with the AVWAP is a point of interest,not necessarily a safe trigger point to place a trade.
The green dots,associated with the odd numbers,show purchase levels
after the AVWAP was tested.Ifyou purchase at the green dots,you could
place a stop below the prior blue arrow at the prior even number.For
instance,ifyou  purchased(7)the  most  recent  relevant  higher  low  was(6). Place the stop under that level.
Notice there is no number 13 above,no it's not because the number 13 is unlucky.There is no 13 because the stock failed to show the proper
strength to bounce higher from the AVWAP.
As we studied with Support and Resistance in Chapter 2,when the price
touches the previous AVWAP,it is up to the trader to decide if they want to purchase a new position or add to an existing position.
The best purchase option occurs when the stock moves away from the
AVWAP touch as new price momentum develops.My preference is to buy if the stock shows renewed momentum.This will allow me to purchase with a price trend in my favor from the start,and with the bonus of a logical place  to set the stop.Risk management is always on the mind of the most
successful  traders.
At times we need to remove an anchor ifa significant price move did not develop and the stock turned sideways.This helps keep your chart
uncluttered.Once you have more experience with the anchoring process, this will become more intuitive.
在除(12)以外的所有情况下，当股票首次接触AVWAP时购买将导致盈  利交易。然而，(12)显示了没有明显的反弹，反而失败，这将导致亏损。 正如本书早些章节所述，AVWAP的首次接触点是一个值得关注的点，但  不一定是放置交易的可靠触发点。
与奇数相关的绿色点显示了在 AVWAP   测试后的购买水平。如果你 在绿色点购买，你可以在之前的偶数处的蓝色箭头下方放置一个止 损。例如，如果你购买了(7),最新的相关更高低点是(6)。在 那个水平下方放置止损。
请注意，上面没有数字13,不是因为数字13不吉利。没有13是 因为股票未能显示出从AVWAP  向上反弹的适当强度。
正如我们在第2章中通过支撑和阻力所研究的那样，当价格触及之前 的 AVWAP 时，交易者需要决定是否要开立新仓位或加仓现有仓位。
最佳购买时机发生在股票远离AVWAP 触及时，新的价格动能正在  发展。我的偏好是如果股票显示出新的动能就买入。这将使我从一开 始就能以有利的趋势价格购买，并且还有一个逻辑上合理的止损设置 位置。风险管理始终是最成功的交易者心中的重点。
有时我们需要删除一个锚点，如果价格没有出现显著变动，而股票 转为横盘整理。这有助于保持你的图表整洁。一旦你对锚定过程有 更多经验，这将变得更加直观。
Handoffs in a Downtrend
Just as Support and Resistance are mirrors ofeach other,the Handoffs in    uptrends and downtrends are similarly opposite.Chart 6.3 shows Handoffs with a stock in a downtrend.
The stock in Chart 6.3 gapped higher at opening(1)and failed to hold the
gains from that gap.The time wasn't right to set the anchor point until(2),  when the stock made a lower-low,at which point we set the anchor point to (1).Remember,we look to anchor at a logical point,such as a lower-high
(on a downtrend)or a higher-low(on an uptrend).
Then the stock rallied up to the(red)AVWAP(3)and turned sharply lower. This is where we set our first AVWAP Handoff(purple).As the stock
continued lower,it experienced a failed attempt to move higher(5).At(4) the stock made a lower-low,so we began another AVWAP Handoff(blue)    back(5).
下行趋势中的交接
正如支撑位和阻力位互为镜像一样，上升趋势和下降趋势中的转手 点也同样是相反的。图6.3显示了处于下降趋势中的股票的转手点。
图6.3中的股票在开盘时(1)出现跳空高开，但未能守住该跳空带来的收益。 直到(2)时，股价形成更低低点，我们才将锚点设置为(1)。记住，我们  会在一个逻辑点锚定，例如下行趋势中的更低高点，或上行趋势中的更高低  点。
然后股价上涨至(红色)AVWAP(3),  然后急剧下跌。这就是我们设置第一 个AVWAP交接点(紫色)的地方。随着股价继续下跌，它经历了一次试图 上涨的失败(5)。在(4)股价创出了更低低点，所以我们开始了另一个
AVWAP  交接点(蓝色)回到(5)。

Only set an anchor once you realize that the stock reached an important
level.This means we will always recognize the Handoff after the move is
underway.At(7),the stock ran into the blue AVWAP from(5)and continued back down.

The next Handoff(light blue)was placed(8)after the stock failed to push up    through    the   prior(black)AVWAP    Handoff.

Going Deeper:Entry and Exit with
Downtrend Handoffs
As we will explore in the next chapter,entries for lower-risk short sales
occur when the stock has downward momentum.Chart 6.4 shows entries
and  stop  points  for  short  sales.Notice  how  the  Handoffs  do  not  always  touch precisely on the prior AVWAP.This is intentional so as to show that not all   trade opportunities are traditional “textbook examples.”
Chart 6.4 Daily chart in a downtrend with entries(green dots using odd numbers)and
stoplevels (blue arrows using even numbers)based on the Handoff technique.Chart:
TC2000.com
This stock is in a Stage 4 Decline(see:Chart in AppendixA)and shows where  the   first   AVWAP(red)is   anchored(1).We   set   the   next   anchor
深入探讨：下行趋势中的入场与离场 (交接技术)
正如我们将在下一章中探讨的，低风险卖空交易的入场发生在股票具  有向下动量时。图表6.4显示了卖空交易的入场点和止损点。请注意， Handoff 并不总是精确地触及之前的AVWAP。  这是有意为之，以   便展示并非所有交易机会都是传统的“教科书示例。”

图6.4下行趋势中的每日图表，基于交接技术，使用奇数编号的绿色点表示入场，使用偶数编号的蓝色箭 头表示止损位。图表来源：TC2000.com
这只股票处于第4阶段下跌(参见：附录A中的图表)并显示了第一个 AVWAP  (红色)的锚定位置(1)。我们设定了下一个锚点
(purple)(2),but this was not an official Handoff because prices didn't touch the first(red)AVWAP.We set it(2)because prices moved steadily lower
from that point.Do not expect perfection in any aspect of analysis or
trading,our goal  is to  capture the  essence  of trend,not  argue  about  what qualifies in a textbook as a Handoff or any other concept.
The “art”of analysis andtrading allow for interpretation within reasonable guidelines.At points(4 and6)there were official Handoffs from the
previous(purple)AVWAP(2).
More important than what qualifies as a Handoffis the opportunity to enter this stock with a short sale.The odd numbers,associated with the green
dots(3,5,7,9,and11),show where we could enter a  short position as the stock gathers momentum to the downside.
The choice to enter the short trade is the same as when we buy a stock.Do   we short at or around the touch ofthe important AVWAP,or wait for prices  to turn away from the AVWAP?An entry at either of these two points would allow for a stopjust above the prior peak(marked by the even numbers).
For example,we could protect a short sale entry(7)with a stop above the prior peak(6).If we  sold the stock short(7)and then it happened to
increase in price above the prior high(6),the definition of the downtrend (lower-highs and lower-lows)would no longer exist,so we would cut our  loss at that point.
The first official entry as this stock touched a prior AVWAP would have
occurred(5),with  a  stop  above(4).The  entries(6,8,and   10)would  not  have had a“most recent and relevant lower-high”nearby to protect the position with a stop,which makes these entries riskier.
(紫色)(2),但这不是一个正式的交接，因为价格没有触及第一个   (红色)AVWAP 。我们设定它(2),因为价格从那时起稳步下降。 不要期望分析或交易的任何方面都完美无缺，我们的目标是捕捉趋势  的本质，而不是争论教科书上定义为交接或其他概念的标准是什么。
分析交易中的“艺术”允许在合理范围内进行解释。在点(4和6)处 有官方的Handoffs,    来自之前的(紫色)AVWAP(2)。
比Handoff  的资格更重要的是有机会以空头交易进入这只股票。与绿 色圆点(3、5、7、9和11)相关的奇数显示了我们可以进入空头位置 的地方，因为股票在向下的方向聚集动量。
进入空头交易的决策与我们购买股票时相同。我们是直接在重要的
AVWAP接触点附近做空，还是等待价格远离AVWAP? 在这两个点中的 任何一个点进入，都允许在之前的峰值(由偶数标记)上方设置止损。
例如，我们可以用之前的峰值(6)上方的止损来保护空头交易入  口 (7)。如果我们以空头交易(7)卖出股票，然后它碰巧在之前 的最高点(6)以上上涨，那么下降趋势(低高点和高低点)的定  义将不再存在，因此我们会在那个点止损。
当这只股票触及之前的AVWAP时，第一个官方入场记录(5)将会发生，
并且会在上方设置一个止损(4)。而入场点(6、8和10)附近没有“最近 且相关的更低高点”来保护仓位设置止损，这使得这些入场点风险更高。
Handoffs in All Timeframes
As  always,it  is  worth  a  mention  that  these  AVWAP  Handoff  concepts   apply to alltimeframes.The principles of the Handoffs apply from longer-term
investing allthe way down to day trading froma1-or 2-minute chart,as shown  in  Charts  6.5  and  6.6.
Chart  6.5  shows  two  trade  days  for  one  stock.On  the  first  day,the  stock  was strong  from  the   start  and  never  pulled  back   for  a  test   of  the   daily  VWAP.On day  two,the   stock  pulled  back(2)to  the   green  AVWAP   from   day   one.

所有时间段的交接
一如既往，值得提及的是，这些AVWAP 交接概念适用于所有时间 周期。交接原则从长期投资一直应用到1分钟或2分钟图表的日内 交易，如图表6.5和6.6所示。
图表6.5显示了某只股票的两个交易日。第一天，该股票从开盘就表现强劲， 并且从未回调以测试每日VWAP。  第二天，该股票回调(2)至第一天绿色的  AVWAP。

2.更安全的选择是在红色点(3)附近做空股票，因为股票已经远离 每日VWAP。

无论我们的选择如何，我们都会在(2)上方放置一个保护性止损单。然 后止损单会跟踪到红色箭头所表示的高点上方。注意，点(4和5)也是  新Handoff   水平的基础，因为下跌的冲刺速度远离了之前的

深入探讨：结合Handoff 和Pinch
一旦你学会定期识别一种AVWAP策略，你就会开始注意到其他策略会在图表上 出现。现在我们可以看看Handoff 和Pinch 如何协同工作。如果你错过了
original trade,there  are  often  new purchase points  after  an  AVWAP Handoff.
When  this  happens,you  will  see  alternative  entries  at  Handoff  points.The stock in Chart 6.7 started with a buy opportunity as it broke a pinch(3).
This might look overwhelming,but follow the chart AVWAP to AVWAP.Each is a different color to make it easier to follow price action.
We  placed  the  anchor(1),the  opening  price,then  we  waited  out  the
downtrend  to  find  a  reversal  indicated  by  the  new  higher-low(4).When  the stock  climbed  back  above  that  AVWAP(3)and  buyers  regained  control,then we would set a new AVWAP in green to the low(2).
The  stock  broke  beyond  the upper AVWAP(red)to  create  a  near-term
higher-high(3).At that point we  could buy the  stock with  a  stop  below(4), the  most  recent  and  relevant  higher-low.

原始交易中，AVWAP     Handoff之后通常会有新的买入点。
当这种情况发生时，你会在Handoff 点看到备选入场点。图6.7中的股票在 突破压力位(3)时开始出现买入机会。这可能看起来令人不知所措，但请跟  随图表中的AVWAP   到  AVWAP。  每个都是不同的颜色，以便更容易跟踪价
格  走  势  。
我们放置了锚点(1),即开盘价，然后我们等待下跌趋势以找到由新的更高 低点(4)指示的反转。当股票回升至AVWAP(3)   以上且买家重新掌控局面 时，我们就会在绿色中设置一个新的AVWAP   到低点(2)。
该股票突破上方AVWAP (红色)以形成一个短期更高高点(3)。在那个 点上我们可以以低于(4)的止损买入该股票，这是最新且最相关的更低高

Chart 6.7 This 30-minute chart shows Handoffs that formed after an AVWAP pinch.
Chart:TC2000.com
As the stock climbed,we would raise the stop up under the successive
higher-lows  represented  by  the  green  arrows.When  the  higher-low(5)is broken  the  stop  is  triggered(represented  by  a  red  dot).
At(6),the  stock  continued  down  through  the  green  AVWAP  from(2)and
below the red AVWAP from(1).A buy at either of those two AVWAPs would   have  resulted  in  near-term  losses.A  purchase  near  the  green   dot(7)would have been in a profitable position right from the start.As it showed the
near-term  strength,we  can  anchor  a  new  Handoff point  and  purchase  the stock.
You may notice the purchase(7)is  almost  identical  to the prior  exit  and wonder what the point of making two trades was.If the  stock was
purchased(3)and  held  through  the  selloff(6),the  trade  would  have temporarily   gone   negative.
Notice  that  the  price  dropped  from$105(A)to  $87(B)on  this  selloff.This
was  a   severe  drop.The  original  purchase  was  near$88(3)and  the  exit
would have been  at$95,a  gain  of 7 points,orjust under  10%.The  peace  of
mind that comes from taking a profit before the stock drops significantly is    reason enough to be out of the stock.There was no assurance that the stock would recover and turn higher.Locking in the gain was the smart thing to    do.
The purchase(7)put you back  into  the  stock  when  the  momentum  was
positive.Every  swing  trader  wants  to be  in  stocks  with  strong  trends,lock in  gains when  the momentum  slows  or  reverses,and  avoid  the  negative
periods.
图表6.7这个30分钟图表显示了在AVWAP 挤压后形成的转手。图表：
TC2000.com
随着股价上涨，我们会将止损位提高到由绿色箭头表示的连续更低
高点。当更低高点(5)被突破时，止损位被触发(由红色圆点表示)。
在(6)处，股价继续下跌穿过(2)处的绿色AVWAP,    并低于(1) 处的红色AVWAP 。 在任意一个AVWAP 处买入都会导致短期亏损。
在绿色圆点(7)附近买入将从一开始就处于盈利位置。随着短期强 度的显现，我们可以锚定一个新的Handoff   点并买入该股票。
您可能会注意到买入(7)几乎与之前的退出完全相同，并想知道进行两  次交易的意义何在。如果股票在(3)处买入并在(6)处的抛售中持有， 交易将暂时变为负数。
请注意，在该抛售中，价格从$105 (A)   降至$87 (B) 。 这是一个严重的下 跌。原始买入价格在$88(3)附近，退出价格将是$95,盈利7点，或接近  10%。在股价大幅下跌之前获利了结所带来的安心感本身就足以让您离场。 没有保证该股票会恢复并上涨。锁定收益是明智之举。
这次买入(7)让你在势头正好的时候重新回到了股票中。每一个波 段交易者都希望在趋势强劲的股票中持仓，在势头减缓或反转时锁 定利润，并避免负面的时期。
Notice how the next pullback from(7)found buyers right along the first
Handoff(8).Once the stock continued back up through $100,we created a
new AVWAP Handoff(8)and that AVWAP continued to hold up to the end of the  chart.
The green arrows represent the higher-lows under which we can raise our stop levels from the purchase(7).At the end of this chart,the stop would
have been  at  approximately$111,from  the  purchase near$94.
legram:
注意看，从(7)开始的下一个回调正好在第一个Handoff(8) 沿线找 到了买家。一旦股票继续回升超过$100,我们就创建了一个新的
AVWAP        Handoff(8), 并且那个AVWAP 持续支撑到图表的末尾。
绿色箭头表示我们可以在购买(7)时将止损位提高的高低价位。在这张 图表的末尾，止损位将大约在111美元，从接近94美元的购买点开始。
Telegram:@Group
KEY TAKEAWAYS·It is normal for the rate of change in a trend to slow down and speed up.·We set new anchor points from the levels buyers and sellers become more aggressive.·Multiple Handoffs look like “layers”as the point of control changes with renewed momentum.·AVWAP Handoffs can be used to trade more accurately on all timeframes.·A  Handoff  level  can  often  become  the   anchor  point   of  a new  Pinch  in  a  trend.
KEY TAKEAWAYS
·It is normal for the rate of change in a trend to slow down and speed up.
·We set new anchor points from the levels buyers and sellers become more aggressive.
·Multiple Handoffs look like “layers”as the point of control changes with renewed momentum.
·AVWAP Handoffs can be used to trade more accurately on all timeframes.
·A  Handoff  level  can  often  become  the   anchor  point   of  a new  Pinch  in  a  trend.
关键要点趋势的变化率正常情况下会放缓和加速。我们从买卖双方变得更加激进的级别设置新的锚点。多次转手看起来像“层”,因为控制点随着新的势 头而变化。AVWAP 转手可用于在所有时间框架上更准确地交易。一个交接级别通常可以成为趋势中一个新的捏合的锚点。
关键要点
趋势的变化率正常情况下会放缓和加速。
我们从买卖双方变得更加激进的级别设置新的锚点。
多次转手看起来像“层”,因为控制点随着新的势 头而变化。
AVWAP 转手可用于在所有时间框架上更准确地交易。
一个交接级别通常可以成为趋势中一个新的捏合的锚点。
CHAPTER 7
BUY PULLBACKS
AND BREAKOUTS?
“Whenever  you  find  yourself  on  the  side of  the  majority,it  is  time  to  pause   and
reflect.”
—Mark Twain
Chapter      Objectives
1.Recognize a Pullback
2.Recognize a Breakout
3.Don't buy the dip,buy strength after the dip
4.Know the difference between a dip and a downtrend
5.Don't short the rip,short weakness after the rip
6.Understand why some breakouts fail
7.How to manage risk
第七章
买入回调和突破?
“当你发现自己站在多数人一边时，就 是停下来反思的时候了。”
—马克 · 吐温
章 节 目 标
识别回撤■识别突破不要抄底，在回调后买入 力量了解回调和下跌趋势的区别■不要追涨，在回 调后做空弱势了解为什么有些突破会失败如何管理
风险 
W
ith an understanding of how a trend's rate of movement changes,we can now examine two popular strategies,buying a Breakout and buying a
Pullback.A couple of simple adjustments to the general Pullback and
Breakout trade strategies will make these strategies much more profitable. Of course,the improvements to these strategies come from the addition of   AVWAP analysis.
Pullbacks
The nature of markets is that they experience a directional thrust and then either consolidate sideways through time,meaning that the price stabilizes and stays within a somewhat narrow range,or they experience some short- term profit taking,which creates a "Pullback."APullback is also often
referred to as a "dip."One of the basic foundations oftechnical analysis is  that a trend,once established,is more likely to continue than reverse.Because of this fundamental rule,it's important to study Pullbacks carefully.
After any period of frenzied trading,calmer heads need to prevail.Recall  what we learned in Part Two,Chapter Two about Support &Resistance一 each is only identified with certainty in hindsight.Pullbacks are akin to
this.We give a Pullback the benefit of the doubt and prepare a purchase, but if it continues to decline in price,we do not participate.The
reemergence of trend on the shorter timeframe is our opportunity to take part in a low-risk,high-probability trend continuation trade.This is the
basis of trend alignment.
When the trend on the longer timeframe is still intact,we should treat Pullbacks as "innocent until proven guilty."However,ifthe Pullback
continues to a point where the longer timeframe no longer exhibits a    pattern of higher-highs andhigher-lows,we  should abandon the  setup until it aligns on multiple timeframes.
了解趋势运动速度的变化，我们可以Wow  检查两种流行的策略， 买入突破和买入回撤。对一般的回撤和突破交易策略进行一些简单的调
整，会使这些策略更有利可图。当然，这些策略的改进来自于 AVWAP   分析的添加。
回调
市场的本质是它们会经历一个方向性的推动，然后要么通过时间横向  整理，这意味着价格稳定并保持在相对狭窄的范围内，要么经历一些   短期获利回吐，这会形成一个“回调”。回调也经常被称为“回调”。 技术分析的一个基本基础是，一旦趋势确立，它更有可能继续而不是   反转。由于这个基本规则，仔细研究回调■非常重要：
在任何疯狂交易之后，冷静的头脑需要占上风。回想我们在第二部 分第二章学到的关于支撑位和阻力位的内容——每一个都只有在事 后才能被确定地识别出来。回调与此类似。我们对回调持谨慎态度 并准备买入，但如果价格继续下跌，我们不参与。在较短的时间框 架上重新出现的趋势是我们参与低风险、高概率趋势延续交易的机 会。这是趋势一致性的基础。
当较长时间周期上的趋势仍然完好时，我们应该将回调视为“无 罪，直到被证明有罪”。然而，如果回调持续到较长时间周期不 再显示出更高高点和高低点的模式时，我们应该放弃该设置，直 到它在多个时间周期上对齐。
Don't Buy the Dip
We often hear "buy the dip"as a strategy to purchase a stock.This refers to the desire to buy a stock that is in a longer-term uptrend,as it experiences  a near-term price correction(a Pullback).It makes sense to want to buy the dip.We want to pay less than the recent high.Trading activity corrects the  strong momentum,then pauses,and can then either turn back higher or
fail.The possibility of trend failure is why we do not blindly buy on a Pullback.
Buy Strength After the Dip
Instead,we want to anticipate what is most likely to happen next to the
stock and create our trade plan as it's price drops to a level of interest.We wait for price momentum to confirm that the selling has subsided.Then,
when buyers regain control of the  short-term trend,we take partin the
emergent strength,i.e.,the price movement upward.This is the essence of trend  alignment.
We want to buy as the stock moves back up above the AVWAP from the
prior high.It tells us with absolute certainty that buyers have taken back    control from the prior high point.We do not have to guess.When the price  is above the AVWAP from the recent peak,it means the average buyer from that point is now in a profitable trade.Also,the average short seller will be in a position of weakness as their average sale price is below the current
level.There is no technical tool better than AVWAP to identify the transition of power from buyers to sellers and sellers to buyers.
Let others pave the way and create a near term level of Support before you purchase strength after a Pullback.Imagine you are at the beach and there is a group of people standing on top ofa cliff peering over the water,
tentatively deciding whether tojump into the refreshing water 40 feet
不要买入谷底
我们经常听到“买入回调”作为一种购买股票的策略。这指的是希望 在较长周期上涨趋势中，股票经历短期价格修正(回调)时买入。想 要买入回调是合理的。我们希望以低于近期高点的价格买入。交易活 动会修正强劲的动能，然后暂停，然后可能反转上涨或失败。趋势失 败的可能性是我们不盲目在回调时买入的原因。
在谷底后买入强势
相反，我们想要预测股票接下来最可能发生的情况，并在其价格下降  到感兴趣的水平时创建我们的交易计划。我们等待价格动量确认卖盘  已经减弱。然后，当买家重新控制短期趋势时，我们参与新兴的强势， 即价格上涨的走势。这就是趋势一致性的本质。
我们希望在股票从先前高点回升并超过AVWAP  时买入。它告诉我 们买家已经从先前高点夺回控制权，我们不必猜测。当价格高于近 期峰值的AVWAP   时，这意味着从那个点开始，平均买家现在处于 盈利交易中。此外，平均空头卖家将处于弱势地位，因为他们的平 均卖出价格低于当前水平。没有比AVWAP   更好的技术工具来识别 买家到卖家的权力转移和卖家到买家的权力转移。
让其他人铺路，在您购买回调后的力量之前，先创建一个近期的支持 水平。想象您在海滩上，有一群人站在悬崖顶上俯瞰着水面，犹豫着 是否要跳入清凉的水中40英尺
below.No one has jumped from this cliff before.As a thrill seeker,it might
tempt you tojump,but do you want to be the first to make the leap?What if there is a rockjust below the surface that you cannot see?Of course,no one shouldjump if it is unsafe,but if you are going to go,don't you want to make sure that no one gets hurt before you do?Let others take the big risk.Use a  smarter approach to risks in the markets and in life.
Chart 7.1 shows why we do not blindly buy a dip in an uptrend.There were  three dips in this stocks strong uptrend.The first dip(1)saw the stock drop from$29.20  to  $22.60(a  22.6%drop)in  3  hours.Imagine  how  you  would  feel ifyou bought the "Pullback,"such as when the stock was $28,$27,$26,$25   and the stock continued down to $22.
The second dip(2)saw a smaller decline from$29.50 to $26.77,“just”9.3% in an hour and a half.

Chart  7.130-minute  intervals  with  “dips”in  red  and  proper  buy  points  in  green.Chart:
TC2000.com
The  third“dip”(3)saw  the  stock  drop  close  to  50%injust  six  days.If  instead of buying  on  weakness,you  waited  until  the  stock  got  back  above  the
AVWAP  from  the  prior  peak(one  of  the  green  dots),you  would  have  made your  purchase  when  buyers   controlled   the   trend.
Notice  there   is  no   “green  dot”after  the  peak   at$34.The   stock  never   got
back  above  the  red  AVWAP  from  that  peak,so  no  purchase  would  occur.
Rather  than  give  into   emotional  thoughts   like  “it's  down  too  much,”a
disciplined  approach  would  have  kept  a  buyer  from  buying  as  it  declined
from$34  all  the  way  down  to  $17  and  taking  a  large  loss.You  will  never  buy at  the  low  when  you  buy  on  strength,but  you  will  avoid  unnecessary  losses and you will have  a  logical place to  set  your  stop.
Not all“dips”end up being a simple Pullback.They can represent trend failure,which is why we wait to buy strength after the dip.
Do Not Buy Stocks in Downtrends
As  we  see  in  the  Chart  7.2,when  the  50-DMA  is  sloped  lower,the  weakness   is not  a  "dip."It  is  a  stock  in  a  downtrend  and  it  should  not  be  considered  for a  long  position.
Many  people  try  to  buy  a  “dip”in  a  stock  in  a  downtrend.That  is  simply
wrong.It  is  not  a  “dip”purchase  if  the  stock  is  in  a  downtrend.It  is  buying  a stock  that  is  more  likely  to  continue  lower  than  it  is  to  reverse.The
accumulation   process(Stage    1,seen    on    the   market    structure    chart)can    take  months  or  even  years  before  the  stock  is  ready  to  turn  higher  again.
If  they(collective   action   of  buyers   and   sellers)don't   scare   you   out   in   the decline  phase,they  will  wear  you   out  in  the  long   accumulation  process.
图表7.130分钟间隔，红色显示“下跌”,绿色显示合适的买入点。图表：TC2000.com
第三次“回调”(3)中，股价在六天内下跌了接近50%。如果你不 是在弱势时买入，而是等到股价回升到上一个峰顶的AVWAP   (绿色 点之一)之上时再买入，你会在买家掌控趋势时完成购买。
请注意，在34美元的峰顶之后没有“绿色点”。股价从未回升到那个   峰顶的红AVWAP  之上，因此不会发生购买。与其屈服于“下跌太多” 等情绪化想法，自律的方法会让人在股价从34美元下跌到17美元的过   程中保持观望，从而避免重大亏损。在强势时买入你永远不会在低位
买入，但你会避免不必要的亏损，并且会有一个合理的止损位。
并非所有“回调”最终都会成为简单的回调——它们可能代表趋势失 败，这就是为什么我们在回调后等待买入强势的原因。
不要在下跌趋势中买入股票
如图表7.2所示，当50-DMaA  呈下降趋势时，这种弱势并非“回调”。 它是一只处于下跌趋势中的股票，不应考虑作为多头仓位。
许多人试图在下跌趋势中的股票中买入“回调”。这完全错误。如果 股票处于下跌趋势中，那就不算是“回调”买入。这是买入一只更有 可能继续下跌而不是反转的股票。积累过程(阶段1,可在市场结构  图表中看到)可能需要数月甚至数年，直到股票准备好再次上涨。
如果他们在下降阶段(买方和卖方的集体行动)没有把你吓出去，他 们就会在长期的积累过程中让你筋疲力尽。
Don't waste your time and money buying stocks in downtrends,no matter how  low  the  price  is  relative  to  recent  history.Don't  let  FOMO  rule  your
decisions.Wait for buyers to reestablish control before you participate in the trend.

Chart 7.2 Nine months of daily data.In a downtrend,the sum of the declines is greater  than the sum of the rallies.This simple math tells us there is more opportunity to profit
on the short side.Chart:TC2000.com
Many traders give into the temptation to buy a stock in the decline phase, which  is  a  type   of  FOMO.They  see  the   stock  rally   from   a  certain  previous
level  and  cannot   stand  being  on  the   sidelines   as  it  reaches  this  “bargain”
price again.Each little bounce in the downtrend gives them hope the stock has made a low,only to be disappointed when the stock eventually cannot  hold the temporary gains.
不要浪费你的时间和金钱在下跌趋势中购买股票，无论价格相对于 最近的历史有多么低。不要让FOMO  支配你的决策。等待买方重 新建立控制权，然后你才参与这个趋势。
下降50天 移动平均即使你能够在短期低点购买，概率倾向于 趋势-延续更低并 且 那 些 购 买 可 能 会 导 致 亏 损 。464,00 62.00  60.00  58.00  56.0054.00 52.00 50.00 48.00 46.00 44.0042.00 40.0038.00 360323028.00 26.00 24.0022.00 20.00 18.00  16.00  1403

图7.2九个月的每日数据。在下跌趋势中，下跌总和大于上涨总和。这个简单的数学 告诉我们，做空方面有更多盈利机会。图：TC2000.com
许多交易者会屈服于在下跌阶段买入股票的诱惑，这是 一 种
FOMO。 他们看到股票从某个先前水平反弹，并且无法忍受在它再 次达到这个“廉价”价格时袖手旁观。下行趋势中的每 一 次小反弹 都让他们希望股票已经触底，但最终股票无法维持暂时性收益时，
他们会感到失望。
Market  Psychology:Support  &
Resistance In the Rearview Mirror
It is not possible to know if the stock will find Support and turn higher,or if the “dip”will turn into a larger,more serious bout of selling that leads to a   reversal of the primary trend.We  should wait for the odds to be in our favor when we purchase a  stock.
Would you rather guess a low,or buy the stock when we know for fact that buyers have control?A buy above a flat to rising AVWAP gives us certainty that  buyers  are  in  control.When  we  purchase  at  potential  Support  levels
(areas  of interest),the riskis  that the  Support  will  not hold  and  there  is  not always a clear level to set our stops and limit any loss.We never know how  far the price will continue to fall,which makes risk management a guessing game.A more professional approach is to wait for objective levels to form
on  the  chart.
Buy  strength  after  the  dip. We should view a price Pullback to a level of interest  as  a  potential  opportunity  on  the  chart,not  a  place  to  buy  the
stock.This area of interest guides us to look for a shorter timeframe for evidence  that  buyers  have  regained  control.
Don't Short the Rip
Stocks  in  a  downtrend  are just  the  opposite.We  hear  people  say"sell  the
rip”in a stock in a downtrend.The problem is what constitutes enough of a "rip"to  sell  short  and  where  to  set  the  stop  to  protect  against  large  rallies  and resulting  losses?We  examine  this  in  Chart  7.3.
Chart 7.3 shows the danger of selling the stock short too early.Where
would you have shorted the strength of that stock as it rallied?Would you
I    1市场心理：支撑与 阻力在后视镜中
I    1
无法知道股票是否会在找到支撑并转向上涨，或者“回调”会演变成 更大、更严重的抛售，从而导致主要趋势反转。我们在买入股票时， 应该等待机会对我们有利时再行动。
你宁愿猜测一个低点，还是在我们知道买家实际掌控时买入股票?在 平坦到上升的AVWAP   上方买入，能让我们确信买家掌控局面。当我 们以潜在支撑位(兴趣区域)买入时，风险在于支撑位可能不稳固， 而且并不总是有明确的水平来设置止损以限制任何损失。我们永远不 知道价格会继续下跌多远，这使得风险管理变成了一场猜测游戏。更 专业的做法是等待图表上形成客观水平。
在回调后买入强势。我们应该将价格回调到兴趣水平视为图表上的 潜在机会，而不是买入股票的地方。这个兴趣区域引导我们寻找较 短的时间框架，以证明买家已重新掌控局面。
不要做空急跌
处于下跌趋势的股票则恰恰相反。我们听到人们说“卖出急跌”在下跌趋势 中的股票。问题是，什么构成足够大的“急跌”可以做空，以及在哪里设置 止损以防范大幅反弹和由此产生的损失?我们在图表7.3中对此进行了分析。
图表7.3显示了过早卖空股票的危险。在股价上涨时，你会选择在哪个位置 做空该股票的强势?你会
sell  at  11%in  area(1),the  14%rally  in  area(2),or  the   17%rally  in  area(3)?
It is safer to short AFTER the peak and the stock breaks below the AVWAP of those  rallies(red  dots).When  we  short  with  the  downward  momentum  in
our favor,we reduce the price risk because we have a safe place for our
stop(above  the  most  recent   lower-high).This   approach  helps  us   leverage time because we do not have to guess when the sellers have taken back
control.

Breakout Trades
Stocks that Breakout of narrow price ranges can provide some of the most  dynamic price moves.It is wise for traders to look for stocks that are near a Breakout level and then monitor those stocks on shorter timeframes for
在区域(1)以11%的价格卖出，区域(2)的14%上涨，还是区域(3)的17%上涨?
在峰值之后做空更安全，并且当股票跌破这些反弹的AVWAP   (红色   点)时做空。当我们在有利的向下动能时做空，我们减少了价格风险， 因为我们有一个安全的止损位(在最近的较低高点之上)。这种方法  帮助我们利用时间，因为我们不必猜测卖家何时重新掌控局面。

突破交易
突破狭窄价格区间的股票可以提供一些最具动态的价格变动。交易者明智的 做法是寻找接近突破水平的股票，然后在较短的时间框架内监控这些股票以
clues that they might be close to their own respective momentum moves.It is quite satisfying,and profitable,to buy a stock right at the start of a new
trend and hold it for large gains as the trend remains intact.This is the goal of trend trades.
Defining a“Breakout”
There are many versions of a Breakout.Typically,it refers to a move to a
new high in the timeframe we are analyzing the stock.Many of us learned    to buy the Breakout,but what is a Breakout,really?If a stock rallied 10+%in four days,is it a good Breakout?Always remember to answer these two
questions:where it has come from,and where does it have the potential to go?
Don't Paint All Breakouts with the Same Brush
The break past a narrow price range can offer a great opportunity for trend continuation.We can buy those stocks but,as always,with a stop set in case the  trend  reverses.
Many times,I observe people on social media referring to a "Breakout"in a stock that,technically,has already made a higher-high.They don't
understand that the quality of the Breakout is riskier than it might appear. Narrow price ranges produce higher quality Breakouts.Riskier Breakouts    typically emerge after the stock has made a large percentage prior move.It  is a matter of“where has the stock come from?”If it has used a lot of energy to get to the point of Breakout,it will be more difficult to keep risk to a
minimum.
Charts 7.4 and7.5 show different stocks on daily charts,and Breakouts with different  risk  parameters.
寻找它们可能接近各自动量移动的线索。在新的趋势开始时立即买入 股票，并在趋势保持完整时持有以获得大幅盈利，这是非常令人满意 和有利可图的。这就是趋势交易的目标。
定义“突破”
“突破”有很多版本。通常，它指的是我们在分析股票时的时间框架  内向一个新高的移动。我们中的许多人学会了买入突破，但“突破” 到底是什么?如果一只股票在四天内上涨了  %,这是否是一个好的 突破?请始终记住回答这两个问题：它来自哪里，以及它有可能去哪  里?
不要用同一把刷子刷所有的突破
突破狭窄的价格区间可以为趋势提供绝佳的机会
延续。我们可以买入这些股票，但，一如既往地，如果趋势反转，请设置止损。 请设置止损。
很多时候，我观察到社交媒体上的人们提到一只在技术上已经创下更高高点 的股票的“突破”,但他们不明白这种突破的风险比表面看起来要大。窄幅 价格区间会产生更高质量的突破。风险较高的突破通常在股票已经大幅上涨 后出现。这是一个“股票是从哪里来的?”的问题。如果股票已经消耗了大 量能量才能达到突破点，那么控制风险将更加困难。
图表7.4和7.5展示了不同股票的日线图，以及具有不同风险参数的突破。
The stock in Chart 7.4 shows the type of stock we want to buy on a
Breakout.This is a low-risk entry point because it comes from consolidation out of a tight range.The green dot near$72.50 was a good entry because
the  stock  had  spent  little  energy  prior  to  the  Breakout  point.

Chart  7.5  shows  another  stock  with  two   different  purchase  points   in  green   ovals.When  the  stock  crossed  above  the  purple  AVWAP  from  the  prior  high (1),we  knew  that  the  average  long  participant  was  profitable  and  the
average  short  seller  was  in   a  losing  position.This  is  where  buyers  took
control  and  is  the  optimal  place  for  a  low-risk  purchase.We  did  not  know  if the  buyers  would  remain  in  control,so  we  would  set  a  stopjust  below  the
gap   near$27.00(2).As   the   stock   progressed   higher,we   would   raise   the   stop under   the    successive   higher-lows(green    arrows)and   might    have    gotten
stopped   out   near   $29.73(3).
图表7.4中的股票显示了我们在突破时想要买入的股票类型。这是一个低 风险的入场点，因为它来自一个狭窄范围内的盘整。接近72.50美元的
绿色点是一个好的入场点，因为该股票在突破点之前消耗的能量很少。

图7.4绿色点显示这是一个好的入场点，因为它突破了紧密的盘整。图：
TC2000.com
图表7.5显示了另一支股票，其中有两个不同的买入点用绿色椭圆标出。当 该股票从前期高点(1)向上穿越紫色AVWAP 时，我们知道平均多头参与 者是盈利的，而平均空头卖家处于亏损状态。这就是买家掌控市场的位置， 也是进行低风险买入的最佳位置。我们不知道买家是否会继续掌控市场，因 此会在接近27.00美元的缺口附近(2)设置一个止损位。随着股票价格继 续上涨，我们会将止损位设置在连续更高的低点(绿色箭头)下方，并且可 能在29.73美元附近(3)被止损出局。
The second entry(4)shows the "breakout"to the new high.A purchase
there would have been made at$29.75.The Breakout(4)is higher risk
because the stock had already made a large percentage move prior to that entry.Those who purchased on the Breakout(4)arrived late to the trend  compared to the buyers above the purple AVWAP anchored(1).The
difference between these two purchases was a profit of approximately 9% (purchase at 1 to stop at 3)and a breakeven trade(purchase at 4 and stop at  3)
It is often taught that you should place an initial protective stop based on a fixed percentage(3%or 5%)from the entry point.Although better than no- stop strategy,the best approach is to set stops based on the definition of
trend.
When we buy a stock as it breaks past a near-term Resistance level(1)and  the stock is in alignment with the larger timeframe trend,we want to place our stop below "the most recent and relevant higher-low."If it breaks that  low(that is,the price drops below that low),the emergent trend has failed  because  the  definition  ofthe  uptrend(higher-highs  and  higher-lows)no
longer exists.Why would you want to continue to hold that stock?
第二个入场点(4)显示了“突破”到新高的情况。在那里买入的价格为  29.75美元。突破(4)的风险更高，因为该股票在此之前已经做出了较大 的百分比涨幅。与在紫色AVWAP  上方(1)买入的买家相比，在突破
(4)时买入的参与者错过了趋势的早期阶段。这两次买入之间的差异是一 次约9%的利润(在1处买入并在3处止损)和一次盈亏平衡交易(在4  处买入并在3处止损)。
通常被教导应根据固定百分比(3%或5%)从入场点设置初始保护性 止损。尽管比无止损策略更好，但最佳方法是根据趋势的定义设置止 损。
当我们在股价突破短期阻力位(1)时买入，并且股价与较长的时间
周期趋势一致时，我们希望将止损位设置在“最近且最相关的更高低 点”下方。如果股价跌破那个低点(即价格低于那个低点),那么新  兴趋势已经失败，因为上升趋势(更高高点和更高低点)的定义不再  存在。你为什么要继续持有那只股票?

Get the Entry Right
The ability to hold a winning trade is largely a function of where you
enter the stock.Areyou in a position of strength or weakness from the start?
Success    is      often     simply     the     difference    between     a     well-planned     and     executed trade at a strong(analytically supported)entry point,and a weak
(emotionally determined)entry point.And guess what?That really is the  difference between a professionally executed trade versus an amateurish entry.
The number one consideration when you make a purchase is where your stop will go.If you are wrong,you want to be able to limit your loss.The

正确获取入场点
能够持有一个盈利交易很大程度上取决于你何时进入股票。从一开
始你是处于强势还是弱势位置?
成功往往只是精心策划和执行的交易与一个薄弱(由情绪决定)的入场点的区别。猜 猜看?这就是专业执行的交易与业余的入场的真正区别。
当你进行购买时，首要考虑的是你的止损位将设在哪里。如果你判断失误， 你希望能够限制你的损失。 The
closer     the      stop     is     to      your     entry,the      more     shares      you     can      trade,which
magnifies        the        upside        potential.

条  目A 。 红色阴影区域显示了Pullback   买家会寻找购买的地方。众所周知，在下跌过程中买入是 一种猜测游戏。本条目不能保护我们免受可能反转成长期下跌趋势的影响，这可能导致重大损失。
stock as the decline is underway.This entry does not protect us against a potential reversal into a longer-term downtrend,which could result in
large  losses.
Entry   B.The green dots show the ideal point to enter the stock as it
crossed above the AVWAP from the prior peak.This is where we know with certainty the buyers have regained control from the previous high.A
purchase here assures us that momentumis in our favor,and we also have  a logical place for our stop(underneath the pullback low).This is called the “AVWAP Cross Purchase.”
Entry   C.Is the traditional "Breakout"buy as the price makes a new high.
As you can see,the Breakout points come much later than the AVWAP Cross Purchase buyers.As an example,the first AVWAP Cross Purchase was at
$6.50 versus the breakout buy of$7.74.Not only was the AVWAP Cross
Purchase $1.24,or 19%,lower than the Breakout buy,the stop could have been  tighter(less  cents  per  share)than  the  breakout  purchase.
Study the other purchase areas at the green dots,to compare the
advantage ofthe AVWAP Cross Purchase to the other entry(Pullback and Breakout)techniques.
Advantage ofthe AVWAP Entry versus Shorting Rips
and Breakdowns
Chart 7.7 labels five different moves.In each of these five rallies(rips),    there are several choices where to enter a short position.We review the pros and cons of each of three different entry techniques below.
The red highlighted areas(A)show counter-trend rallies in the overall downtrends.The green dots(B)show short sale points where the price
在下跌过程中，将股票视为买入是不明智的。本条目不能保护我们 免受可能反转成长期下跌趋势的影响，这可能导致重大损失。
条目 B。绿色点显示了股票在越过先前的峰值上方AVWAP   时进入  的理想点。这就是我们确定买家从先前高点重新获得控制的点。在这 里购买可以确保势头在我们这边，我们还为我们的止损提供了一个合 理的位置(在回调低点下方)。这被称为“AVWAP   跨越购买。”
条 目C 。传统的“突破”购买，当价格创下新高时。如您所见，突破 点比AVWAP 跨越购买买家出现得晚得多。例如，第一个AV
WAP  跨越购买是在6.50美元，而突破购买是7.74美元。AV
WAP 跨越购买不仅比突破购买低1.24美元，或19%,止损也可以更 紧(每股分摊的几分钱更少) 。  
研究绿色点处的其他购买区域，以比较AVWAP  跨越购买与其他入场 (回调和突破)技术的优势。
AVWAP 入场相对于做空 Rips  和 Breakdowns     的优 势
图7.7标注了五种不同的移动。在这五种反弹 (rips)   中，每个都有几个 选择做空的位置。我们将在下文回顾每种三种不同入场技术的利弊。
红色高亮区域(A) 显示了整体下跌中的逆势反弹。绿色点(B) 显示了价格
crossedbelow the relevant AVWAP,and the labels(C)show traditional
short  sale breakdown(to new  lows)sales.
Entry   A.The red shaded areas show where a short seller on a rally(rip) would look to enter a short position.As we know,it is a guessing game to short the high in the stock as the rally is underway.This entry does not
protect us against a potential reversal higher,which could result in large losses.

Entry   B.The green dots show the ideal point to enter the stockas it
crossed down below the AVWAP from the prior low.This is where we know with certainty the sellers have regained control from the previous low.A
short sale here assures us that momentum is in our favor,and we also have a logical place for our stop(above the rally high).This is called the “AVWAP Cross Short Sale.”
低于相关AVWAP  的交叉点，并且标签(C)显示了传统的卖空分解 ( 降 至 新 低 ) 销 售 。
条目A。红色阴影区域显示了在反弹 (rip)    中做空者可以进入空头 头寸的位置。众所周知，在反弹过程中做空股票是一场猜测游戏。
这个条目不能保护我们免受潜在的更高反转，这可能导致重大损失。

图7.7概述了三种不同的卖空入场技术 (A、B、C)。图：TC2000.com
条目 B。绿色点显示了股票在跌破先前低点的AVWAP   时进入的理  想点位。这是我们知道卖方从先前低点重新获得控制权的确定位置。 在此处做空确保动量有利于我们，并且我们还有一个合理的止损位  (在反弹高点之上)。这被称为“AVWAP   跌破做空”。
Entry  C.Is the traditional"Breakdown"short sale as the price makes a
new  low.As  you  can   see,the  Breakdown  points  come  much  later  than  the    AVWAP  Cross  sellers.As  an  example,the  first  AVWAP  Cross  Short  Sale  was at$160.50  versus  the  Breakdown  sale  of$140.45.Not  only  was  the  AVWAP   Cross  Short  Sale  $20.05,or   14.3%,higher  than  the  Breakdown  sale,but  the   stop   could   have   been   tighter(less   cents   per   share)than   the   Breakdown
short.
Study  the  other  short  sale  areas  at  the  green  dots,to  compare  the
advantage  of  the  AVWAP  Cross  Short  Sale  to  the  other  entry  techniques.
Market  Psychology:Why  Breakouts and Breakdowns Fail
Breakouts:As we know,the markets discount the past and anticipate what is  to  come.Large   stockholders  who   accumulate  stock  at  lower  prices  often   sell a portion of their stock on the Breakout ifthe stock experienced a run- up prior to the break higher.
Breakdowns:In  a  downtrend,short  sellers  will  cover  a  portion  of  their
bearish  bets  when  the  stock  breaks  to  a  new  low  when  the  stock  already experienced  a  large  move  lower  in  the  days  prior  to  the  Breakdown.
There is a phrase “sell(or cover)when you can,not when you have to.” Smart  money  holders  take  advantage  of  the  liquidity  provided  by  the
Breakout  chasers(people  who  buy  when  a  stock  makes  a  new  short-term high after a large percentage move)and take profits on a portion of their position.This increased selling activity can result in the failure of a
Breakout in the near-term.
条 目C。 传统的“跌破”做空，当价格创下新低时。如您所见，跌 破点出现的时间远晚于AVWAP   跌破做空。例如，第一个
AVWAP跌破做空发生在160.50美元，而跌破卖发生在140.45美 元。不仅AVWAP   跌破做空比跌破卖高20 . 05美元，即14 . 3%,而 且止损位可以更紧(每股分摊的几分钱更少)。
研究绿色圆点处的其他短期卖空区域，以比较AVWAP   交叉短期卖空与 其他入场技术的优势。
市场心理：为什么突破和跌破会失败
突破：众所周知，市场会折现过去并预期未来。在股价上涨前以较 低价格积累股票的大股东，如果股价在突破前已经大幅上涨，通常 会在突破时卖出部分股票。
跌破：在下跌趋势中，当股价跌破前期已经大幅下跌的新低时， 空头卖家会平掉部分看跌仓位。
有一个短语“在可以的时候卖出(或平仓),而不是在必须的时候。”聪明的资  金持有者利用Breakout 追逐者(在股票经历大幅百分比上涨后创出短期新高时买 入的人)提供的流动性，并在其部分头寸上获利。这种增加的卖出活动可能导致  短期内Breakout 失败。
Be careful not to chase Breakouts;make the smarter entry when price
crosses the key AVWAP so you can be in ahead of the crowd and with less risk.
When you are involved in the stock before the crowd,it is a good idea to
cash out a portion of your position as the Breakout occurs.We want to trim  a portion of the trade on strength and trail our stop with or in the direction of trend(raise it up under the new higher-lows).This is where you may
have heard the phrase “trim and trail.”
Risk Management
Our constant focus on where a stock has come from prior to ourentry helps us determine whether a Breakout trade is consideredlow-or high-risk.Ifa  stock had a strong move prior to a Breakout,it is less likely it will continue. We compensate for the higher risk with smaller trade size.
When we initiate our trade at the onset of fresh momentum.This puts the  stock in alignment with the longer,more powerful trend and we avoid the   risk of time(waiting for the move to happen).We also minimize the price    risk and avoid unnecessary initial losses as the stock is in corrective mode.
小心不要追逐Breakout;      当价格跨越关键的AVWAP 时，做出更 明智的入场，这样你就可以领先于人群并且风险更小。
在众人之前参与股票时，当突破发生时，将部分仓位获利了结是一个 好主意。我们希望在强势时削减部分仓位，并随趋势方向移动止损位 (在新形成的更高低点上方提高止损位)。这就是你可能听到“削减 并跟踪”这个短语的地方。
风险管理
我们对股票在我们入场之前从何而来的持续关注，帮助我们确定突破交 易是低风险还是高风险。如果一只股票在突破之前有强劲的走势，它继 续上涨的可能性就较小。我们通过较小的交易规模来弥补更高的风险。
当我们在新动力的初期启动我们的交易时。这使得股票与更长时间、更强大 的趋势保持一致，并且我们避免了时间风险(等待行情发生)。我们还最小 化了价格风险，并避免了不必要的初始亏损，因为股票处于修正模式。
KEY TAKEAWAYS·When  we  “buy  the  dip”we  are  in  an  immediate  position of weakness because we are not sure if the buyers willquickly regain  control.Wait  for the upward  momentum   on the  shorter timeframe before making  a purchase.This puts you in an initial position of strength.·Buy   strength   after   the   dip.·There is no technical tool better than AVWAP to identify  the transition of power from buyers to sellers and sellers to  buyers.·Avoid the mentality that you  are  buying  a  bargain when the stock is in a downtrend,stocks in downtrends are“guilty until proven  innocent.”·If we “short the rip”we never know if the momentumwill continue higher and cause large losses.It is better to wait for the stock to continue lower on the shortertimeframe before we consider a short sale.·Always  remember  to  answer  these  two  questions:whereit has come from,and where does it have the potential to
KEY TAKEAWAYS
·When  we  “buy  the  dip”we  are  in  an  immediate  position of weakness because we are not sure if the buyers will
quickly regain  control.Wait  for the upward  momentum   on the  shorter timeframe before making  a purchase.This puts you in an initial position of strength.
·Buy   strength   after   the   dip.
·There is no technical tool better than AVWAP to identify  the transition of power from buyers to sellers and sellers to  buyers.
·Avoid the mentality that you  are  buying  a  bargain when the stock is in a downtrend,stocks in downtrends are
“guilty until proven  innocent.”
·If we “short the rip”we never know if the momentum
will continue higher and cause large losses.It is better to wait for the stock to continue lower on the shorter
timeframe before we consider a short sale.
·Always  remember  to  answer  these  two  questions:where
it has come from,and where does it have the potential to
关键要点当我们“买入回调”时，我们处于一个弱势位置，因为 我们不确定买家是否会迅速重新掌控局面。在较短的周 期上等待上涨动力出现后再进行购买。这让你处于一个 初始的强势位置。· 在回调后买入。没有比AVWAP   更好的技术工具来识别买方到卖方的权力转移和卖方到买方的权力转移。避免在股票处于下跌趋势时认为自己买到了便宜货， 处于下跌趋势的股票是“有罪直到被证明无罪。”如果我们“做空快速上涨”我们永远不知道势头是否将 继续走高并造成重大损失。最好等待股票在较短的时间 框架内继续下跌，然后再考虑做空。始终记得回答这两个问题：它来自哪里，以及它有什么潜力

没有比AVWAP   更好的技术工具来识别买方到卖方的权
力转移和卖方到买方的权力转移。

go?·The ability to hold a winning trade is largely a function of where you enter the stock.Are you in a position of    strength or weakness from the start?·   Not all breakouts and breakdowns are the same.Consider how the stock got to the trigger(where has it comefrom?)before you decide to get involved.· The lowest risk entries occur when the short-term trend first  comes  into  alignment with the  longer-term trend. CHAPTER 8
MULTI-DAY AVWAPS FOR SHORTER-TERM
TRADERS
"Follow the evidence wherever it leads,
and question everything.”
—Neil  deGrasse  Tyson
Chapter Objectives
1.Understand  fresh  momentum  trend  dynamics
2.Identify  low-riskentries  into  the  second-and  third-day  price moves(up or down)
3.Avoid costly FOMO purchases and short sales
4.How to gain an edge on “red to green”buyers
5.How to  gain  an  edge  on“green  to red”sellers
第8章
多日AVWAPS 用于短期
交易者
“遵循证据，无论它引向何方，
并质疑一切。”
—尼尔 ·德格拉斯·泰森
章节目标
1.理解新鲜动量趋势动态
2. 识别进入第二天和第三天价格 行情(上涨或下跌)的低风险入场点
3.避免代价高昂的FQMO  购买和卖空
4. 如何在与“红转绿”买家竞争中占据优势
5. 如何在与“绿转红”卖家竞争中占据优势
here are many instances when a stock makes a significant move,but you
I   didn't see it in time to get involved on the first day ofthe momentum.If the stock experiences a fresh breakout after the first day,and looks like it
may have room to continue further,it is not too late to participate.Even
though I have seen the second-day strategy that we will learn about in this chapter play out thousands oftimes,it still amazes me how a prior day
AVWAP is often the exact turning point for a stock.
The day after a stock makes a significant move can provide a low-risk,high- probability entry for those who watch the action closely the next morning.   In this chapter we'll learn from examples on intraday timeframes of
roughly five days.Don't confuse the following information as applicable only to day traders.The principles used to find good entry points can be used for better timed purchases by longer-term participants as well.
When YourThink You Missed a Move Day One:Why the Stock Moved
Don't get hung up trying to figure out the reasons behind the initial move. We're looking at price action.It may be a company reported earnings
significantly different than analysts expected,a true “earnings surprise.” Surprise;in earnings news,general news,or from other sources can be
thought of as a catalyst for price change that disrupts the balance of supply and demand.For example,if the  surprise was good,earnings were higher
than expected,many institutions will now want to buy a meaningful
position.All this new demand needs to be filled,so the stock surges higher.
On the day of the earnings report,they buy as much as they can,often
aggressively,and the stock closes at or near the high of the day. When the stock closes near the high of the day,it may be short-term extended
这里有很多股票出现重大波动但你在第一时间没有看到参与动量 的情况。如果股票在第一天之后出现新的突破，并且看起来还有继续 上涨的空间，那么参与还为时不晚。尽管我已经见过数千次我们将在  本章学习的第二天策略的实施情况，但前一天AVWAP 仍然是股票经 常出现转折点的精确时刻，这仍然让我感到惊讶。
股票出现重大波动后的第二天可以提供低风险、高概率的入场机会， 对于那些第二天早上密切关注市场动态的人来说。在本章中，我们将 通过大约五天的日内时间框架的例子来学习。不要将以下信息误解为 仅适用于日内交易者。用于寻找良好入场点的原则也可以被长期参与 者用于更好地把握购买时机。
你以为错过了什么:一次波动
第一天：为什么股票会波动
不要纠结于试图弄清楚最初行动的原因。我们关注的是价格行为。这 可能是一家公司公布的业绩与分析师预期差异很大，一个真正的“业 绩惊喜”。惊喜；在业绩新闻、一般新闻或来自其他来源的惊喜，可 以被视为一个导致供需平衡被打破的价格变化催化剂。例如，如果惊 喜是好的，业绩高于预期，许多机构现在将想要买入一个有意义的头 寸。所有这些新的需求都需要得到满足，因此股票会飙升。
在盈利报告发布当天，他们会尽可能多地买入，通常非常激进，并且  股票收盘价达到或接近当日最高价。当股票收盘价接近当日最高价时， 可能是短期过度延伸
(used up too much buy power in the short-term)and in need of a slight
pullback(profit   taking)the   next   morning.
Day Two:Upside Price Action Follow-Through
There are three main players driving the market on day two:profit takers, short  sellers,and  market  makers.
Profit  takers   making the best of the large move seek to capture profit on   some or all oftheir long position by selling some stock at or near the high at the  open.
Short   sellers   who do not believe the stock can follow through on
downward momentum and,sell accordingly.Their sales add downward pressure at the open of the second day.
Market      makerswho need to purchase many shares on behalfof their
clients may try to scare some supply loose by offering the stock lower than   the previous day's close.For example,the market maker may have an order to buy 500,000 shares of the stock that day.Tofill that order and get the
best price possible for the customer,he may short some stock in the pre-   market or right at the open.This initial selling gives the illusion the stock is weak and scares some long holders into selling stock to them at lower
prices early in the day.The long holders would be doing this to capture some of their profits or cut losses.
The market maker's goal is to buy more shares at a lower price than they sold short the initial shares.If they sold short 10,000 shares,but could
purchase 50,000 shares at a lower price than the previous day's close,this would leave them with a net long position of 40,000 shares at prices that    are likely to be near the low of the day.Of course,this is a risky game for
(短期内用尽了太多的买入力量)并且在第二天需要小幅回调(获 利了结)。
第二天：向上价格行动的延续
在第二天，有三个主要因素在推动市场：获利了结者、做空者和做市商。
获利了结者利用大幅波动，试图通过在开盘时以或接近高价卖出部分 股票，来获利了结部分或全部多头头寸。
做空者不认为股票能延续下跌势头，并相应地卖出。他们的销售 在第二天开盘时增加了下行压力。
需要代表客户购买大量股票的做市商可能会试图通过以低于前一天收 盘价的价格提供股票来吓唬一些供应松动。例如，做市商当天可能有 一个购买50万股该股票的订单。为了完成该订单并为客户获得最佳价 格，他可能在盘前或开盘时做空一些股票。这种初步的卖出会给人们 一种股票疲软的错觉，并吓唬一些多头持有者在当天早期以较低价格 向他们卖出股票。多头持有者会这样做是为了获利了结部分利润或止 损。
做市商的目标是以低于他们做空初始股票的价格买入更多股票。如 果他们做空了10,000股，但可以以低于前一天收盘价的价格购买
50,000股，这将让他们在价格可能接近当日低点的位置上持有 40,000股的净多头头寸。当然，这对他们来说是一场冒险。
them.They might end up selling too many shares at a low price and hurt their average execution price at the end of the day.
How to Take Advantage of Price Action (Day Two and
Beyond)
Our opportunity  comes  in the morning  of the  second,or  even  a  subsequent day for even the third or fourth day.If the stock opens lower than the
previous day's close,we want to be ready to purchase the  stock under these conditions:
1.If the stock can hold above the prior day VWAP,see charts on the
next page,it shows buyers still have control from the start of the day the  move  began.
2.After  the  early  morning  weakness,the  stock  stabilizes  above  the  2-
day AVWAP and climbs above the daily VWAP.This tells us the
buyers have regained control of the trend for the new day and it is their  game  to  lose.
Here are the actions to take:
1.We purchase the stock as it climbs back above the daily VWAP and place our stop below the low
2.If our  stop  does not trigger,we hold the  stock  as it increases  and
raise  our  stop  to  under  the  “most  recent  and  relevant  higher-low” fo  the  timeframe  we  intendto  hold  the  trade.
Short-term entry tactics described above can be used to establish a position in the stock which might be held for a day trade,or even a longer-term
trade   or  investment.The  more  accurate  the  entry,regardless  of  the
他们可能会以低价卖掉太多股票，从而损害他们当日的平均成交价。
如何利用价格行动(第二天及以后)
我们的机会出现在第二天早上，甚至对于第三天或第四天也是如此。 如果股票开盘价低于前一天的收盘价，我们希望在以下条件下准备购 买股票：
1.如果股票能够维持在先前一天VWAP  以上，参见下一页的图表， 这表明买方从当天开始运动时仍然掌控着局面。
2.在早上的弱势之后，股票在2天AVWAP   以上稳定，并 攀升至每日VWAP  以上。这表明买方重新掌控了新天的趋 势，这是他们的游戏，他们输不起。
以下是采取的行动：
1.当股票回升至每日VWAP  以上时，我们购买股票，并将止损位设在 其下方。
2.如果我们的止损没有触发，我们持有股票等待其上涨，并将止损位 提高到我们打算持有交易的“最近且相关的高点”之下。
上述短期入场策略可用于在股票中建立仓位，该仓位可能持有进行日内交易， 甚至更长期的交易或投资。无论计划的持有时间如何，入场越准确，你越有能 力设置更紧的止损位，并且越有更多时间在有利动量的情况下操作。
planned  hold  time,the  more  ability  you  have  to  set  tighter  stops  and  the more  time  you  have  with  momentum  in  your  favor.
Chart 8.1 provides our first example of a stock with a strong move on day
one that gave a low-risk buy opportunity on day two.The blue VWAP begins on day one and continues to be the second day AVWAP the next morning.
On the first minute of day two,the purple VWAP starts.It is the “2nd-day   AVWAP.”Keep in mind the prior day AVWAP doesn't reflect a full two days until the close of the second day.
In the chart 8.1 below,you can see this stock opened on a gap higher near $73.50(1)on  the  first  day.After  a  little  uncertainty  in  the  first  ninety
minutes,the  buyers  quickly  established  dominance  by  holding  above  the VWAP.
We know the buyers had control because the price stayed above VWAP on a testjust after noon(A)and the  slope of the VWAP rose  at that  same time.
The stock then closed near the high of the day at approximately $73.75(3).
计划的持有时间越长，你越有能力设置更紧的止损位，并且越有 更多时间在有利动量的情况下操作。
图表8.1提供了第一个股票的例子，该股票在第一天有强劲的走势，并在第  二天给出了低风险的买入机会。蓝色的VWAP  在第一天开始，并继续到第二 天成为上午的AVWAP。
在第二天的第一分钟，紫色的VWAP 开始。它是“第二天AVWAP” 。 请记住，前一天的AVWAP 直到第二天收盘时才反映完整两天的数据。
在下面的图表8.1中，你可以看到这只股票在第一天以接近73.50美元的跳空高开 开盘(1)。在第一小时九十分钟的一点点不确定性之后，买家通过保持在VWAP
上方迅速确立了主导地位。
我们知道买家。因为价格在中午刚过的一个测试中保持在VWAP之上 (A),     并且VWAP的斜率在同一时间上升。然后股票收盘于当天的最高价附近，约 为73.75美元(3)。

图8.1该图表展示了为期两天的股票走势，使用2分钟蜡烛图。插入部分显示了第二 天开头的1分钟蜡烛图，以提供更详细的视图。图表：TC2000.com
第二天，股票开盘时接近0.50美元的低价(4),因为早期的卖家过早地卖   出(在股票有机会显示卖家是否有动量之前)。精明的参与者从一开始就准   备好在VWAP 处购买股票。你可以看到，在蓝色的前一天AVWAP 和反弹上， 这不是一个完美的接触(4),但买家一直在等待那个区域，因为股票在价   格再次交叉到两个VWAP 之上时徘徊在该水平附近。
初始波动率帮助了那些试图在初始“折扣”时尽可能多地收购股票的市场做 市商，这个“折扣”来自前一天
close.After  a  couple  of  minutes,it  became  apparent  there  were  aggressive buyers waiting at that level.The stock quickly erased the initial down gap,  then closed higher by almost one dollar.
If you pay close attention to the stock on the morning of day two,you want to buy if the second-day AVWAP is still rising,and(5)the stock is back
above  the  new  day's(purple)VWAP,at  the  green  dot
A good way to confirm that buyers have regained control on day two is if the day two VWAP is now rising.This may happen as soon as the first three to    five minutes of the new day,so you need to pay close attention.
Ifyou  purchase  the  stock  when  both  days'VWAPs  are  rising,the
momentum  is  in  your  favor.Once  you  have  purchased  the  stock(5),the
stop can go below the low of the morning(4).If that low breaks,it would
mean sellers took control from the start of the move and there would be no reason to  continue to hold the  stock.
In Chart 8.1,buyers who waited for the stock to turn positive before
purchasing  it  paid  approximately   $0.40  higher(6)than  those  who  bought the stock as it crossed above the daily VWAP(5).If buyers(6)used a stop
below the morning low,they would not have been able to buy as many
shares(based  on  the use  of  1R-Multiple  of risk)as  those  who  purchased  at the lower price when the stock reclaimed the VWAP for the day(5).
Buy Red to Green?
Many market participants like to purchase at the point stocks go from
negative  on  the  day(red)to  positive  on  the  day(green).When  a  stock  is  in   a negative position compared to the prior day's close,it is  "red”and when  it is in a positive position compared to the prior day's close it is “green.”
的收盘价。几分钟后，很明显在该价位有积极的买家在等待。股票 迅速抹去了最初的向下跳空缺口，然后几乎上涨了一美元后收高。
如果你仔细关注第二天早上的股票，如果你想要买入，当第二天的
AVWAP仍在上涨，并且(5)股票回到高于新一天(紫色)VWAP 的绿色 点，你就要买入。
一个很好的方法来确认买方在第二天重新获得控制权是如果第二天的
VWAP 现在在上涨。这可能在新的第一天的前三到五分钟内发生，所以你需 要密切关注。
如果你在两个交易日的VWAP   都在上涨时购买股票，那么势头对你 有利。 一旦你购买了股票(5),止损可以低于早晨的低点(4)。如果  那个低点被跌破，这意味着卖方从一开始就控制了走势，那么就没  有理由继续持有股票。
在图表8.1中，那些在股票转为正数之前才购买它的买方，比那些在 股票跨越每日VWAP(5)   时购买的买方高出约$0.40(6)。如果买方 (6)使用了低于早晨低点的止损，他们就不会能够购买那么多股票
(基于使用1 R-Multiple    的风险),就像那些在股票重新获得每日 VWAP(5)   时以较低价格购买的人一样。
购买红变绿?
许多市场参与者喜欢在股票从当日负转正(红色)时买入。当一只股 票与前一日的收盘价相比处于负位置时，它是“红色”,而当它与前 一日的收盘价相比处于正位置时，它是“绿色。”
Notice the day two entry technique will get you in the stock ahead of momentum buyers who like to buy a “red to green”move.
注意，当日二入场技巧将让你在动量买家之前进入股票，这些买家喜 欢买入“红转绿”的行情。

图8.2该图显示，第二天的入场技巧也适用于低价股。最佳买入时机是在初始回调 后(详情见插图)。图表：TC2000.com
As  shown  in  Chart  8.2,when  we  buy  strength  after  the  stock  regains
upward  momentum  in  the  morning  of  day  two,we  can  get  involved  before the  stock  goes  “red  to  green.”
如图8.2所示，当我们在第二天上午股票恢复上涨势头时买入强势， 我们可以在股票从“红转绿”之前参与其中。
Here,the   stock  traded  below  the   second-day  VWAP(green)for   about   four   minutes(1)but  held  above  the  blue  2-day  AVWAP.On  the  fifth  minute  of    the   second    day,the    stock   crossed    up   through    the(green)VWAP(2),which caused  the  slope  of  that  VWAP  to  flatten  and  then  turn  higher.Looking  at
这里，股票在第二天VWAP  (绿色)下方交易了大约四分钟(1),但保持 在蓝色2天AVWAP 上方。在第二天第五分钟，股票向上穿越了(绿色)
VWAP(2),        这导致该VWAP的斜率变平然后转为上升。看看
the inset,a purchase near$5.90 would have been quite reasonable,with a stop below the low of the day(1).
Back to the full chart which includes the inset,the stock went on to a day   two intraday high ofover $6.60 which means those who purchased(2)had the potential to take up to $0.70(11.9%)that day,or decide to hold for a
longer period.For someone who makes the purchase here with the intent of a longer-term hold,they would have the comfort of a great entry from   day one of the trade.
Alternative  Entry  Technique
The next example,in Chart 8.3,shows a “less than perfect”setup because  that is how the market works.Not every trade willfollow all the guidelines for any strategy you use.Markets are risky.We pay the price of the
unknown in exchange for the hope ofa profit.Our edge comes from our strategies and risk management.Ifyou want to experience consistent     perfection in your trades,just stay in cash.Perfection does not exist.
Chart 8.3 is a little trickier.As you can see from the inset box,the stock    initially looked like it would hold above both the daily(purple)and 2-day (blue)AVWAP(1).Instead,there was a quick shakeout(2)about five
minutes into the trading day.If you had purchased early this may have triggered a stop.
There are a couple of ways we could have avoided the frustration ofan
early loss.The first technique is to wait for the first five minutes of the day before you enter the trade.The downside is you might miss some profits at the beginning of the day.
插入图，在5.90美元附近买入将是非常合理的，止损设在当天下方低点 (1)。
返回包含内嵌图的完整图表，该股票继续上涨，创下了日内第二高  点超过$6.60,这意味着那些购买了(2)的人当天有潜力获利高达$ 0.70(11.9%),或者选择持有更长时间。对于在这里购买并打算
长期持有的人来说，他们将从第一天开始就感到交易入场的舒适。
替代入场技巧
下一个例子，在图表8.3中，显示了一个“不完美”的设置，
因为市场就是这样运作的。并非每一笔交易都会遵循你使用的   任何策略的所有指南。市场是有风险的。我们用对未知的代价   来换取获利的希望。我们的优势来自我们的策略和风险管理的。 如果你想在交易中体验持续完美，那就保持现金。完美不存在。
图表8.3稍微有点棘手。正如从内嵌框中可以看到的，该股票最初 看起来似乎将保持在每日(紫色)和2天(蓝色)AVWAP(1)    之 上。然而，在交易日的五分钟内，出现了一次快速的洗盘(2)。 如果你早些时候购买了，这可能会触发止损。
我们可以采取几种方法来避免早期亏损的挫败感。第一种技术是在进 入交易前等待一天中的前五分钟。缺点是你可能会错过当天的部分利 润。

The   second,and   less   risky   entry   technique,is   to   wait   for   5-10   minutes   from the   open   to   buy   near(3)before   you   make   a   purchase.Ifyou   waited   for   a
new  high  to  buy,you  would  have   gotten   involved   near$15.50   and   your   risk  would  have  been  less  than  $0.20  cents  per  share  ifyour  stop  was  below  the  low  of  that   day.This  is   still  an  excellent  entry  with  limited  risk  and  positive momentum   from   the   onset   of   the   trend.

with   strong    demand,we   may    see    the   pattern    ofearly   weakness    before   trend

第二种，风险较低的交易进入技术，是在开盘后等待5- 10分钟，在
(3)附近买入。如果你等待一个新高买入，你会在$15 .50附近参与，
并且如果你的止损位低于当天的低点，你的风险每股会低于$0 . 20。
这仍然是 一 个风险有限的优秀入场点，并且从趋势开始时就具有正向 动 能 。
第三天及以后：上升趋势
AVWAP  可在趋势的第二天之后很好地使用。在一个需求强劲的股票中，我们 可能会看到在趋势之前出现早期弱势的模式
continuation several days in a row as shown in Chart 8.4.

Chart 8.4这张图表显示了三天的交易，使用2分钟蜡烛图。插图显示了如何在第二天和 第三天重复次日入场。图表： TC2000.com
尽管股票并没有完美地下跌到前一天的VWAP  (紫色和绿色箭头),但 它在前两天和第三天显示出初始弱势，然后在开盘后不久得到解决。
The insets on days two and three show the initial stock weakness rid the   stock of the early profit takers.As the stock climbed above the daily VWAP (green  circles)and  buyers  had   control,this  became   a  purchase
opportunity.Red  circles  markthe  price  where  you  place  the   stop(below the  morning  low).
第两天和第三天的内嵌图显示了初始库存疲软清除了早期的获利了结者。 当股价上涨超过每日VWAP  (绿色圆圈)且买家掌控局面时，这成为了一 个买入机会。红色圆圈标记了您放置止损的位置(在早晨低点下方)。
Short  Sales  with  Multi-Day  AVWAPs                 多 日AVWAP   的短期销售
Techniques that work for a stock in an uptrend are also relevant to short  sales.We will review some examples of stocks that found Resistance at,or near,a prior day's AVWAP when the stock's trend is lower.These stocks    then became low-risk,high-probability short sale candidates.
Market Psychology of the Short Setup
When a stock experiences a sharp move lower on day one and closes near  the low of that day,there will likely be sellers in the following day or days. There are also three groups of participants in the short sale market:
bargain  hunters,short   sellers,and  market  makers.
Bargain      hunters(longs)show up in the morning of day two,with the
beliefthat it is a good idea to buy the stock “on sale.”These buyers might be eager to add back on the open strength with the thought they missed the
low the day before.This increased purchase activity causes the price togo up.In a bout of FOMO,bargain hunters start buying even more,thinking    that the stock has reversed course from the previous day's decline.The
early strength convinces them that selling was overdone and "it has to go higher,because it is a good company.”
Short   sellers   without conviction in their position might get spooked by
the early strength and cover their position in order to avoid profit erosion.
Market   makers   who have to sell large quantities of the stock that day will helpencourage the bargain hunters and short sellers to chase prices
higher,by bidding the stock up in the pre-market.
For example,if the market maker needed to sell 750,000 shares they might attempt to create excitement early in the day.They do this by bidding the  stock higher in the morning.The market maker may purchase 10,000 or
适用于上涨趋势中的股票的技术也适用于卖空。我们将回顾一些在 股价趋势较低时，在先前的每日AVWAP  处或附近找到阻力位的股 票的例子。这些股票随后成为低风险、高概率的卖空候选股。
短期设置的市场心理
当一只股票在第一天经历剧烈下跌并收于当天的低点附近时，接下来的一  天或几天里很可能会有卖家。在短期卖空市场中，有三类参与者：抄底者、 卖空者和做市商。
抄底者(多头)在第二天早上出现，认为买入这只“打折”的股票是  个好主意。这些买家可能急于在开盘时追加买入，想着他们前一天错  过了低点。这种增加的购买活动导致价格上涨。在FOMO   (害怕错过) 情绪的驱使下，抄底者开始购买更多，认为这只股票已经扭转了前一  天的下跌趋势。早上的强势让他们相信卖空过度了，“它必须更高，
因为它是一家好公司。”
立场不坚定的卖空者可能会被早上的强势吓到，平仓以避免利润侵蚀。
当日必须卖出大量该股票的市场做市商将通过在盘前竞价将股价推高， 从而鼓励 bargain       hunters和 short       sellers追涨价格。
例如，如果做市商需要卖出750,000股，他们可能会试图在一天早些时候  制造一些兴奋。他们通过在早上抬高股票报价来实现这一点。做市商可能会 在早上购买10,000股或
more shares in the morning to drive the price higher so they can sell as many shares as possible at the higher morning prices.
When the stock opens higher,that market maker willthen sell the 10,000 shares they purchased and as many additional shares as they can at the    more favorable prices to work off the 750,000 share balance they have left to  sell.
If the market makers can sell 10%of the orders(75,000 shares)while the
stock is above the daily VWAP,they will be thrilled because they know that the balance of their sell order will probably push the stock(and the daily
VWAP)lower as the day progresses.Remember,this is“market impact
cost”(MIC)as discussed in Part One,Chapter 3.The initial selling gets them a quick start at what is often close to the highest prices of the day.This
helps minimize their MIC throughout the rest of the day.
If you missed the move lower on day one and did not want to short the stock near the first day close,your opportunity comes in the morning of day two. If the stock opens higher than the previous day close,you want to be ready  to sell the stock short under the following conditions.
How it unfolds:
1.The stock holds below the prior day's VWAP(see chart below).This shows sellers still have control from the start of the day the move    began.
2.Afterearly morning  strength,the  stock  stabilizes below the  2-day AVWAP,and price drops below the daily VWAP.This tells us the
更多股票，以推动价格上涨，这样他们就可以在较高的早上价格卖出尽 可能多的股票。
当股票开盘价较高时，该做市商将随后卖出他们购买的10,000股， 并在更有利的价格下卖出尽可能多的额外股票，以清偿他们剩余的 750,000股待售余额。
如果做市商能在股票高于当日VWAP 时卖出订单的10%(75,000股), 他们将非常高兴，因为他们知道其卖单余额很可能会随着白天的进行  将股票(以及当日VwapP)    推低。记住，这是第一部分第3章中讨论  的“市场影响成本” (MIC)。  初始卖出让他们在接近当日最高价时  快速开始。这有助于在整个白天的其余时间里最小化他们的MIC。
第二天：下行价格行动跟进行动
如果你错过了第一天下跌的行情并且不希望在第一天收盘附近做空股 票，你的机会出现在第二天的早晨。如果股票开盘价高于前一天收盘 价，你希望在以下条件下准备好做空该股票。
如何展开：
1.股价低于前一日的VWAP   (见下图)。这表明卖方从当天开 始移动时仍占据主导地位。
2.上午早些时候力量之后，股价在2天AVWAP  下方稳定，价格跌破 每日VWAP。这告诉我们
sellers have regained control of the trend for the new day and it is then their game to lose.
3.We sell the stock short as it drops back below the daily VWAP and place our stop above the high of the morning.
4.If our stop doesn't trigger,we hold the stock and lower our stop to
just above the “most recent and relevant lower-high”for the timeframe we intend to hold the trade.
Short-term entry tactics like this can be used to establish a position in the stock which might be held for a day trade,or even a longer-term
investment.
Charts 8.5,8.6,and 8.7 show some examples of how we can use this information to identify low risk/high probability entries into short positions.
Chart 8.5 is an example of a stock which experienced strong selling on day one,where it dropped from$61 to a low of$57.
卖方已经重新控制了新天的趋势，然后轮到他们输掉比赛。
3. 当股票价格回落至每日VWAP  下方时，我们做空该股票，并将止损 单设置在早晨高点之上。
4.如果我们的止损单未被触发，我们将持有该股票，并将止损单下调 至我们打算持有的交易时间框架中“最近且相关的较低高点”之上。
这种短期入场策略可用于在股票中建立头寸，该头寸可能被持有以进行日 内交易，甚至可能成为长期投资。
图表8.5、8.6和8.7展示了我们如何利用这些信息来识别空头头寸的 低风险/高概率入场点。
图8.5是一个股票在第一天经历强劲卖盘的例子，它从61美元下跌至57美元 的低点 。

The   next    day,the   stock    opened   higher,initially    looking    like   buyers    might
gain  back   control.Once  it  dropped  below   the  blue   AVWAP  from  day  one  and the purple daily VWAP(green circle),it was clear the sellers were back in   control.
For  those  who  resisted  FOMO  buys  and  kept  their  focus  on  price  action,the cross  back  below  those  two  AVWAPs  marked  an  excellent  short  sale
opportunity.
As  always,once  in  the   stock,the   stop  would  go   above  “the  most  recent  and   relevant lower-high,"which was above the morning high at$59.50.As the   stock   continued   lower  through  the   day,it  would  be  prudent  to   cover  part   of
图8.5这张图表展示了两天内的股票走势，使用2分钟蜡烛图。插入部分显示了第二 天开始时的1分钟蜡烛图，以便更详细地观察短期卖空情况。图表：TC2000.com
第二天，该股票开盘走高，最初看起来买方可能重新获得控制权。 一 旦它跌破第 一 天的蓝色AVWAP   和紫色每日VWAP     ( 绿 色 圆 圈 ) , 很 明显卖方重新掌握了控制权。
对于那些抵制了FOMO 买入并专注于价格行动的人来说，这两条AV WAP  线下的回调构成了一个绝佳的短期卖空机会。
一如既往，一旦进入股票，止损位会高于“最近且相关的更低高点”,该点位于上午高 点59.50美元之上。随着股票在一天中继续下跌，明智的做法是获利了结部分仓位，以 降低整体风险，并将剩余仓位的止损位调整到符合预期持有时间的适当水平。
the position profitably to reduce the overall risk and lower the stop on the balance to  a  level  appropriate to the  anticipated hold time.
Sell Green to Red?
Notice the day two entry technique will get you in the stock ahead of the
momentum buyers  who  like  to  sell  short  a“green  to  red”move.Many
market participants like to sell short at the point stocks go from positive at the  start  of  the  day(green)to  negative  on  the  day(red).When  we  short  as  the stock crosses below the daily VWAP,it can get us into the stock well
before  the  net  change  traders.
Chart 8.6 shows a less than perfect example to demonstrate some of the nuances  of the  setup.
As I've often said,if you only look for the “cookie cutter entries,"you will   miss  many  nuanced  opportunities  for  accurate  entries  into  long  and  short positions.
Chart 8.6 shows day one with a lot of volatility near the open.If you waited to enter the trade as the stock dropped below the day one VWAP(A),you    would have been able to participate in the initial weakness with a stop
above  the  first  lower-high  shown(B)and  then  lower  the  stop  accordingly.
获利了结部分仓位，以降低整体风险，并将剩余仓位的止损位调整到符合预 期持有时间的适当水平。
将绿变红?
注意第二天入场技巧，这将让你在动量买家(喜欢做空“绿变红”行 情)之前进入股票。许多市场参与者喜欢在股票从开盘时正值(绿) 变为当日负值(红)时做空。当我们在股票跌破每日VWAP 时做空， 可以让我们在净变化交易者之前就进入股票。
图8.6展示了一个不太完美的例子，以说明该设置的某些细微差别。
如我常说的，如果你只寻找“现成入场点”,你将错过许多用于准确进入 多空头寸的细微机会。
图表8.6显示了第一天开盘附近波动很大。如果你等到股票跌破第一 天 的VWAP(A)      时才入场交易，你将能够参与最初的弱势，并以第 一个较低的高点 (B)  上方设置止损，然后相应地降低止损。

图8.7这张看跌图表由5分钟蜡烛图构成。它显示了在第一天、第二天和第三天用绿色圆 点标记的短期卖空入场区域。-图表：TC2000.com
有时，一个处于强劲下跌趋势的股票会在前几天的AVWAP  处找到供应。图 表8.7中的股票在第一天 (A)  出现向下跳空，并最初在VWAP (绿色箭头) 处找到支撑。当天稍晚，该股票跌破VWAP    ( 蓝 色 ) , 然 后VWAP   成 为 阻
力 ( 红 色 箭 头 ) , 该 股 票 收 盘 于 当 天 的 最 低 点 。
在第二天，股票跳空上涨 (B),      并显示出一些初始波动性，然后跌破 第一天的每日(紫色) VWAP 和(蓝色)AVWAP 。 第二天上的绿色圆 点显示了极佳的短期卖空位置，止损位在早晨高点(红色箭头)之上。
在第三天，股票再次向上跳空 (C),     并直接触及第一天(蓝色)的
AVWAP。这标志着当天的最高点。大约十分钟后，股票回落至新的两日 (紫色)AVWAP 和每日(黑色)VWAP 下方。在此处的卖空(绿色点) 获 利
advantage  of  the  failure  of  the  early   strength  and  then  benefited  from strong    selling    pressure.
It is  always  a good idea to  cover part of the position when the  stock
experiences  a  quick  selloff,and  then  lower  your  stops  on  the  balance  to  a level  that  doesn't  allow  the  position  to  turn  to  a  loss.
Risk Management
When a  stock makes  a  strong move  on  day  one it can be tempting to get
involved  in  the  trade   at  the   start  of  trading  the  next  morning.Rather  than jump  in  with  no  strategy  and  hope  the  trend  will  continue,we  use  the  day two AVWAP in conjunction with the daily VWAP to identify the lowest risk entry   for   trend   continuation.
A  disciplined  approach  like  this  allows  us  to  get  involved  in  the  trade  at  the lowest  risk  point.Because  we   enter  the  trade   at  the   start  of  new
momentum  we  also  reduce  the  risk  oftying  up  our  capital  in  a  stock  as  we wait  for  it  to  move.Also,this  approach  gives  us  greater  profit  potential.
1      We refer to it as the 2-day AVWAP,but it is not a full two days.As an example,at   10:00 a.m.Eastern on day two,it is the AVWAP of one day,plus 30 minutes.It would be a 420-minute AVWAP(390 minutes from the previous day plus 30 minutes of the new   day).
利用了早期强度的失败，然后受益于强大的卖压。
当股票经历快速抛售时，覆盖部分仓位总是一个好主意，然后降低 止损位到不会让仓位转为亏损的水平。
风险管理
当股票在第一天出现强劲走势时，可能会诱人在第二天交易开 始时参与交易。与其毫无策略地跳进去并希望趋势会继续，我们使 用第二天AVWAP   与 每 日VWAP   结 合，以识别趋势延续的最低风 险入场点。
采用这种自律的方法使我们能够在风险最低的点位参与交易。因为我们是在 新动量的开始时进入交易，所以我们减少了在等待股票动起来时将资本押在 一只股票上的风险。此外，这种方法也给了我们更大的盈利潜力。
1我们称之为2天AVWAP, 但它不是完整的两天。例如，在第二天东部时 间上午10:00,它是前一天的AVWAP   加30分钟。这将是一个420分钟的 AVWAP   (前一天的390分钟加上新一天的30分钟)。
KEY TAKEAWAYS·The  previous(or   several   days)AVWAP   is   an   importantreference  level  for  stocks  that  experienced  a  momentummove.·The   more   accurate   the   entry,regardless   of   the   planned hold  time,the  tighter  you  can   set  your   stop,and  themore  time you have with  momentum  in  your  favor.·This  strategy  will  help  you  catch  more  winners  that  have broken  out(or  down)at  the  beginning  of  a  multi-daymomentum    campaign.·Whether  you  use  this  technique  for  a  day  trade,multi-   day,or  longer  hold,it  can  help  you  enter  a  trend  at  the lowest-risk  point  possible.·Day   two(and   three)AVWAP   entries   provide   anadvantage   over   net   price   change   traders(red-to-green buyers   and   green-to-red   sellers).·    Because  we  enter  the  trade  at  the  start  of newmomentum we also reduce the risk of tying up our

关键要点
关键要点
对于经历了一次动量行情的股票来说，之前的(或几天 的 )AVWAP  是一个重要的参考水平。
输入越准确，无论计划持仓时间如何，你都可以设置 更紧的止损，并且更有利于利用动量。
这种策略将帮助你捕捉更多在多日动量战役初期突破 (或下跌)的赢家。
无论你使用这种技巧进行日内交易、多日交易还是长 期持仓，它都能帮助你以最低风险点进入趋势。
第二天(和第三天)的AVWAP  入场比净价变动交易 者(红转绿买入和绿转红卖出)更有优势。
因为我们是在新动力的开始时进入交易，所以我们也 会 降 低 我 们
capital in a stock as we wait for it to move.Also,this approach gives us greater profit potential.
