CHAPTER 9
AVWAP GAP TRADING
"In a time of rapid change,standing still is the most dangerous course of action."
—Brian Trac
Chapter Objectives
1.Identify  and  understand  the  four  different  types  of  gaps
2.Avoid  chasing  a  stock  that  gaps
3.Disciplined  strategies  for  trading  stocks  that  gap
Agaponrepresents  a  sudden  shift  in  a  stock's  valuation  that  leaves  an  area the  chart without  any  trade  activity.They  are  easily  seen  when
Agap
on
successive candles do not touch or overlap.Agap is a  simple
第九章
AVWAP  缺口 交易
“在快速变化的时代，停滞不前是最危险的行
动方案。”—布莱恩 ·崔西
章节目标，
1.识别和理解四种不同的缺口类型2.避免追逐跳空高 开的股票3.跳空高开股票交易的纪律性策略
A?代表股票估值突然发生变动，导致图表上出现无交易活动的区域。当连续 的蜡烛图不接触或重叠时，它们很容易被观察到。一个缺口是一个简单的
representation of a rapid shift in the supply/demand dynamics for the
stock.A gap higher(bullish)occurs when the price opens above the high of the prior day.Agap lower(bearish)occurs when the price opens below the
close of the prior day.See Chart 9.1 for examples of bullish and bearish gaps.
Four Types of Gaps
All price gaps are not the same,there are different classifications of gaps. This chapter will discuss why gaps are important to recognize and
understand,as well as specific AVWAP strategies to trade them.There are four commonly accepted gap classifications:Common,Breakaway,
Continuation,and Exhaustion.
Chart 9.1 This stock shows examples of gaps up(green highlights)and down(red
highlights)on a daily chart.Chart:TC2000.com
股票供需动态快速变动的表现。缺口向上(看涨)发生在价格开盘高 于前一天的收盘价时。缺口向下(看跌)发生在价格开盘低于前一天 的最高价时。参见图表9.1了解看涨和看跌缺口的示例。
四种缺口类型
所有价格缺口并不相同，存在不同的缺口分类。本章将讨论为何识别和理 解缺口很重要，以及针对缺口的具体 AVWAP  交易策略。通常有四种公认 的缺口分类：普通缺口、突破缺口、持续缺口和竭尽缺口。
图9.1该股票显示了日线图上的向上缺口(绿色高亮)和向下缺口(红色高亮)的 示例。图：TC2000.com
Common Gaps
A common gap occurs regularly in a stock because ofnormal trade
imbalances from day-to-day.Minor news,such as an analyst's upgrade or downgrade,may cause a common gap,or it couldjust be a buyer or seller  who is motivated by factors known only to them.
Common gaps do not lead to longer-term trend shifts.Common gaps are typically"filled"or “closed”when trades occur in the prior gap range.   Common gaps typically take no longer than a few days to fill.Chart 9.2    shows common gaps higher and lower.
In Chart 9.2,the blue circles represent the common gaps.The highlighted area shows how the smaller first gap(1)filled almost immediately,while   gap(2)filled the next day(blue arrow).Gaps(3 and6)did not get filled for the time shown on this chart.Most common gaps get filled.
Common gaps offer excellent short-term trade opportunities,especially in
a stock where there is an existing Stage 2 Uptrend or Stage 4 Downtrend
(See the Market Structure Chart in AppendixA).For stocks stuck in Stage 1 Accumulation or Stage 3 Distribution,there is typically no edge to trade a    common gap.
常见缺口
普通缺口会因日常交易不平衡而定期出现在股票中。轻微消息，如 分析师的升级或降级，可能导致普通缺口，或者可能只是受其自身 仅知晓因素驱动的买方或卖方。
常见缺口不会导致长期趋势变化。常见缺口通常在之前的缺口范 围内发生交易时被“填补”或“封闭”。常见缺口通常在几天内 被填补。图9.2显示了更高和更低的常见缺口。
在图9.2中，蓝色圆圈代表常见缺口。高亮区域显示了较小第一个缺口(1) 几乎立即被填补，而缺口(2)在下一个交易日(蓝色箭头)被填补。缺口 (3和6)在图表显示的时间内没有被填补。大多数常见缺口会被填补。
普通缺口提供了绝佳的短期交易机会，尤其是在存在现有阶段2上升 趋势或阶段4下降趋势的股票中(参见附录A 中的市场结构图)。对
于陷入阶段1积累或阶段3分配的股票，通常没有交易普通缺口的优势。
Chart 9.2 This 30-minute chart shows common gaps that appear when there is an order
imbalance at the open,but it is not a significant enough event to lead to a longer-term
trend.Chart:TC2000.com
Chase the Gap or Wait for AVWAP?
In 2008,I wrote one of my first articles about the AVWAP,"Chase the Gap or Wait for VWAP?”Over the last two decades,the strategy outlined in that
article has served me well and I still use it today.
The article laid out techniques to trade stocks with a common gap.This
strategy provides  a  low-riskentry  into  a  stock  which  has  experienced  a
gap.When  a  stock  gap  is higher,we  are told there  are two  choices:buy the  open strength and hope it holds or buy as the stock pulls back from the gap
图9.2这张30分钟图表显示了在开盘时出现订单不平衡时常见的缺口，但这并不是 一个足以导致长期趋势的重大事件。图表：TC2000.com
追逐缺口还是等待 AVWAP?
2008年，我写了一篇关于AVWAP的早期文章之一，“追逐缺口还是等待
VWAP?”  在过去的二十年中，那篇文章中概述的策略对我非常有益，我至 今仍在使用它。
这篇文章概述了使用常见缺口交易股票的技术。这种策略为经历过缺口的 股票提供了一个低风险的入场点。当股票缺口较高时，我们被告知有两个 选择：买入开盘强度并希望其保持稳定，或者买入股票从缺口回落时
strength.A third option,wait for the AVWAP,is the technique we explore
by using a one-minute timeframe.Keepin mind,the same concepts apply to the longer timeframes with the AVWAP from the gap.
To trade a common gap successfully we need to consult shorter,intraday timeframes.Chart 9.3 is constructed of 1-minute candles.The green
highlighted area shows the gap higher from the previous day close near
$99/share(2),up to an open price of $102.75.Anyone who purchased the   stock at the open of the first few minutes of the day had to choose between two options.
The first option is to hold the stock as it plummeted back down to $99 in the first few minutes(2),or to stand aside,let the stock settle down and wait for evidence the buyers were back in control before getting involved.
The second option was to wait for the stock to rally back above the daily
VWAP(1).This is where the buyers were back in control of the stock for the day.A purchase at this point would put you in the stock after the shakeout. If the move was to fail after entry,a stop under the low ofthe day(2)would  limit any loss.A stop would go under(2)because it is "the most recent and   relevant higher low.”
强度。第三种选择是等待AVWAP, 这是我们使用一分钟时间框架探索的技 术。请记住，相同的概念也适用于从缺口开始的AVWAP  的较长时间框架。
要成功交易一个普通跳空缺口，我们需要参考更短、日内的时间周期。图  9.3由1分钟蜡烛图构成。绿色高亮区域显示了从前一天收盘价附近99美元/ 股(2)跳空高开至102.75美元的开盘价。任何在当天前几分钟开盘时买入 股票的人都必须在两个选项之间做出选择。
第一个选项是持有股票，看它在前几分钟(2)暴跌回99美元，或者   选择观望，让股票平复下来，等待买家重新掌控市场的证据后再参与。
第二种选择是等待股票回升至每日VwaP(1)   以上。这是当天买方重 新掌控股票的时机。在此点买入将使你能在洗盘后持有股票。如果入 场后行情失败，则会在日内最低价(2)下方设置止损以限制损失。
止损会设在(2)下方，因为它被定义为“最近且最相关的更高低点。”

the   trend   of   longer   timeframes,the   condition   of   the   overall   market   and

图9.3这是一份1分钟K线图，展示了如何使用“追逐缺口或等待VWAP” 策略的看涨示 例。图源：TC2000.com
股票全天持续上涨， Vwap  在当天稍晚时(3)遭遇快速测试并找到买方。是 否值得为超过一天的交易持有该股票，取决于交易者。这一决定将取决于更 长时间框架的趋势、整体市场状况和
personal  risk  tolerance  levels.My  preference  is  to  take  partial  profits  and let  the  winner  run.
In  Chart  9.4,we  see  the  opposite,a  stock  which  gapped  lower,rallied  for about 45 minutes and then broke below the VWAP of the day.
Chart 9.4 is a 1-minute chart of a stock which closed on day one at
approximately   $105.30(1).The   stock  gapped  lower(blue  highlight)to  open at about $104.60 on day two.
If you had shorted this stock at the open,you would have shorted near the   low of the first hour of the day,$103.90(2).It was worse for the person who shorted at the open,because the stock went positive on the day for a few
minutes(3)and  that  might  have  caused  them  to  panic  and  cover  the  short at a loss.
Rather than short the open,it makes more sense to see if the buyers fail to take control,and then short the stock once the stock drops back below the  daily VWAP(4).When you avoid the initial choppy action in the stock,you   are more likely to enter the trade at the correct time,with a logical place    for your stop being above the high of the day(3).Agood entry goes a long   way in the ability to hold the stock for longer timeframes.
Of course,there will be times when the stock gaps higher and continues to   rally  straight up  through the  course  of the  day,or  gaps  lower  and  continues to sell off for the day.
个人风险承受能力水平。我的偏好是获利部分并让赢家继续运行。
在图9.4中，我们看到相反的情况，一只股票跳空低开，反弹了大约45分 钟，然后跌破当天的VWAP。
图9.4是一只股票的1分钟图表，它在第一天大约收于105.30美元(1)。 该股票在第二天跳空低开(蓝色高亮)至约104.60美元。
如果你在开盘时做空这只股票，你会在当天的第一个小时的低点附  近做空，103.90美元(2)。对于在开盘时做空的人来说情况更糟， 因为该股票在当天有几个小时内为正(3),这可能会让他们恐慌并 在亏损的情况下平仓。
与其在开盘时做空，不如看看买家是否无法掌控局面，然后在股票  回落至每日VWAP  以下时做空(4)。当你避免股票的初始波动行为 时，你更有可能在正确的时间进入交易，你的止损位可以设置在当  天的最高点(3)以上。 一个好的入场点对于能够长时间持有股票的 能力有很大帮助。
当然，有时股票会跳空高开并全天持续上涨，或者跳空低开并全天持 续下跌。

Gap/AVWAP Several Days
Sometimes  a  stock  will  experience  a  large  gap  when  it  might  take  a  few
days  for  the  market  to  digest  the  gains  or  losses  before  the  primary  trend
resumes.People  who  get  excited  about  the  news  will  chase  the   stock  on  the open  and  pay  higher  than  necessary,as   seen  in   Chart  9.5.On  the   first  day,   the  stock  gapped  from$29.60  to   $30.40(blue  highlight).We  anchor  our
VWAP  to  the  first  candle  of  the  day(1,see  inset  for  detail).

At(2)the stock cleared the AVWAP and it would make sense to purchase the  stock  at($30.30)with  a  stop  below the low  of the  day(3).

缺口/AVWAP  多日
有时一只股票会出现较大的缺口，而市场可能需要几天时间来消化这些收益 或损失，然后主要趋势才会恢复。对新闻感到兴奋的人会在开盘时追涨这只 股票，并支付不必要的更高价格，如图9.5所示。第一天，该股票从29.60美 元跳升至30.40美元(蓝色高亮)。我们将我们的VwépP 锚定在当天的第一 根蜡烛上(1,详细情况请参见插图)。

图9.5这张图表使用了两天交易中显示的2分钟蜡烛图。图表：TC2000.com
在(2)处，股票清除了AVWAP,   此时以($30.30)购买股票，并在当天的最 低价(3)下方设置止损是有意义的。
After a quick surge up to$32.50,the stock experienced some profit taking.It found enough demand at the VWAP(4)to provide support for the next leg    higher.The stock finished near the high of the day.
Ifyou missed the entry on day one,the stock gapped higher again on day
two(blue highlight)and you should set your VWAP anchor to the first
candle of the day(5).After a couple of minutes below the purple AVWAP,
the stock crossed back up through the VWAP(6).A purchase(6)would have made sense,with a stop below the low of the day(7).As we know,all trades  will not be winners and this trade would have been stopped out with a
small loss.
About 10 minutes later,the stock crossed back up through the VWAP(9).It can be a frustrating experience when it crosses back above the AVWAP so
soon after a small loss.The taste of the prior loss might have preventedyou from a logical new entry(9).
Ifyou stuck to your strategy,you would purchase the stock again and set   the new stop under the new low of the day(8).This buy turned into a nice winner as it rallied from the purchase price of$34up as high as $38 later  that  day.
After it hit the high of$38,it pulled back to the VWAP(10)and briefly
bounced before it made a lower high and broke below the VWAP(11).Ifyou used this level as a stop,it would have resulted in a sale at$36.25,a day
trade gain of$2.25 or 6.7%.
Ifyou held the stock from the day one purchase price of$30.30(2),you
would be in a stronger position and might have trailed your stop up under    the   blue    AVWAP   from    day    one.This   would    have   kept    you   in    the    stock   with    a  stop near$35 at the end of day two.Another alternative would have been to allow the initial volatility of day two to settle down and then raise your stop on half the position to under the day two VWAP(purple)and the balance
在快速上涨至$32.50后，股票经历了一些获利了结。它在VWAP(4) 处找到 了足够的买盘，为下一波上涨提供了支撑。股票收盘价接近当天的最高价。
如果你错过了第一天入场的机会，第二天(蓝色高亮)股票又跳空高 开，你应该将你的VWAP  锚点设置为当天的第一根K 线(5)。在紫
色AVWAP 下方停留几分钟之后，股票再次穿过VWAP(6) 。   在 这
一点进行买入(6)是有意义的，止损可以设置在当天的最低点(7)。 正如我们所知，并非所有交易都会盈利，这笔交易最终会以小亏损被   止损出局。
大约10分钟后，股票再次穿过VWAP(9) 。  当它很快又回到AVWAP之上  时，这会是一个令人沮丧的经历。之前的亏损感可能阻止了你进行一个理性 的新入场(9)。
如果你坚持你的策略，你会再次买入股票，并将新的止损设置在当 天的新的最低点(8)。这次买入变成了一笔漂亮的盈利，因为它 从买入价34美元反弹，当天最高达到了38美元。
在触及$38的高点后，它回落至VWAP(10)   并短暂反弹，然后形成 一个更低的高点并跌破VWAP(11)。  如果你将此水平用作止损位，
将会在$36.25处卖出，实现$2.25的日内交易利润，涨幅为6.7%。
如果你从第一天就持有该股票，购买价格为$30.30(2),你将处于  更有利的位置，并且可能将止损线设在第一天蓝色AVWAP   下方。这 将使你在第二天结束时仍持有该股票，止损线设在接近$35的位置。 另一个选择是让第二天初期的波动性平复下来，然后将一半头寸的止  损线设在第二天紫色 VWAP 下方，剩余部分
below the blue AVWAP from day one.With this strategy you would have
sold half the stock from the purchase of$30.30 at$36.25(11)and to
continue to hold the balance with a stop under the day one blue AVWAP at $35.There is never one best way to set stops,only a best way for your risk tolerance and your expected hold time.
Breakaway Gaps
A breakaway gap occurs when a stock breaks free of a longer-term
consolidation(Stage  1,Accumulation  or  3,Distribution),usually with  a
large increase in volume.The breakaway gap acts as an ignition to
momentum that can last months to years.An intermediate to longer-term
trader or investor will want to learn to recognize a breakaway gap because   of the longer-term implications for the stock.When breakaway gaps occur    with a news catalyst such as an earnings surprise,it is more likely the stock will continue to trend in the gap's direction than it is to fail.If the news that  motivated the gap is unexpected and meaningful,it is more likely to lead to  a  sustained  trend.
Upside Breakaway Gaps
Chart 9.6 shows a breakaway gap that led to a longer-term trend.The large gap(1)showed a group of motivated buyers.We anchor our AVWAP to that point.A few days after the initial gap,the stock briefly pulled back and
found buyers(2)at the AVWAP anchored from the gap.The support at the AVWAP showed a strong appetite for the stock and a purchase(3)made
sense because it made a higher-high after the AVWAP was tested,with a stop below the pullback low(2)because it was the “most recent and
relevant  higher-low.”
设在蓝色AVWAP 下方。采用这种策略，你将卖出一半在$30.30购买   的股票，价格为$36.25(11),并继续持有剩余部分，止损线设在第一  天蓝色AVWAP 下方，价格为$35。设置止损线从来没有一种最佳方法， 只有一种最适合你风险承受能力和预期持有时间的方法。
突破缺口
突破缺口发生在股票突破长期整理区间(第一阶段，积累或第三阶段， 分配)时，通常伴随着成交量的大幅增加。突破缺口作为动量的点火  器，可以持续数月甚至数年。中短期至长期交易者或投资者需要学会  识别突破缺口，因为这对股票具有长期影响。当突破缺口伴随着新闻  催化剂(如盈利意外)发生时，股票更有可能继续沿缺口方向趋势，  而不是失败。如果推动缺口的消息出乎意料且意义重大，它更有可能  引发持续趋势。
向上突破缺口
图9.6显示了一个突破缺口，导致了中长期趋势。这个大缺口(1)显! 示了一群有动力的买家。我们将我们的AVWAP 锚定在那个点上。在  初始缺口几天后，股票短暂回调并在AVWAP 锚定的缺口处找到了买  家 ( 2 ) 。AVWAP 处的支撑显示了强烈的股票需求，并且由于在
AVWAP 被测试后形成了更高的高点，因此这次购买(3)是有意义 的，同时设置了低于回调低点(2)的止损，因为它被确定为“最近 且最相关的更高低点。"

Chart  9.6  Notice  how  the  momentum  remained  strong  after  the  breakaway  gap(1)for
over   one   year.Chart:TC2000.com
As the stock continued higher,it wasn't until 15 months after the initial gap that the stock undercut the AVWAP(4).A holder from the purchase(2)
until it broke below the AVWAP(4)recognized a profit of approximately   33%($20.50 to $27.50).Stops will never get you out at the high,but they will get you out when the supply/demand equation from the original
catalyst changes.
It is unusual for breakaway gaps to be filled because they represent a
powerful shock to the supply/demand equation.The news motivator and increased volume confirm a large and immediate interest by institutions
who compete to put large amounts of money to work in the stock at the
same time.Many times,people who learned “all gaps get filled”will wait for a purchase at a lower price,which never happens.This group will often
become   buyers   later    in   the   cycle   when   they    can   no   longer    stand   aside    and

随着股票继续上涨，直到初始缺口15个月后，股票才跌破
AVWAP(4) 。   从购买(2)到跌破AVWAP(4)      的持有人实 现了约33%的利润($20.50至$27.50)。止损永远不会在最高 点让你出局，但当原始催化剂的供需关系发生变化时，它们会  让 你 出 局 。
缺口通常不会被填补，因为它们代表了供需方程的一个强大冲击。消 息推动者和交易量的增加证实了机构投资者对同时将大量资金投入股 票的浓厚兴趣。很多时候，那些学习了“所有缺口都会被填补”的人 会等待更低的价格买入，但这从未发生。在这个周期中较晚的时候，
这些人通常会变成买家，当他们再也无法袖手旁观时，
watch it continue to go higher without them.They become FOMO buyers, often at the worst times when prices are far from the start of the move.

The strongest stocks will continue higher for several days or longer before   they experience a price or time correction.In these cases,if you do not buy  on the first day of the move,you may miss out on the initial powerful surge. Ifyou miss the initial move,there are often(but not always)better

regain control.A reclaiming ofthe AVWAP doesn't always lead to immediate continuation.If your stop does not get triggered,be patient and trust your   stop.Allow the market to prove itself.Take comfort in“a trend once

图9 . 7该图表使用15分钟蜡烛构建，显示了经历突破性跳空的股票日内交易情况。图表： TC2000.com
最强的股票将继续上涨几天或更长时间，然后才会经历价格或时间的 修正。在这种情况下，如果你不在第一天买入，你可能会错过最初的 强劲上涨。如果你错过了最初的上涨，通常(但不总是)在回调后会 有更好的机会在强势时买入股票。在AVWAP  周围反复波动可能需要 几天的时间，买方才会重新获得控制权。重新获得AVWAP  并不总是 导致立即的延续。如果你的止损单没有被触发，要有耐心并相信你的 止损单。让市场证明自己。在“一旦确立的趋势更有可能继续而不是 反转”这句话中找到安慰。图9.7中的股票
shows it how it took a couple of days to absorb selling from profit takers before the stock continued higher.
The blue shaded area shows the large gap from$18.65 to$22/share,a gap of 18%.Clearly,there was a catalyst that got participants excited about
owning  the  stock.We  anchor  the   AVWAP  from  the  first  candle  of  the  gap
(A).The buyers on the open were quickly overwhelmed by owners who
wanted to lock in their large overnight gains and the stock continued lower over the next couple of days.At(1)the stock rallied up to the AVWAP from  the gap and got rejected.
The buyers took control(2)as the stock cleared the AVWAP from the gap.A purchase at that point made sense with a stop under any of the lows(3,4,   or 5)depending on personal preferences and risk tolerance.As with all
trading,there is no right circumstance for every trader.I will often use a tighter stop or sometimes stagger my stops.
A staggered stop approach might be to use stops on 1/3rd of the position
under each of those lows.Points(6)and(7)show how the buyers kept the   price above the gap and prevented the price from breaking the AVWAP the next day.This type of action would encourage me to keep my stop under
(3).Ifthe stock failed to hold the AVWAP,my concern would be it gives up the entire gain.Once the stock was back above $22/share,stops might be raised up under(7).
Downside Breakaway Gaps
A breakaway gap which starts or accelerates a downtrend is a sign of
significant trouble and shows lower expectations for the stock in the future. Ifyou find yourselfin the unfortunate position of owning one of these
stocks,it is usually best to cut the loss quickly and move on.It is better to
accept  the   loss   and   discomfort  right   away   rather  than  wait   for  more   serious
展示了它花了几天时间来吸收获利了结者的卖盘，然后股票才继续上涨。
蓝色阴影区域显示了从$18.65到$22/股的大幅差距，差距为18%。 显然，有一个催化剂让参与者对持有该股票感到兴奋。我们从缺口
(A)  的第一根蜡烛线锚定AVWAP 。开盘时的买家很快被希望锁定 其巨大隔夜收益的持有人压倒，股票在接下来的几天里继续下跌。在 (1)处，股票上涨至缺口AVWAP 并遭到拒绝。
买家在(2)处掌控了局面，因为股票清除了缺口AVWAP。在那个时点买入是有道理 的，止损可以设在任何低点(3、4或5)之下，具体取决于个人偏好和风险承受能  力。像所有交易一样，没有适合每个交易者的正确情况。我经常会使用更紧的止损， 或者有时会分散我的止损。
一种分散止损的方法可能是在每个低点之下对1/3的头寸设置止损。点(6) 和(7)显示买家如何将价格维持在缺口之上，并阻止价格第二天跌破
AVWAP。   这种行动会让我倾向于将止损保持在(3)之下。如果股票未能守  住 AVWAP,    我的担忧是它会放弃全部收益。 一旦股票回升至$22/股以上， 止损可能会被提高到(7)之下。
向下突破缺口
一个开始或加速下跌趋势的突破缺口是一个重大麻烦的迹象，表明对 未来股票的预期较低。如果你不幸持有这类股票，通常最好快速止损 并离场。与其等待更严重的情况，不如立即接受损失和不适。
price weakness to set in.The stock is not a "bargain on sale,"it is a broken
stock and if,"they don't scare you out with the initial gap lower,they will often wear you out,"as the stock will need a lot oftime to heal before it
heads higher again.In chart 9.8 we see an example of a downside breakaway.

Here(9.9)is a bearish example of a breakaway gap.The blue shaded area
shows the gap from$33 down to $28(approximately-15%)When the stock gaps lower,we anchor our AVWAP to the start of trading after the gap(1). The stock continued down as low as $25.50 that day,which put the “dip
buyers”in a losing position with no reasonable place to set their stop.
People who shorted the stock seemedto have a good trade for the first day, but on the second day,buyers gained control as the stock made it back up
through the AVWAP(2).Later that day,and into the next day,buyers
defended the stock and bought pullbacks to the gap AVWAP(3,4,and5).

图 9 . 9 蓝 色 阴 影 区 域 显 示 了 在 此 日 内 时 间 框 架 上 的 向 下 突 破 缺 口 。 图 ：

这里(9.9)是一个看跌的突破缺口示例。蓝色阴影区域显示了从
33美元下跌至28美元的缺口(大约-15%)。当股票缺口下跌时，我  们将AVWAP 锚定在缺口后的交易开始处(1)。那天股票继续下跌  至25.50美元，这使得“抄底买家”处于亏损状态，且没有合理的止  损位置。做空该股票的人在第一天似乎有一个不错的交易，但在第二 天，当股票回升至AVWAP  时，买家控制了局面(2)。那天稍晚些  时候，以及第二天，买家捍卫了该股票，并买入缺口AVWAP  的回调 (3、4和5)。
It took a couple of days to digest the news before the stock continued lower. At(6)the sellers took back control of the stock from the gap as the stock
broke below the gap AVWAP.This was the correct place to short the stock because price evidence told us the sellers were in control again.
Of course,we did not know the stock would continue lower,so we had to set a stop to protect against a reversal.The lower-highs we could use to place   our stop above are(7,8,and9).Just as in the previous long example,we
could have used a staggered stop approach.As the stock continuedlower,   the job was to manage the stops above the most recent and relevant lower- highs.From there,the rest is up to the market.
Continuation Gaps
A continuation gap is also known as a running or measuring gap.We find  these gaps in stocks where there is an established trend that likely began with a breakaway gap.Because the trend already exists,these gaps
represent a continuation,and often an acceleration,of the trend.It is
common for earnings reports to be the catalyst for these gaps.Like the
breakaway gap,the continuation gap is not always filled.It will frequently leave behind those who wait for the gap to be filled.The charts that follow will make that clear.
The continuation gap offers some of the best opportunities to participate in a trend ifyou weren't involved with the earlier move.Most long holders of    the stock feel good about owning it and don't want to sell shares.This
creates tight supply,and with increased demand,these stocks are often in  the “sweet spot”of their trends.During this phase,there is little volatility and short-term pullbacks are bought up quickly.Because these gaps
typically occur somewhere near the midpoint of a major trend cycle,
continuation gaps are also known as “measuring gaps.”They are found somewhere near the middle of a full-trend cycle.
在股票继续下跌之前，需要几天时间来消化这个消息。在(6)处，卖 方重新控制了股票，因为股票跌破了缺口AVWAP 。 这是做空股票的 正确位置，因为价格证据表明卖方再次掌控了局面。
当然，我们不知道股票会继续下跌，所以我们必须设置一个止损位以 防止反转。我们可以用来放置止损位的较低高点是(7、8和9)。就像 之前的长期示例一样，我们可以使用交错止损方法。随着股票继续下 跌，工作就是管理最近和相关的较低高点的上方止损位。从那时起， 剩下的就取决于市场了。
持续缺口
持续缺口也被称为运行或测量缺口。我们在存在既定趋势的股票中 找到这些缺口，该趋势很可能以突破性缺口开始。由于趋势已经存 在，这些缺口代表了趋势的持续，并且通常是趋势的加速。盈利报 告通常是这些缺口的催化剂。就像突破性缺口一样，持续缺口并不 总是会被填补。它经常会留下那些等待缺口被填补的人。接下来的 图表将使这一点变得清楚。
延续缺口为那些未能参与早期行情的人提供了参与趋势的绝佳机会。  大多数长期持有该股票的投资者对持有它感到满意，并不想卖出股票。 这造成了紧俏的供应，随着需求的增加，这些股票通常处于其趋势的  “甜蜜点”。在这个阶段，波动性很小，短期回调很快被买入。由于  这些缺口通常发生在主要趋势周期的中点附近，延续缺口也被称为
“测量缺口”。它们出现在完整趋势周期的大约中间位置。
Exhaustion Gaps
Exhaustion gaps occur near the end ofa major trend.The stock will reverse the direction of the gap and close at the extreme lower end.When a stock
that has been in an uptrend and has experienced a large percentage move,  the company will often report positive news to cause a gap.Initial reactions to this news motivates the people who have been on the sidelines who have been waiting for a pullback before they get involved to give into FOMO and   buy the stock.The people who have owned the stock andenjoyed the large   gains see the opportunity to sell their highly appreciated shares to the
FOMO buyers.They use the liquidity from the good news to sell large
quantities of stock near the highs.The sales into “good news”that drove
the stock higher,will catch a lot of participants off guard because the stock sells offon“good news.”The market discounts the past and trades on
future expectations.Those who purchase the stock in anticipation of good news will sell when the news is released.Good news comes out at tops and bad news comes out at bottoms.If you trade off the news,you may find
yourself delivering  newspapers.
The stock in the daily timeframe(9.10)shows three distinctive gaps:
breakaway,continuation,and     exhaustion.
疲劳间隙
竭尽缺口发生在主要趋势的末期。股票将反转缺口的方向，并在极低 的末端收盘。当一只处于上升趋势且经历了较大百分比涨幅的股票， 公司通常会发布利好消息以造成缺口。对这条消息的初步反应会促使 那些一直观望、等待回调再参与的人因害怕错过 (FOMO)    而买入股 票。那些持有股票并享受了巨大涨幅的投资者看到机会，将他们高度 增值的股票卖给FOMO 买家。他们利用利好消息带来的流动性，在接 近高点时卖出大量股票。卖入“利好”消息推动股票上涨的销售，会 让很多参与者措手不及，因为股票在“利好”消息发布时卖跌。市场 折现过去，交易未来预期。那些预期利好消息而买入股票的人，在消 息发布时会卖出。利好消息出现在顶部，坏消息出现在底部。如果你 根据消息进行交易，你可能会发现自己正在送报纸。
日线图(9.10)显示有三个明显的缺口：突破缺口、持续缺口和衰竭 缺 口 。

图表9.10这个每日图表显示了大约一年半的贸易。
图表：TC2000.com
1- 突破缺口发生在1月份，价格为160美元。这个缺口接近封闭但未被 填补。交易这个股票的机会 (A)   出现在股票从缺口反弹至AV
WAP上方时。止损位 (B)   会在回调低点下方。注意缺口处的 AVWAP   (绿色)在点 (C 和D) 的回调时找到了买方。
2-延续性缺口(2)发生在8月的210美元。这是一个较大的缺口，因为市场在此之前已经经 历了大幅上涨(这消耗了市场供应)。有一些做空者被高价困住，为了尽量减少损失，随着 股价继续上涨，他们甚至支付了更高的价格。大约一周半后，股价终于跌破那个缺口 (E)
形成的新AVWAP(蓝色),因为获利了结者入场。这些获利了结者产生的供应很快被新买 家的需求所淹没，几周后(F),  股价被推回缺口AVWAP  (蓝色)之上。这就是在
AVWAP  下方洗盘后，新仓位适合买入的地方。新的买入(F) 的止损单将放在 (E) 下方。 股价花了将近 一 个月的时间才找到重新上涨的动能 (G),       但这值得等待，因为股价从那个 水平开始经历了 一 次大幅上涨。
sellers was quickly overwhelmed as demand from new buyers pushed the
stock back above the gap AVWAP(blue)just a couple of weeks later(F).This is where it made sense for new positions to be purchased,after the
shakeout below AVWAP.A stop on the new purchase(F)would be placed under(E).It took almost a month for the stock to find renewed upward
momentum(G)but it was worth the wait because the stock experienced a major run from that level.
This “measuring gap”is used to give a trader an idea of what would be a
reasonable estimate(or measure)of where to expect the next major
activity level.The measuring gap gets its name from the tendency for a
rally,which starts at a continuation gap,to match the gains the rally has
already shown between the breakaway gap and the continuation gap.Put
another way,you can get a good projection of the remaining potential gains between the gap and the next major activity level.
In this chart,the breakaway gap ran 50 points(from$160 to $210),so a
minimum upside target starting at the continuation gap at $210 is $260
($210+$50).This stock clearly exceeded that level and shows why it is best to trail stops up under higher-lows for an exit than it is to exit at a price
target.
3-The    exhaustion     gap.This gap occurred in January of the following
year at approximately $355.We never know ifa gap is the exhaustion gap until after the fact,when the stock cannot continue higher.Yet there are  clues that tell us the long run up from$160 is in jeopardy of tapering off.   Unlike the breakaway gap,the exhaustion gap on this chart immediately
reversed  course(H)after  the  gap  higher.At(H)there  were  sellers  waiting for an opportunity to sell,and the gap higher turned out to be their
opportunity to do so.After a week of downward pressure,the stock
stabilized above the AVWAP(purple)(I)and went to make a new high (J).
卖方的供应很快被新买家的需求所淹没，几周后 (F),  股价被推回  缺口AVWAP  (蓝色)之上。这就是在AVWAP 下方洗盘后，新仓位  适合买入的地方。新的买入 (F)   的止损单将放在 (E)   下方。股价花 了将近一个月的时间才找到重新上涨的动能 (G),  但这值得等待，
因为股价从那个水平开始经历了一次大幅上涨。
这个“测量缺口”用于给交易者一个关于合理估计(或测量)预期下 一个主要活动水平的想法。测量缺口得名于反弹从持续缺口开始时， 往往会匹配反弹在突破缺口和持续缺口之间已经显示的涨幅。换句话 说，你可以得到一个关于缺口和下一个主要活动水平之间剩余潜在收 益的良好预测。
在这个图表中，突破缺口运行了50点(从$160到$210),所以从$210的持续缺口开 始的最小上行目标为$260($     50)。这只股票显然超过了那个水平，并显示  了为什么最好在较高低点下方设置跟踪止损以退出，而不是在价格目标处退出。
3-疲劳缺口。这个缺口发生在次年1月左右，约为$355。我们只有在事后， 当股票无法继续上涨时，才知道一个缺口是否是疲劳缺口。然而，有一些  迹象表明，从$160开始的长期上涨有可能会逐渐减弱。与突破缺口不同， 这张图表上的疲劳缺口在向上跳空后立即反转了方向 (H) 。 在 (H)   处， 有卖方在等待机会卖出，而向上跳空最终成为了他们卖出的机会。在经历  了一周的下跌压力后，股票在AVWAP   (紫色) (I) 上方稳定下来，并创  出新高 (J)。
After that high failed to hold,the stock made no upward progress for the next couple of months.The stock was “exhausted”and needed to rest.
In chart(9.11)we see the same three distinctive gaps on a daily timeframe, this time with a stock in a downtrend.
1-The  breakaway   gap   occurred at $1200 and it continued lower for four days before it reclaimed the AVWAP(red).When the stock dropped below   the gap AVWAP(A)the sellers were back in control and it made sense to
sell the stock short with a stop above(B).This would have been a difficult   position to hold as the price crossed back and forth above the AVWAP and   (C)it broke above the previous high it had made approximately two weeks earlier.
2-The   continuation    gap   occurred at $910.After a couple of days of
trades above the gap AVWAP(red),it broke lower(D)and remained below that AVWAP(blue)through the end of the chart.The AVWAP(blue)from
the gap was not tested from underneath,which showed how motivated the   sellers were.Using the measuring technique for this gap we would come up with a minimum downside target of $620.This target is achieved by
subtracting the continuation gap level of$910 from the breakaway gap
level of$1200,which is $290.We then subtract $290 from$910
($910-$290=$620).Clearly,this measurement is only a guideline since the    stock touched the $620 level about a month after the gap and it continued    lower.We want to have an approximation(measurement gap)of where the stock could go,but stop losses that trail down above the most recent and
significant lower-highs will keep you in the trade longer.
3-The   exhaustion   gap   occurred at $430,after a large drop and prices  continued to decline.Do not look at exhaustion gaps as a reason to trade against the primary trend.Instead,an exhaustion gap can mean the
beginning ofa Stage 1 Accumulation,the stock is just “exhausted”and
在那次高点未能守住之后，接下来的几个月里，股票没有做出任何上涨的 进展。股票“已经疲劳”了，需要休息。
在图表(9.11)中，我们看到在日线图上出现了同样的三个显著缺口，这次 股票处于下跌趋势。
1-突破缺口发生在$1200,随后连续四天下跌，最终收复了
AVWAP  (红色)。当股票跌破缺口AVWAP(A)      时，卖方重新掌 控局面，此时做空股票并以(B) 上方设置止损是有道理的。这将是 一个难以持有的头寸，因为价格在AVWAP  上方来回波动，并且(  C) 它突破了大约两周前创下的前高。
2-持续缺口发生在$910。在缺口AVWAP (红色)上方交易了几天后，它下跌 (D),      并保持在
该AVWAP   (蓝色)下方，直到图表结束。来自缺口的AVWAP   (蓝色)从未从下方得到测试，这显示了 当时的动力。从缺口处形成的AVWAP(蓝色)
从未丛下方得到测试，这显示了当时的动力。
卖家们。使用测量这种差距的技术，我们会得出  .
以620美元为最低下限目标。此目标通过 …..
从脱离缺口中减去$910的延续缺口
1200美元，即290美元。然后我们从910美元中减去290美元  ($910-$   $620)。显然，这个测量只是一个指导方针，因为
股票在缺口出现后大约一个月触及了620美元的水平，并继续 较低。我们想要有一个近似值(测量差距),以了解 .
股票可能去哪里，但止损位应设置在最近的主要
显著低高点之上，这将使你更长时间地持有交易。
3-疲劳缺口出现在$430,在大幅下跌后价格继续下跌。不要将疲 劳缺口视为逆势交易的理由。相反，疲劳缺口可能意味着第一阶  段积累的开始，股票只是“耗尽了”并且
needs time to heal.This is mentioned because many people try
(unsuccessfully)to trade against the trend in an attempt to buy the stock “at the low.”

Psychology:Don't Focus on Labels
Too many people get hung up on labeling the type of gap that occurred.The right way to think about gaps is to recognize what they represent in terms   of a sudden supply/demand shift rather than label them.Sometimes you
will think a gap might be an exhaustive gap when it turns out to be a
second or third continuation gap.The important thing to recognize is the
需要时间来恢复。这是提到的原因是许多人尝试(不成功地)逆势 交易，试图以“低价”买入股票。

心理学：不要关注标签
太多人纠结于给出现的缺口贴上类型标签。正确看待缺口的方式是认  识到它们代表了突然的供需变化，而不是去给它们贴标签。有时你以  为一个缺口可能是竭尽缺口，结果它却是一个第二或第三种延续缺口。 重要的是要认识到
opportunity the gaps present for trend continuation or reversal and trade them appropriately.There is no more objective tool than AVWAP from the  gap to measure if buyers or sellers are in control.
Risk Management:Gap Anomalies
There are some equities and ETFs that experience gaps nearly every day:
·Thinly  traded  stocks(little  trade  volume)are  prone  to  daily common gaps.
·Stocks  that  trade  American  Depositary  Receipts(ADRs)gap
nearly every day because they must open at the same price in the United States that they trade on their primary overseas
exchange.
·Commodity related ETFs such as oil and gold trade a nearly 24-   hour market.The price change for the commodity outside of the NYSE hours needs to be adjusted at the 9:30 a.m.NY open.This   change results in a gap nearly every day.
Because ADRs and commodity ETFs gap nearly every day,it is difficult to
manage risk.My preference is to not trade them.There are plenty of other stocks and ETFs where risk management is easier.Chart 9.12 shows the
daily gaps in an ETF.
把握趋势延续或反转的机遇窗口，并据此进行交易。从缺口位置衡 量买方或卖方谁占据主导地位，AVWAP   是最客观的工具。
风险管理：缺口异常
有一些股票和ETF 几乎每天都会出现缺口：
4成交量小的股票(交易量小)容易出现每日常见缺口。
*交易美国存托凭证 (ADR)  的股票几乎每天都会出现缺口， 因为它们必须在纽约以与它们在主要海外交易所交易相同的价 格开盘。
与商品相关的ETF,  如石油和黄金，交易时间接近24小时。在  纽约证券交易所交易时间之外的商品价格变化需要在上午9:30的 纽约开盘时进行调整。这种调整导致几乎每天出现缺口。
由于ADRs 和商品ETF 几乎每天都在跳空，因此管理风险很困难。 我的偏好是不交易它们。有大量其他股票和 ETF,   其中风险管理更 容易。图9.12显示了ETF  的每日跳空。
Chart 9.12 Only a few of the gaps are circled in the daily ETF chart above.Chart:
@Trendspider
As you consider a trade set up,take a closer look at how frequently the
stock gaps and decide ifyou can reasonably manage risk in the trade.This is part of recognition of "the personality"of the stock and if it makes sense for you to trade.Commodity related ETFs gap nearly every day because the
commodities they represent are traded nearly 24 hours per day.
Is It Really a Gap?
Most of the time,when a stock gaps higher or lower at the start of trading, it does not represent the first trades of the day for the stock.Stocks that
report news outside of regular trading hours(RTH)will begin to trade the    moment the news is announced in the pre-or post-market trading hours.    The extended hours(or EH)of pre-and post-market trade availability differ between brokerage firms.If it is important to you to trade extended hours,   find a reputable brokerage firm with the longest hours available to trade.
图9.12在上述每日ETF图表中，只有少数几个缺口被圈出。图：
@TrendSpider
在考虑交易设置时，仔细看看股票跳空的频率，并决定你是否能合理  地管理交易中的风险。这是识别股票“个性”的一部分，以及是否对  你来说交易是合理的。与商品相关的ETF 几乎每天都在跳空，因为它 们所代表商品的交易几乎每24小时都在进行。
这真的是一个缺口吗?
大多数情况下，当一只股票在交易开始时出现跳空高开或低开时，这 并不代表该股票当天的第一笔交易。在常规交易时间 (RTH)    之外发 布新闻的股票，将在新闻宣布的盘中或盘后交易时段开始交易。盘中 和盘后交易的延长时段(或EH) 的可用性在不同的经纪公司之间有  所不同。如果您希望进行延长时段交易，请寻找提供最长交易时间的 信誉良好的经纪公司。
Always  be  sure  to  check  a  chart  which  includes  pre-or  post-market  trade    data  when  you  trade  a  stock  with  a  gap.If  the  stock  was  unusually  active  in the  extended  hours,it  is  helpful  to  anchor  a  AVWAP  from  the  start  of the
extended  hours  trades.When  you  use   the  extended  hours  AVWAP  along
with  the  regular  trading  hours  AVWAP,this  combination  is  helpful  to  find  key  levels  for  the  stock.This  type  of  analysis  applies  mainly  to  day  trades.

Charts  in  9.13  show  the  same  stock  with  extended  hours(EH)on  the  left  and regular  trading  hours(RTH)on  right.On   the   left,you   can   see   that   trades
occurred  at  all  the  levels  in  between  the  gap  level  and  even  well  above  the high  of the  RTH  trades.On  the  right,there  is  a  clear  gap  from  the  close  of   day  one  to  the  opening  of  day  two.I  usually  only  reference  the  extended
hours  trades  if  the  stock  traded  unusual  volume  during  extended  hours.

9. 13中的图表显示了同一支股票在左侧的延长交易时间 (EH)    和 右 侧 的常规交易时间 (RTH)     的情况。在左侧，你可以看到交易发生在间 隙水平之间的所有级别，甚至远高于RTH 交易的最高点。在右侧，从 第一天收盘到第二天开盘之间存在明显的间隙。我通常只在股票在延  长交易时间内交易异常成交量时参考延长交易时间的交易。
Futures versus ETFs
Like the RTH for equities,major ETFs like the SP500 ETF(SPY)also trade in the overnight(ON)session of the SP500 Futures.On days when the SPY
opens with a large gap,it's helpful to study the AVWAP from the start of the overnight session for the futures.There will often be important levels
where the futures market may find buyers and sellers at the ON AVWAP,
but the level may not be visible on the RTH SPY because there is not as
much “price memory”from the start of the RTH.The relationship between   the SPY and SP500 Futures is important ifyou trade either of those markets on a short-term basis.
Dividends
When a cash or stock dividend is paid to shareholders,the amount of the dividend is removed from the share price.If a stock closes the day at
$33/share and the next day the company pays their shareholders a
dividend of $0.50/share,the price of the stock is adjusted lower by
$0.50/share.The stock price adjustment is reflected with the share price opening at$32.50(assuming there are no other supply and demand
imbalances that impact the opening price).The lower open for this stock will cause a gap on the chart.These gaps are not due to an ordinary
imbalance in supply and demand,so I do not consider these worthy as a trade candidate on the day of the dividend.
What about “Fading the Gap”?
When people “fade the gap”it simply means they want to take a position on the other side of the trend or direction of a gap.They want to short a stock   that gaps higher or buy a stock that gaps lower.The focus of this book is to   trade with the trend,to buy stocks in uptrends,sell short stocks in
downtrends and avoid the neutral times(Stages 1 and3).You always want
期货与ETFs
与股票的RTH 类似，主要的ETF如SP500      ETF(SPY) 也在SP500 期 货的夜间 (ON)   交易时段进行交易。在SPY以较大间隙开盘的日子  里，研究期货夜间交易时段从开始时的AVWAP  是有帮助的。期货市 场通常会在ON  AVWAP处找到买家和卖家的重要水平，但由于
RTH 的“价格记忆”较少，该水平可能不会在RTH  SPY上可见。如   果你在短期交易SPY或SP500 期货市场，那么它们之间的关系很重要。
股息
当现金或股票股利支付给股东时，股利金额会从股价中扣除。如果 一只股票在某天收盘价为每股33美元，而次日公司向股东支付每股 0.50美元的股利，则股价会下调0.50美元。股价调整会反映在开盘 价上，假设没有其他供需失衡影响开盘价，该股票的开盘价将为每 股32.50美元。这种股价的低位开盘会在图表上形成缺口。这些缺  口并非由于普通的供需失衡造成，因此我认为在股利支付当天，这 些缺口不值得作为交易候选。
“淡化管理差距”如何?
当人们“淡忘缺口”时，它仅仅意味着他们想要在缺口的趋势或方向另一侧 采取立场。他们想做空跳高股或买入跳低股。本书的重点是与趋势交易，买 入上升趋势中的股票，做空下降趋势中的股票，并避免中性时期(阶段1和  3)。你总是想
to give a trend the benefit of doubt that it will continue for a longer
timeframe.When a stock in an uptrend gaps lower,they can be great buy candidates.Stay focused on the trades in relation to the daily VWAP as
well as the important AVWAPs from longer timeframes.Gaps occur in all stocks at some point,so it is important to be prepared with an objective
approach to handle them.
Risk Management:Placing Stops
Perhaps the most difficult part of any trade is the management of the stops while the trade is working in your favor.In the examples,I have outlined
several scenarios for how to go about placing and updating stops.As with everything in the market,only hindsight is 20/20.
To compensate for the risk of the unknown,my preference is to use several stops.The first one is the tightest(meaning  smallest dollar increment)
because it protects the initial capital.How tight you set the stop depends
on your personal risk tolerances.I set the second stop after the stock has
moved in my favor.I set the second stop tightly enough that I can lock in
some gains ifthe stock reverses,which lowers the overall risk.I set the
third stop to give the stock a little more “room to breathe.”This(hopefully) prevents getting stopped out before it turns into a larger winner.
给趋势一个继续存在更长时间段的假设。当上升趋势中的股票跳低时， 它们可以是很好的买入候选。也要关注与每日VWAP  以及来自更长时  间段的重要AVWAP  相关的交易。缺口在所有股票中都会出现，因此  重要的是以客观的态度做好准备来处理它们。
风险管理：设置止损
或许任何交易中最困难的部分是在交易对你有利时管理止损。在示例 中，我概述了如何放置和更新止损的几种情况。与市场中的所有事情 一样，只有事后诸葛亮才能看得清楚。
为了弥补未知风险，我的偏好是使用多个止损点。第一个止损点是最 紧密的(意味着最小的美元增量),因为它保护初始本金。你如何设 置止损点取决于你的个人风险承受能力。我将第二个止损点设在股票 有利可图之后。我将第二个止损点设置得足够紧密，以便如果股票反 转，我可以锁定一些利润，从而降低整体风险。我将第三个止损点设 置为给股票留出一些“呼吸空间”。这(希望)可以防止在它变成更 大的赢家之前被止损出局。
KEY TAKEAWAYS·Gaps occur on a regular basis;without a strategy we are prone to FOMO trades.·No trade method will get you into 100%of the winners.   That should not be your goal.The goal is to find the low- risk,high-probability trades and a large part of thatcomes from the confidence in your approach.As it issaid,“it is better to be on the sidelines in cash,wishing you were in than it is to be in the market wishing you    were out.”·Stops will never get you out at the high,but they will get you out when the supply/demand equation from theoriginal catalyst changes.·Day two entry techniques allow us to participate in astock when we might have normally missed the day-one gap  opportunity.·Be aware of extended hours trading in gap stocks.·Unusual  circumstances  such  as  dividends,ETFs,and futures create special gap situations.
KEY TAKEAWAYS
·Gaps occur on a regular basis;without a strategy we are prone to FOMO trades.
·No trade method will get you into 100%of the winners.   That should not be your goal.The goal is to find the low- risk,high-probability trades and a large part of that
comes from the confidence in your approach.As it is
said,“it is better to be on the sidelines in cash,wishing you were in than it is to be in the market wishing you    were out.”
·Stops will never get you out at the high,but they will get you out when the supply/demand equation from the
original catalyst changes.
·Day two entry techniques allow us to participate in a
stock when we might have normally missed the day-one gap  opportunity.
·Be aware of extended hours trading in gap stocks.
·Unusual  circumstances  such  as  dividends,ETFs,and futures create special gap situations.
关键要点 
缺口会定期出现；如果没有策略，我们很容易进行 FOMO 交易。
没有交易方法能让你100%获利。那不应该是你的目标。 目标是找到低风险、高概率的交易，而这很大程度上来  自于你对方法的信心。正如所说，“现金观望比在市场  中希望退出要好。”
止损永远不会让你在高位出局，但它们会在原始催化剂 的供需方程变化时让你出局。
第二天入场技巧让我们能在通常可能错过首日跳空机会时 参与股票。
注 意 跳 空 股 的 盘 后 交 易 。
股息、ETF和期货等非正常情况会创造特殊的跳空局面。

CHAPTER 10
THE SHORT SQUEEZE
"The average trader is naturally a
chronic bull.It is human nature to prefer
optimism to pessimism.”
-Philip Carret
Chapter Objectives
1.Understand   short   interest   and   the   short   interest   ratio
2.Identify  the  price  levels  and  trends  of  where  short  sellers  are involved
3.Understand   why   short   squeezes   occur
4.Identify   two   types   ofshort    squeezes;knee-jerk   and   structural
T    he  appeal  of selling short is easy to understand because stocks can
drop  much  faster  than  they  rise.There  are  unique  risks  involved  when
you sell a stock short.The biggest risk to a short seller is that the stock
第10章
短挤压
“平均交易者天生就是慢性多头。倾向 于乐观而非悲观是人类的天性。”
—菲利普·卡雷特
章节目标
1.理解短期卖空和短期卖空比率
2.确定卖空者涉及的价位和趋势
3. 了解为何会发生卖空逼空
识别两种卖空逼空类型；突发性 (knee-jerk) 和结构性 (structural)
卖空的优势很容易理解，因为股票下跌的速度通常比上涨的速度快。 当你卖空股票时，会涉及独特的风险。对卖空者来说最大的风险是股票
price rises instead of drops.A rising price in a heavily shorted stock can
lead to dramatic upward price movement as losses mount in the accounts of those  who  are  short.The  short  sellers  magnify  the  upward  price  movement  as they buy the stock to try to minimize their losses.This can lead to
dramatic  upside  price  moves  where  trend  traders  can  profit.
This  momentum  creates  a  double  demand(new  long  purchases  and  shorts  covering)for  a  stock  when  there  is not much  supply  offered.Additionally,   supply is often tight for a stock in a strong uptrend as holders want to hold their  profitable  position.When  the  stock  rises  rapidly,the  shorts  lose
money,and  as  they  try  to  cover  their  bearish  bets,they  compete  for  supply from new  longs.Because  there  is  extra  competition  to  buy  the  stock,the
shorts  feel  pressure  from  mounting  losses,and  they  become  “squeezed.” Before we explore the dynamics of a short squeeze,let's cover some
terminology  and  learn  how  to  interpret  short  sale  data.
Short Interest
"Short  interest"refers  to  the  number  ofshares  sold  short  and  not  covered
(bought  back).Because  these   shares  are   still  open   short  positions,they
represent  a  source  of  future  demand.The  short  sellers  either;buy  the  stock at lower prices to lock in gains,or they buy at higher prices to minimize
losess.
It is useful to know when a stock is sold short.Exchanges mandate that
brokerage  firms  accurately  keep  and  report  the numbers  of shares  sold
short  and not yet  covered.Twice  each month,the  firms  tally  all  short  sales and  send  the  data  to  the  various  exchanges.The  exchanges  then  combine  the  firms'data  and  publicly  disseminate  the  information.
FINRA releases the number of shares sold short twice per month.The
number reported to the public is never the real time number.In fact,it is a
价格上涨而不是下跌。在大量卖空的股票中，价格上涨会导致那些卖 空者的账户损失累积，从而引发剧烈的向上价格波动。卖空者在试图 减少损失时买入股票，从而放大了向上的价格运动。这可能导致剧烈 的上涨行情，趋势交易者可以从中获利。
这种动量在供应量不多时，会为股票创造出双重需求(新多头购买和  空头回补)。此外，在强劲的上升趋势中，由于持有者希望持有其盈  利头寸，股票的供应量通常很紧张。当股票快速上涨时，空头会亏损， 而他们试图回补其看跌头寸时，会与新的多头竞争供应。由于购买股  票的竞争加剧，空头会因不断累积的亏损而感到压力，并变得“被挤  压”。在我们探讨空头挤压的动态之前，让我们先解释一些术语，并  学习如何解读卖空数据。
卖空兴趣
“卖空兴趣”指的是已卖出但未回补的股票数量。由于这些股票仍然 是未平仓的空头头寸，它们代表着未来需求的一个来源。空头交易者 要么;在较低价格买入股票以锁定利润，要么;在较高价格买入以最 小化亏损。
了解一只股票何时被卖空是有用的。交易所要求经纪公司准确记录 和报告已卖出但尚未回补的股票数量。每月两次，这些公司会统计 所有卖空头寸并发送数据给各个交易所。然后，交易所会合并各公 司的数据，并公开发布这些信息。
FINRA 每月发布两次卖空股份数量。向公众报告的数字永远不会是实时数字。 事实上，它是一个
minimum oftwo weeks old.For instance,the total number of shares for
stocks as ofJanuary 15(in the table below)is reported to FINRA by January 20 and is released as public information on January 27.That means the
stocks continued to trade for a full seven business days,or longer,before FINRA releases the information to the public.As we willsee,the
information is still useful to determine the trend of short sales and the price levels where the short sellers are involved.

Short Interest Ratio/Days to Cover
The  Short  Interest Ratio(SIR),or days to  cover,is the number of shares  sold short(short  interest)for  an  individual  stock,dividedby  its  average  daily
trading volume over the previous two weeks.We interpret the  SIR as the number  of days  it  would  theoretically  take  to  cover(buy  back)the  shares
至少两周。例如，截至1月15日的股票总股数(下表所示),于1月 20日向FINRA 报告，并于1月27日作为公共信息发布。这意味着在 FINRA 向公众发布信息之前，这些股票继续交易了整整七天或更长 时间。正如我们将看到的，这些信息仍然有助于确定卖空趋势以及 卖空者参与的价格水平。

短期兴趣比率/覆盖天数
市净率 (SIR),       或称周转天数，是指个股的卖空股数(卖空量)除 以其过去两周的平均每日交易量。我们将市净率解释为理论上需要多 少天才能覆盖(回购)卖空的股数
that were sold short based on the average daily volume.I use the term "theoretically"because the shorts are not the only participants in the market.

Table 10.2 shows the number ofshares sold short was 13,918,435.At the
time of the report,the average daily volume for this stock was 2,047,326.
When we divide the short interest by the average daily volume,we get the number known as "Days to Cover”(DTC).We also refer to this as "Short
Interest Ratio”(SIR).In this example,the SIR equals 6.8.This means that if the shorts wanted to cover their position in full,it would take themjust
under seven days if they were the only volume in the market.Of course,it would actually take a lot longer to buy all that stock back since other
traders are also actively buying or selling the stock.
The higher the SIR is,the more difficult it is to exit a short position and    the greater the upward impact will be on price.I consider an SIR of 5 or  greater to be significant enough to think a short squeeze could develop in the  stock.
基于平均每日交易量。我使用“理论上”一词，因为卖空者并非
市场的唯一参与者。

表10.2显示，卖空的股数为13,918,435。在报告发布时，该股票的平 均每日成交量为2,047,326。当我们用短期卖空除以平均每日成交量， 就会得到一个被称为“偿还天数” (DTC)    的数字。我们也称其为   “短期卖空比率” (SIR) 。  在这个例子中，SIR 等于6.8。这意味着  如果空头想要完全平仓，如果他们是市场上唯一的成交量，那么他们  只需要不到七天的时间。当然，由于其他交易者也在积极买入或卖出  该股票，实际买回所有这些股票的时间会远长于此。
SIR 越高，退出空头头寸就越困难，对价格的上行影响也越大。 我认为SIR  达到5或更高时，足以认为股票可能出现空头挤压。
The Effect of Volume on SIR                                                        成交量对SIR 的影响
If a stock had a short position of 4,800,000 shares and an average daily
volume of 800,000,the SIR would be 6.0.This means it would take six full
days ofaverage daily volume for the  short  sellers to  cover their bearish
bets.If the same stock traded an average of 2.4 million shares per day,the    short  interest  for  the  stock  wouldbe  2.0,or  two  days  to  repurchase.Using    the  same  stock,but  with  an  average  daily  volume  ofjust  200,000  shares,the SIR would then be 24,meaning it would take 24 days of buying to cover the    positions.
When their short position is at a loss and the stock has strong upward
momentum,the  short  sellers  feel  “trapped”in  their  losing  position.They know their buying will add to the upward momentum.From a “trapped”
short's  standpoint,the  lower  the  SIR,the  better  as  their  buys  will  not  have as large of an impact on price.When analyzing an opportunity to make a
trade  that  takes  advantage  of  a  potential  short  squeeze  candidate,a  higher SIR is desirable as it is more difficult for the trapped short sellers to cover   their positions.The buys they need to make to  cover their  short positions   have the potential to  create  significant  upside momentum  as  more  and
more  short  sellers  compete  to  closeout  their  losing  trades.
You may see differences in the reported SIR from various data sources.The discrepancy occurs ifthe average daily volume used in the calculation is
not from the last two weeks.Some data providers use a 50-day average of
volume rather than the average of the last two weeks.It is important to
note that  a  large  outstanding  short  position  or  short  interest  ratio  by  itself is not a reason to buy a stock in anticipation ofa short squeeze.It is an
excellent gauge of potential demand for a stock which should be a part of every   trader's   arsenal.
Ifa股票的空头头寸为480万股，平均日成交量为80万股，则SIR为6.0。这意 味着空头需要六天的平均日成交量来平仓其看跌仓位。如果同一股票的平均 日成交量为240万股，则该股票的空头兴趣为2.0,即需要两天来回购。使用 同一股票，但平均日成交量为20万股，则SIR 将变为24,这意味着需要24天 的买入来平仓仓位。
当他们的空头头寸亏损且股票有强劲上涨势头时，空头交易者会感  到“被困”在自己的亏损头寸中。他们知道他们的买入会增加上涨  势头。从“被困”的空头的角度来看， SIR 越低越好，因为他们的买 入对价格的影响不会那么大。在分析一个利用潜在空头挤压候选者  的交易机会时，较高的SIR 是理想的，因为被困的空头交易者更难平 仓。他们需要做出的买入以平掉空头头寸有可能创造显著的上涨势  头，因为越来越多的空头交易者在竞争平掉他们的亏损交易。
您可能会发现来自不同数据源的报告中SIR  存在差异。如果计算中使 用的平均每日成交量不是来自最近两周，就会出现这种差异。 一些数 据提供者使用50天的成交量平均值，而不是最近两周的平均值。需  要注意的是，本身巨大的未平仓空头头寸或空头兴趣比率并不是买入 股票以期待空头挤压的理由。它是衡量股票潜在需求的绝佳指标，应 该是每位交易者武器库中的一部分。
Short Sellers are Often Correct                                                  空头交易者往往是对的
Short sellers with large positions against a stock are typically sophisticated speculators who have done extensive research on their targeted company.  They are often correct,and they make large profits as the stock declines.
There are also those short sellers who have the right idea based on their
fundamental analysis,but the timing of their short sales is off.That can lead to their positions being squeezed.When short trades are correct about a
trend,they will add to their positions as seen in Chart 10.3.

The stockin Chart 10.3 was in a steady downtrend(red arrow)and the
short interest continued to rise(green arrow)as the prices fell.The short sellers were emboldened by the lower prices and added to their bearish
bets as the stock price dropped.
对某只股票持有大量头寸的空头通常是复杂的投机者，他们对目标公 司进行了广泛的研究。他们通常很正确，并且随着股票下跌而获得巨 额利润。还有一些空头，他们的想法基于基本面分析是正确的，但他 们的短期销售时机不对。这可能导致他们的头寸被挤压。当空头交易 正确判断趋势时，他们会增加他们的头寸，如图10.3所示。

Short Interest Trend
When  we  look  at  the  changes  in  SIR  during  reporting  periods,we  can  spot the  trend  of  the  short  sellers  and  then  recognize  the  value  of  the
information.
In  Table  10.4  you  can  see  that  in  late  May  there  were  only  225,000  shares
sold  short  in  this   stock(1),but  it  hadjumped  to   13.9  million   shares  by
January   15(2).That  means  the  shorts  added   13.7  million  shares  to  their
short  position  in  six  months.The  average  daily  volume  increased  from
746,000 to 2 million,and the  SIR  climbed  from  less  than  one  to  6.8  days.The information  in  this  table  is  used  in  Chart   10.5.

短期兴趣趋势
当我们查看报告期SIR的变化时，我们可以发现做空者的趋势，然后认识到这些信 息的价值。

Now we know when the short sellers became more aggressive.Next,we   want to know at what price they shorted.If they shorted at prices higher than the current price,they would not feel pressure to buy back because they are in a profitable position.When the average short position is
initiated at lower prices than the current price,the short sellers are in a losing position,which makes them vulnerable to a squeeze.Chart 10.5
below,shows how rising prices motivates short sellers to cover their positions.

现在我们知道卖空者何时变得更加激进。接下来，我们想知道他们以什么  价格卖空。如果他们以高于当前价格的价格卖空，他们就不会感到压力要  买回，因为他们处于盈利地位。当平均卖空头寸在低于当前价格时启动时， 卖空者处于亏损地位，这使得他们容易受到挤压。下方的图10.5显示了价  格上涨如何促使卖空者平仓。

As we see in Chart  10.5,the short position increased from 2.0 million shares to 13.9 million shares from the end of September to January  15.The AVWAP from9/25  to1/15  was  about  $13.01.We  can  assume  this  is  the  approximate price most  of the  short positions were  initiated.When the  stock broke  past  the  range(A),it  closed  near$20  that  day.That  means  the  average  short  at   that  point  was  down  approximately  $7/share.That's  more  than  a  50%loss   overnight.
Notice how the number  ofshares  in the  short position  droppedby  6.2
million shares,from  13.9 million,down to  7.7 million  shares in the next    month.This  drop is  clear  evidence that the  short  sellers  took  some  large losses and they remained in a vulnerable position on the balance of the   trade  as  the  stock  made  higher-highs  and  higher-lows  after  that  gap
higher.

图10.5这张每日图表显示了随着价格上涨，卖空头寸的减少。图表：Koyfin.com
从图表10.5中我们可以看到，空头头寸从9月底增加到1月15日的
13.9百万股。从9月25日到1月15日的AVWAP   约为13.01美元。我们  可以假设这是大多数空头头寸启动的大致价格。当股票突破区间(  A) 时，那天收盘价接近20美元。这意味着在那个时间点的平均空头 亏损约7美元/股。这相当于一夜之间超过50%的亏损。
注意看，空头头寸中的股票数量减少了620万股，从1390万股下降 到下个月的770万股。这个减少是明确的证据，表明空头交易者遭 受了重大损失，并且在股票在缺口上方形成更高的高点和更低低  点后，他们在交易余额中仍然处于脆弱的境地。
Market  Psychology:When  do  Short
Squeezes Occur?
A short squeeze develops when those who sold the stock short,with the
expectation it would continue to decline in price,change their minds about their trades and attempt to cover their positions before the stock advances and large losses accumulate.The occurrence of a rapidly rising stock
price with a large short interest is known as a short squeeze.The  shorts buys become part of the “market impact cost”as their buys negatively
affect the position they are in.There are several groups of participants
who play a part when a stock gets squeezed:fearful buyers,forced buy-ins, margin calls,target short squeezes,and stock loan calls are some of the
ones we explore below.
Fearful  Buyersr 
If you have ever been short in a stock that continues higher against your
position,you understand the fear that higher prices elicit.To eliminate the mounting losses and the emotional trauma of holding a big loser,short
buyers may panic with their purchases.These purchases cause the stock to advance at arapid pace as the pressure of holding a losing position mounts  on the short seller,and the short seller gets “squeezed.”
The primary motivation to cover a bearish position,as the stock rises,is the fear ofunlimited losses.When you buy a stock at$30/share,your maximum loss potential is $30.00/share.When you sell a stock short at$30,the
potential for loss is,in theory,unlimited.The stock may rise to $60,a 100    percent loss,or it could climb to higher levels resulting in losses of greater than 100%.It is the fear of such an advance that can make for an explosive  upside moves in a heavily shorted stock.In Chart 10.6 we see a clear
example of shorts covering their position as the stock rises.
市场心理：何时会发生短头挤压?
当那些做空股票的人改变主意，试图在股票上涨并累积巨大损失之前 平仓时，就会发生空头挤压。股票价格快速上涨且存在大量空头头寸 的情况被称为空头挤压。空头买入成为“市场冲击成本”的一部分， 因为他们的买入行为对他们的头寸产生负面影响。当股票被挤压时， 有多个参与者发挥作用：恐慌性买家、被迫买入、保证金追缴、目标 空头挤压和股票借贷追缴是我们下面探讨的一些。
恐慌的买家                         
如果你曾经做空一只持续上涨的股票，你就能理解高价带来的恐惧。 为了消除不断累积的亏损和持有重大亏损标的的情绪创伤，空头买家 可能会在购买时恐慌。这些购买行为导致股价快速上涨，因为空头卖 家持有的亏损头寸压力不断累积，空头卖家因此被“挤压。”
覆盖空头头寸的主要动机，随着股价上涨，是害怕无限亏损。当你以   每股30美元的价格买入股票时，你的最大亏损潜力是每股30.00美元。 当你以每股30美元的价格做空股票时，理论上亏损的可能性是无限的。 股价可能上涨至每股60美元，造成100%的亏损，或者它可能继续上
涨，导致亏损超过100%。正是对这种上涨的恐惧，可能导致在大量 做空股票中爆发性的上涨行情。在图10.6中，我们看到空头在股价上 涨时覆盖其头寸的一个明显例子。

Chart  10.6  The  daily  chart  shows  short  interest  decline  dramatically  after  the  stock

Chart 10.6 illustrates what a short squeeze should look like.The stock broke past resistance(A)and then settled in for a few days.Once the stock made it past the AVWAP(B)from(A),the buyers regained control of the trend.The   short interest below the price action shows how the upward momentum
motivated short sellers to reduce their position from 16.9 million to 11.39 million  shares.
Short squeezes can occur for many reasons,including news events that
change investor perception of the worth of a company.A short squeeze can also develop as long holders of the stock attempt to push the price higher   in an attempt to tap into the emotional buying that trapped short sellers
often provide.If buyers are in control of the stock(it is in a Stage 2
Uptrend),they know short sellers are vulnerable.So long holders will often buy extra shares as the stock rises,with the hope the buyers can create
enough fear in the short sellers so they buy back their position;resulting in the price moving higher.This can be like pouring gasoline on a fire,it only   serves to make it burn hotter and stronger.

图10.6日线图显示，股票上涨后，卖空量急剧下降。图： Koyfin.com
图10.6说明了空头挤压应该是什么样子。股价突破了阻力位 (A),
然后又稳定了几天。一旦股价从 (A) 超过了AVWAP(B),      买方重 新控制了趋势。价格行为下的空头兴趣显示了向上的势头如何激励空 头卖家将他们的头寸从1690万股减少到1139万股。
短期挤压可能由多种原因引发，包括改变投资者对公司价值认知的新 闻事件。短期挤压也可能因长期持有股票者试图推高股价，以利用被 套牢的做空者常提供的情绪化买入行为而发展。如果买家掌控了股票 (即处于阶段2上升趋势),他们知道做空者处于脆弱状态。因此，
长期持有者会在股价上涨时购买额外股票，希望买家能让做空者产生 足够恐惧 ， 从而回购其仓位 ； 导致股价进一步上涨 。 这就像往火上倒 汽油 ， 只会让火势更猛烈 。
Forced Buy-Ins
Sometimes short sellers find themselves in a position of being forced by   their brokerage firm to purchase the shares they had sold short,to cover their short positions.There are two reasons for “forced buy-ins,”margin calls and targeted short squeezes.
Margin Calls
When losses in a short position have gone so far against a customer that
the equity levels in their account fall below exchange requirements,the
brokerage firm is required by regulatory bodies-the SEC,NASD,as well as   others-to demand the customer either to deposit more margin money into their account or buy the shares to close the short position.If the customer   does not deposit the additional money,the brokerage will buy the shares to close out the short position and get the customer's account in compliance.
Another reason for a forced buy-in of a short position comes when the
shares shorted are no longer available tobe borrowed against.When long holders of the stock,who have allowed shares to be borrowed for a short
position,sell their long position,the short sellers who borrowed those
shares will have an illegal “naked”short position.If this occurs,it is the
responsibility of the brokerage firm to demand that short sellers either find other shares to borrow,or force customers to buy the stock.If the short
seller cannot locate other shares to borrow,the short seller is required by securities regulations to purchase shares,or the brokerage firm will do it  for them.The forced buy-ins are not "handled with care."The brokerage    firm is only concerned with making the buys before the close of business,   before the risk is assumed by the firm.This can lead to dramatic upside
movement in a heavily shorted stock.
强制买入
有时做空者会发现自己被迫由其经纪公司购买此前卖空的股票，以 平仓。‘被迫买入’有两种原因：保证金追缴和目标性短期挤压。
追加保证金通知
当客户在空头头寸中的亏损程度达到一定程度，导致其账户中的权益 水平低于交易所要求时，监管机构——包括美国证券交易委员会(
SEC) 、 全国证券交易商协会 (NASD)    以及其他机构——将要求客 户要么向其账户存入更多保证金，要么买入股票以平仓空头头寸。如 果客户未能存入额外资金，经纪公司将买入股票以平仓空头头寸，并 使客户账户符合规定。
另一个导致强制买入空头头寸的原因是，被借入的股票不再可用于抵   押。当允许借出股票以建立空头头寸的股票多头持有者卖出其多头头  寸时，借入这些股票的空头卖家将面临非法的“裸”空头寸。如果发   生这种情况，经纪公司的责任是要求空头卖家要么找到其他股票借入， 要么强制客户买入股票。如果空头卖家无法找到其他股票借入，证券  法规要求他们必须购买股票，或者由经纪公司代为购买。强制买入不  会“小心处理。”经纪公司只关心在营业结束前完成买入，在风险由  公司承担之前。这可能导致被大量卖空的股票出现剧烈上涨。
Targeted Short Squeezes
There is a more sinister way the short sellers can be squeezed,called a
forced buy-in.When large,long holders wish to inflict maximum damage on short sellers,they will allow their stock to be borrowed until a time where   the buyers have taken control of the trend.If an institution that is in a long position of a stock,let's say one million shares,suddenly demands that the   shares they loaned out be delivered back to that firm,the short sellers who  borrowed the shares are stuck looking for new shares to borrow.If the
short seller cannot locate new shares to borrow,they must purchase the    shares they are short.This is effective to place pressure on shorts because of its cold-hearted implementation.In effect,the long holder set the shorts up to be squeezed.No one said Wall Street was a nice place.
Stock   Loan   Calls
When you purchase shares you can request that the company issue an
actual stock certificate,but this is rare.Most investors purchase stocks “in street name,"which means that the brokerage firm holds the shares as a
convenience to the customer.A source of revenue for brokerage firms is to loan customer shares to be shorted.Depending upon how the investor
(you)purchased shares and set up your brokerage account,you can either allow or not allow a brokerage to loan out your shares to short sellers.If
your shares are in a cash account,the brokerage cannot loan your shares.If your shares are in a margin account(and therefore with an hypothecation   agreement),it allows the brokerage firm to “hypothecate”(lend out)these   shares to other customers who may want to establish a short position.The   brokerage will charge customers fees to borrow stock for short positions.
A way to prevent your long positions from being lent out is to enter a
“good-until-canceled”(GTC)sell order on the stocks at a price you believe    has little chance of being transacted.For instance,ifyour stock is trading at
定向短期挤压
空头卖家还有更阴险的方式被挤压，称为强制买入。当大型多头持有 者希望对空头卖家造成最大损害时，他们会允许其股票被借出，直到 买家控制了趋势为止。如果一个持有股票多头头寸的机构，比如一百 万股，突然要求其借出的股票返还给该公司，借入这些股票的空头卖 家将陷入寻找新股票借入的困境。如果空头卖家无法找到新的股票借 入，他们必须购买他们卖空的股票。这种方法之所以有效，是因为其 冷酷无情的实施方式。实际上，多头持有者设下了让空头被挤压的陷 阱。没人说华尔街是个好地方。
股票借贷要约
当你购买股票时，你可以要求公司发行实际的股票凭证，但这很少见。 大多数投资者以“街名”方式购买股票，这意味着经纪公司为客户保  管股票以提供便利。经纪公司的一种收入来源是向客户出借股票以供  卖空。根据你购买股票的方式以及如何开设你的经纪账户，你可以允  许或禁止经纪公司出借你的股票给卖空者。如果你的股票在现金账户  中，经纪公司不能出借你的股票。如果你的股票在保证金账户中(因  此有质权协议),它允许经纪公司“质权”(借出)这些股票给可能  想建立卖空头寸的其他客户。经纪公司会向客户收取借入股票用于卖  空 positions   的费用。
一种防止你的多头仓位被借出的方法是，在你认为交易可能性很小的价格上， 对股票下达一个“有效至撤销”(GTC) 的卖单。例如，如果你的股票正在  以
$30,you enter a GTC sell order at $200.Because of the pending order to
liquidate  your  long  position  at$200,the  brokerage  firm  cannot  lend  out  the shares  in  your  account.
Two Types of Short Squeezes
People  often  call  any  short-term  stock  bounce  in  a  downtrend“a  short
squeeze."Most  quick  rallies  in  a  downtrend  include  short  sellers  covering their   positions   during,and   in   part,causing,the   rise.Not   all“short
squeezes"lead  to  a  continued  upside  price  increase.Below  we  examine  two different  types  of  short   squeezes;the  short-term  knee-jerk  squeeze,and
the  longer-term   structural   short   squeeze.
Knee-Jerk Short Squeeze
This  squeeze occurs in a longer-term downtrend with a large  short
position.When a stock in an established Stage 4 Decline is accompanied by a  large  short  position,short  sellers  are  in  control  of  the  trend.Their
accumulated profits make short sellers less likely to panic and cover at the first signs of a bounce.When prices are in a Stage 4 Decline,short sellers
can dig their heels in and  stay  short until their bearish opinion changes or, in the most severe down market,the stock becomes delisted in a
bankruptcy.Still,some  short  sellers  will  panic  and  cover  their  position after even a  small bounce.
Chart  10.7  shows  a  knee-jerk  short  squeeze.Notice  how,after  the  large  gap down  in  November,short  sellers  covered  some  of their  shares,which  you
can  see  in the  declining  short  interest.As the  stock  continued  lower  over
the next  few  months,short  sellers  became  emboldened  and  nearly  doubled  their  short  position(green  arrow).While  many  participants  try  to   "buy  the
$30的价格交易，你下达一个$200的GTC 卖单。由于存在在$200平 仓多头仓位的有效订单，券商不能借出你账户中的股票。
两种类型的短期挤压
人们通常将下行趋势中的任何短期股票反弹称为“短期挤压”。下行 趋势中的快速反弹通常包括空头在上涨过程中以及部分导致上涨的过 程中平仓。并非所有“短期挤压”都会导致持续的上行价格增长。下 面我们考察两种不同类型的短期挤压：短期本能挤压和长期结构性短 期挤压。
本能短期挤压
这种挤压发生在长期下行趋势中，存在大量空头头寸。当一只处于确 立的第四阶段下跌阶段的股票伴随着大量空头头寸时，空头控制着趋 势。他们累积的利润使空头在反弹的最初迹象出现时不太可能恐慌并 平仓。当价格处于第四阶段下跌阶段时，空头可以坚守立场，继续持 空，直到他们的看跌观点改变，或者在最为严重的熊市中，股票因破 产而退市。尽管如此， 一些空头在即使小幅反弹后仍会恐慌并平仓。
图10.7显示了一个膝跳式短空挤压。注意，在11月出现大幅下跌后，做空者卖 出了一些股票，这在不断下降的做空兴趣中可以看出。随着股票在接下来的  几个月里继续下跌，做空者变得更加大胆，并将他们的做空头寸几乎翻了一  番(绿色箭头)。虽然许多参与者试图“买入低点”,作为多头头寸，但做  空者知道没有所谓的“跌太多”。因此，他们继续持有他们的空头头寸。
dip,"as a long position,short sellers know there is no such thing as “down too much.”Therefore,they continue to hold their short position.
Stage 4 Decline stocks can experience quick and large rallies,but those short-term   bursts    typically   fail    as   longer-term    selling    pressure   is    too    strong to overcome.
.
Chart 10.7 This daily chart shows short interest increase,even on the short-term
bounce  in  February.Chart:Koyfin.com
Psychology:Trading against the trend
Stocks in a downtrend will attract “momentum short sellers”who pile on
extra shares of short stock after the short-term rallies.You may be tempted to buy the short-term rallies because they can result in quick trading gains. However,when the longer timeframe is lower,long purchases are very
risky trades.These short-term bounces are best left to the most risk-
tolerant traders who specialize in the shortest timeframes.The best course of action is to stay with the primary trend rather than fight them.
低点，”作为多头头寸，做空者知道没有所谓的“跌太多”。因此，他们 继续持有他们的空头头寸。
第4阶段跌势中的股票可能会出现快速且大幅的反弹，但这些短期爆发 通常失败，因为长期卖压过于强大，难以克服。
IM
图10.7这张每日图表显示了短期兴趣的增加，即使在2月份的短期反弹中也是如此。 图表：Koyfin.com
心理学：逆势交易
处于下跌趋势的股票会吸引“动量卖空者”,他们在短期反弹后会增 加卖空股票的数量。你可能会被短期反弹所吸引，因为它们可以带来 快速的交易收益。然而，当更长的时间周期较低时，长期买入是非常 冒险的交易。这些短期反弹最好留给最能够承受风险的交易者，他们 专门从事最短的时间周期。最好的做法是坚持主要趋势，而不是与之 对抗 。
Structural  Short  Squeeze                                                           结构性空头挤压
A second short squeeze is what I call a"structural short squeeze."It occurs when a stock in an established Stage 2 Uptrend has a large short position    that is"out of the money."
When we combine the price data along with the short interest trend of the short sellers,we can determine the approximate price level where the
short positions were initiated.We use this information to determine the "pain point"where the  short  sellers(in  the  aggregate)are  in  a  losing
position.
Once the average short seller is losing money,the stock is vulnerable to a   squeeze,and a subsequent increase in price.If most short positions were    initiated at lower levels,the growing losses in a rising stock motivate short sellers to reconsider their positions and purchase the stock.
When they cover their shorts,additional demand fuels the market,which adds further pressure to the average short seller.This type of squeeze
setup(Chart 10.8)can lead to substantial moves higher.This is based on the large number of short sellers who are wrong about the stocks price   decline.
The stock in Chart 10.8 shows an initial advance from(A)to(B).During that rally from$32 to $52,the short sellers remained stubborn about their view  ofthe stock,as shown by little change in the short position(blue arrow).
After the rally began to pullback,we anchor a AVWAP to(B).We can see the short sellers remained complacent and even added a few shares to their
bearish bets,to  11.7 million short shares.
第二种卖空挤压，我称之为“结构性卖空挤压”。它发生在处于已 建立的阶段2上升趋势中的股票有一个“亏损”的大卖空头寸时。
当我们结合价格数据以及卖空者的短期兴趣趋势时，我们可以确定卖空头 寸的初始价格水平。我们使用这些信息来确定卖空者(总体而言)处于亏 损状态的“痛点”。
一旦平均卖空者开始亏损，股票就容易受到挤压，并随后价格上涨。 如果大多数卖空头寸是在较低水平上开仓的，那么在上涨的股票中不 断增长的亏损会促使卖空者重新考虑他们的头寸并购买股票。
当他们平掉卖空头寸时，额外的需求会推动市场，这给平均卖空者  增加了更大的压力。这种挤压设置(图表10.8)可能导致大幅上涨。 这是基于大量卖空者对股票价格下跌判断错误。
图表10.8中的股票从 (A)  到 (B)   出现初步上涨。在从32美元上涨到52美  元的反弹期间，卖空者对其对股票的看法仍然固执己见，如卖空头寸(蓝色 箭头)变化不大所示。在反弹开始回撤后，我们将AVWAP  锚定在 (B)。
我们可以看到卖空者仍然complacent 甚至增加了几百万股卖空头寸，达到 1170万股。

The  stockin  Chart   10.9  shows  when  the  shorts  remained  stubborn.Focus  on (B),where  the  buyers  clearly  took  control  of  the   stock.We  knew  for  certain   the  buyers  were   in  control  from  that  peak(B)where   it  crossed  above  the
AVWAP  anchored  from  the  high(A).Short  sellers  who  increased  their position  from  3.9  million  to   12.3  million  shares  at  or  near(B)were  in   trouble  because  the  stock  was  above  that  AVWAP.
The  interesting  part   is  that  the  short  position   was  at  the  highest  level,13.7 million  shares,while  the  stock  broke  to  an  all-time  high(after  C).The
AVWAP(green)from  the  last  higher-low(C)was  rising  under  the  stock  as  it traded  in  a  tight  range.With  buyers  clearly  in  control  and  short  sellers  in  a  large  losing  position,this  is  the  type  of  stock  you  want  to  identify  as  a
structural    short    squeeze    candidate.
图10.9这张每日图表显示，随着股价上涨，卖空者并未减少其敞口。图：
Koyfin.com
图10.9中的股票显示，卖空者态度顽固。关注(B) 处，买方明显掌控了该股 票。我们从(B) 处的峰值(该峰值高于从高点(A) 锚定的AVW2AP)    就确定 买方掌控了该股票。在(B) 处或附近将头寸从390万股增加到1230万股的  卖空者遇到了麻烦，因为该股票高于那个 AVWAP。
有趣的是，空头仓位达到了最高水平，137万股，而股票突破历史新  高 (C 点之后)。从上 一 个更高低点 (C 点 ) 开 始 的AVWAP    (绿色) 在股票交易时呈上升趋势，且交易区间狭窄。在买方明显掌控局面而 空头在大幅亏损的情况下，这就是你想识别为结构性空头挤压候选股 的类型。
Here are some general points to help you determine the stocks that may become structural squeeze candidates:
1.Uptrend    on    the     daily    timeframe.At a minimum,the stock must be above the rising 50-day moving average.Stocks at or near all-
time highs are best because there is no real motivated source of
supply from holders looking to get out at break even,and allof the longs are in a winning position.If the stock is in a downtrend,it is  not a good squeeze candidate,as short sellers are in control and
have no reason for aggressive purchases.
2.Absence   of   any   hedging   vehicles.Some common ways for short sellers to hedge bearish bets are with options;a different class of
common  stock,warrants,convertibles,preferred  stock,or  any  other hedge products.If there is an inability to hedge against a short
exposure,it will leave the short seller in a more vulnerable position.
3.Short        interest should be high relative to average volume.The    higher the SIR,the greater the difficulty short sellers will have in purchasing  their  shares.
4.Level   of   potential    squeeze.Check to see the approximate level  that most shorts were initiated.We can approximate this with the AVWAP.When the stock rises above this level,the average short
seller is losing money.That makes the shorts exposed to a squeeze.
Stocks with double sources of demand(longs and shorts)and tight supply (especially if the stock is at or near an all-time high)can lead to excellent upside  trade  opportunities.
Short  sellers  are  usually  savvy  speculators.However,like  any  group  of market  participants,they  aren't  always  right. When shorts are wrong
以下是一些帮助你确定可能成为结构性挤压候选股的股票的一般要点：
1. 日线图上呈现上升趋势。至少，股价必须高于上升的50日移动 平均线。股价处于或接近历史最高位的股票最佳，因为持有人没 有实际的动力在盈亏平衡点时卖出，而且所有多头都处于盈利位 置。如果股价处于下跌趋势，则不是好的挤压候选对象，因为空 头在掌控局面，并且没有理由进行激进性购买。
2.缺乏任何对冲工具。空头为了对冲看跌赌注，常见的方法是使用期权； 不同类别的普通股票、认股权证、可转换证券、优先股票或任何其他对   冲产品。如果无法对空头敞口进行对冲，将使空头处于更脆弱的位置。
3. 空头仓位相对于平均交易量应较高。SIR 越高，空头在购买 其股票时将面临更大的困难。
4.潜在挤压水平。检查大多数空头最初建仓的大致水平。我们   可以用AVwaP  来近似估算这一点。当股价上涨超过这一水平时， 平均空头开始亏损。这使得空头面临被挤压的风险。
具有双重需求来源(多头和空头)且供应紧张(尤其是如果股票处 于或接近历史最高点)的股票可能导致绝佳的上行交易机会。
做空者通常是精明的投机者。然而，像任何市场参与者一样，他们 并不总是正确的。当做空者判断错误时
about the direction of a stock,their move to cover can lead to some
excellent trend opportunities for traders who can recognize the squeeze situation develop.
Telegram:@GroupBuys     Bot
关于股票的走势，他们的平仓行动可能为能够识别挤压情况形成
的交易者带来一些绝佳的趋势机会。
Telegram:@GroupBuys   Bot
KEY TAKEAWAYS·Short squeezes are motivated by short sellers who fear unlimited losses that  can  arise  from being  in  a  losing   position.·The  higher  the  SIR  is,the  more  difficult  it  is  to  exit  ashort  position  and  the  greater  the  upward  impact  will  be on price.I consider an SIR of 5 or greater to besignificant  enough  to  think  a  short  squeeze  could develop  in  the  stock.·Knee-jerk   short   squeezes   are   typically   short   lived.·Structural short squeezes can lead to longer-term uptrends.·We want to identify structural short squeeze candidates because  they  can  lead  to  dramatic  upside  moves  where  trend traders can profit.
KEY TAKEAWAYS
·Short squeezes are motivated by short sellers who fear unlimited losses that  can  arise  from being  in  a  losing   position.
·The  higher  the  SIR  is,the  more  difficult  it  is  to  exit  a
short  position  and  the  greater  the  upward  impact  will  be on price.I consider an SIR of 5 or greater to be
significant  enough  to  think  a  short  squeeze  could develop  in  the  stock.
·Knee-jerk   short   squeezes   are   typically   short   lived.
·Structural short squeezes can lead to longer-term uptrends.
·We want to identify structural short squeeze candidates because  they  can  lead  to  dramatic  upside  moves  where  trend traders can profit.
关键要点短期挤压是由做空者驱动的，他们担心在亏损头寸中可能 出现的无限损失。SIR 越高，退出空头头寸就越困难，对价格的上行影响  也越大。我认为SIR 达到5或更高就足以认为股票中可能 发展出短期挤压。突发性短期挤压通常持续时间较短。结构性短期挤压可能导致更长期的上涨趋势。我们想要识别结构性短多挤压候选对象，因为它们可 能导致剧烈的上行行情，趋势交易者可以从中获利。
关键要点
短期挤压是由做空者驱动的，他们担心在亏损头寸中可能 出现的无限损失。
SIR 越高，退出空头头寸就越困难，对价格的上行影响  也越大。我认为SIR 达到5或更高就足以认为股票中可能 发展出短期挤压。
突发性短期挤压通常持续时间较短。
结构性短期挤压可能导致更长期的上涨趋势。
我们想要识别结构性短多挤压候选对象，因为它们可 能导致剧烈的上行行情，趋势交易者可以从中获利。
CHAPTER 11
IPO TRADES WITH
THE AVWAP

"The IPO is the zero point for every
stock.”
—Brian Shannon
Chapter      Objectives
1.How AVWAP adds objective structure to IPOs

第11章
IPO交易与
AVWAP
“如果你知道‘零点’,你就可以测量任何事 情。”—W.D.Gann
“IPO 是每支股票的零点。”
—布莱恩 ·沙伦
章  节 目 标      
1.AVWAP 如何为IPO 添加客观结构
2.IPO   AVWAP从交易的第一分钟到多年都很有用 更晚
private company first sells shares of stock to the publicto raise capital.The A    process is known as the “Initial Public Offering”or "IPO."It is referred
to as “going public”because it is the first time the public can own a piece of the company through an offering on a public exchange.It is the“birth”of a  stock.
Initial Public offerings are a unique opportunity to study price action from the inception of a stock as a publicly traded company.Because there is a
defined starting point to anchor an AVWAP from,an IPO offers the purest look at supply and demand from a fixed starting point shared by all
participants.
Why Anchor to the IPO?
All IPOs start their life as a public company with a single trade.That first
trade is the “opening print”where all of the buy andsell orders are
matched.After that first print,the stock trades freely in the open market. The opening print is usually the largest volume of stock on a 1-minute
timeframe.The large volume of the opening print is the aggregate ofall the buy and sell orders.After the opening print,the stock trades like any other  stock,subject to the laws of supply and demand.
The AVWAP has been my primary analysis tool for IPOs since Ifirst began to experiment with it.Chart11.1 is a blog post from www.Alphatrends.net in
2007.
私人公司首次向公众出售股票以筹集资金。该过程被称为“首次公开 募股”或 “IPO” 。 它被称为“上市”,因为这是公众首次可以通过在公 开交易所的发行拥有公司的一部分。它是“股票的诞生”。
首次公开募股 (IPO)   提供了一个独特的机会，可以研究一只股票作为公开 交易公司时的价格行为。由于有一个明确的起点来锚定平均成交量加权平  均价格 (AVWAP),IPO     为所有参与者提供了一个从固定起点观察供需关 系的纯粹视角。
为何锚定IPO?
所有IPO 都以一家公开交易公司的形式开始其生命周期，并仅进行一 笔交易。这笔第一笔交易是“开盘成交”阶段，在此阶段所有买入和 卖出订单被匹配。在此第一笔交易之后，该股票在公开市场上自由交 易。开盘成交通常是一分钟时间框架内股票成交量最大的阶段。开盘 成交的成交量是所有买入和卖出订单的总和。开盘成交之后，该股票 像其他任何股票一样交易，受供需规律的影响。
自■开始尝试使用以来，AVWAP一直是我分析IPO的主要工具。图11.1是2007年来自 www.Alphatrends.net的一篇博客文章。
Since Coming Public

For the first couple of weeks,daily chart data is of little value without an
AVWAP.Ifyou trade  from  a  chart with  daily  data,wait  for  more  data  to  build to make sense of the chart.
Ifyou want to use the 50-DMA,you need to wait until the fiftieth day the stock trades.If you want to trade the first day the stock comes to life, look  at  intraday  charts  and  use  VWAP/AVWAP.

在最初的几周内，如果没有AVWAP,    每日图表数据几乎没有价值。如果你 从包含每日数据的图表进行交易，请等待更多数据积累以理解图表。
如果您想使用50日均线，您需要等到股票交易的第50天。如果您想交 易股票上市的第一天，请查看日内图表并使用VWAP/AVWAP。
Start Charting the Shortest Timeframes
I start my analysis of IPOs on the first day with a 1-minute chart.The 1-
minute chart allows me to see price action develop in real time.As the stock builds more price and volume data history,my analysis will move out from a 1-minute  timeframe  to  5-minutes,15,30,65  timeframes  andlonger.Of
course,it is always by using a multiple timeframe analysis where we find the most value.
The first trades of an IPO are similar to gap trades.There is a sudden
supply/demand shift,which becomes an important anchor point for the
stock.There is no subjectivity about where to set the anchor in an IPO.We set it from the first trade.
The following examples use several timeframes to emphasize how
important the IPO AVWAP is from the first trade of a new stock to several years after the IPO.
Chart 11.2 is a 1-minute timeframe,it begins the moment the stock traded through the end ofits first day as a public company.There are two
(A)VWAPs on this chart.The first VWAP(purple)is anchored to the first minute of trading.The second AVWAP(blue)is anchored to the second
minute of trading.
The stock was a "hot IPO,"which means there was a lot of demand right out of the gate.We know that because the stock immediately rallied so strongly that it triggered an exchange halt(1)after a quick rise of 10%.
开始绘制最短的时间框架
我会在第一天使用1分钟图表开始对IPO进行分析。1分钟图表让我能够实时  看到价格走势的发展。随着股票积累更多的价格和成交量历史数据，我的分 析将从1分钟时间框架扩展到5分钟、15分钟、30分钟、65分钟以及更长的时 间框架。当然，我们总是通过使用多时间框架分析来发现最大的价值。
IPO 的首笔交易与缺口交易相似。存在突然的供需转变，这成为股 票的重要锚点。在IPO  中设置锚点的位置没有主观性。我们从首笔 交易开始设置。
以下示例使用多个时间框架来强调新股从首笔交易到IPO  后数年， IPO  AVWAP的重要性。
图表11.2是一个1分钟时间框架，它从股票开始交易的时刻开始， 到其作为上市公司第一天的结束时。这张图表上有两个(A)
VWAP。  第一个 VWAP   (紫色)锚定于交易的第一分钟。第二个 AVWAP  (蓝色)锚定于交易的第二分钟。
该股票是一只“热门IPO”,    这意味着从一开始就有很大的需求。我们知道 这一点，因为该股票立即大幅上涨，引发了交易所暂停交易(1),涨幅在 10%之后迅速达到。

图表11.2一分钟图表。当一只股票首次作为IPO   开始交易时，锚定第一分钟和第二分钟 是有帮助的。图表：TC2000.com
当五分钟内发生10%或更多的波动时，纳斯达克会暂停股票交易几分钟。 从第一分钟开始，AVWAP   显著落后于该股票，直到当天结束。
如果你等待开盘价回调至AVWAP,    你会错过这次行情，因为它从未 触及第一分钟AVWAP    (紫色)。如果你知道从第二分钟锚定，而第 二分钟并未包含所有开盘量，你就会有机会
to purchase  the  stock  on  two  occasions(2  and3)as  the  stock  tested  and  then rallied away from the second minute AVWAP(blue).Stops for these buys would be placed below the low at the blue arrows.
Graduate to Multi-Day AVWAPS
Chart 11.3 continues to build on the stock from Chart 11.2.
This is the same stock as Chart  11.2,two days after the IPO.This chart is  constructed with 5-minute data.The circled area shows how the AVWAP from the IPO found buyers on the day three as the stock opened on a gap down.
It will surprise you how often buyers or sellers congregate near the IPO
AVWAP,even years after the stocks come public.Institutions will often buy  on pullbacks to the IPO AVWAP,so we want to be ready to act in that area as well.After day one of an IPO,it is no longer necessary to anchor from the
second minute as the divisor increases and the impact of the  first-minute trades    lessens.
在两次(2和3)购买股票的机会，因为股票测试并从第二分钟AVWAP (蓝色)反弹。这些买入的止损位将放在蓝色箭头的低点下方。
晋升至多日AVWAPS
图表11.3继续基于图表11.2的股票构建。
这是图表11.2的同一股票，IPO 后的两天。这张图表使用5分钟数据构建。 圆圈区域显示了IPO  AVWAP如何在第三天找到买家，因为股票以向下   跳空开盘。
你会惊讶于买家或卖家在IPO   AVWEAP附近聚集的频率，即使股票 上市多年也是如此。机构通常会在回调至IPO    AVWAP时买入，因此 我们也想在那个区域做好准备。 IPO 的第一天后，不再需要从第二分 钟作为基准，因为随着除数的增加，第一分钟交易的影响减弱。

Two  days  later,the  stock  rallied  to  the  IPO  AVWAP(2).After  it  moved

两天后，该股票上涨至IPO      AVWAP(2)。在它穿过该区域的供应后， 它在AVWAP(3)      上方形成了一个更高的高点。这将是一个低风险的入 场点，初始止损位在最新的相关更高低点(4)下方。
当该股票上涨超过每股13美元时，就是时候将止损位提高到(5)下方。在   (6)处，止损位(5)被跌破并止损出局。当然，有长期目标的人可能不会  设置如此紧密的止损位，而更厌恶风险的交易者可能设置了更紧密的止损位。

Here is an example of the first three days of trades for an IPO with 10-

second day(2)and the day after that(3).With the benefit of hindsight,we
can see a purchase(2 or 3)would have worked,but the better buys were(A, B).These were better buy levels because the stock had upward momentum   and a stop could go below the pullback low.A look at the one-minute chart    on the open of day two and day three would have been the best opportunity to purchase this  stock with  a"second-day"entry technique.

The IPO AVWAP anchored(1)in Chart11.6 was briefly undercut(2)before   the stockbroke to a new high(3).A purchase(3)would make sense with a   stop below the low(2).There are several higher-lows(discussed below),so the stop should have been raised to protect the gains over the following

In Chart11.7 we see a stock that was trapped under its IPO AVWAP for months.
The stock in Chart 11.7 looked like it would be a successful IPO for the first few days,since it opened near the low of the day(1)and closed wellabove  the  IPO  AVWAP  for  the  first  few  days.
It broke below the IPO AVWAP(2)but recovered(3).At(3)it looked like
buyers had control again,but it didn't last long,and the  stock broke below (2)and  made  a  lower-low(4).This  is  where  we  have  confirmation  that
sellers   established   their   dominance(4).
