Chart 11.7 Daily chart with IPO AVWAP as resistance.Chart:TC2000.com
Over the next  11  months,the stock rallied up to the IPO AVWAP(5,6,7,and 8)and sellers maintained control as the stock failed to close back above the  IPO AVWAP.As downward pressure accelerated away from the AVWAP,
there  were  excellent   short   sale   opportunities(A,B,C)with  protective   stops above   the   preceding   highs(5,6,and7).
Chart 11.8 shows how the IPO AVWAP flipped from Resistance to Support and then back to Resistance.Chart  11.8  is constructed of weekly candles.
Some people prefer to look at longer timeframes with fewer data points for "less noise."With one week being  five days,there  are  fewer candles to
represent  the  same  data.As  with  alltechnical  analysis,the  IPO  AVWAP concepts  are the  same  on  all  timeframes.
The  anchor  is  set  to  the  first  candle(1)ofan  IPO,regardless  of the
timeframe.Over the next three weeks,the  stock remained below AVWAP until(2)where  it  could  have  been  purchased  with  a  stop  under(A).
As the  stock progressedhigher,it  found buyers  on pullbacks to the IPO AVWAP(3 and 4).
图表11.7日线图，IPO AVWAP 作为阻力位。图表：TC2000.com
在接下来的11个月里，股票上涨至IPO     AVWAP(5,6,7 和8),而卖方维  持控制权，因为股票未能收于IPOAVWAP   上方。随着下行压力加速远离  AVWAP,  出现了绝佳的做空机会(A,B,C),     并设置了保护性止损位在之前 的高点(5,6和7)上。
图表11.8展示了IPO    AVWAP 如何从阻力位变为支撑位，然后又回   到阻力位。图表11.8由周K线构成。有些人更喜欢查看时间跨度更长、 数据点更少的时间框架，以减少“噪音”。由于一周有五天，因此用   更少的K线来表示相同的数据。与所有技术分析一样，IPO
AVWAP   的概念在所有时间框架上都是相同的。
锚点设置为IPO 的第一根K线(1),无论时间框架如何。在接下来的三 周内，股价一直保持在AVWAP  下方，直到(2)处，此时可以在 (A)
下方设置止损买入。
随着股价上涨，它在IPOAVWAP(3     和4)的回调位找到了买家。

The  IPO AVWAP  can be useful  four  years  after the  stock  comes  public.Chart 11.9  is  constructed  of  weekly  candles,showing  nearly  three  years  of  trades  for  the  stock.We  set  our  anchor  to  the  first  week  of  the  IPO(1).After  five
weeks  below  the  IPO  AVWAP,the  stock  was  a  good  buy(2)when  it  cleared the IPO AVWAP and cleared the prior week high.
The  stop  on  this  long  would  be  placed(A)and  then  raised  up  under  the  low  of(3)where  the  stock  bounced  from  the  IPO  AVWAP.At(4)the  long  position would be  stopped  out  as  the  stock  made  a  lower  low.

图11.9这是三年每周的时间框架，带有IPO  AVWAP。图：TC2000.com
IPO AVWAP 在股票上市四年后可能很有用。图11.9由每周的蜡烛 图构成，显示了该股票近三年的交易情况。我们将锚点设置为 IPO
的第一周(1)。在IPO AVWAP下方五周后，当该股票突破IPO AVWAP  并突破前一周高点时，它是一个很好的买入点(2)。
在这个长线上的止损将被放置在(A),  然后抬升至(3)的低点下方，这是股票 从 IPO    AVWAP反弹的地方。在(4)处，随着股票形成更低低点，多头头寸  将被止损平仓。
A couple of weeks later,the stock broke below the prior week low(5).This would have been a good place to enter a short position with a stop above   (B).If a trader progressively lowered the stops tojust above the lower-
highs,the short would have been stopped out(6).This is where the stock broke above the IPO AVWAP and above the prior week high.
A couple of months later,the stock pulled back,and found buyers,at the IPO AVWAP(7),which had been set over 2 years prior.
At(8)the stock cleared the prior week high after it successfully defended  the IPO AVWAP.A purchase(8)made sense with a stopjust under the low (7)
Historical IPO Example
Chart 11.10.Weekly chart with daily detail inset.Chart:Finance.Yahoo.com
Google(Alphabet)Inc.came public in 2004.The daily Chart 11.10 shows the first year of trades in the stock.The inset shows greater detail of the first
几周后，股票跌破上周低点(5)。这将是进入空头头寸并设置止损在 (B) 上方的好地方。如果交易者逐步将止损降低到略高于更低高点， 空头头寸将被止损平仓(6)。这是股票突破IPO   AVWAP和上周高  点的地方。
几个月后，股价回落，找到了买家，在两年前设定的IPO  AVWAP(7) 处。
在(8)处，股价成功守住了IPO  AVWAP,并清除了上周的高点。在低点
(7)下方设置止损位的买入(8)是合理的。

Google(Alphabet)Inc.于2004年上市。每日图表11.10显示了该股票交 易的第一年。插图显示了第一年的更多细节。
couple weeks of trades.
The AVWAP starts on the first day of the IPO(1).On day 7 of trading(see
inset)the  stock undercut the IPO AVWAP(2)and it would have made  sense to be stopped out there since sellers were in control.
About two weeks later,the stock climbed back above the IPO AVWAP(3).A new long purchase could be made here with a worst-case stop below the   low(A).
It wasn't until six months later,that the stock tested the IPO AVWAP(4).
For those who didn't already own the  stock it made  sense to purchase(5)as it rallied away from the AVWAP.A stop on this purchase,and any existing   long position,would go under the low(4).The stock has been one of the
great stocks of all time.
几周的交易。
AVWAP 在首次公开募股(IPO) 的第一天(1)开始。在交易的第7天(见插 图)时，该股票跌破IPO    AVWAP(2),因此在此处停止交易是有道理的， 因为卖方当时占据主导地位。
大约两周后，股票回升至IPO    AVWAP(3)  以上。在这里可以进行新的多
头买入，止损位设在低点 (A) 以下。
直到六个月后，该股票才测试了IPOAVWAP(4)。    对于那些还没有
持有该股票的人来说，在它上涨远离 AVWAP   时购买(5)是有道理的。 如果停止这次购买，以及任何现有的多头头寸，将会跌破低点(4)。
该股票是有史以来最伟大的股票之一。

KEY TAKEAWAYS·IPOs are obvious anchor points.·From the first minute of trades to several years later,the IPO AVWAP proves to be a valuable reference point.·Buyers and sellers will make decisions that lead to the    formation of Support and Resistance at the IPO AVWAP.·As with other strategies,the IPO AVWAP is not the only valuable anchor point on the stock.·Use the knowledge from previous chapters to find theother anchor points that are suitable for your timeframe and risk tolerance.·Ifyou want to trade a stock on its IPO day you need to use a  VWAP.·On the first day of an IPO,anchor an AVWAP at thesecond   minute   of   trading   for   objective   analysis   without the noise of the first minute opening print trade.
KEY TAKEAWAYS
·IPOs are obvious anchor points.
·From the first minute of trades to several years later,the IPO AVWAP proves to be a valuable reference point.
·Buyers and sellers will make decisions that lead to the    formation of Support and Resistance at the IPO AVWAP.
·As with other strategies,the IPO AVWAP is not the only valuable anchor point on the stock.
·Use the knowledge from previous chapters to find the
other anchor points that are suitable for your timeframe and risk tolerance.
·Ifyou want to trade a stock on its IPO day you need to use a  VWAP.
·On the first day of an IPO,anchor an AVWAP at the
second   minute   of   trading   for   objective   analysis   without the noise of the first minute opening print trade.
关键要点IPO  是明显的锚点。从交易的第一分钟到几年后，IPOAVWAP     证明是一个有 价值的参考点。买方和卖方将做出决策，导致在IPO    AVWAP处形成支 撑和阻力。与其他策略一样，IPO    AVWAP不是股票上唯一的宝贵 锚点。使用前几章的知识，找到适合你时间框架和风险承受能 力的其他锚点。如果你想在首次公开募股当天交易一只股票，你需要使用VWAP。在IPO 的第一天，在交易的第二分钟锚定一个AVWAP,以便进行客观分析，避免第一分钟开盘时的噪音交易。
关键要点
IPO  是明显的锚点。
从交易的第一分钟到几年后，IPOAVWAP     证明是一个有 价值的参考点。
买方和卖方将做出决策，导致在IPO    AVWAP处形成支 撑和阻力。
与其他策略一样，IPO    AVWAP不是股票上唯一的宝贵 锚点。
使用前几章的知识，找到适合你时间框架和风险承受能 力的其他锚点。
如果你想在首次公开募股当天交易一只股票，你需要使用VWAP。
在IPO 的第一天，在交易的第二分钟锚定一个AVWAP,
以便进行客观分析，避免第一分钟开盘时的噪音交易。
IN CLOSING
"Man's mind,stretched to a new idea,
never goes back to it's original
dimension."
—Oliver Wendell Holmes Jr.
What will you do with this information?It is my hope that you recognize the power and flexibility of the Anchored VWAP for innumerable timeframes
and setups in the markets.
There is no wrong way to use what I've laid out for you.Iexpect some

APPENDIXA:
THE FOUR STAGES
OF MARKET STRUCTURE
All trade strategies should be based on a solid comprehension of market
structure.There is a definite cyclical flow of money in and out of assets and we can observe this rhythm on charts of all timeframes.Graphic A-1 is a
reference to the various  stages  ofa  stock's  life  cycle.For  a  high-definition downloadable electronic copy of this please see page 234.
Stage     1     Accumulation  refers to the period when a  stock has no trend,it
trades sideways.It occurs after a drop in prices.It is the process of buyers
附录 A: 市场结构 的四个阶段
所有交易策略都应基于对市场结构的深刻理解。资金在资产之间有明 确的循环流动，我们可以在所有时间框架的图表上观察到这种节奏。 图 A-1 是股票生命周期各个阶段的参考。要获取此高清可下载的电
子副本，请参阅第234页。
第一阶段积累是指股票没有趋势，它横盘整理的时期。它发生在价格下跌之 后。这是买方
gaining control from sellers.We know it is in Stage 1 only after the buyers    have regained control of the stock and it enters a Stage 2 Uptrend.Until it is in uptrend,it is a trendless market that should be avoided by trend traders.
Stage     2     Markup(Uptrend)is the bullish phase for stocks or markets. The markup stage is an uptrend,as defined by higher-highs and higher- lows.This is the time to be long.Stocks in uptrends are considered to be  “innocent until proven guilty.”
Stage    3     Distribution.After a prolonged advance,sellers will start to
overwhelm the buyers.This causes the stock or market to turn sideways.  We know that it is Stage 3 only after a decline has begun.Until the decline begins,it is just a neutral period that should be avoided by trend traders.
Stage    4     Decline(Downtrend) is the bearish phase of a stock's life.This is when to be on the lookout for short sale opportunities.The Decline stage is  defined by lower-lows and lower-highs.Stocks in downtrends are
considered“guilty until proven  innocent.”
从卖方手中获得控制权的过程。只有在买方重新控制股票并进入第二阶段上 升趋势后，我们才知道它处于第一阶段。在进入上升趋势之前，它是一个无 趋势的市场，趋势交易者应避免。
阶段2标记(上升趋势)是股票或市场的看涨阶段。标记阶段是 上升趋势，由更高的高点和高低点定义。这是做多的时候。处于 上升趋势中的股票被认为是“无罪，直到被证明有罪。”
阶段3配送。在一段长时间的上涨后，卖方将开始压倒买方。这会导致 股票或市场横盘整理。只有在下跌开始后，我们才知道这是阶段3。在 下跌开始之前，这只是一个中性的时期，趋势交易者应避免。
阶段4下跌(下跌趋势)是股票生命周期的看跌阶段。这是需要警惕 短期卖空机会的时候。下跌阶段由更低低点和更低高点定义。处于下 跌趋势的股票被认为是“有罪直到被证明无罪”。

总而言之，我们想要：
*避免横盘中性时期、阶段1累积和阶段3分配。
*在趋势更高的市场中做多，阶段2溢价/上升趋势。
*保持简短或避免趋势较低的市场，阶段4衰退/下跌。
Trend Formation                                                            趋势形成
The direction of the expansions and contractions forms trends on a chart.A move  in  the  trend's  direction  on  a  higher(longer-term)timeframe  is
referred  to  as   an  “impulse  wave.”In  the   short-term,countertrend  moves are     calleda“pullback¹ .”
The rally high is called the“swing high”and the pullback low is known as  the“swing  low.”The  trend's“legs  or  thrusts"will  see  an  expansion  of  the range higher,followed by a contraction of the range in the corrective leg.  These are show in charts A-2 and A-3.
Trade with the Trend
When  a  stock  has  higher-highs(HH)and  higher-lows(HL)it  is  in  an
uptrend.Only  in  retrospect,after  prices  pull  back   fromeach  peak,can  we identify the HH.
Chart  A-2  shows  three  higher  thrusts,represented  by  the  green  arrows.   The  red  arrows  show  the  “corrective  waves”or  pullbacks.Keep  in  mind,a pullback  only  occurs  in  a  primary  uptrend.Stocks  in  downtrends  are
considered"guilty  until  proven  innocent,"and  should  be  avoided  by  long traders.
扩张和收缩的方向在图表上形成趋势。在更高(更长周期)的时间框 架内，沿着趋势方向的运动被称为“脉冲波”。在短期内，逆势运动 <i>1</i>被称为“回调。”
顶部反弹称为“摆动高点”,回调低点被称为“摆动低点。”趋势 的“腿或推动力”将看到范围向更高处扩张，然后在修正腿中范围 收缩。这些在图表A-2 和A-3 中显示。
顺应趋势交易
当一只股票有更高的高点 (HH)   和更高的低点 (HL)    时，它处于上升趋 势中。只有在价格从每个峰值回调后，我们才能回顾性地识别HH。
图 表A-2 显示了三个较高的推力，由绿色箭头表示。红色箭头显示了 “修正浪”或回调。请记住，回调只在主要上升趋势中发生。处于  下降趋势的股票被认为是“无罪直到被证明有罪”,应避免由长线  交易者交易。

The     very      definition     of     a      trend     is      what      gives     us     the      most      compelling     reason

Therefore     the      best      odds     for      profitability      lie      in     trading      in      the     direction      of     the primary              trend.

趋 势 的 定 义 正 是 给 我 们 成 为 趋 势 交 易 者 的 最 有 力 理 由 。 上 升 趋 势 由 一 系   列HH       和  HL      标 记 。 这 意 味 着 涨 势 的 总 和 将 大 于 跌 势 的 总 和 。 因 此 ， 盈 利 的 最 佳 机 会 在 于 顺 着 主 要 趋 势 进 行 交 易 。
注 意 ， 图 表A-2   上 的 最 后 一 个 高 点 旁 边 有 一 个 问 号 。 随 着 趋 势 转 变 为 修 正 模 式 ， 我 们 不 知 道 它 是 否 会 是 高 点 ， 或 者 是 否 会 直 接 失 败 并 反 转 趋 势 。
Just like Support and Resistance,we know only after the fact if it will be a higher-low,sowe wait for evidence of a turn back higher before we
consider a purchase.If the stock does turn back up,the most recent low is known as the “swing low.”
Regardless of the timeframe,from years using the weekly chart down to
just one day using a one-minute chart,the behavior ofa stock in an uptrend is the same.The uptrend action looks like a staircase,with prior levels of
Resistance that act as Support for price.
The opposite is also true for downtrends that are defined by a series of
lower-highs  andlower-lows.Chart  A-3.illustrates  how,in  a  downtrend,the sum of the declines will be greater than the sum ofthe rallies.

就像支撑位和阻力位一样，我们只有在事后才知道它是否会是更低 的高点，因此我们会等待更高反转的证据再考虑购买。如果股票真 的反转上涨，最近的高点被称为“摆动低点。”
无论时间跨度如何，从使用周线图多年的情况，到仅使用一分图一天的 短期情况，上升趋势中的股票行为都是相同的。上升趋势的动作看起来像楼 梯，先前的阻力位成为价格的支持位。
对于由一系列低高点(lower-highs) 和低低点 (lower-lows) 定义的下跌 趋势，情况也是如此。图表A-3说明了在下跌趋势中，下跌总和将大于上涨  总和。

Price and Time Corrections
Markets alternate between periods of price advancement in an uptrend, and price contraction as it consolidates the decline in a downtrend.The
expansion of the price range uses up a lot ofenergy and the market needs to “rest.”The rest period can occur by a price pullback or a sideways,
“correction through time.”
A time correction is a stronger candidate for a trend to continue higher
than a price correction.The lack of a deeper price pullback in a time
correction indicates a continued strong bid for shares.A deeper price
correction shows a less agressive bid for the stock.Regardless of how a
correction occurs,it is a chance for the stock to rebuild energy and accept or reject new prices.
It is considered more bullish when a stock corrects through time(as shown in Chart A-4 with the green shaded areas)than a price pullback(indicated  by the red arrows).A price correction is still bullish as long as a HLis
formed.Both time and price corrections should be monitored for evidence of buyers regaining control so we can make a low-risk purchase in the
direction of the primary trend.
图表A-3这张图表由每日价格蜡烛线构成。它显示了下跌趋势中的低高点( lower-highs)    和低低点 (lower-lows) 。  图表：TradingView.com
价格和时间修正
市场在上升趋势中交替出现价格上涨期，并在下降趋势中通过巩固 下跌趋势出现价格收缩。价格区间的扩张消耗了大量能量，市场需 要“休息”。休息期可以通过价格回调或横盘整理，“通过时间进 行修正”来实现。
时间修正比价格修正更有可能是趋势继续走高的强有力候选者。在时间修 正中缺乏更深的价格回调表明对股票的持续强劲需求。更深的价格修正则 显示出对股票的较不积极的需求。无论修正如何发生，它都是股票重建能 量和接受或拒绝新价格的机会。
当股票通过时间修正(如图表A-4中的绿色阴影区域)而不是价格回调 (由红色箭头指示)时，被认为更看涨。只要形成了一个HL,  价格修 正仍然是看涨的。应同时监控时间和价格修正，以寻找买家重新掌控  的迹象，以便我们可以在主要趋势的方向上进行低风险买入。

Chart  A-4  Price  vs.Time  Corrections:The  green  areas  show  a  time  correction,whereas
the  red  arrows  show  price  corrections  in  an  uptrend.Chart:TC2000.com
The opposite action unfolds for a stock in a downtrend,as seen in Chart A-5.
On Chart A-5,time corrections in a downtrend(red shaded areas)are   considered vulnerable because they show a lack of aggressive demand. Weak bidders for the stock are eventually overwhelmed and the stock   continues  lower.The  price   corrections(green  arrows)are  short-term  rallies which end up in failure as the longer-term downtrend prevails.

APPENDIX B:
MULTIPLE
TIMEFRAMES
Telegram:@Group
AVWAP is a primary part of my analysis,which I integrate into my multiple timeframe analysis.Time is one of the few variables that we can control in  our pursuit of market profits.Of course,we cannot control time itself,but    we can control our entries and exits and the length of time we choose to
hold our trades or investments.
The period oftime that we allow our market activities to work for(or
against)us is completely subjective.Whether you are a day trader,long-   term investor,or somewhere between,the goal is to always cut our losers and hold our winners.The most effective way to achieve this goal is to
B 附录：多时 间框架
Telegram:@Gro
AVWAP   是我分析的主要部分，我将其整合到我的多时间框架分析  中。时间是我们追求市场利润时可以控制的少数变量之一。当然，我 们不能控制时间本身，但我们可以控制我们的入场和出场，以及我们 选择持有交易或投资的时间长度。
我们允许市场活动为我们(或反对我们)发挥作用的时间是完全主 观的。无论你是日内交易者、长期投资者，还是介于两者之间，目 标始终是止损并持有盈利。实现这一目标最有效的方法是
listen objectively to the message of the market.This is accomplished through  technical  analysis.
Often,the message of the market will be one of confusion,and that is an
important message to recognize.If there is no clear trend or potential trade setup,the message of the market is clear,“be patient,cash is a position.”
We may want to constantly be engaged in the market,but it is better to
observe and wait for the “fat pitch”trade to set up before getting involved in a new trade.
Choose Your Timeframe
One of the most important aspects to your success in the markets is to
identify and stick to a timeframe that is best suited to your personality.
Some people are more attracted to day trading in-and-out of highly volatile stocks,while others may be more interested in a buy and hold approach.
I am not the first person to observe that the number of trades one makes will typically decrease over the number of years that you are in the
markets.The fact is some people are great day traders and that is where they should focus there energy.There are many excellent long-term
investors and that shouldbe their focus.The bottom line is to find the timeframe that works best for you.
Many traders use a combination of timeframes for different strategies.This is how bond managers must work.They diversify their timeframes by the
purchase of 2,5,10,20-years and longer maturities.They are forced to trade various timeframes.Do what works for you and go slow until you figure out the timeframe that is most suitable for you.
客观地倾听市场的信息。这是通过技术分析实现的。
通常，市场的信息会是混乱的，而这是一个重要的信息需要识别。如 果没有明显的趋势或潜在的交易设置，市场的信息是明确的，“保持 耐心，现金是一种头寸。”我们可能想要不断地参与市场，但最好观 察并等待“肥美的投注”交易设置好后再参与新的交易。
选择你的时间框架
对你市场成功最重要的方面之一是识别并坚持最适合你性格的时间框 架。有些人更倾向于日内交易波动性很大的股票，而其他人可能更感 兴趣于买入持有策略。
我不是第一个观察到一个人所做的交易数量通常会随着你在市场 中的年数而减少的人。事实是一些人是伟大的日内交易者，那就 是他们应该集中精力的地方。有许多优秀的长期投资者，那应该 是他们的焦点。底线是找到最适合你的时间框架。
许多交易者使用不同的时间框架来执行不同的策略。这是债券经理必 须这样做的方式。他们通过购买2年、5年、10年、20年及更长期限  的债券来分散时间框架。他们被迫交易各种时间框架。做对你有效的 事情，慢慢来，直到你找到最适合你的时间框架。
Only you can know the best timeframe for your personality,and you will
likely make a lot of mistakes as you figure it out.A long-terminvestor uses the longer-term market exposure to smooth out returns.This requires a
tolerance  for  short-term  volatility.Shorter-term  traders  attempt to  exploit the volatile periods for quicker returns and need to make quick and
accurate  decisions.Because  of their  shorter  timeframe  focus,shorter-term traders can experience a fullcycle of emotions in a single market session    that will take longer-term investors years to experience.This leaves
shorter-term traders more vulnerable to costly,emotional decisions.
Timeframe Considerations
·Are you a fast thinker or  slower thinker?
·Can you quickly observe and objectively make decisions or do you get panicked when you must act on shorter timeframes?
·Are you a slower,methodical participant who must plot and plan each  detail?
·What  suits  your  personality  best?
·What is your capital base?People with small accounts may feel    they have to be more active while larger account holders may be more  patient.
·How much time do you have to commit to the markets?
We need to use even-sized bars/candles for accurate analysis.A common   mistake made in technical analysis is to use timeframes where there are an uneven number of periods each day.
只有你能知道最适合你性格的时间框架，在弄清楚之前，你很可能会犯很多 错误。长期投资者使用长期市场敞口来平滑回报。这需要容忍短期波动性。 短期交易者试图利用波动性时期来获得更快的回报，并且需要做出快速准确 的决策。由于他们的短期时间框架关注，短期交易者在单个市场会话中可能 会经历完整情绪周期，而长期投资者需要数年才能经历。这使得短期交易者 更容易做出代价高昂的情绪化决策。
时间范围考量
你是快速思考者还是较慢思考者?
你能快速观察并客观地做决定，还是当你必须在较短时间范围内 行动时你会感到恐慌?
你是较慢、有条理的参与者，必须规划并计划每个细节吗?
什么最适合你的个性?
你的资本基础是多少?小额账户的人可能会觉得他们必须更活跃， 而大额账户持有者可能会更有耐心。
你有多少时间可以投入到市场?
我们需要使用偶数大小的条形图/蜡烛图进行准确分析。技术 分析中常见的错误是使用每天周期数不等的周期。
This approach unfairly weighs one period over the others and therefore
skews any technical tools we use in our analysis.Take the example with a   chart constructed of 60-minute data(the hourly timeframe.)The market is  open from 9:30 a.m.to 4:00 p.meach day,which is a total of 6.5 hours,or 390 minutes.Ifyou were to use a chart constructed of hourly bars(candles)you would see 7 periods on the chart,but this would not accurately reflect the
price action.If we are to do any analysis of data,we need to make sure we
have a consistent data set,ifthe first period was just 30 minutes(9:30-10:00 a.m.)and the rest were 60 minutes(10:00-11:00,etc.)the data would be
flawed.It would be like measuring a standard 12-inch foot with 1
measurement of 1 centimeter and the other  11measurements with inches. When you add those 12 units up,it does not equal12 inches.
To obtain equal measurement of price and volume data in our analysis,the number of minutes per candle used must all be divisible into 390.I've
demonstrated this in Table B-1.

这种方法不公平地权衡了一个周期而忽略了其他周期，因此会扭曲我 们分析中使用的任何技术工具。以一个由60分钟数据(即小时周期) 构建的图表为例。市场每天从上午9:30开盘到下午4:00收盘，总计
6.5小时，或390分钟。如果你使用由小时条形图(蜡烛图)构建的图 表，你会看到图表上有7个周期，但这并不能准确反映价格走势。如  果我们要对数据进行任何分析，我们需要确保我们有一个一致的数据 集，如果第一个周期只有30分钟(9:30-10:00),而其余周期都是
60分钟(10:00-11:00等),数据就会出错。这就像用1次1厘米的测量 值和11次英寸的测量值来测量一个标准的12英寸脚一样。当你把这

Timeframe Confusion
Trend trades may seem easy when you see a stock in a strong uptrend.
Many participants  fail  to understand that  a  stock  can  have  multiple trends on  different  timeframes.They  only  see  the  longer-term  upward  trajectory  of the stock and overlook and any strong pullbacks in the uptrend that can  result  in  quick  losses.
The remedy to this conflict is to analyze multiple timeframes together for a more  complete  picture.
A stock in a longer-term uptrend over the last year may be in a downtrend  over the last 2 weeks and may have just begun to turn higher on a shorter-
表B-1说明  之间的关系
时间范围混淆
趋势交易在看到一只股票处于强劲上升趋势时可能看起来很容易。
许多参与者未能理解一只股票可以在不同的时间范围内有多个趋势。 他们只看到股票的长期上升趋势，而忽略了上升趋势中可能导致的  快速亏损的任何强劲回调。
解决这一冲突的方法是分析多个时间段，以获得更全面的图景。
过去一年处于长期上升趋势的股票在过去两周可能处于下降趋势，并且可能 刚刚开始在一个较短的时间框架内转向上涨。
term timeframe.These conflicting trends can create timeframe confusion or an emotionally driven purchase of a stock after a longer-term move is well   underway.The purchase of a stock that has already moved in the near term  makes it more difficult to control risk.
Focus on the Trend,not the Label
The media is always focused on whether we are “in a bull or bear market.”A swing trader's job is to make money regardless of market conditions.While   most stocks will trade in-line with the trends of the overall market,there
are always exceptions.Even in the strongest bull markets there are periods of weeks to months where the overall environment does not favor new
purchases of stocks.
In the "bearish-periods”of a bull market,it doesn't make sense to buy
stocks that are in near-term downtrends.It is better to either stay on the
sidelines in cash and protect your capital or to make tactical short sales.
Just the same,in a bear market,some of the fastest short-term moves occur on the upside.Trading these rallies is a risky strategy and only the most
skilled traders should attempt to take advantage of these countertrend
moves.Whenever atrade is taken against the direction of the primary
trend,it should be done with smaller risk in position size and less overnight exposure.
这些相互冲突的趋势可能导致时间框架混淆，或者在长期趋势已经明 显的情况下因情绪驱动而买入股票。在短期内已经发生波动的股票的 买入使得控制风险更加困难。
关注趋势，而非标签，
媒体总是关注我们是否“处于牛市或熊市”。波段交易者的工作是在  任何市场条件下赚钱。虽然大多数股票会与整体市场的趋势一致交易， 但总有例外。即使在最强劲的牛市中，也有几周到几个月的时间，整  体环境并不利于购买新股票。
在牛市的“熊市时期”,购买处于短期下跌趋势的股票没有意义。 最好要么保持现金在场外保护你的资本，要么进行战术性短卖。同样， 在熊市中，一些最快的短期行情发生在上涨方面。交易这些反弹是一  种高风险策略，只有最熟练的交易者才应该尝试利用这些逆势行情。  每当交易与主要趋势相反时，应该在仓位规模上使用较小的风险，并  减少隔夜敞口。

As we know,stocks in downtrends are considered“guilty until proven
innocent,"which means we do not trust the rally attempts.It is common for inexperienced traders to get excited about a large move higher with a stock in a downtrend.These are typically"sucker rallies"as they make a lower-    high in the short-term trend and then roll back over with a new wave of
shares sold by fearful sellers.

图B-3一只从上升趋势转为下降趋势的股票的30分钟图表。图表：TC2000.com
众所周知，处于下跌趋势的股票被认为是“有罪直到被证明无罪”, 这意味着我们不信任反弹尝试。对于缺乏经验的交易者来说，看到处 于下跌趋势的股票出现大幅上涨而感到兴奋是很常见的。这些通常是 “诱多”行情，因为它们在短期趋势中形成一个较低的高点，然后又 因恐慌性卖盘而回落。
The stock in Chart B-2 experienced several strong rallies in the downtrend. The three highlighted sucker rallies even made it up through the declining AVWAP anchored to the peak,but they failed to break the downward trend.
In Chart B-3,a closer examination on the 30-minute timeframe ofthe last
rally above the AVWAP shows the better trade opportunity was to short the stock at the green highlighted area where the stock made a lower-low
below the AVWAP anchoredto the start ofthe rally.
Price Targets
Once I have determined if it looks like there is potential for profit relative
to the perceivedrisk,I prefer not to stay focused on a price "target,"but to   "listen"to the stock to tell me when to exit.Many people focus too much on  an upside target and tell the market what they want for a profit.As a result, they fail to listen to the message of the market.The market does not honor   target requests and a profitable trade can turn into a loser if we stubbornly  wait for the stock to hit our target.
Once I have determined my risk/reward ratio,my price targets are   "higher"for  longs  and  “Lower”for  shorts.Ourjob  is  to  listen  to  the  market,adjust,and  raise  our  stops  to  protect  our  gains  as  the  price progresses  in the trend.
Multiple Timeframe Analysis
Our analysis should begin with a chart constructed of daily price history for the last year or so.This timeframe is simply to make sure our trade
candidate is in a primary uptrend(for longs)or downtrend(for shorts).We
图表B-2中的股票在下跌趋势中经历了多次强劲反弹。三个被高亮的诱多行 情甚至使其突破了锚定在峰位的下降AVWAP, 但它们未能打破下跌趋势。
在图表B-3中，对最后一个高于AVWAP  的30分钟时间段的更仔细检 查显示，更好的交易机会是在绿色高亮区域做空股票，该区域在
AVWAP  下方形成了一个更低低点，而AVWAP  锚定在涨势的起点。
价格目标
一旦我确定了相对于感知风险是否有盈利潜力，我更倾向于不专注于 一个价格“目标”,而是“倾听”股票告诉我在何时退出。许多人过 于关注一个上行目标，并告诉市场他们想要的利润。结果，他们未能 倾听市场的信息。市场不承认目标请求，如果我们固执地等待股票触 及我们的目标，一个盈利的交易可能会变成亏损。
一旦我确定了风险/回报比率，我的价格目标对多头是“更高”, 对空头是“更低”。我们的任务是倾听市场，调整，并在价格在 趋势中推进时提高止损以保护我们的利润。
多时间框架分析
我们的分析应从过去一年左右的时间构建的每日价格历史图表开始。这个时 间段只是为了确保我们的交易候选者在主要上升趋势(对于多头)或下降趋 势(对于空头)中。我们
want  to  be  sure  there  aren't  any  large  potential  levels  of  Resistance  or Support nearby that might slow or halt the momentum.
Trend Alignment
We want to get involved in the stock as the intermediate-term trend(days to weeks)comes “into alignment”with the longer,more powerful trend.   This approach allows us to enter the longer-term trend as the
intermediate-term trend develops.When the trends of various timeframes move  in  the  same  direction,they  are  “aligned.”The  goal  is  to  find  the  ideal point ofentry,set our initial stop-loss,and then to manage our winners.    Many  of  the  strategies  we  have  explored  are  guided  by  this  very  concept.   The strategies section covered the use of shorter timeframes to fine tune   our   entry   points.
Multiple  timeframe  trend  alignment  gives  us   a  greater  confidence  of  trend continuation  and  that  allows  us  to  be  more  aggressive  in  our  position  size. Determination  of the  size  of  a  trade  is  based  largely  on  where  we  enter  a
trend  and  how  we  can  control  our  perceived  risk.Besides  the  location  of  our trade   entry,other   reasons   to   adjust   position   size   would   include;overall
market conditions,news risk such as upcoming earnings reports or a Fed meeting,and even our own personal well-being.
To become proficient at trend alignment strategies,make it a habit to look   at  stocks  on  multiple  timeframes  to  gain  a  better  comprehension  of  how  the timeframes   flow   together.Observe   how   trends   from   shorter   timeframes
coexist,interact,and build upon,the longer-term market structure.One tenet of technical analysis is,"a trend once established is more likely to
continue than reverse.”The long-term trend is the sum of many shorter-   term trends,therefore,we need to wait for evidence the trends are back in alignment  before  we  get  involved.
想要确保附近没有可能的大型阻力或支撑水平，这些水平可能会减缓或 停止动量。
趋势对齐
我们希望在中期趋势(几天到几周)与长期、更强劲的趋势“对齐”时参 与股票。这种方法允许我们在中期趋势发展时进入长期趋势。当不同时间 框架的趋势朝着同一方向移动时，它们就是“对齐”的。目标是找到理想 的入场点，设置初始止损位，然后管理我们的盈利。我们所探索的许多策 略都受到这一概念的指导。策略部分涵盖了使用较短时间框架来微调我们 的入场点。
多重时间框架趋势对齐让我们对趋势延续有更大的信心，这使我们能 够更激进地调整仓位大小。交易的规模主要基于我们入场趋势的位置 以及我们如何控制感知风险。除了交易入场位置，调整仓位大小的其 他原因还包括：整体市场状况、新闻风险(如即将到来的盈利报告或 美联储会议),甚至我们自己的个人福祉。
要精通趋势对齐策略，养成在多个时间框架下观察股票的习惯，以更   好地理解时间框架如何相互流动。观察较短时间框架的趋势如何共存、 互动和相互构建，形成长期的市场结构。技术分析的一个原则是，
“ 一旦确立的趋势更有可能继续而不是反转。”长期趋势是许多短期 趋势的总和，因此，我们需要等待趋势重新对齐的证据出现，才能参 与其中。
The Longer-Term and the 50-Day Moving Average
“When in doubt,zoom out”
~J.C.Parets
Always be aware of the longer timeframe,even ifyou do not plan to hold a stock for a long while.The longer-term trends should be respected as it
takes a lot ofenergy in the opposite direction to reverse them.Defer to the longer and more powerful trend ifin doubt.If the long-term trend is up,
give the benefit of doubt to the bulls and vice versa.Longer timeframes    offer greater opportunity for profit,while shorter-term timeframes offer the  fastest(more  seductive)opportunity to turn  a  quick profit.
If you cannot find clarity on a longer timeframe,interpret it as the market   telling you to avoid the stock for now.Cash is a position.When uncertainty reigns,cash affords you the objective position to wait for your signals for a low-risk entry.As you get better at timelier entries with multiple
timeframes,your profitability increase,and you will also find satisfaction from not buying a stock that continues lower.
A quick and easy reference point to determine the primary trend is the
slope of the 50-day moving average(“DMA”).If the stock is above a rising 50-DMA,consider it“innocent until proven guilty”and therefore is a
candidate for a long trade.If the stock is below a 50-DMA that is sloped
lower,it is “guilty until proven innocent.”Avoid these latter stocks from
the long side or consider them as a candidate for a short sale.When a stock crosses above and below a flat 50-DMA,it shows us a trendless stock that
offers no advantage for a long or short sale.The message of the market is
clear in these instances,these stocks shouldbe avoided.The direction of
the 50-DMA is an efficient way to be sure we know the trend of the stock on the longer timeframe.
长期趋势与50日移动平均线
“不确定时，缩小范围”
J.C.Parets
始终关注长期周期，即使你并不打算长期持有股票。长期趋势应受到 尊重，因为反向逆转它们需要大量能量。如有疑问，应顺应长期且更 强大的趋势。如果长期趋势向上，则对多头有利，反之亦然。长期周 期提供了更大的盈利机会，而短期周期则提供了最快(更具诱惑力) 的快速盈利机会。
如果你在长期周期上无法找到清晰信号，可以将其理解为市场在告 诉你暂时避免该股票。现金也是一种头寸。当不确定性笼罩时，现 金为你提供了客观的立场，让你等待低风险的入场信号。随着你在 多时间周期下更好地把握入场时机，你的盈利能力将提高，你也会 发现不买入持续下跌的股票带来的满足感。
确定主要趋势的一个快速且简单的参考点是50日移动平均线(“
DMA”)    的斜率。如果股票高于一条上升的50-DMA,   就考虑它
“无罪，直到被证明有罪”,因此是长线交易的候选对象。如果股票  低于一条斜率向下的50-DMA, 它就是“有罪，直到被证明无罪”。  避免从多头方面持有这些后者的股票，或者考虑它们作为卖出候选对  象。当一只股票在一条平坦的50-DMA 上方和下方穿越时，它显示出  一只无趋势的股票，这对长线或短线交易都没有优势。在这些情况下， 市场的信息是明确的，这些股票应该被避免。50-DMA  的方向是一种  有效的方法，可以确保我们知道股票在较长时间框架内的趋势。
All moving averages should be used as a reference point to compare price
trends.They should not be considered as automatic levels to do business
when they are touched,but rather as a reason to observe the price action
on a shorter-term timeframe,where we formulate a plan.We generally give the benefit of doubt to buyers when the 50-DMA trend is higher and to the    sellers when the slope is lower.Note,the charts are for the same stock;on    the left Chart B-4 shows the weekly moving average over a 10-week period,  while Chart B-5 is the 50-day moving average.The increased detail in Chart B-5   arises   from   that    fact   that   there   are    are   five   trade   days   per   week.

我们通常对买家持有利态度，而当斜率较低时，我们对卖家持有利态 度。注意，这些图表是同一只股票的；左侧的图表B-4显示了10周期  的周移动平均线，而图表B-5是50日移动平均线。图表B-5中细节的增 加是由于每周有五个交易日这一事实 。

Once we have identified the trend on the daily timeframe,the next step is
to analyze the intermediate-term timeframe for clues of a possible low-risk, high-probability trade  set up.
Intermediate-Term and the 5-Day Moving Average
An intermediate-term timeframe helps us to determine if there is a trade
setting up in a low-risk manner.This timeframe allows us to enter the stock as price momentum comes into alignment with the longer timeframe.For
the intermediate-term trend,I prefer to use a 30-minute timeframe(for a   period of approximately 25-40 days)with a 5-day moving average(5-DMA) as a trend reference point in a similar way to how we use the 50-DMA on a  daily timeframe.

一旦我们在日线图上确定了趋势，下一步就是分析中期时间框架，寻 找可能的低风险、高概率交易机会。
中期时间框架和5日移动平均线
一个中期时间框架帮助我们判断是否以低风险的方式正在建立交易。 这个时间框架允许我们在价格动能与较长时间框架一致时进入股票。 对于中期趋势，我倾向于使用一个30分钟时间框架(大约25-40天的 时间段),并使用5天移动平均线(5-DMA)   作为趋势参考点，就像 我们使用日线图上的50-DMA 一样。
Note:Do not confuse the 5-day moving average with a 5-period moving
average.You cannotjust set the moving average to “5”on any timeframe
and see the 5-DMA.It is a 5-DMA only when the chart is constructed of daily candles.The only time you will observe a true 5-DMA on a daily timeframe   is when the market is closed;prior to the close it will only be four full days   plus whatever part of the day has elapsed since the open.To compensate
for this,I never look at the 5-DMA on a daily timeframe,only on shorter (intraday)timeframes.Here is how we accomplish this.

Notice that the location of the moving average for the same stock on
different timeframes is in the same location and has the same slope.We
want to keep our analysis consistent across various timeframes,so we
convert the daily moving average to intraday timeframes with this handy
table(B-7).
As noted earlier in the chapter,the market is open 390 minutes per day.
Over five days it is open for 1,950 minutes.For example,if we look at the
market on a 65-minute timeframe,that means we want to use a 30-period    moving average to replicate the average over the last 5 days(1,950 minutes

The breakdown below outlines how we want to analyze the intermediate-    term trends to plan our trade.When a stock is in a longer-term uptrend,we then   look   to   a   shorter   timeframe   for   trend   alignment.

为多头组合时间周期
下方的分解概述了我们如何分析中期趋势以规划我们的交易。当一只股票处 于长期上升趋势中时，我们会转向较短的时间框架来寻找趋势一致性。
Stage    1     Accumulation.This is where we plan our trades.We observe,  analyze,and   ANTICIPATE   the   point   where   buyers   will   take    control.This    is the time to assess our price objectives and stop levels to determine our
plan of action for when the stock gives us a reason to get involved.This is  when we want to answer;where has the stock come from and where it has the potential to go?Then we can determine if there is a sufficient
risk/reward ratio setting up tojustify the purchase of a new long trade.If the 5-DMA is in decline,or beginning to flatten out,that is a clue to leave   our activities to analysis and not take action at this stage.
Stage     2      Markup(Uptrend).As the stock makes a short-term higher-
high,which is in alignment with the longer-term uptrend,we want to buy the   stock.This   is   when   we   PARTICIPATE   in   what   appears   to  be   a
continuation of the uptrend on the longer-term timeframe.Stage 2 is also   where we manage our winners by raising the stop tojust under successive higher-lows as the stock rallies.This is the fun part.The 5-DMA should be   flat or starting to advance at this stage.We generally want to buy the stock as it makes it's first higher-high on this timeframe.
第一阶段：积累。这是我们规划交易的地方。我们观察、分析并预  期买方将掌控市场的时刻。这是评估我们的价格目标和止损位，以 确定当股票给我们参与的理由时我们的行动计划的时候。这时我们 需要回答：股票来自何方，以及它有潜力去哪里?然后我们可以确 定是否存在足够的风险/回报比来证明建立新的多头交易的合理性。 如果5-DMA正在下降，或者开始变得平缓，那是一个线索，提示我 们暂时将活动留给分析，而不是在这个阶段采取行动。
阶段2标记(上升趋势)。当股票形成一个短期更高高点，且与长
期上升趋势一致时，我们想要买入该股票。这是我们参与看似是长期 时间框架上上升趋势延续的时候。阶段2也是我们通过将止损位提
高到连续更高低点下方来管理盈利的时候。当股票上涨时。这是有趣 的部分。5日均线在这一阶段应该是平缓的或开始上涨。我们通常希 望在它在这一时间框架上形成第一个更高高点时买入该股票。

Stage  3  Distribution.This is when the stock shows signs offatigue and   may precede a price pullback,or it may need a “correction through time.” This is a good point to EXIT the position,or at least sell some to lock in
partial  profits,and  tighten  the  stop  on  the  balance,rather  than  continue  to expose our capital to risk.The angle of ascent of the 5-DMA will slow down   or  begin  to  turn  sideways  at  this  point.

阶段3分配。这是当股票显示出疲态并可能预示着价格回调，或者它 可能需要“通过时间进行修正”的时候。这是一个退出头寸的好点， 或者至少卖掉一些以锁定部分利润，并收紧剩余头寸的止损位，而不 是继续让我们的资本暴露于风险中。5日均线的上升角度在这一点会 放缓或开始走平。

Stage 4 Decline(Downtrend).Once the definition of a trend(higher-
highs and higher-lows)no longer exists on the timeframe when we entered the stock,there is no reason for a swing trader to continue to hold.When
the primary trend is higher,it is likely that the breakdown of price into an intermediate-term downtrend is the start of a pullback,not a longer-term  reversal.This means that the odds do not favor profitable short sales.It is  better to AVOID these stocks and look for better setups elsewhere.

阶段4下跌(下跌趋势)。一旦我们进入股票时的时间框架上不再存 在趋势的定义(更高的高点和高低点),就没有理由让摆动交易者继 续持有。当主要趋势向上时，价格分解为中期下跌趋势很可能是回调 的开始，而不是长期反转的开始。这意味着机会并不倾向于盈利的短 线卖出。最好避免这些股票，并在其他地方寻找更好的设置。
在图表B-8中我们看到日线图(50-DMA),    而在图表B-9中，相同的数据以65
分钟时间为单位(5天/30周期MA)。  应 该
be easy to see why the use of more than one timeframe allows us much
greater  accuracy to  determine  where the trend  of the  daily  and  intraday
timeframes  become   aligned.The  numbers   on  the   chart(B-9)are  the
shorter-term  trend.Notice  on  the  65-minute  timeframe,substages  can  be   skipped by the stock,we always give the benefit of the doubt to the longer- term   timeframe.
Combine Timeframes for Shorts
The approach to short sales is the exact opposite.We start with a  Stage 4 (Decline)stock  on  the  daily  timeframe  and  then  look  to  the  intermediate- term timeframe in this way:
Stage     1      Accumulation.This  is where we  exit  our  short  sale trades.This   is when the stock shows signs of fatigue.It may precede a price bounce,or it may need a “correction through time.”This is a good point to EXIT the
position or at least buy some back to lock in partial profits and tighten the  stop  on  the  balance,rather  than  continue  to  expose  our  capital  to  risk.The angle of descent of the 5-DMA will slow down or begin to turn sideways at    this  time.
Stage      2       Markup(Uptrend).Once  the  definition  of  a  trend(lower-highs and  lower-lows)no  longer  exists  on  the  timeframe  we  entered  the  stock,
there is no reason for a swing trader to continue to be short.When the
primary trend is lower,it is likely that the breakout of price into an
intermediate  term  uptrend  is  the  beginning  of  a  bounce,not  a  longer-term  reversal.This means the  odds  do  not  favor  profitable  short  sales.It  is  better to AVOID these stocks and look for better setups where trends are coming    into  alignment  on  the  downside.
很容易看出为什么使用多个时间单位能让我们更准确地确定日线图
和日内时间单位的趋势何时一致。图表 (B-9) 上的数字是短期趋势。 注意在65分钟时间单位上，股票可以跳过子阶段，我们总是倾向于   相信长期时间单位。
合并短期时间段
短期卖出的方法正好相反。我们从日线图上的阶段4(衰退)股票 开始，然后以这种方式查看中期时间段：
阶段1积累。这是我们退出短期卖出交易的地方。这是股票显示出疲态的时候。 它可能预示着价格反弹，或者它可能需要“通过时间进行修正”。这是一个   退出头寸或至少买回一些以锁定部分利润并收紧余额止损的好时机，而不是   继续让我们的资本暴露于风险中。此时，5-DMA的下降角度将放缓或开始走   平。
阶段2标记(上升趋势)。 一旦我们进入的股票的时间框架上不再存   在趋势(低高点和小低点)的定义，那么就没有理由让波段交易者继   续做空。当主要趋势向下时，价格突破到中期上升趋势中很可能只是   反弹的开始，而不是长期反转。这意味着盈利做空的机会不大。最好   避开这些股票，寻找更好的设置，在这些设置中，趋势正在向下趋同。
Stage    3    Distribution. This is when the stock shows signs of fatigue and
may precede a price decline.In the short-term stage 3,we observe,analyze, and   ANTICIPATE    the    point   where    sellers    willtake    control.This   is   the    time
to assess our price objectives and stop levels to determine our plan of    action when the stock gives us a reason to get involved.This is when we want to be sure we have answered;where has the stock come from and  where it has the potential to go?We can then determine ifthere is
sufficient risk/reward ratio setting up tojustify a short sale trade.
Stage     4     Decline(Downtrend).As the stock makes a short-term lower-  low,which is in alignment with the longer-term down-trend,we want to    sell   the   stock   short.This   is   when   we   PARTICIPATE   in   what   appears   to   be   a continuation of the downtrend on the longer-term timeframe.Stage 4 is
also where we manage our winners by lowering the stopjust above successive lower highs as the stock declines.This is the fun part.
The 5-DMA should be flat or starting to decline at the start of this stage and we generally want to short the stockas it makes its first lower-low on this   timeframe.
阶段3分配。这时股票显示出疲态，并可能预示着价格下跌。在短期  阶段3,我们观察、分析和预期卖家将掌控局面的时刻。这时我们需   要评估我们的价格目标和止损位，以确定当股票给我们参与的理由时  我们的行动计划。这时我们需要确保我们已经回答了：股票来自何方， 以及它有可能去哪里?然后我们可以确定是否存在足够的风险/回报
比来证明做空交易的合理性。
阶段4下跌(下跌趋势)。当股票形成一个短期更低低点，且与长期 下跌趋势一致时，我们想做空该股票。这是当我们参与看似是长期  时间框架下跌趋势延续的阶段。阶段4也是我们通过将止损位设置在 连续更低高点之上来管理盈利的时候。这是有趣的部分。
在进入这个阶段时，5-DMA 应该保持水平或开始下跌，我们通常希 望在它在这个时间框架上形成第一个更低低点时做空该股票。

当日线图上的主要趋势较低时，我们避免做多并考虑做空。右侧的 65分钟图显示了我们在子阶段中想要采取的各种行动点。当短期趋 势与长期趋势一致时 ， 我们希望参与做空 。
Steps for Multiple Timeframe Analysis                                                      多时间框架分析步骤
1.Identify the stock as a long or short candidate with the daily
timeframe.Do not fight the direction of the 50-day moving average.
2.Consult  the  intermediate-term  timeframe  to  establish  whether  the
potential profit is worth the perceived risk.Do not fight the direction of the 5-day moving average.
3.  Consult a shorter timeframe to fine tune the entry.
Multiple Timeframe Analysis Checklist
·Be aware of the trends on multiple timeframes.
·Are the trends aligned or do they show confusion?
·How do timeframes fit together,or do they diverge?
·The greater the number of timeframes you study to confirm the trend,the greater the probability that your trade will succeed.
·Price  action that moves  against the larger timeframe tends to reverse back into alignment.
·Use a minimum of three different timeframes for analysis.
There is a tendency for traders to feel as if they must be continually
engaged in an active position,but when there are mixed trend signals
across various timeframes,it is best to have a more cautious stance until trends align and show lower-risk entries.Cash is a position.
1.使用日线图识别股票是做多候选还是做空候选。不要与50日移动平 均线的方向作对。
2.咨询中期时间框架，以确定潜在利润是否值得所感知的风险。 不要与5日移动平均线的方向作对。
3.咨询较短时间框架以微调入场。
多时间框架分析检查清单
*注意多个时间框架上的趋势。
*趋势是否一致，还是显示出混乱?
*时间框架如何契合，或者它们是否背离?
*—你研究的时间框架越多，用来确认趋势，你的交易成功的可 能性就越大。
*价格走势若与较长的时间框架相悖，往往会反转至一致。
*至少使用三个不同的时间框架进行分析。
交易者有一种倾向，感觉必须持续保持活跃仓位，但当不同时间框 架出现混合趋势信号时，最好保持更谨慎的态度，直到趋势一致并 显示出较低风险的入场点。现金也是一种仓位。
Timeframe   Transition                                                                            时间框架转换
Common wisdom says to stick to the timeframe you intended at the onset of your trade,and  for  good  reason.All  too  often,short-term  traders  will  find  a   reason  tojustify  hanging  onto  an  unprofitable  trade  longer  than  originally   planned.Similarly,someone who  intends  to  hold  a  stock  for  the  long-term
should fight the urge to take a quick profit.
The only time you should allow a short-term trade to be transitioned to a
longer timeframe is if the stock is in a profitable position and you can still
manage risk for the trade.It is acceptable to  start  a trade as a day trade,and when the stock moves in your favor,take some of the risk off with the sale
of a piece ofit and then hold the balance for gains into the next day or
coming  days.For  a  longer-term  investor,the  only  reason  to  cut  the  trade early is to protect  capital ifthe  story has  changed  or  ifthe  stop-loss  is
violated.
The decision to hold longer than expected should be made from a position of strength,not  weakness.We  always  want  to  protect  capital  first  and  then
maximize the gains if the market allows it.
It is said that bulls and bears make money and pigs get slaughtered.I have updated  that  phrase  to;“Bulls  and  bears  make  money,greedy  pigs  get
slaughtered,and  disciplined  pigs  get  rich.”Ifyour  goal  is  large  gains,do  it in a disciplined way.
“Simplicity    is    the    ultimate
sophistication.”
-Leonardo    da    Vinci
普遍的观点是说要坚持在交易开始时你打算的时间框架，这是有充分 理由的。短期的交易者往往会发现一个理由来证明他们应该比原计划 更长时间地持有亏损交易。类似地，打算长期持有股票的人应该抵制 快速获利冲动。
只有在股票处于盈利位置且你仍能管理交易风险时，才应该允许短期 交易过渡到更长的时间周期。可以以日内交易的方式开始交易，当股 票走势有利时，通过出售部分头寸来降低风险，然后持有剩余部分以 获取次日或未来几日的收益。对于长期投资者而言，提前平仓的唯一 理由是如果市场情况发生变化或止损被触发，以保护资本。
决定持有时间超出预期应该基于强势而非弱势。我们始终要优先保护 资本，如果市场允许，再最大化收益。
据说牛熊赚钱，猪被宰割。我更新了这个说法为：  “牛熊赚钱，贪 婪的猪被宰割，自律的猪变富。”如果你追求大幅收益，就要以自 律的方式去做。
“简单即是终极的复杂。”
-列奥纳多 ·达 ·芬奇

Exhaustion Gap
A continuation gap is also known as a running or
measuring  gap.We  find  these  gaps  in  stocks  where  there   is an established trend that likely began with a breakaway gap.Because  the  trend  already  exists,these  gaps
represent  a  continuation,and  often  an  acceleration,of  the trend.
Exhaustion  gaps  occur near the  end  of a major trend.The stock will reverse the direction of the gap and close at the extreme    lower-end.
A gap down occurs when the daily open price is lower than the  previous  day's  close.
A gap up occurs when the daily open price is higher than the  previous  day's  close.
The placement of a new anchor points to establish a new AVWAP is to measure the acceleration of a trend.

A  trader  or  investor  owns  a  financial  position  they  expect to  increase   in   value.

The effect a buyer or seller has on the price of the market where  they  are  involved.
A securities dealer who commits to buy or sell at specified times  and  prices.

A price move that is counter to the primary trend,but is not  strong  enough  to  reverse  the  trend.
The R-Multiple is the amount that you profited or lost in
terms of your initial risk(e.g.if your initial risk is $100 and you gained $250,your profit is 2.5R).
For the US  stock market,it refers to the trade hours of the NYSE and NASDAQ,9:30 a.m.to 4 p.m EDT,excluding stock  market   holidays.

我们交易是为了赚钱。价格是成功的客观衡量标 准。价格行为最受关注。在技术分析中。 -价格是 我们唯一 能赚钱的东西。

与主要趋势相反的价格变动，但不足以逆转趋势。
R倍数是指您相对于初始风险所获得的利润或亏损金额(例如， 如果您的初始风险是$100,而您获得了$250,则您的利润是   2.5R)。
对于美国股市，它指的是纽约证券交易所和纳斯达克的交易时 间，即东部时间上午9:30至下午4:00,不包括股市假日。

overwhelm    the    buying(demand)and    prices     "resist"going higher.

Rip
Refers to a short-term,quick rally in a downtrend.
指在下跌趋势中的一次短期、快速反弹。
Setup
A trade plan that has a predetermined entry point,an approximate  price  objective  and  a  stop  loss  level.
设置.
一个具有预定入场点、 一个
大致价格目标和止损水平的交易计划。
Short Interest(SIR)
The number of shares sold short(short interest)for an    individual  stock,divided  by  its  average  daily  trade  volume over  the  previous  two  weeks.
卖空余额 (SIR)
某证券卖空的股份数量(卖空余额)。 个股，除以其平均每日交易量
在过去的两周内。
Short Position
The sale of a stock that is not owned by the seller.Traders with  a  short  position  expect  the  stock  to  decline  in  price.
卖空头寸
出售由卖方不拥有的股票。交易者
持有空头头寸的预期股票价格将下跌。
Short Squeeze
A  short  squeeze  develops  when  those  who  sold  the  stock   short,with  the  expectation  it  would  continue  to  decline  in price,change their minds about the trade and attempt to  cover  their  position  before  the  market  advances  and  they  accumulate   large/larger   losses.The   occurrence   of   a
rapidly  rising  stock  price  with  a  large  short  interest  is known as a short squeeze.
卖空挤压
当那些做空股票的人改变主意，试图在市场上涨之前平 仓，并积累巨大/更大的损失时，就会发生空头挤压。
快速上涨的股票价格伴随着巨大的空头头寸的发生被称 为空头挤压。
Market Structure Chart:
Stage1-Accumulation
Neutral  period  of  a  stock  that  is  preceded  by  the  decline.
The  early  part  of  this  stage  is  the  time  to  exit  short
positions.The  later  part   of  this  stage  is  when  we  anticipate and  plan  new  long  trades.
市场结构图：
阶段1-累积
股票的中性期，该期由下跌preceded 。  这个阶段的早期 是退出空头头寸的时间。这个阶段的后期是我们预期和  计划新的多头交易的时间。
Stage 2-Markup (Uptrend)
The  phase   of  a  stock  where  prices  rise.These   stocks   are
defined  by  higher-highs  and  higher-lows.This  is  when  we participate  in  long  trades  and  avoid  short  sales.
阶段2-涨价, (上升趋势)
股票上涨的阶段。这些股票由更高的高点和高点定义。 这是我们参与多头交易并避免空头卖出的时候。
Stage  3-Distribution
Neutral  period  of  a  stock  that  is  preceded  by  an  Uptrend.
阶段3-分配
一只股票的中性期，该期之前是上升趋势。
Stage  4-Decline (Downtrend)
Stop Loss
Trend  Alignment
5-DMA
50-DMA
This is when to exit long positions and plan for new short positions.
The phase of a  stock where prices decline.These  stocks   are  defined  by  lower-highs  and  lower-lows.This  is  when we avoid long trades and participate in short sales.
A type of order which is used to limit the loss in a stock position.
Use  of  multiple  timeframe  analysis;longer-term  to  identify trend  and  shorter-term  to  make  timing  decisions  to  enter   the  trend  at  a  low-risk,high-probability  point.
5-Day Moving Average.The simple moving average as seen  on  intraday  charts.
50-Day Moving Average.The average closing price of a stock over the last 50 days.

ACKNOWLEDGEMENTS
When you have been involved in a business that you have a great passion for as long as Ihave,30+years,you pick up a lot of knowledge from books, articles,and conversations with people.I have done my best to
acknowledge the large number of people who have had a positive influence on my career and have expanded my knowledge of the financial markets.It  is my sincere hope that I have not missed anyone or that Ihave
inadvertently given credit to the wrong person.
Prior to handing this book over to my editor,my wife Leanne helped make
the writing so much easier to understand with her reminders that,while
these concepts are second nature to me,I needed to explain concepts more   thoroughly.She also did ALOT of the “heavy lifting”of the editing,this book would be a disaster without her.
I was quite naive when I thought my book was finished prior to handing it over to my wonderful editor Tamela Rich.I had never heard of
"developmental editing"before seeing her in action.She helped me
organize the manuscript in its present form,then brought together a great team of people who helped with the design,layout,proofing,and all the
things that make a good book great.
致谢
当你像我这样，在一个你充满极大热情的行业里工作了□ 年，你就   会从书籍、文章以及与人们的交谈中获得很多知识。我已经尽力感谢  了那些对我的职业生涯产生积极影响并扩展了我对金融市场知识的人。 我真诚地希望我没有遗漏任何人，或者无意中把功劳给了错误的人。
在将这本书交给我的编辑之前，我的妻子Leanne  帮助使写作更容易 理解，她提醒我，虽然这些概念对我来说是常识，但我需要更详细地 解释这些概念。她还做了大量的“重活”编辑工作，如果没有她，这 本书将是一场灾难。

VWAP(pronounced   Vee-Wap   not   Vee-Wop,wink)was   in   a   conversation
with Jay Woods at a CMT Symposium in NYC in 2016.He encouraged me and provided  useful  feedback  along  the  way.Thank  you  Jay.
Another  early  supporter  was  Jared  Blikre  of  Yahoo  Finance.I'm  not  sure  he
thought this book would actually get written.There were times I had my doubts   too.
Tommy  Thornton  was  a  great  resource  for  information  about  how  a  multi- billion  dollar  hedge  fund  uses  the  Anchored  VWAP.
It  was  the  early  work  of the  late  Dr.Paul  Levine  that  became  the  basis  for    much  of today's  Anchored VWAP  analysis.His  work was  clearly  ahead  of its time.As it is said,we stand on the shoulders of giants,and Dr.Levine is the true forefather of this analysis.

Chartered  Market  Technician,Brian  Shannon  has  been  a  securities
professional  for  over  three  decades.He  developed  and  applied  the  little-  known AVWAP theory to his daily trading and has used the AVWAP since  the  early 2000s.He has been instrumental in getting this  analysis tool  on nearly  a  dozen  charting  platforms.
Brian  is  an  internationally  recognized  expert  in  technical  analysis,with  a focus  on  shorter-term  timeframes.He  has  taught  tens  of thousands  of
traders to become better traders with his highly acclaimed book,Technical Analysis Using Multiple Timeframes(over 18,000 copies sold),and on his
twitter    channel    Twitter.com/Alphatrends
As  a  consistently  profitable  trader,he  founded  Alphatrends,
www.Alphatrends.net,a  service  dedicated  to  market  analysis  and  education for swing traders.Today Brian continues to offer a daily masterclass on the  use of the AVWAP in his videos for Alphatrends.net subscribers.For those
who do not subscribe to Alphatrends,you can benefit from his free Friday videos   on  YouTube.com/Alphatrends
Brian lives in Colorado,where he and his wife Leanne(and dog Zinzan)lead an active lifestyle enjoying all the outdoor activities of their home state.
twitter.com/Alphatrends
特许市场技术师，布莱恩 ·沙伦 (Brian    Shannon) 已有三十多年 的证券专业经验。他开发并应用于日常交易的鲜为人知的
AVWAP 理论，并在21世纪初开始使用AVWAP 。 他在将这一分析 工具应用于近十种图表平台方面发挥了关键作用。
布莱恩是国际公认的技术分析专家，专注于短期时间框架。他通过备受赞  誉的书籍《多时间框架技术分析》(销量超过18,000册)以及他的推特频  道Twitter.com/Alphatrends, 已向数万名交易者传授了如何成为更好的 交易者。
作为一名持续盈利的交易者，他创立了Alphatrends,
www.Alphatrends.net,        一个专注于波段交易者市场分析和教育的服务。 如今，布莱恩继续在Alphatrends.net     订阅者的视频课程中提供每日大师班， 讲解AVWAP的使用方法。对于未订阅Alphatrends   的人，可以在
YouTube.com/Alphatrends      上免费观看他的周五视频。
布莱恩住在科罗拉多州，在那里他和妻子莉安(以及狗Zinzan)   过着积极的生活 方式，享受他们家乡的所有户外活动。
